WP 或 WT 必须以该身份行事，以分配给其直接合作伙伴、受益人或所有者或包含在其直接合作伙伴、受益人或所有者的分配份额中的可报告金额。 WP 或 WT 可以以该身份行事，将可报告金额分配给非美国非豁免接收者的间接合作伙伴、受益人或所有者（包含在其分配份额中的美国非豁免接收者除外），或包含在其分配份额中。第 4 章美国收款人的预扣税率池）。担任该职务的 WP 或 WT 必须承担第 3 章和第 4 章主要预扣税款的预扣责任，并且必须对其美国合作伙伴、受益人和所有者承担某些报告要求。如果某个 WP 或 WT 已向您提供_[文件](#en_US_2024_publink1000224819 "Documentation")_（稍后讨论）表明其充当此类金额的 WP 或 WT，则您可以将 WP 或 WT 视为收款人。

See Revenue Procedure 2017-21, 2017-6 I.R.B. 791, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21), for more information on becoming a WP or WT.  
有关成为 WP 或 WT 的更多信息，请参阅收入程序 2017-21、2017-6 IRB 791（可在[IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21)上获取）。

_**WP agreement and WT agreement.**_

The WP agreement and WT agreement and the application procedures for the agreements are in Revenue Procedure 2017-21, earlier. An entity applies for WP or WT status at [IRS.gov/Businesses/Corporations/Qualified-Intermediary-System](https://www.irs.gov/Businesses/Corporations/Qualified-Intermediary-System). The WP or WT will be assigned a WP-EIN or WT-EIN to be used only when acting in that capacity.

  

_**WP协议和WT协议。** _

WP 协议和 WT 协议以及协议的申请程序位于之前的 2017-21 年收入程序中。实体在[IRS.gov/Businesses/Corporations/Qualified-Intermediary-System](https://www.irs.gov/Businesses/Corporations/Qualified-Intermediary-System)上申请 WP 或 WT 身份。 WP 或 WT 将被分配一个 WP-EIN 或 WT-EIN，仅在以该身份行事时使用。

A WP or WT that is an FFI (other than a retirement fund) must also register with the IRS at [IRS.gov/Businesses/Corporations/FATCA-Foreign-Financial-Institution-Registration-System](https://www.irs.gov/businesses/corporations/fatca-foreign-financial-institution-registration-system) to obtain its applicable chapter 4 status and GIIN.  
作为 FFI（退休基金除外）的 WP 或 WT 还必须通过[IRS.gov/Businesses/Corporations/FATCA-Foreign-Financial-Institution-Registration-System](https://www.irs.gov/businesses/corporations/fatca-foreign-financial-institution-registration-system)向 IRS 注册，以获得其适用的第 4 章身份和 GIIN 。

_**Documentation.**_

A WP or WT must provide you with a Form W-8IMY that certifies that the WP or WT is acting in that capacity and provides all other information and certifications required by the form, including its WP-EIN or WT-EIN. When you make a withholdable payment to a WP or WT, the WP or WT generally may also provide a certificate of a chapter 4 status permitted of a WP or WT (and GIIN, if applicable). The WP or WT, when acting in such capacity, is not required to provide a withholding statement and is not required to disclose any information regarding its direct partners, beneficiaries, or owners, or any indirect partner, beneficiary, or owner for which it acts as a WP or WT that is not a U.S. nonexempt recipient (except for a U.S. nonexempt recipient included in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees). A chapter 4 withholding rate pool also means a payment of a single type of income that is allocated to U.S. payees when the WP provides the certification required on Form W-8IMY for allocating payments to this pool. When a WP or WT is not acting as a WP or WT with respect to an amount distributed to, or included in the distributive share of, an indirect partner, beneficiary, or owner, it must provide you with a nonwithholding foreign partnership or nonwithholding foreign trust withholding certificate on a Form W-8IMY and documentation for its indirect partners, beneficiaries, and owners that are not included in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool.

  

_**文档。** _

WP 或 WT 必须向您提供 W-8IMY 表格，证明 WP 或 WT 正在以该身份行事，并提供该表格所需的所有其他信息和证明，包括其 WP-EIN 或 WT-EIN。当您向 WP 或 WT 支付可预扣付款时，WP 或 WT 通常还可能提供 WP 或 WT 允许的第 4 章状态证明（以及 GIIN，如果适用）。 WP 或 WT 在以此类身份行事时，无需提供预扣税表，也无需披露有关其直接合作伙伴、受益人或所有者，或其代表的任何间接合作伙伴、受益人或所有者的任何信息作为非美国非豁免收款人的 WP 或 WT（包含在第 4 章美国收款人预扣税率池中的美国非豁免收款人除外）。第 4 章预扣税率池还意味着当 WP 提供表格 W-8IMY 所需的证明以将付款分配给该池时，分配给美国收款人的单一类型收入的支付。当 WP 或 WT 不作为 WP 或 WT 就分配给间接合伙人、受益人或所有者的金额或包含在间接合伙人、受益人或所有者的分配份额中时，它必须向您提供非预扣税外国合伙企业或非预扣税外国合伙企业W-8IMY 表上的信托预扣税证书以及未包含在第 4 章预扣税率池中的间接合作伙伴、受益人和所有者的文件。

#### Foreign Persons外国人

**Rules relevant to chapters 3 and 4.**

A payee is subject to withholding only if it is a foreign person. A foreign person includes a nonresident alien individual, foreign corporation, foreign partnership, foreign trust, foreign estate, and any other person that is not a U.S. person. It also includes a foreign branch of a U.S. financial institution if the foreign branch is a QI. In most cases, the U.S. branch of a foreign corporation or partnership is treated as a foreign person. The determination of whether a foreign person is treated as an entity (that is, as opposed to being disregarded as separate from its owner), or as a foreign corporation, foreign partnership, or foreign trust is made under U.S. tax rules.

  

**与第 3 章和第 4 章相关的规则。** 

仅当收款人是外国人时才需缴纳预扣税。外国人包括非居民外国人、外国公司、外国合伙企业、外国信托、外国财产和任何其他非美国人。如果美国金融机构的外国分支机构是 QI，则还包括该外国分支机构。在大多数情况下，外国公司或合伙企业的美国分支机构被视为外国人。外国人是否被视为实体（即，而不是被视为与其所有者分离），还是外国公司、外国合伙企业或外国信托，是根据美国税务规则确定的。

If an amount is both a withholdable payment and an amount subject to chapter 3 withholding and the withholding agent withholds under chapter 4, it may credit this amount against any tax due under chapter 3.  
如果一笔金额既是应预扣付款又是受第 3 章预扣税约束的金额，并且扣缴义务人根据第 4 章预扣税款，则可以将该金额抵扣根据第 3 章应缴的任何税款。

**Nonresident alien.**

A nonresident alien is an individual who is not a U.S. citizen or a resident alien. A resident of a foreign country under the residence article of an income tax treaty is a nonresident alien individual for purposes of withholding.

  

**非居民外国人。** 

非居民外国人是指非美国公民或居民外国人的个人。根据所得税协定的居住条款，外国居民是扣缴税款的非居民外籍个人。

_**Married to U.S. citizen or resident alien.**_

Nonresident alien individuals married to U.S. citizens or resident aliens may choose to be treated as resident aliens for certain income tax purposes. However, these individuals are still subject to the chapter 3 withholding rules that apply to nonresident aliens for all income except wages. Wages paid to these individuals are subject to graduated withholding. See [_Wages Paid to Employees—Graduated Withholding_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224978 "Wages Paid to Employees—Graduated Withholding"), later.

  

_**与美国公民或外国居民结婚。** _

与美国公民或居民外国人结婚的非居民外国人可以出于某些所得税目的选择被视为居民外国人。然而，这些个人仍须遵守适用于非居民外国人所有收入（工资除外）的第 3 章预扣税规则。支付给这些人的工资须实行分级扣缴。请参阅稍后[_支付给员工的工资——分级预扣税_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224978 "Wages Paid to Employees—Graduated Withholding")。

**Resident alien.**

A resident alien is an individual who is not a citizen or national of the United States and who meets either the green card test or the substantial presence test for the calendar year.

  

**居住的外国人。** 

外籍居民是指非美国公民或国民但在该日历年通过绿卡测试或实际居住测试的个人。

*   Green card test. An alien is a resident alien if the individual was a lawful permanent resident of the United States at any time during the calendar year. This is known as the green card test because these aliens hold immigrant visas (also known as green cards).  
    绿卡测试。如果该外国人在一年中的任何时间是美国的合法永久居民，则该外国人是居民外国人。这被称为绿卡测试，因为这些外国人持有移民签证（也称为绿卡）。
    
*   Substantial presence test. An alien is considered a resident alien if the individual meets the substantial presence test for the calendar year. Under this test, the individual must be physically present in the United States on at least:  
    实质性存在测试。如果外国人符合该日历年的实质性居住测试，则该外国人被视为外国人居民。根据此测试，个人必须至少在以下情况下实际居住在美国：
    

1.  31 days during the current calendar year; and  
    当前日历年中的 31 天；和
    
2.  183 days during the current year and the 2 preceding years, counting all the days of physical presence in the current year, but only 1/3 the number of days of presence in the first preceding year, and only 1/6 the number of days in the second preceding year.  
    当年及前两年183天，计算当年所有实际居住天数，但仅占前一年居住天数的三分之一，仅计算天数的六分之一在前第二年。
    

In most cases, the days the alien is in the United States as a teacher, student, or trainee on an “F,” “J,” “M,” or “Q” visa are not counted. This exception is for a limited period of time.  
在大多数情况下，持有“F”、“J”、“M”或“Q”签证的外国人作为教师、学生或实习生在美国的天数不计算在内。此例外是在有限的时间内。

For more information on resident and nonresident status, the tests for residence, and the exceptions to them, see [Pub. 519](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-519).  
有关居民和非居民身份、居住测试及其例外情况的更多信息，请参阅[Pub。 519](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-519) .

_**Note.**_

If your employee is late in notifying you that their status changed from nonresident alien to resident alien, you may have to make an adjustment to Form 941 if that employee was exempt from withholding of social security and Medicare taxes as a nonresident alien. For more information on making adjustments, see chapter 13 of [Pub. 15 (Circular E)](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-15) .

  

_**笔记。** _

如果您的员工迟迟通知您其身份从非居民外籍人士更改为居民外籍人士，并且该员工作为非居民外籍人士无需预扣社会保障税和医疗保险税，您可能需要对 941 表格进行调整。有关进行调整的更多信息，请参阅[Pub 第 13 章。 15（通告E）](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-15) 。

_**Resident of a U.S. territory.**_

A bona fide resident of Puerto Rico, the U.S. Virgin Islands (USVI), Guam, the Commonwealth of the Northern Mariana Islands (CNMI), or American Samoa who is not a U.S. citizen or a U.S. national is treated as a nonresident alien for the withholding rules explained here. A bona fide resident of a territory is someone who:

  

_**美国领土的居民。** _

波多黎各、美属维尔京群岛 (USVI)、关岛、北马里亚纳群岛联邦 (CNMI) 或美属萨摩亚的真正居民，如果不是美国公民或美国国民，则被视为非居民外国人此处解释了扣留规则。领土的真正居民是指：

*   Meets the presence test,满足存在测试，
    
*   Does not have a tax home outside the territory, and  
    在境外没有纳税所，并且
    
*   Does not have a closer connection to the United States or to a foreign country than to the territory.  
    与美国或外国的联系不比与领土的联系更紧密。
    

For more information, see [Pub. 570](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-570).  
欲了解更多信息，请参阅[发布。第570章](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-570)

**Foreign corporations.**

A foreign corporation is one that does not fit the definition of a domestic corporation. A domestic corporation is one that was created or organized in the United States or under the laws of the United States, any of its states, or the District of Columbia.

  

**外国公司。** 

外国公司是不符合国内公司定义的公司。国内公司是指在美国或根据美国、其任何州或哥伦比亚特区的法律创建或组建的公司。

_**Guam or CNMI corporations.**_

A corporation created or organized in, or under the laws of, Guam or the CNMI is not considered a foreign corporation for the purpose of withholding tax for the tax year if:

  

_**关岛或北马里亚纳群岛公司。** _

在关岛或北马里亚纳群岛创建或组织的公司，或根据关岛或北马里亚纳群岛法律创建或组织的公司，如果满足以下条件，则就该纳税年度的预扣税而言，不被视为外国公司：

*   At all times during the tax year less than 25% in value of the corporation's stock is owned, directly or indirectly, by foreign persons; and  
    在纳税年度的任何时候，外国人直接或间接拥有公司股票价值的25%以下；和
    
*   At least 20% of the corporation's gross income is derived from sources within Guam or the CNMI for the 3-year period ending with the close of the preceding tax year of the corporation (or the period the corporation has been in existence, if less).  
    截至公司上一纳税年度结束的 3 年期间（或公司存在期间，如果较短），公司总收入的至少 20% 来自关岛或北马里亚纳群岛境内的来源。
    

_**Note.**_

The provisions discussed below under _USVI and American Samoa corporations_ will apply to Guam or CNMI corporations when an implementing agreement is in effect between the United States and that territory.

  

_**笔记。** _

当美国与关岛或北马里亚纳群岛共和国之间的执行协议生效时，下文讨论的_美属维尔京群岛和美属萨摩亚公司的规定将适用于关岛或北马里亚纳群岛_公司。

_**USVI and American Samoa corporations.**_

A corporation created or organized in, or under the laws of, the USVI or American Samoa is not considered a foreign corporation for the purposes of withholding tax for the tax year if:

  

_**美属维尔京群岛和美属萨摩亚公司。** _

在美属维尔京群岛或美属萨摩亚或根据其法律创建或组织的公司，在以下情况下，就该纳税年度的预扣税而言，不被视为外国公司：

*   At all times during the tax year less than 25% in value of the corporation's stock is owned, directly or indirectly, by foreign persons;  
    在纳税年度的任何时候，外国人直接或间接拥有公司股票价值的25%以下；
    
*   At least 65% of the corporation's gross income is effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business in the USVI, American Samoa, Guam, the CNMI, or the United States for the 3-year period ending with the close of the tax year of the corporation (or the period the corporation or any predecessor has been in existence, if less); and  
    截至纳税年度结束的 3 年期间，公司总收入的至少 65% 与在美属维尔京群岛、美属萨摩亚、关岛、北马里亚纳群岛或美国的贸易或业务活动有效相关公司的成立时间（或者公司或任何前身的存在期限，如果较短）；和
    
*   No substantial part of the income of the corporation is used, directly or indirectly, to satisfy obligations to a person who is not a bona fide resident of the USVI, American Samoa, Guam, the CNMI, or the United States.  
    公司收入的很大一部分不会直接或间接用于履行对非美属维尔京群岛、美属萨摩亚、关岛、北马里亚纳群岛或美国的真正居民的义务。
    

**Foreign private foundations.**

A private foundation that was created or organized under the laws of a foreign country is a foreign private foundation. Gross investment income from sources within the United States paid to a qualified foreign private foundation is subject to withholding at a 4% rate (unless exempted by a treaty) rather than the ordinary statutory 30% rate.

  

**外国私人基金会。** 

依照外国法律设立或者组织的非公开基金会为外国非公开基金会。支付给合格外国私人基金会的来自美国境内的总投资收入须按 4% 的税率（除非条约豁免）缴纳预扣税，而不是普通的法定 30% 税率。

**Other foreign organizations, associations, and charitable institutions.**

An organization may be exempt from income tax under section 501(a) and chapter 4 withholding tax even if it was formed under foreign law. In most cases, you do not have to withhold tax on payments of income to these foreign tax-exempt organizations unless the IRS has determined that they are foreign private foundations.

Payments to these organizations, however, must be reported on Form 1042-S if the payment is subject to chapter 3 withholding, even though no tax is withheld.

You must withhold tax on the unrelated business income (as described in Pub. 598) of foreign tax-exempt organizations in the same way that you would withhold tax on similar income of nonexempt organizations when the organization does not provide you a Form W-8ECI to certify that the income is effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business of the organization.

  

**其他外国组织、协会、慈善机构。** 

根据第 501(a) 条和第 4 章预扣税的规定，即使组织是根据外国法律成立的，该组织也可以免缴所得税。在大多数情况下，您无需为向这些外国免税组织支付的收入预扣税款，除非美国国税局已确定它们是外国私人基金会。

但是，如果向这些组织支付的款项需要缴纳第 3 章预扣税，则即使没有预扣税款，也必须在 1042-S 表格中报告该款项。

您必须对外国免税组织的不相关业务收入（如 Pub. 598 中所述）预扣税款，其方式与您在该组织未向您提供 W-8ECI 表时对非免税组织的类似收入预扣税款的方式相同证明该收入与该组织的美国贸易或业务有效相关。

**U.S. branches of foreign persons.**

In most cases, a payment to a U.S. branch of a foreign person is a payment made to the foreign person. However, you may treat payments to _[U.S. branches of foreign banks and foreign insurance companies](#en_US_2024_publink1000224801 "U.S. branches of foreign banks and foreign insurance companies.")_ (discussed earlier) that are subject to U.S. regulatory supervision as payments made to a U.S. person, if you and the U.S. branch have agreed to do so, and if their agreement is evidenced by a withholding certificate, Form W-8IMY. For this purpose, a territory financial institution acting as an intermediary or that is a flow-through entity is treated as a U.S. branch.

  

**外国人在美国的分支机构。** 

在大多数情况下，向外国人的美国分行付款就是向外国人支付的款项。_[但是](#en_US_2024_publink1000224801 "U.S. branches of foreign banks and foreign insurance companies.")_，如果您和美国分行同意这样做，并且如果他们的协议由预扣税证书（表格 W-8IMY）证明。为此，充当中介机构或流通实体的领土金融机构被视为美国分支机构。

#### Additional Rules Specific to Chapter 4  
第 4 章的附加规则

A payee may be subject to chapter 4 withholding only if it is a foreign entity. A foreign entity for chapter 4 purposes means any entity that is not a U.S. person and includes a territory entity as defined in Regulations section 1.1471-1(b)(129).  
仅当收款人是外国实体时，才需要缴纳第 4 章预扣税。就第 4 章而言，外国实体是指非美国人的任何实体，包括《条例》第 1.1471-1(b)(129) 条中定义的领土实体。

A foreign entity is subject to chapter 4 withholding if it is a nonparticipating FFI or a passive NFFE that does not provide the appropriate certification regarding its substantial U.S. owners. A nonparticipating FFI is an FFI other than a _[participating FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015541 "Participating FFI.")_, _[deemed-compliant FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015533 "Deemed-compliant FFI.")_, or _[exempt beneficial owner](#en_US_2024_publink100015474 "Exempt beneficial owner.")_. See _[Definitions](#en_US_2024_publink100015531 "Definitions")_, later, for the definitions of these terms.  
如果外国实体是非参与 FFI 或被动 NFFE，且未提供有关其主要美国所有者的适当证明，则该外国实体需缴纳第 4 章预扣税。非参与 FFI 是_[指参与 FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015541 "Participating FFI.")_ 、_[视为合规 FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015533 "Deemed-compliant FFI.")_或_[豁免受益所有人](#en_US_2024_publink100015474 "Exempt beneficial owner.")_之外的 FFI。有关这些术语的_[定义](#en_US_2024_publink100015531 "Definitions")_，请参阅后面的定义。

A passive NFFE is:被动 NFFE 是：

*   An NFFE other than a publicly traded corporation,  
    除上市公司外的 NFFE，
    
*   Certain affiliated entities related to a publicly traded corporation,  
    与上市公司相关的某些附属实体，
    
*   Certain territory entities,  
    某些领土实体，
    
*   Active NFFEs, or活跃的 NFFE，或
    
*   Excluded FFIs.不包括 FFI。
    

For chapter 4 purposes, a U.S. person does not include a foreign insurance company that has made an election under section 953(d) if it is a specified insurance company and is not licensed to do business in any state. Notwithstanding the foregoing, a withholding agent should treat such entity as a U.S. person for purposes of documenting the entity’s status for purposes of chapters 3 and 4.  
就第 4 章而言，美国人不包括根据第 953(d) 条做出选择的外国保险公司（如果该公司是指定保险公司且未获许可在任何州开展业务）。尽管有上述规定，扣缴义务人应将此类实体视为美国人，以便根据第 3 章和第 4 章记录该实体的身份。

#### Documentation文档

#### Documentation for Chapter 3  
第 3 章的文档

For purposes of chapter 3, in most cases, you must withhold 30% from the gross amount paid to a foreign payee unless you can reliably associate the payment with valid documentation that establishes either of the following.  
就第 3 章而言，在大多数情况下，您必须从支付给外国收款人的总金额中预扣 30%，除非您能够可靠地将付款与可证明以下任一情况的有效文件关联起来。

*   The payee is a U.S. person.  
    收款人是美国人。
    
*   The payee is a foreign person that is the beneficial owner of the income and is entitled to a reduced rate of withholding under the Internal Revenue Code, or an applicable income tax treaty.  
    收款人是外国人，是收入的受益所有人，有权根据《国内税收法》或适用的所得税条约享受降低的预扣税率。
    

For rules related to when a withholding agent may rely on an otherwise valid withholding certificate received electronically from a third-party repository, see Regulations section 1.1441-1(e)(4)(iv)(E).  
有关扣缴义务人何时可以依赖从第三方存储库以电子方式收到的有效扣缴证书的相关规则，请参阅法规第 1.1441-1(e)(4)(iv)(E) 节。

If withholding is applied under chapter 4 on a payment, no withholding will be required on such payment under chapter 3.  
如果根据第 4 章对付款适用预扣税，则无需根据第 3 章对该付款进行预扣税。

#### Documentation for Chapter 4  
第 4 章的文档

If you make a withholdable payment, you must determine the chapter 4 status of payees, beneficial owners, intermediaries, and flow-through entities receiving the payment to the extent required for chapter 4 purposes. You must also determine the chapter 4 status of persons that own an interest in an entity receiving a withholdable payment that you treat as an owner-documented FFI, provided you are either a U.S. financial institution, participating FFI, or reporting Model 1 FFI. To establish chapter 4 status, you must generally obtain a valid withholding certificate or documentary evidence that you can reliably associate with the payment. If you make a payment to a passive NFFE, you must obtain either a certification that the NFFE does not have any substantial U.S. owners, or the name, address, and TIN of each substantial U.S. owner of the NFFE (or, under an applicable IGA, each controlling person that is a specified U.S. person).  
如果您支付可预扣的付款，您必须在第 4 章目的所需的范围内确定收款人、受益所有人、中介机构和接收付款的流通实体的第 4 章状态。如果您是美国金融机构、参与 FFI 或报告模式 1 FFI，您还必须确定在接受预扣付款的实体中拥有权益的人员的第 4 章身份，并将该实体视为所有者记录的 FFI。要建立第 4 章状态，您通常必须获得有效的预扣税证书或可以可靠地与付款关联的文件证据。如果您向被动 NFFE 付款，您必须获得该 NFFE 没有任何实质美国所有者的证明，或者该 NFFE 的每个实质美国所有者的姓名、地址和 TIN（或者根据适用的 IGA ，每个控制人都是指定的美国人）。

You can reliably associate a payment with a Form W-8 for purposes of establishing a payee’s chapter 4 status in most cases if, prior to the payment, you:  
在大多数情况下，如果您在付款之前满足以下条件，则可以可靠地将付款与 W-8 表格关联起来，以便确定收款人的第 4 章状态：

*   Obtain a valid form that contains the information required for chapter 4 purposes,  
    获取包含第 4 章所需信息的有效表格，
    
*   Can reliably determine how much of the payment relates to the form, and  
    能够可靠地确定有多少付款与表格相关，并且
    
*   Have no actual knowledge or reason to know that any of the information, certifications, or statements in, or associated with, the form is unreliable or incorrect for chapter 4 purposes.  
    没有实际知识或理由知道表格中或与之相关的任何信息、证明或声明对于第 4 章的目的来说是不可靠或不正确的。
    

See _[Standards of Knowledge for Purposes of Chapter 4](#en_US_2024_publink100015503 "Standards of Knowledge for Purposes of Chapter 4")_, later, for the reason to know standards that apply for chapter 4 purposes.  
请参阅后面_[第 4 章的知识标准](#en_US_2024_publink100015503 "Standards of Knowledge for Purposes of Chapter 4")_，了解适用于第 4 章目的的标准。

For the requirements for documenting specific chapter 4 statuses of persons receiving withholdable payments, see Regulations section 1.1471-3(d). For rules related to when a withholding agent may rely on an otherwise valid withholding certificate received electronically from a third-party repository, see Regulations section 1.1441-1(e)(4)(iv)(E). Also see Regulations section 1.1471-3(d) for the extent to which a withholding agent may rely on documentary evidence (other than a Form W-8) to establish the chapter 4 status of an entity payee, including the forms of documentary evidence permitted for each specific chapter 4 status. For the requirements for documentary evidence, see Regulations section 1.1471-3(c)(5). If you make a withholdable payment to an entity payee and cannot reliably associate the payment with a valid withholding certificate or valid documentary evidence, you must apply the chapter 4 presumption rules described in [_Presumption Rules for Chapter 4_](#en_US_2024_publink100015522 "Presumption Rules for Chapter 4"), later.  
有关记录第 4 章接收预扣付款人员具体身份的要求，请参阅《条例》第 1.1471-3(d) 节。有关扣缴义务人何时可以依赖从第三方存储库以电子方式收到的有效扣缴证书的相关规则，请参阅法规第 1.1441-1(e)(4)(iv)(E) 节。另请参阅《条例》第 1.1471-3(d) 节，了解扣缴义务人可以在多大程度上依赖文件证据（除表格 W-8 外）来确定实体收款人的第 4 章身份，包括允许的文件证据的形式对于每个特定的第 4 章状态。有关文件证据的要求，请参阅法规第 1.1471-3(c)(5) 条。如果您向实体收款人支付了应扣税款，并且无法可靠地将付款与有效的扣缴凭证或有效的文件证据关联起来，则必须应用稍后[_第 4 章推定规则_](#en_US_2024_publink100015522 "Presumption Rules for Chapter 4")中所述的第 4 章推定规则。

You may rely on the same documentation for purposes of both chapters 3 and 4 provided the documentation is sufficient to meet the requirements of each chapter. For example, you may use a Form W-8BEN-E to obtain both the chapter 3 and chapter 4 statuses of an entity providing the form.  
您可以依赖相同的文档来实现第 3 章和第 4 章的目的，前提是该文档足以满足每章的要求。例如，您可以使用表格 W-8BEN-E 来获取提供该表格的实体的第 3 章和第 4 章状态。

#### Additional Documentation Rules Applicable to Chapters 3 and 4  
适用于第 3 章和第 4 章的附加文件规则

In most cases, you must reliably associate the payment with valid documentation to apply reduced withholding and must get the documentation before you make the payment. The documentation is not valid if you know, or have reason to know, that it is unreliable or incorrect. See [_Standards of Knowledge for Purposes of Chapter 3_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224865 "Standards of Knowledge for Purposes of Chapter 3") and _[Standards of Knowledge for Purposes of Chapter 4](#en_US_2024_publink100015503 "Standards of Knowledge for Purposes of Chapter 4")_, later.  
在大多数情况下，您必须可靠地将付款与有效文件关联起来以申请减少预扣税，并且必须在付款前获取文件。如果您知道或有理由知道该文档不可靠或不正确，则该文档无效。请参阅稍后[_第 3 章的知识标准_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224865 "Standards of Knowledge for Purposes of Chapter 3")和_[第 4 章的知识标准](#en_US_2024_publink100015503 "Standards of Knowledge for Purposes of Chapter 4")_。

If you cannot reliably associate a payment with valid documentation, you must use the _[presumption rules](#en_US_2024_publink1000224878 "Presumption Rules")_ discussed later to determine the rate of withholding. For example, if you do not have documentation or you cannot determine the part of a payment that is allocable to specific documentation, you must use the presumption rules of section 1441.  
如果您无法可靠地将付款与有效文件关联起来，则必须使用稍后讨论的_[推定规则](#en_US_2024_publink1000224878 "Presumption Rules")_来确定预扣税率。例如，如果您没有文件或无法确定可分配给特定文件的付款部分，则必须使用第 1441 条的推定规则。

The specific types of documentation are discussed in this section. However, see [_Withholding on Specific Income_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224897 "Withholding on Specific Income"), later, as well as the instructions to the particular forms. As the withholding agent, you may also want to see the [Instructions for the Requester of Forms W-8BEN, W-8BEN-E, W-8ECI, W-8EXP, and W-8IMY](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-w-8).  
本节讨论特定类型的文档。但是，请参阅稍后的[_特定收入预扣税_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224897 "Withholding on Specific Income")以及特定表格的说明。作为扣缴义务人，您可能还需要查看[W-8BEN、W-8BEN-E、W-8ECI、W-8EXP 和 W-8IMY 表格请求者须知](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-w-8)。

**Sections 1446(a) and (f) withholding.**

Under section 1446(a), a partnership must withhold tax on its ECTI allocable to a foreign partner or, for a partnership that is a PTP, the PTP or a nominee for a PTP distribution must withhold on the amount of the distribution subject to section 1446(a) withholding made to a foreign partner. In most cases, a partnership (or nominee when applicable) determines if a partner is a foreign partner and the partner's tax classification based on the withholding certificate provided by the partner. This is the same documentation that is provided for chapter 3 withholding, but may require additional information, as discussed under each of the forms in this section.

  

**第 1446(a) 和 (f) 条预扣税。** 

根据第 1446(a) 条，合伙企业必须对其分配给外国合伙人的 ECTI 预扣税款，或者，对于 PTP 合伙企业，PTP 或 PTP 分配的提名人必须根据第 1446(a) 条规定对分配金额预扣税款1446(a) 向外国合作伙伴预扣税款。在大多数情况下，合伙企业（或适用时的代理人）根据合伙人提供的预扣税证明来确定合伙人是否为外国合伙人以及合伙人的税收分类。该文件与第 3 章预扣税提供的文件相同，但可能需要其他信息，如本节每种表格中所述。

For information on section 1446(f) withholding, go to _[Section 1446(f) Withholding,](#en_US_2024_publink100016312 "Section 1446(f) Withholding")_ later.  
有关第 1446(f) 条预扣税的信息，请参阅稍后的_[第 1446(f) 条预扣税](#en_US_2024_publink100016312 "Section 1446(f) Withholding")_。

**Documentation rule for joint payees.**

If you make a payment to joint payees (such as holders of a joint account), you need to get documentation from each payee. If you make a payment to joint payees and cannot reliably associate the payment with documentation from all of the payees, you must generally presume the payment is made to an unidentified U.S. person. If the payment is a withholdable payment and any of the payees do not appear, by name or other information in the account file, to be an individual, you must treat the entire amount as a payment made to an undocumented foreign person. However, if one of the joint payees has provided you with a Form W-9, you must treat the payment as made to that payee.

  

**联合收款人的文件规则。** 

如果您向联名收款人（例如联名账户持有人）付款，您需要从每个收款人处获取文件。如果您向联合收款人付款，并且无法可靠地将付款与所有收款人的文件关联起来，则您通常必须假定付款是向身份不明的美国人支付的。如果付款是可预扣付款，并且账户文件中的任何收款人的姓名或其他信息都不是个人，则您必须将全部金额视为向无证外国人支付的款项。但是，如果联合收款人之一向您提供了 W-9 表格，您必须将付款视为向该收款人支付。

**Form W-9.**

In most cases, you can treat the payee as a U.S. person if the payee gives you a Form W-9. The Form W-9 can be used only by a U.S. person and must contain the payee's TIN. U.S. persons are not subject to chapter 3 withholding (or withholding under section 1446(a) or (f)), but may be subject to:

  

**W-9 表格。** 

在大多数情况下，如果收款人向您提供 W-9 表格，您就可以将收款人视为美国人。 W-9 表格只能由美国人使用，并且必须包含收款人的 TIN。美国人无需缴纳第 3 章预扣税（或根据第 1446(a) 或 (f) 条规定的预扣税），但可能需缴纳：

*   Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding under section 3406,  
    根据第 3406 条提交 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税，
    
*   Reporting as a U.S. account holder of a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI, and  
    报告为参与 FFI 或注册的视为合规 FFI 的美国账户持有人，以及
    
*   Classification as a recalcitrant account holder of a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI for chapter 4 purposes (including chapter 4 withholding) when the FFI is unable to report the information required with respect to the account holder.  
    当 FFI 无法报告账户持有人所需的信息时，出于第 4 章的目的（包括第 4 章预扣税款），被归类为参与 FFI 或注册的视为合规 FFI 的顽固账户持有人。
    

**Forms W-8.**

In most cases, a foreign payee of the income should give you a form in the Form W-8 series.

  

**W-8 表格。** 

在大多数情况下，收入的外国收款人应向您提供 W-8 系列表格中的表格。

If certain requirements are met, the foreign person can give you documentary evidence, rather than a Form W-8 for chapter 3 or 4 purposes. You can rely on documentary evidence in lieu of a Form W-8 for an amount paid outside the United States with respect to an offshore obligation. Refer to [_Offshore obligations_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224830 "Offshore obligations."), later, to determine whether a payment qualifies as such a payment.  
如果满足某些要求，外国人可以向您提供书面证据，而不是用于第 3 章或第 4 章目的的 W-8 表格。对于在美国境外支付的离岸债务金额，您可以依靠书面证据来代替 W-8 表格。请参阅稍后的[_离岸义务_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224830 "Offshore obligations.")，以确定付款是否符合此类付款的条件。

**Other documentation.**

Other documentation may be required to claim an exemption from, or a reduced rate of, chapter 3 withholding on pay for personal services. The nonresident alien individual may have to give you a Form W-4 or a Form 8233. These forms are discussed in [_Pay for Personal Services Performed_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224965 "Pay for Personal Services Performed") under _Withholding on Specific Income_, later.

  

**其他文档。** 

可能需要提供其他文件才能申请第 3 章个人服务工资预扣税的豁免或降低税率。非居民外籍人士可能需要向您提供 W-4 表格或 8233 表格。这些表格将在稍后_根据特定收入预扣税_[_支付个人服务费用_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224965 "Pay for Personal Services Performed")中讨论。

#### Beneficial Owners实益拥有人

If all the appropriate requirements have been established on a Form W-8BEN, W-8BEN-E, W-8ECI, W-8EXP, or, if applicable, on documentary evidence, you can treat the payee as a foreign beneficial owner.  
如果表格 W-8BEN、W-8BEN-E、W-8ECI、W-8EXP 或文件证据（如果适用）上已规定了所有适当的要求，则您可以将收款人视为外国受益所有人。

**Claiming treaty benefits for purposes of chapter 3.**

You may apply a reduced rate of withholding under chapter 3 to a foreign person that provides a Form W-8 claiming a reduced rate of withholding under an income tax treaty only if the person provides a U.S. or foreign TIN and certifies that:

  

**出于第 3 章的目的主张条约优惠。** 

您可以根据第 3 章向提供表格 W-8 并根据所得税条约申请降低预扣税率的外国人应用降低的预扣税率，前提是此人提供了美国或外国 TIN 并证明：

*   It is a resident of a treaty country;  
    是条约国的居民；
    
*   It is the beneficial owner of the income;  
    它是收入的受益所有人；
    
*   If it is an entity, it derives the income within the meaning of section 894 (it is not fiscally transparent); and  
    如果是实体，则获得第 894 条含义内的收入（财务不透明）；和
    
*   It meets any limitation on benefits provision contained in the treaty, if applicable, and specifies the category of the limitation on benefits provision.  
    它满足条约中包含的对福利规定的任何限制（如果适用），并指定对福利规定的限制的类别。
    

If the payment you make is a withholdable payment to an entity, a requirement to withhold under chapter 4 may apply based on the chapter 4 status of the payee regardless of whether a claim of treaty benefits may apply to such payee or other person receiving the income.  
如果您向某个实体支付的款项是应预扣税款，则根据收款人的第 4 章身份，可能会适用第 4 章规定的预扣税款，无论协定待遇索赔是否适用于该收款人或其他接收收入的人。

An entity derives income for which it is claiming treaty benefits only if the entity is not treated as fiscally transparent for that income. See [_Fiscally transparent entities claiming treaty benefits_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224790 "Fiscally transparent entities claiming treaty benefits."), discussed earlier under _Flow-Through Entities._  
仅当该实体在该收入方面不被视为财务透明时，该实体才能获得可享受税收协定优惠的收入。请参阅前面在_“流通实体”_下讨论的[_声称享受税收协定优惠的财政透明实体_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224790 "Fiscally transparent entities claiming treaty benefits.")。

Limitations on benefits (LOB) provisions in income tax treaties generally prevent third country residents (unless the treaty contains a derivative benefits rule) and others that do not have a substantial nexus to the treaty country from obtaining treaty benefits. For example, a foreign corporation may not be entitled to a reduced rate of withholding unless a minimum percentage of its owners are citizens or residents of the United States or the treaty country. Foreign entities that are residents of a country whose income tax treaty with the United States contains an LOB article are eligible for treaty benefits only if they satisfy one of the objective tests under the LOB article or obtain a favorable discretionary determination from the U.S. competent authority.  
所得税条约中的福利限制（LOB）条款通常会阻止第三国居民（除非条约包含派生福利规则）和与条约国没有实质性联系的其他人获得条约福利。例如，外国公司可能无权享受降低的预扣税率，除非其所有者的最低比例是美国或条约国的公民或居民。作为与美国签订所得税协定包含 LOB 条款的国家的居民的外国实体，只有在满足 LOB 条款下的客观测试之一或获得美国主管当局有利的酌情决定的情况下，才有资格享受税收协定优惠。

The exemptions from, or reduced rates of, U.S. tax vary under each treaty. You must check the provisions of the tax treaty that apply. See [_Tax Treaties_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties"), later, for information on how to access tax treaties.  
每个条约的美国税收豁免或降低税率各不相同。您必须检查适用的税收协定的规定。有关如何访问税收协定的信息，请参阅稍后的[_税收协定_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties")。

If you know, or have reason to know, that an owner of income is not eligible for treaty benefits claimed or if the United States does not have an income tax treaty in force with that country, you may not reduce the rate of withholding. You are not, however, responsible for misstatements on a Form W-8, documentary evidence, or statements accompanying documentary evidence for which you did not have actual knowledge, or reason to know, that the statements were incorrect. Certain withholding agents, such as financial institutions, have limited reason to know requirements for this purpose. See Regulations section 1.1441-7(b) for these requirements.  
如果您知道或有理由知道收入所有者没有资格享受所申请的税收协定优惠，或者美国与该国家/地区没有生效的所得税协定，则您不得降低预扣税率。但是，您不对 W-8 表格、文件证据或文件证据中的错误陈述负责，而您实际上并不知道或没有理由知道这些陈述是不正确的。某些扣缴义务人，例如金融机构，了解此目的的要求的理由有限。有关这些要求，请参阅法规第 1.1441-7(b) 节。

_**Exceptions to TIN requirement.**_

A foreign person does not have to provide a U.S. or foreign TIN to claim a reduced rate of withholding under a treaty for chapter 3 purposes if the requirements for the following exceptions are met.

  

_**TIN 要求的例外情况。** _

如果满足以下例外情况的要求，外国人无需提供美国或外国 TIN 即可根据第 3 章条约要求降低预扣税率。

*   Income from marketable securities (discussed next).  
    来自有价证券的收入（接下来讨论）。
    
*   Unexpected payments to an individual (discussed under [_U.S. or Foreign TINs_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225029 "U.S. or Foreign TINs"), later).  
    向个人意外付款（稍后在[_美国或外国 TIN_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225029 "U.S. or Foreign TINs")下讨论）。
    

The allowance to provide a foreign TIN (rather than a U.S. TIN) does not apply to a payment to compensate an individual for personal services.  
提供外国 TIN（而非美国 TIN）的津贴不适用于补偿个人个人服务的付款。

See [_U.S. or Foreign TINs_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225029 "U.S. or Foreign TINs"), later, for when a foreign person is required to provide a foreign TIN for purposes other than making a treaty claim.  
请参阅稍后的[_美国或外国 TIN_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225029 "U.S. or Foreign TINs") ，了解何时要求外国人出于条约索赔以外的目的提供外国 TIN。

_**Marketable securities.**_

A Form W-8 provided to claim treaty benefits does not need a U.S. or foreign TIN if the foreign beneficial owner is claiming the benefits on income from marketable securities for chapter 3 purposes. For this purpose, income from a marketable security consists of the following items.

  

_**有价证券。** _

如果外国受益所有人出于第 3 章的目的索取有价证券收入的收益，则提供用于索取协定收益的 W-8 表格不需要美国或外国 TIN。为此，有价证券的收入包括以下项目。

*   Dividends and interest from stocks and debt obligations that are actively traded.  
    来自交易活跃的股票和债务的股息和利息。
    
*   Dividends from any redeemable security issued by an investment company registered under the Investment Company Act of 1940 (mutual fund).  
    根据 1940 年《投资公司法》（共同基金）注册的投资公司发行的任何可赎回证券的股息。
    
*   Dividends, interest, or royalties from units of beneficial interest in a unit investment trust that are (or were upon issuance) publicly offered and are registered with the SEC under the Securities Act of 1933.  
    来自公开发行（或发行时）并根据 1933 年《证券法》在 SEC 注册的单位投资信托受益单位的股息、利息或特许权使用费。
    
*   Income related to loans of any of the above securities.  
    与上述任何证券贷款相关的收入。
    

_**Offshore obligations.**_

An offshore obligation is an account maintained at an office or branch of a bank or other financial institution located outside the United States or an obligation, contract, or other instrument with respect to which the payer of the payment is either engaged in business as a broker or dealer in securities or a financial institution that engages in significant activities at an office or branch located outside the United States.

  

_**离岸义务。** _

离岸债务是指在位于美国境外的银行或其他金融机构的办事处或分行开设的账户，或者付款人作为经纪人从事业务的债务、合同或其他票据证券交易商或在美国境外的办事处或分支机构从事重大活动的金融机构。

A payment is made outside the United States if you complete the acts necessary to effect the payment outside the United States. However, an amount paid by a bank or other financial institution on a deposit or account usually will be treated as paid at the branch or office where the amount is credited unless the other requirements of Regulations section 1.6049-5(e)(2) are met with respect to the branch or office, unless the amount is collected by the financial institution as an agent of the payee.  
如果您在美国境外完成了付款所需的操作，则该付款将在美国境外进行。然而，银行或其他金融机构在存款或账户上支付的金额通常将被视为在该金额记入贷方的分行或办事处支付，除非条例第 1.6049-5(e)(2) 条的其他要求得到满足。就分行或办事处而言，除非该金额由金融机构作为收款人的代理人收取。

If a payment is made outside the United States with respect to an offshore obligation, a payee may give you documentary evidence, rather than a Form W-8, to establish that the payee is a foreign person. See Regulations section 1.6049-5(c)(1) for the requirements for documentary evidence for offshore obligations. For accounts opened on or after July 1, 2014, through December 31, 2014, you may use the rules regarding the use of documentary evidence under Regulations sections 1.6049-5(c)(1) and (c)(4) as in effect prior to the issuance of the temporary regulations.  
如果在美国境外就离岸债务付款，收款人可能会向您提供书面证据（而不是 W-8 表格）来证明收款人是外国人。有关离岸义务的文件证据的要求，请参阅法规第 1.6049-5(c)(1) 节。对于在 2014 年 7 月 1 日或之后至 2014 年 12 月 31 日期间开设的账户，您可以使用现行条例第 1.6049-5(c)(1) 和 (c)(4) 条中关于文件证据使用的规则暂行规定发布前。

You may rely on documentary evidence given to you by an NQI or a flow-through entity with its Form W-8IMY. This rule applies even though you make the payment to an NQI or flow-through entity in the United States. In most cases, the NQI or flow-through entity that gives you documentary evidence will also have to give you a _[withholding statement](#en_US_2024_publink1000224846 "Withholding statement.")_, discussed later.  
您可以依赖 NQI 或流通实体通过 W-8IMY 表格向您提供的书面证据。即使您向美国的 NQI 或流通实体付款，此规则也适用。在大多数情况下，为您提供书面证据的 NQI 或流通实体还必须向您提供_[预扣税声明](#en_US_2024_publink1000224846 "Withholding statement.")_（稍后讨论）。

_**Documentary evidence.**_

You may apply a reduced rate of withholding to income from _[marketable securities](#en_US_2024_publink1000224829 "Marketable securities.")_ (discussed earlier) paid outside the United States for chapter 3 purposes with respect to an offshore obligation if the beneficial owner gives you documentary evidence in place of a Form W-8. To claim treaty benefits, the documentary evidence must be one of the following.

  

_**文件证据。** _

如果受益所有人向您提供文件证据来代替 W-8 表格，您可以对出于第 3 章目的与离岸义务相关的在美国境外支付的_[有价证券](#en_US_2024_publink1000224829 "Marketable securities.")_（如前所述）的收入适用较低的预扣税率。要享受条约优惠，文件证据必须是以下之一。

1.  A certificate of residence that:  
    居住证明：
    
    1.  Is issued by a tax official of the treaty country of which the foreign beneficial owner claims to be a resident,  
        由外国受益所有人声称为其居民的条约国税务官员签发，
        
    2.  States that the person has filed its most recent income tax return as a resident of that country, and  
        说明此人已作为该国居民提交了最近的所得税申报表，并且
        
    3.  Is issued within 3 years before it is presented to you.  
        在提交给您之前的 3 年内发布。
        
    
2.  Documentation for an individual that:  
    个人的文件：
    
    1.  Includes the individual's name, address, and photograph;  
        包括个人的姓名、地址和照片；
        
    2.  Is an official document issued by an authorized governmental body; and  
        是由授权政府机构颁发的正式文件；和
        
    3.  Is issued no more than 3 years prior to being presented to you.  
        在提交给您之前发布不超过 3 年。
        
    
3.  Documentation for an entity that:  
    实体的文件：
    
    1.  Includes the name of the entity,  
        包括实体名称、
        
    2.  Includes the address of its principal office in the treaty country, and  
        包括其在条约国的主要办事处地址，以及
        
    3.  Is an official document issued by an authorized governmental body.  
        是由授权政府机构颁发的正式文件。
        
    

In addition to the documentary evidence, a foreign beneficial owner that is an entity must provide a statement that it derives the income for which it claims treaty benefits and that it meets one or more of the conditions set forth in a limitation on benefits article, if any (or similar provision), contained in the applicable treaty and must identify the specific limitation on benefits provision. In the case of a withholdable payment made to an entity, you must also obtain the applicable documentation to establish that withholding does not apply under chapter 4.  
除了文件证据外，作为实体的外国受益所有人还必须提供一份声明，证明其获得了其要求享受协定待遇的收入，并且满足福利限制条款中规定的一项或多项条件，如果适用条约中包含的任何（或类似条款）必须明确对福利条款的具体限制。如果向实体支付应预扣税款，您还必须获取适用的文件，以证明预扣税不适用于第 4 章。

**Form W-8BEN.**

This form is used by a foreign individual to:

  

**W-8BEN 表格。** 

外国人使用此表格来：

*   Establish foreign status;  
    建立外国身份；
    
*   Claim that such individual is the beneficial owner of the income for which the form is being furnished or a partner in a partnership subject to withholding under section 1446(a) or a transferee of an interest in a partnership under section 1446(f); and  
    声称该个人是所提供表格的收入的受益所有人或根据第 1446(a) 条规定需缴纳预扣税的合伙企业的合伙人，或根据第 1446(f) 条规定的合伙企业权益的受让人；和
    
*   If applicable, claim a reduced rate of, or exemption from, withholding under an income tax treaty.  
    如果适用，根据所得税条约要求降低预扣税率或免除预扣税。
    

A withholding agent, in some cases, may substitute its own form for a Form W-8BEN for individuals.  
在某些情况下，扣缴义务人可以用自己的表格代替个人的 W-8BEN 表格。

Form W-8BEN may also be used to claim that the foreign individual is exempt from Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding for income that is not subject to chapter 3 withholding and is not a withholdable payment. For example, a foreign person may provide a Form W-8BEN to a broker to establish that the gross proceeds from the sale of securities are not subject to Form 1099 reporting or backup withholding.  
W-8BEN 表格还可用于声称外国个人免于缴纳 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税，其收入不受第 3 章预扣税的约束，且不属于应预扣税款。例如，外国人可以向经纪人提供 W-8BEN 表格，以确定出售证券的总收益无需缴纳 1099 表格报告或备用预扣税。

_**Date of birth requirement for certain account holders.**_

If you are a U.S. office or branch of a depository institution, custodial institution, investment entity, or specified insurance company (each as defined in Regulations section 1.1471-5(e)) documenting an individual account holder (as defined in Regulations section 1.1471-5(a)(3)) of an account that is a financial account (as defined in Regulations section 1.1471-5(b)), you must obtain the individual account holder’s date of birth on the Form W-8BEN in order for the form to not be invalid for a payment of U.S. source income reportable on Form 1042-S. If the individual’s date of birth is not provided on the Form W-8BEN, the form is still valid if you otherwise have the date of birth in your account files for the account holder or you obtain the date of birth on a written statement (including a written statement transmitted by email) from the account holder and associate the written statement with the Form W-8BEN. See the related Foreign TIN requirement discussed under _[Foreign TIN requirement for account holders.](#en_US_2024_publink100015526 "Foreign TIN requirement for account holders.")_, later, which also generally applies with respect to accounts described in this paragraph.

  

_**某些账户持有人的出生日期要求。** _

如果您是存款机构、托管机构、投资实体或指定保险公司（各自的定义见《条例》第 1.1471-5(e) 条）的美国办事处或分支机构，记录了个人账户持有人（《条例》第 1.1471-5(e) 条的定义） 5(a)(3)) 的账户是金融账户（定义见条例第 1.1471-5(b) 条），您必须获取个人账户持有人的日期在 W-8BEN 表格上注明出生日期，以便该表格对于在 1042-S 表格上报告的美国来源收入的支付不无效。如果 W-8BEN 表格中未提供该个人的出生日期，且您在账户持有人的账户档案中另有出生日期，或者您通过书面声明（包括书面声明）获得出生日期，则该表格仍然有效。账户持有人通过电子邮件发送的书面声明，并将该书面声明与 W-8BEN 表格相关联。请参阅_[帐户持有人的外国 TIN 要求中讨论的相关外国 TIN 要求。](#en_US_2024_publink100015526 "Foreign TIN requirement for account holders.")_ ，稍后，这通常也适用于本段中描述的帐户。

**Form W-8BEN-E.**

This form is used by a foreign entity to:

  

**W-8BEN-E 表格。** 

外国实体使用此表格来：

*   Establish foreign status;  
    建立外国身份；
    
*   Establish an entity's chapter 4 status to the extent required for chapter 4 purposes;  
    在第 4 章目的所需的范围内建立实体的第 4 章地位；
    
*   Claim that such entity is the beneficial owner of the income for which the form is being furnished or a partner in a partnership subject to withholding under section 1446(a) or (f) (excluding a partnership or grantor trust); and  
    声称该实体是所提供表格的收入的受益所有人或根据第 1446(a) 或 (f) 条须缴纳预扣税的合伙企业的合伙人（不包括合伙企业或设保人信托）；和
    
*   If applicable, claim a reduced rate of, or exemption from, chapter 3 withholding under an income tax treaty.  
    如果适用，根据所得税条约申请第 3 章预扣税的降低税率或豁免。
    

Form W-8BEN-E may also be used to claim that the foreign entity is exempt from Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding for income that is not subject to chapter 3 withholding and is not a withholdable payment. For example, a foreign entity may provide a Form W-8BEN-E to a broker to establish that the gross proceeds from the sale of securities are not subject to Form 1099 reporting or backup withholding.  
W-8BEN-E 表还可用于声称外国实体免于缴纳 1099 表报告和备用预扣税，以获得不受第 3 章预扣税约束且不属于应预扣税款的收入。例如，外国实体可以向经纪人提供 W-8BEN-E 表格，以确定出售证券的总收益无需缴纳 1099 表格报告或备用预扣税。

An entity payee may also provide a Form W-8BEN-E to establish that certain income from notional principal contracts is not effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business. In addition, a foreign hybrid entity claiming treaty benefits on its own behalf should provide you with a Form W-8BEN-E with respect to the income for which treaty benefits are being claimed. In certain cases, a similar agreed form may be associated with the payment instead of a Form W-8BEN-E.  
实体收款人还可以提供 W-8BEN-E 表格，以证明来自名义主合同的某些收入与美国贸易或业务的行为没有实际联系。此外，代表其自身主张税收协定优惠的外国混合实体应向您提供与所主张税收协定优惠收入相关的 W-8BEN-E 表格。在某些情况下，付款可能会关联类似的商定表格，而不是表格 W-8BEN-E。

**Form W-8ECI.**

This form is used by a foreign person to:

  

**W-8ECI 表格。** 

外国人使用此表格来：

*   Establish foreign status,  
    建立外国身份，
    
*   Claim that such person is the beneficial owner of the income for which the form is being furnished, and  
    声称此人是所提供表格的收入的受益所有人，并且
    
*   Claim that the income is effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business in the United States. (See [_Effectively Connected Income_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224898 "Effectively Connected Income"), later.)  
    声称该收入与在美国进行的贸易或业务有实际联系。 （参见后面的[_有效关联收入_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224898 "Effectively Connected Income")。）
    
*   Claim that the person is a dealer in securities for the exception to withholding under Regulations section 1.1446(f)-4(b)(6). See _[Section 1446(f): PTP Interests](#en_US_2024_publink1000115526 "Section 1446(f): PTP Interests")_, later.  
    声称该人是证券交易商，但根据条例第 1.1446(f)-4(b)(6) 条规定的预扣税除外。请参阅稍后_[第 1446(f) 节：PTP 利益](#en_US_2024_publink1000115526 "Section 1446(f): PTP Interests")_。
    

ECI for which a valid Form W-8ECI has been provided is generally not subject to chapter 3 or chapter 4 withholding.  
已提供有效 W-8ECI 表格的 ECI 通常无需缴纳第 3 章或第 4 章的预扣税。

If a partner submits this form to a partnership, the income claimed to be effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business is subject to withholding under section 1446. If the partner has made, or will make, an election under section 871(d) or 882(d), the partner must submit Form W-8ECI, and attach a copy of the election, or a statement of intent to elect, to the form.  
如果合伙人向合伙企业提交此表格，则声称与美国贸易或业务行为有效相关的收入应根据第 1446 条进行预扣税。如果合伙人已经或将要根据第 871 条做出选择（ d) 或 882(d)，合伙人必须提交 W-8ECI 表格，并在表格中附上选举副本或选举意向声明。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_If the partner's only ECI is the income allocated from the partnership and the partner is not making the election under section 871(d) or 882(d), the partner should provide Form W-8BEN or W-8BEN-E to the partnership.  
如果合伙人唯一的 ECI 是从合伙企业分配的收入，并且合伙人没有根据第 871(d) 或 882(d) 条做出选择，则合伙人应向合伙企业提供 W-8BEN 或 W-8BEN-E 表格。_.

**Form W-8EXP.**

This form is used by a foreign government, international organization, foreign central bank of issue, foreign tax-exempt organization, foreign private foundation, or government of a U.S. territory to:

  

**W-8EXP 表格。** 

外国政府、国际组织、外国发行中央银行、外国免税组织、外国私人基金会或美国领土政府使用此表格来：

*   Establish foreign status,  
    建立外国身份，
    
*   Establish the entity's chapter 4 status to the extent required for chapter 4 purposes,  
    在第 4 章目的所需的范围内建立该实体的第 4 章地位，
    
*   Claim that such person is the beneficial owner of the income for which the form is being furnished, and  
    声称此人是所提供表格的收入的受益所有人，并且
    
*   Claim an exemption from withholding under both chapter 3 and chapter 4 for such entity or that the entity is a foreign private foundation subject to the 4% tax. See section 1443 for the withholding required for a payment made to such an entity.  
    根据第 3 章和第 4 章要求此类实体免除预扣税，或者该实体是外国私人基金会，需缴纳 4% 的税款。有关向此类实体付款所需的预扣税，请参阅第 1443 节。
    

If the government or organization named on the form is a partner in a partnership carrying on a trade or business in the United States, the ECTI allocable to the partner is subject to withholding under section 1446.  
如果表格上指定的政府或组织是在美国开展贸易或业务的合伙企业的合伙人，则分配给该合伙人的 ECTI 须根据第 1446 条规定进行预扣。

See also [_Foreign Governments and Certain Other Foreign Organizations_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225026 "Foreign Governments and Certain Other Foreign Organizations"), later.  
另请参见稍后的[_外国政府和某些其他外国组织_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225026 "Foreign Governments and Certain Other Foreign Organizations")。

#### Foreign Intermediaries and Foreign Flow-Through Entities  
外国中介机构和外国流通实体

Payments made to a foreign intermediary or foreign flow-through entity that is not a QI that assumes primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibility, a WP, a WT, or a branch treated as a U.S. person (see [_U.S. branches of foreign banks and foreign insurance companies_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224801 "U.S. branches of foreign banks and foreign insurance companies."), earlier) are treated as made to the payees on whose behalf the intermediary or entity acts except when the intermediary or flow-through entity is subject to chapter 4 withholding. See [_Flow-Through Entities_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224783 "Flow-Through Entities") and [_Foreign intermediaries_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224792 "Foreign Intermediaries"), earlier. The Form W-8IMY provided by a foreign intermediary or flow-through entity must be accompanied by additional information for you to be able to reliably associate the payment with a payee. The additional information required depends on the type of intermediary or flow-through entity and the extent of the withholding responsibilities it assumes.  
向不属于承担第 3 章和第 4 章主要预扣责任的 QI、WP、WT 或被视为美国人的分行（参见[_外国银行的美国分行和外国银行分行）的_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224801 "U.S. branches of foreign banks and foreign insurance companies.")外国中介机构或外国流通实体支付的款项[_保险公司_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224801 "U.S. branches of foreign banks and foreign insurance companies.")（之前）被视为向中介或实体代表其行事的收款人支付，除非中介或流通实体须缴纳第 4 章预扣税。请参阅前面的[_流通实体_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224783 "Flow-Through Entities")和[_外国中介机构_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224792 "Foreign Intermediaries")。外国中介或流通实体提供的 W-8IMY 表格必须附有其他信息，以便您能够可靠地将付款与收款人关联起来。所需的额外信息取决于中介或流通实体的类型及其承担的预扣责任的程度。

**Form W-8IMY.**

This form is used by foreign intermediaries and foreign flow-through entities, as well as certain U.S. branches for chapter 3 or 4 purposes, or when applicable, for section 1446(a) or (f) purposes, to:

  

**W-8IMY 表格。** 

外国中介机构和外国流通实体以及某些美国分支机构出于第 3 章或第 4 章的目的，或在适用的情况下，出于第 1446(a) 或 (f) 条的目的，使用此表格来：

*   Represent that a foreign person is a QI or NQI;  
    表示外国人是QI或NQI；
    
*   Establish the entity’s chapter 4 status when required for chapter 4 purposes;  
    当需要满足第 4 章的目的时，建立该实体的第 4 章地位；
    
*   When applicable, certify that the entity is a participating FFI, a registered deemed-compliant FFI, or a QI that may provide a withholding statement allocating a payment to a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees;  
    适用时，证明该实体是参与 FFI、已注册的视为合规 FFI 或可提供将付款分配给美国收款人第 4 章预扣税率池的预扣税声明的 QI；
    
*   Represent, if applicable, that the QI is assuming primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibility and/or primary Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding responsibility;  
    如果适用，表示 QI 承担第 3 章和第 4 章的主要预扣税责任和/或主要 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税责任；
    
*   Represent that a foreign partnership or a foreign simple or grantor trust is a withholding foreign partnership or a withholding foreign trust;  
    表示外国合伙企业或外国简单信托或设保人信托是预扣税外国合伙企业或预扣税外国信托；
    
*   Represent that a foreign flow-through entity is a nonwithholding foreign partnership, or a nonwithholding foreign trust;  
    表示外国流通实体是非预扣税的外国合伙企业或非预扣税的外国信托；
    
*   Represent that the provider is a U.S. branch of a foreign bank or insurance company and either is agreeing to be treated as a U.S. person or is transmitting documentation of the persons on whose behalf it is acting for the payments;  
    表示提供商是外国银行或保险公司的美国分行，并且同意被视为美国人，或者正在传输其代表付款的人员的文件；
    
*   Represent its status as a qualified securities lender with respect to payments of U.S. source substitute dividends;  
    代表其在支付美国来源替代股息方面作为合格证券出借人的地位；
    
*   Represent its status as a QI acting as a QDD for certain payments; and  
    表示其作为 QI 的状态，充当某些付款的 QDD；和
    
*   Represent that, for purposes of section 1446, it is an upper-tier foreign partnership or a foreign grantor trust and that the form is being used to transmit the required documentation. For information on qualifying as an upper-tier foreign partnership, see Regulations section 1.1446-5.  
    表明，就第 1446 条而言，它是一家高级外国合伙企业或外国设保人信托，并且该表格用于传送所需文件。有关高级外国合伙企业资格的信息，请参阅《条例》第 1.1446-5 条。
    

For purposes of chapter 4, an intermediary or flow-through entity that is a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI receiving a withholdable payment may, instead of providing documentation for each payee, provide pooled allocation information, as described under [_FFI withholding statement_](#en_US_2024_publink100015357 "FFI withholding statement."), later.  
就第 4 章而言，作为参与 FFI 或接收预扣付款的注册视为合规 FFI 的中介或流通实体可以提供汇总分配信息，而不是为每个收款人提供文件，如[_FFI 预扣税声明_](#en_US_2024_publink100015357 "FFI withholding statement.")中所述，之后。

_**FFI withholding statement.**_

An FFI withholding statement must be provided by a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI (including a U.S. branch of a participating FFI that is not treated as a U.S. person) that is an NQI, nonwithholding foreign partnership, nonwithholding foreign trust, or a QI that makes an election to be withheld on for chapter 4 purposes (that is, a QI that does not assume chapter 3 or 4 withholding responsibility), as described under [_Qualified Intermediary (QI)_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224837 "Qualified Intermediary (QI)"), later.

  

_**FFI 预扣税声明。** _

FFI 预扣税声明必须由参与 FFI 或注册的视为合规 FFI（包括不被视为美国人的参与 FFI 的美国分支机构）提供，该 FFI 是 NQI、非预扣税外国合伙企业、非预扣税外国信托或出于第 4 章的目的做出选择扣缴的 QI（即不承担第 3 章或第 4 章扣缴责任的 QI），如后面的[_合格中介机构 (QI)_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224837 "Qualified Intermediary (QI)")中所述。

An FFI withholding statement may include either payee-specific information or pooled information. If the withholding statement includes pooled information, the withholding statement must indicate the portion of the payment allocable to:  
FFI 预扣税声明可能包括收款人特定信息或汇总信息。如果预扣税表包含汇总信息，则预扣税表必须注明可分配给以下人员的付款部分：

*   A chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees,  
    美国收款人的第四章预扣税率池，
    
*   Each class of recalcitrant account holders under Regulations section 1.1471-4(d)(6) or a single pool for a QI, or  
    条例第 1.1471-4(d)(6) 条规定的每一类顽固账户持有人或 QI 的单个池，或
    
*   A class of nonparticipating FFIs.  
    一类非参与 FFI。
    

If the withholding statement includes payee-specific information, it must indicate both the portion of the payment allocated to each payee and each payee’s chapter 4 status.  
如果预扣税表包含收款人特定信息，则必须注明分配给每个收款人的付款部分以及每个收款人的第 4 章状态。

Any withholding statement provided by an FFI other than an FFI acting as a WP, WT, or QI with respect to the account must also identify each intermediary or flow-through entity that receives the payment and such entity’s chapter 4 status and GIIN, when applicable.  
由作为 WP、WT 或 QI 的 FFI 之外的 FFI 提供的任何预扣税声明还必须标明接收付款的每个中介或流通实体以及该实体的第 4 章状态和 GIIN（如果适用） 。

For additional information on the requirements for FFI withholding statements, see Regulations section 1.1471-3(c)(3)(iii)(B)(2).  
有关 FFI 预扣税表要求的更多信息，请参阅法规第 1.1471-3(c)(3)(iii)(B)(2) 节。

_**Chapter 4 withholding statement.**_

A chapter 4 withholding statement must be provided by the following.

  

_**第四章扣缴声明。** _

必须按以下方式提供第 4 章预扣税声明。

*   A territory financial institution that does not agree to be treated as a U.S. person.  
    不同意被视为美国人的领土金融机构。
    
*   A U.S. branch that is not a U.S. branch of a participating FFI.  
    并非参与 FFI 的美国分支机构的美国分支机构。
    
*   An NFFE or certified deemed-compliant FFI that is an NQI, nonwithholding foreign partnership, or nonwithholding foreign trust and is not the payee.  
    NFFE 或经过认证的视为合规 FFI，属于 NQI、非预扣税外国合伙企业或非预扣税外国信托，且不是收款人。
    

A chapter 4 withholding statement must contain the following.  
第 4 章预扣税声明必须包含以下内容。

*   The name, address, TIN (if any), entity type, and chapter 4 status of each payee.  
    每个收款人的姓名、地址、纳税人识别号（如果有）、实体类型和第 4 章状态。
    
*   The amount allocated to each payee.  
    分配给每个收款人的金额。
    
*   A valid withholding certificate or other appropriate documentation sufficient to establish the chapter 4 status of each payee, and each intermediary or flow-through entity that receives the payment on behalf of the payee.  
    有效的预扣税证书或其他适当文件，足以确定每个收款人以及代表收款人接收付款的每个中介或流通实体的第 4 章身份。
    
*   Any other information the withholding agent reasonably requests in order to fulfill its obligations under chapter 4.  
    扣缴义务人为履行第 4 章规定的义务而合理要求的任何其他信息。
    

A chapter 4 withholding statement is permitted to provide pooled allocation information with respect to payees that are treated as nonparticipating FFIs.  
第 4 章预扣税声明允许提供有关被视为非参与 FFI 的收款人的汇总分配信息。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_A Form W-8 must include a U.S. TIN for a partner to be valid for purposes of a claim of exemption or reduced withholding under section 1446(a) or (f). See the instructions to the applicable Form W-8.  
W-8 表格必须包含合伙人的美国 TIN，才能根据第 1446(a) 或 (f) 条提出豁免或减少预扣税的申请。请参阅适用的 W-8 表格的说明。_.

#### Qualified Intermediary (QI)  
合格中介人 (QI)

In most cases, a QI is any foreign intermediary that has entered into a _[QI agreement](#en_US_2024_publink100015349 "QI agreement.")_ (discussed earlier) with the IRS with respect to the withholding and reporting required under chapters 3 and 4 and for purposes of Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding under section 3406. Additionally, starting January 1, 2023, a QI may also assume certain withholding responsibilities with respect to PTP distributions (including withholding under section 1446(a)) and certain transfers of PTP interests for section 1446(f) purposes when acting as an intermediary. For discussion of those provisions, see _[Publicly Traded Partnership Distributions (PTP Distributions)](#en_US_2024_publink1000225085 "Publicly Traded Partnership Distributions (PTP Distributions)")_ and _[Section 1446(f): PTP Interests](#en_US_2024_publink1000115526 "Section 1446(f): PTP Interests")_, later. A foreign entity that is a QI acting as a QDD or that is acting with respect to payments of substitute interest (as permitted by the QI agreement) can act as a QI even though it is not receiving payments as an intermediary. A foreign entity that has received a QI employer identification number (QI-EIN) may represent on Form W-8IMY that it is a QI. The QI can claim that it is a QI until the IRS revokes its QI-EIN.  
在大多数情况下，QI 是与 IRS 就第 3 章和第 4 章要求的预扣税和报告以及第 3406 条下的 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税的目的签订_[QI 协议](#en_US_2024_publink100015349 "QI agreement.")_（前面讨论过）的任何外国中间人此外，从 2023 年 1 月 1 日开始，QI 还可以承担与 PTP 分配相关的某些预扣税责任（包括根据第 1 节规定的预扣税责任）。 1446(a)) 以及作为中间人时出于第 1446(f) 条目的进行的某些 PTP 利益转让。有关这些条款的讨论，请参阅后面的_[公开交易合伙分配（PTP 分配）](#en_US_2024_publink1000225085 "Publicly Traded Partnership Distributions (PTP Distributions)")_和_[第 1446(f) 节：PTP 权益](#en_US_2024_publink1000115526 "Section 1446(f): PTP Interests")_。作为 QDD 或支付替代利息（经 QI 协议允许）的 QI 外国实体可以充当 QI，即使它不作为中间人接收付款。收到 QI 雇主识别号 (QI-EIN) 的外国实体可以在 W-8IMY 表格上表明其是 QI。 QI 可以声称自己是 QI，直到 IRS 撤销其 QI-EIN。

A QI can be either an _[FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015535 "Foreign financial institution (FFI).")_ or an _[NFFE](#en_US_2024_publink100015475 "Non-financial foreign entity (NFFE).")_. An FFI that is a QI must be a _[participating FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015541 "Participating FFI.")_ (including a _[reporting Model 2 FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015545 "Reporting Model 2 FFI.")_), a _[registered deemed-compliant FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015543 "Registered deemed-compliant FFI.")_ (including a _[reporting Model 1 FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015544 "Reporting Model 1 FFI.")_ and a nonreporting Model 2 FFI treated as a _[registered deemed-compliant FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015543 "Registered deemed-compliant FFI.")_), or an FFI treated as a _[deemed-compliant FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015533 "Deemed-compliant FFI.")_ under an applicable Model 1 IGA that is subject to similar due diligence and reporting requirements with respect to its U.S. accounts as those applicable to a registered deemed-compliant FFI (including the requirement to register with the IRS) (defined in the QI agreement as a “registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI”). Thus, you must identify the chapter 4 status of an FFI, certifying its status as a QI as one of the chapter 4 statuses referenced in the preceding sentence on a Form W-8IMY when a chapter 4 status is required for chapter 4 purposes.  
QI 可以是_[FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015535 "Foreign financial institution (FFI).")_或_[NFFE](#en_US_2024_publink100015475 "Non-financial foreign entity (NFFE).")_ 。属于 QI 的 FFI 必须是_[参与 FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015541 "Participating FFI.")_ （包括_[报告模型 2 FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015545 "Reporting Model 2 FFI.")_ ）、_[已注册的视为合规 FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015543 "Registered deemed-compliant FFI.")_ （包括_[报告模型 1 FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015544 "Reporting Model 1 FFI.")_和被视为_[注册视为合规 FFI 的](#en_US_2024_publink100015543 "Registered deemed-compliant FFI.")_非报告模型 2 FFI），或者根据适用的模型 1 IGA 被视为_[视为合规 FFI 的](#en_US_2024_publink100015533 "Deemed-compliant FFI.")_FFI，其美国账户须遵守与适用于注册的视为合规 FFI 类似的尽职调查和报告要求（包括要求向 IRS 注册）（QI 协议中定义为“已注册的视为合规模型 1 IGA FFI”）。因此，您必须识别 FFI 的第 4 章状态，当第 4 章目的需要第 4 章状态时，将其作为 QI 的状态证明为表格 W-8IMY 上一句中引用的第 4 章状态之一。

**Responsibilities and documentation for chapters 3 and 4.**

Payments made to a QI that does not assume primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibilities are treated as paid to its account holders. However, a QI is not required to provide you with documentation it obtains from its foreign account holders or from U.S. exempt recipients (U.S. persons exempt from Form 1099 reporting). Instead, it provides you with a withholding statement that contains either chapter 3 or chapter 4 withholding rate pool information. A chapter 4 withholding rate pool is a payment of a single type of income that is a withholdable payment that is allocated to payees that are nonparticipating FFIs or recalcitrant account holders (in a single pool). A chapter 4 withholding rate pool also means a payment of a single type of income that is allocated to U.S. payees when the QI provides the certification required on Form W-8IMY for allocating payments to this pool and a withholding statement. A QI may include in its chapter 4 withholding rate pools its direct account holders as well as account holders of another QI or a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI. With respect to a payment to a foreign person for which no chapter 4 withholding is required, a chapter 3 withholding rate pool is a payment of a single type of income that is subject to a single rate of withholding and that is reported on Form 1042-S under a single chapter 4 exemption code. Payments made to U.S. exempt recipients may also be included in a chapter 3 withholding rate pool to which withholding does not apply.

  

**第 3 章和第 4 章的职责和文档。** 

向不承担第 3 章和第 4 章主要预扣税责任的 QI 支付的款项将被视为支付给其账户持有人。然而，QI 无需向您提供其从其外国账户持有人或美国豁免接收人（免于 1099 表格报告的美国人）处获得的文件。相反，它为您提供一份预扣税报表，其中包含第 3 章或第 4 章预扣税率池信息。第 4 章预扣税率池是单一类型收入的支付，即分配给非参与 FFI 或顽固账户持有人（在单个池中）的收款人的可预扣付款。第 4 章预扣税率池还意味着，当 QI 提供表格 W-8IMY 上所需的证明以向该池分配付款和预扣税表时，分配给美国收款人的单一类型收入的付款。 QI 可以在其第 4 章预扣税率池中包括其直接账户持有人以及另一个 QI 或参与的 FFI 或注册的视为合规 FFI 的账户持有人。对于无需根据第 4 章预扣税的规定向外国人支付的款项，第 3 章预扣税税率池是对单一类型收入的付款，须缴纳单一预扣税，并在 1042 表格中报告。 S 属于单一第 4 章豁免代码。向美国豁免收款人支付的款项也可能包含在不适用预扣税的第 3 章预扣税率池中。

A QI is required to provide you with information regarding U.S. nonexempt recipients (U.S. persons subject to Form 1099 information reporting) and to provide you withholding rate pool information separately for each such U.S. person unless it has assumed primary Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding responsibility and meets the requirements to include these recipients in a U.S. payee pool. For the alternative procedure for providing withholding rate pool information for U.S. nonexempt persons not included in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees, see the [Instructions for Form W-8IMY](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-w-8-imy).  
QI 需要向您提供有关美国非豁免受益人（须遵守 1099 表格信息报告的美国人）的信息，并为您单独提供每个此类美国人的预扣税率池信息，除非该机构已承担主要 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税责任，并且满足将这些收款人纳入美国收款人池的要求。有关为未包含在第 4 章美国收款人预扣税率池中的美国非豁免人士提供预扣税率池信息的替代程序，请参阅[表格 W-8IMY 的说明](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-w-8-imy)。

The withholding statement must:  
预扣税声明必须：

1.  Designate those accounts for which it acts as a QI;  
    指定其充当 QI 的账户；
    
2.  Designate those accounts for which it assumes primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibility and/or primary Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding responsibility;  
    指定其承担主要第 3 章和第 4 章预扣税责任和/或主要 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税责任的账户；
    
3.  If applicable, designate the accounts for which it acts as a qualified securities lender with respect to any U.S. source substitute dividend payments;  
    如果适用，指定其作为任何美国来源替代股息支付的合格证券出借人的账户；
    
4.  If applicable, designate those accounts for which it acts as a QDD;  
    如果适用，请指定其充当 QDD 的账户；
    
5.  Provide sufficient information for you to allocate the payment, as applicable, to chapter 3 withholding rate pools and, for payments that are withholdable payments, chapter 4 withholding rate pools of nonparticipating FFIs and recalcitrant account holders when the QI has not assumed primary chapter 3 or 4 withholding responsibility; and  
    当 QI 未采用主要第 3 章或4 隐瞒责任；和
    
6.  Provide sufficient information for you to allocate payments to each U.S. nonexempt recipient or to a pool of U.S. payees to the extent described earlier under this heading.  
    提供足够的信息，以便您按照本标题前面所述的范围将付款分配给每个美国非豁免收款人或一组美国收款人。
    

The extent to which you must have withholding rate pool information depends on the withholding and reporting obligations assumed by the QI.  
您必须掌握预扣税率池信息的程度取决于 QI 承担的预扣和报告义务。

If a QI that is permitted to do so by the QI agreement obtains documentary evidence under the “KYC” rules that apply to the QI under local law, and the documentary evidence is of a type specified in an attachment to the QI agreement, the documentary evidence remains valid until there is a change in circumstances or the QI knows the information is incorrect. A QI may rely on a Form W-8 until its validity expires under Regulations section 1.1441-1(e)(4)(ii) and may rely on documentary evidence not obtained pursuant to “KYC” rules until its validity expires under Regulations section 1.6049-5(c).  
如果 QI 协议允许的 QI 根据当地法律适用于 QI 的“KYC”规则获取文件证据，并且该文件证据属于 QI 协议附件中指定的类型，则该文件证据在情况发生变化或 QI 知道信息不正确之前，证据仍然有效。 QI 可以依赖表格 W-8，直至其根据法规第 1.1441-1(e)(4)(ii) 条的规定失效，并且可以依赖未根据“KYC”规则获得的文件证据，直到其根据法规第 1.1441-1(e)(4)(ii) 条的规定失效为止1.6049-5(c)。

_**Primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibilities not assumed.**_

If a QI does not assume primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibility or primary Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding responsibility for the payment, you can reliably associate the payment with valid documentation only to the extent you can reliably determine the part of the payment that relates to each withholding rate pool for foreign and U.S. payees. Unless the alternative procedure applies and the QI is permitted to include U.S. nonexempt recipients in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees, the QI must provide you with a separate withholding rate pool for each U.S. nonexempt recipient that must be reported on Form 1099. If you and the QI agree, the QI may apply the alternative procedures for U.S. nonexempt recipients by establishing a single withholding rate pool (not subject to backup withholding) for all U.S. nonexempt recipient account holders for whom the QI is required to report on Form 1099 and has provided you with Forms W-9 prior to you making the reportable payment, or, if applicable, designated broker proceeds to which backup withholding does not apply. The QI must provide a Form W-9 or, in the absence of the form, the name, address, and TIN, if available, for each U.S. nonexempt recipient.

  

_**主要第3章和第4章不承担扣留责任。** _

如果 QI 不承担第 3 章和第 4 章的主要预扣税责任或主要 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税责任，则只有在您能够可靠地确定相关付款部分的情况下，您才能可靠地将付款与有效文件关联起来外国和美国收款人的每个预扣税率池。除非适用替代程序并且 QI 被允许将美国非豁免收款人纳入第 4 章美国收款人预扣税率池中，否则 QI 必须为每个美国非豁免收款人提供单独的预扣税率池，并且必须在 1099 表格中报告该预扣税率池。如果您和 QI 同意，QI 可以为美国非豁免收款人应用替代程序，为所有美国非豁免收款人账户持有人建立单一预扣税率池（不受备用预扣税的约束） QI 需要在表格 1099 上进行报告，并在您进行应报告付款之前向您提供表格 W-9，或者在适用的情况下，向您提供不适用备用预扣税的指定经纪人收益。 QI 必须提供 W-9 表格，或者在没有表格的情况下，提供每位美国非豁免收件人的姓名、地址和 TIN（如果有）。

_**Primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibilities assumed.**_

If you make a payment to a QI that assumes primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibilities (but not primary Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding responsibility), you can reliably associate the payment with valid documentation only to the extent you can reliably determine the part of the payment that relates to the chapter 4 withholding rate pools and chapter 3 withholding rate pools, as applicable, and the part of the payment attributable to withholding rate pools for each U.S. nonexempt recipient, unless the alternative procedure applies for Form 1099 reporting and/or backup withholding purposes. The QI must provide a Form W-9 or, in the absence of the form, the name, address, and TIN, if available, for such person.

  

_**主要第3章和第4章承担的扣缴责任。** _

如果您向承担第 3 章和第 4 章主要预扣税责任（但不承担主要 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税责任）的 QI 付款，您可以可靠地将付款与有效文件关联起来，前提是您可以可靠地确定与第 4 章预扣税率池和第 3 章预扣税率池（如适用）相关的付款，以及可归属于每个美国非豁免收款人的预扣税率池的付款部分，除非替代程序适用于 1099 表格报告和/或备份预扣税目的。 QI 必须提供 W-9 表格，或者在没有表格的情况下，提供该人员的姓名、地址和 TIN（如果有）。

_**Primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibilities and Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding responsibilities assumed.**_

If you make a payment to a QI that assumes primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibilities and primary Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding responsibility, you can reliably associate the payment with valid documentation provided that you receive a valid Form W-8IMY. It is not necessary to associate the payment with any chapter 3 or chapter 4 withholding rate pools.

  

_**主要第 3 章和第 4 章预扣税责任以及 1099 表格报告和承担的备用预扣税责任。** _

如果您向承担第 3 章和第 4 章主要预扣税责任以及主要表格 1099 报告和备用预扣税责任的 QI 付款，只要您收到有效的 W-8IMY 表格，您就可以可靠地将付款与有效文件关联起来。无需将付款与任何第 3 章或第 4 章预扣税率池关联。

If you make a payment to a QI that is also a QDD, the QI must provide a withholding statement designating the accounts for which it acts as a QDD even if it assumes primary withholding responsibility for all payments, unless it is acting as a QDD for all payments it receives.  
如果您向同时也是 QDD 的 QI 付款，则 QI 必须提供一份预扣税声明，指定其充当 QDD 的账户，即使它对所有付款承担主要预扣责任，除非它充当 QDD它收到的所有付款。

**Example.**

You make a payment of U.S. source dividends to a QI. It has five customers: two are foreign persons who have provided documentation entitling them to a 15% rate of withholding on dividends; two are foreign persons subject to a 30% rate of withholding on dividends; and one is a U.S. individual who provides it with a Form W-9. Each customer is entitled to 20% of the dividend payment. The QI does not assume any primary withholding responsibility. The QI gives you a Form W-8IMY with which it associates the Form W-9 and a withholding statement that allocates 40% of the dividend to a 15% withholding rate pool, 40% to a 30% withholding rate pool, and 20% to the U.S. individual. You should report on Forms 1042-S, 40% of the payment as made to a 15% rate dividend pool and 40% of the payment as made to a 30% rate dividend pool. The part of the payment allocable to the U.S. individual (20%) is reportable on Form 1099-DIV.

  

**例子。** 

您向 QI 支付美国来源股息。它有五名客户：其中两名是外国人，他们提供了有权享受 15% 股息预扣税的文件；两人为外国人，需缴纳 30% 的股息预扣税；其中一名美国人向其提供了 W-9 表格。每个客户有权获得20%的股息支付。 QI 不承担任何主要预扣责任。 QI 为您提供一份 W-8IMY 表格，它将 W-9 表格和一份预扣税表关联起来，该预扣税表将 40% 的股息分配给 15% 预扣税率池，将 40% 分配给 30% 预扣税率池，将 20% 分配给 30% 预扣税率池。给美国个人。您应在 1042-S 表格中报告向 15% 利率股息池支付的款项的 40%，以及向 30% 利率股息池支付的 40% 款项。分配给美国个人的付款部分 (20%) 应在 1099-DIV 表格中报告。

**Joint account treatment for chapters 3 and 4.**

A QI may apply joint account treatment to a partnership or trust if the partnership or trust meets the following conditions.

  

**第 3 章和第 4 章的联名账户处理。** 

如果合伙企业或信托满足以下条件，QI 可以对合伙企业或信托实行联名账户处理。

*   It is a nonwithholding foreign partnership or nonwithholding foreign trust that is either a simple or grantor trust.  
    它是非预扣税外国合伙企业或非预扣税外国信托，可以是简单信托，也可以是设保人信托。
    
*   It is a certified deemed-compliant FFI (other than a registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI), an owner-documented FFI with respect to the QI, an exempt beneficial owner, an NFFE, or is covered as an account that is excluded from the definition of financial account under Annex II of an applicable IGA or under Regulations section 1.1471-5(a) and has provided the QI with a certification that it has maintained such chapter 4 status during each certification period.  
    它是经认证的视为合规 FFI（注册的视为合规模型 1 IGA FFI 除外）、与 QI 相关的所有者记录的 FFI、豁免受益所有人、NFFE，或作为排除账户涵盖根据适用的 IGA 附件 II 或条例第 1.1471-5(a) 节中的金融账户定义，并向 QI 提供证明，证明其在每个认证期内保持了第 4 章的此类状态。
    
*   It is a direct account holder of the QI.  
    它是QI的直接账户持有人。
    
*   None of its partners, beneficiaries, or owners is a flow-through entity or is acting as an intermediary for a payment made by the QI to the partnership or trust, and none of its partners, beneficiaries, or owners is a U.S. person.  
    其合作伙伴、受益人或所有者均不是流通实体，也不是 QI 向合伙企业或信托付款的中介人，其合作伙伴、受益人或所有者均不是美国人。
    
*   None of its foreign partners, beneficiaries, or owners is subject to withholding or reporting under chapter 4.  
    其外国合作伙伴、受益人或所有者均不受第 4 章规定的预扣税或报告义务。
    
*   It agrees to make available upon request to the QI (or QI’s reviewer) records that establish it has provided the QI with documentation for purposes of chapters 3 and 4 for all of its partners, beneficiaries, or owners.  
    它同意根据要求向 QI（或 QI 审核者）提供记录，证明其已向 QI 提供了用于第 3 章和第 4 章之目的的所有合作伙伴、受益人或所有者的文档。
    

For information on these rules, see section 4.05 of the QI agreement in Revenue Procedure 2022-43, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2022-52\_IRB#RP-2022-43](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2022-52_IRB#REV-PROC-2022-43).  
有关这些规则的信息，请参阅 2022-43 年收入程序中 QI 协议的第 4.05 节，网址为[IRS.gov/irb/2022-52\_IRB#RP-2022-43](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2022-52_IRB#REV-PROC-2022-43) 。

**Agency option.**

A QI may apply the agency option to a partnership or trust under which the partnership or trust agrees to act as an agent of the QI and to apply the provisions of the QI agreement to its partners, beneficiaries, or owners. A QI and a partnership or trust may only apply the agency option if the partnership or trust meets the following conditions.

  

**代理选项。** 

QI 可以将代理选项应用于合伙企业或信托，在该合伙企业或信托下，合伙企业或信托同意充当 QI 的代理人，并将 QI 协议的条款应用于其合伙人、受益人或所有者。仅当合伙企业或信托满足以下条件时，QI 和合伙企业或信托才可以应用代理选项。

*   It is a nonwithholding foreign partnership or nonwithholding foreign trust that is either a simple or grantor trust.  
    它是非预扣税外国合伙企业或非预扣税外国信托，可以是简单信托，也可以是设保人信托。
    
*   It is either a direct account holder of the QI or an indirect account holder of the QI that is a direct partner, beneficiary, or owner of a partnership or trust to which the QI also applies the agency option.  
    它可以是 QI 的直接账户持有人，也可以是 QI 的间接账户持有人，即 QI 也应用代理选项的合伙企业或信托的直接合伙人、受益人或所有者。
    
*   It is an FFI that is a certified deemed-compliant FFI (other than a registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI), an owner-documented FFI with respect to the QI, an NFFE, an exempt beneficial owner, or is covered as an account that is excluded from the definition of financial account under Annex II of an applicable IGA or under Regulations section 1.1471-5(a) and has provided the QI with a certification that it has maintained such chapter 4 status during each certification period.  
    该 FFI 是经过认证的视为合规 FFI（注册的视为合规模型 1 IGA FFI 除外）、与 QI 相关的所有者记录的 FFI、NFFE、豁免受益所有人或被涵盖为该账户被排除在适用 IGA 附件 II 或条例第 1.1471-5(a) 条规定的金融账户定义之外，并已向 QI 提供证明，表明其在每个认证期内保持了第 4 章的此类状态。
    
*   None of its partners, beneficiaries, or owners is a withholding foreign trust, withholding foreign partnership, participating FFI, registered deemed-compliant FFI, registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI, or another QI acting as an intermediary for a payment made by the QI to the partnership or trust.  
    其合作伙伴、受益人或所有者均不是预扣税外国信托、预扣税外国合伙企业、参与型 FFI、注册视为合规 FFI、注册视为合规模型 1 IGA FFI 或充当支付方付款中介的其他 QI。 QI 为合伙企业或信托机构。
    
*   It agrees to permit the QI to treat its direct and indirect partners, beneficiaries, or owners as direct and indirect account holders, respectively, of the QI under the QI agreement.  
    它同意允许 QI 将其直接和间接合作伙伴、受益人或所有者分别视为 QI 协议下 QI 的直接和间接账户持有人。
    
*   It agrees to comply with the compliance procedures of the QI agreement.  
    其同意遵守QI协议的合规程序。
    

For information on these rules, see section 4.06 of the QI agreement in Revenue Procedure 2022-43, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2022-52\_IRB#RP-2022-43](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2022-52_IRB#REV-PROC-2022-43).  
有关这些规则的信息，请参阅 2022-43 年收入程序中 QI 协议的第 4.06 节，网址为[IRS.gov/irb/2022-52\_IRB#RP-2022-43](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2022-52_IRB#REV-PROC-2022-43) 。

**Form 1042-S reporting.**

A QI is generally permitted to report payments made to its foreign account holders on a pooled basis rather than reporting payments to each account holder specifically. Pooled basis reporting is not available for payments to certain account holders, such as nonqualified intermediaries, _[flow-through entities](#en_US_2024_publink1000224783 "Flow-Through Entities")_ (discussed earlier) and certain of their account holders and owners, private arrangement intermediaries, and, in certain circumstances, qualified intermediaries, withholding foreign partnerships, and withholding foreign trusts. Notwithstanding these requirements, separate Forms 1042-S are not issued to account holders that the QI is permitted to include in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool.

  

**1042-S 表格报告。** 

一般情况下，QI 可以汇总报告向其外国账户持有人支付的款项，而不是专门向每个账户持有人报告支付的款项。汇总基础报告不适用于向某些账户持有人（例如不合格中介机构、_[流通实体](#en_US_2024_publink1000224783 "Flow-Through Entities")_（前面讨论过）及其某些账户持有人和所有者、私人安排中介机构以及在某些情况下的合格中介机构）支付的款项，预扣外国税合伙企业，以及扣留外国信托。尽管有这些要求，但不会向 QI 被允许纳入第 4 章预扣税率池的账户持有人发放单独的 1042-S 表格。

**Collective refund procedures.**

A QI may seek a refund of tax withheld under chapters 3 and 4 on behalf of its account holders when the QI has not issued a Form 1042-S to the account holders that received the payment that was subject to overwithholding. The account holders, therefore, are not required to file claims for refund with the IRS to obtain refunds, but rather may obtain them from the QI. A QI may obtain a refund of tax withheld under chapter 4, however, to the extent permitted under the QI agreement.

  

**集体退款程序。** 

如果 QI 未向收到预扣款项的账户持有人签发 1042-S 表格，则 QI 可以代表其账户持有人申请退还根据第 3 章和第 4 章扣缴的税款。因此，账户持有人无需向 IRS 提出退款申请即可获得退款，而是可以从 QI 处获得退款。然而，在 QI 协议允许的范围内，QI 可以获得根据第 4 章扣缴的税款退还。

#### Nonqualified Intermediary (NQI)  
非合格中介（NQI）
