If you are making a payment to an NQI or U.S. branch that is using Form W-8IMY to transmit information about the branch's account holders or customers for chapter 3 or 4 purposes, you can treat the payment (or a part of the payment) as reliably associated with valid documentation from a specific payee only if, before making the payment:  
如果您向 NQI 或美国分行付款，且该分行使用 W-8IMY 表格传输有关分行账户持有人或客户的信息以用于第 3 章或第 4 章，则您可以将这笔付款（或部分付款）视为仅当付款前满足以下条件时，才能与特定收款人的有效文件可靠关联：

*   You can allocate the payment to a valid Form W-8IMY;  
    您可以将付款分配到有效的 W-8IMY 表格中；
    
*   You can reliably determine how much of the payment relates to valid documentation provided by a payee (a person that is not itself a foreign intermediary, flow-through entity, or U.S. branch with a chapter 4 withholding rate pool) (see [_Pooled withholding information_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224849 "Pooled withholding information for chapters 3 and 4."), later); and  
    您可以可靠地确定有多少付款与收款人（本身不是外国中介机构、流通实体或具有第 4 章预扣税率池的美国分支机构的人）提供的有效文件相关（请参阅[_汇总预扣税信息_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224849 "Pooled withholding information for chapters 3 and 4.")，之后）;和
    
*   You have sufficient information to report the payment on Form 1042-S or Form 1099, if reporting is required.  
    如果需要报告，您有足够的信息在 1042-S 表格或 1099 表格上报告付款情况。
    

**Withholding statement.**

The NQI or U.S. branch must give you certain information on a withholding statement that is associated with the Form W-8IMY for chapter 3 or 4 purposes. A withholding statement must be updated to keep the information accurate prior to each payment. See, however, Regulations section 1.1441-3(e)(4)(iv)(C) for when a withholding agent may instead accept an alternative withholding statement.

  

**扣留声明。** 

NQI 或美国分支机构必须向您提供与 W-8IMY 表格相关的预扣税声明的某些信息，以用于第 3 章或第 4 章的目的。每次付款前必须更新预扣税单，以保持信息准确。但是，请参阅法规第 1.1441-3(e)(4)(iv)(C) 条了解扣缴义务人何时可以接受替代扣缴声明。

_**For chapter 4 purposes.**_

An NQI receiving a withholdable payment must provide a withholding statement which satisfies the requirements of an FFI withholding statement or, if the NQI is not a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI, a chapter 4 withholding statement.

  

_**用于第 4 章的目的。** _

收到应扣付款的 NQI 必须提供满足 FFI 扣缴声明要求的扣缴声明，或者，如果 NQI 不是参与的 FFI 或注册的视为合规 FFI，则必须提供第 4 章扣缴声明。

An FFI withholding statement may allocate the payment to chapter 4 reporting rate pools (as appropriate), including a chapter 4 withholding rate pool for nonparticipating FFIs, recalcitrant account holders (in each class of account holders, as described in the chapter 4 regulations), and, for an NQI that is a participating FFI (including a reporting Model 2 FFI) or a registered deemed-compliant FFI (including a reporting Model 1 FFI), U.S. payees. However, an NQI may allocate a payment of a reportable amount (regardless of whether the payment is a withholdable payment) to a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees when the NQI satisfies the requirements for providing such a pool, including the requirement to certify to its status as a participating FFI, including a reporting Model 2 FFI, or registered deemed-compliant FFI, including a reporting Model 1 FFI.  
FFI 预扣税报表可以将付款分配给第 4 章报告税率池（如适用），包括针对非参与 FFI、顽固账户持有人（按第 4 章规定所述的各类账户持有人）的第 4 章预扣税率池，对于参与 FFI（包括报告模型 2 FFI）或注册的视为合规 FFI（包括报告模型 1 FFI）的 NQI，美国收款人。然而，当 NQI 满足提供此类池的要求（包括证明的要求）时，NQI 可以将应报告金额的付款（无论该付款是否为可预扣付款）分配给美国收款人的第 4 章预扣税率池。其作为参与 FFI 的身份，包括报告模型 2 FFI，或注册的视为合规 FFI，包括报告模型 1 FFI。

If the FFI withholding statement instead includes payee-specific information for purposes of chapter 4, it must indicate both the portion of the payment allocated to each payee and each payee’s chapter 4 status. The withholding statement must also identify each intermediary or flow-through entity that is receiving a payment (excluding any intermediary or flow-through entity that is an account holder or interest holder in another QI, WP, or WT), each such entity’s chapter 4 status and GIIN (if applicable) when required for chapter 4 purposes, and the chapter 4 withholding rate pools associated with each such entity.  
如果 FFI 预扣税声明包含用于第 4 章目的的收款人特定信息，则它必须表明分配给每个收款人的付款部分以及每个收款人的第 4 章状态。预扣税声明还必须标明正在接收付款的每个中介或流通实体（不包括作为另一个 QI、WP 或 WT 的账户持有人或利益持有人的任何中介或流通实体），每个此类实体的第 4 章出于第 4 章目的需要时的身份和 GIIN（如果适用），以及与每个此类实体相关的第 4 章预扣税率池。

A chapter 4 withholding statement must contain the name, address, TIN (if any), entity type, chapter 4 status of each payee, the amount allocated to each payee, and a valid withholding certificate or other documentation sufficient to establish each payee’s chapter 4 status for payees that are not included in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of nonparticipating FFIs. The withholding statement must also identify each intermediary or flow-through entity that is receiving a payment (excluding any intermediary or flow-through entity that is an account holder or interest holder in another QI, WP, or WT), each such entity’s chapter 4 status and GIIN (if applicable), and the chapter 4 withholding rate pools associated with each such entity. An allocation of a payment to an NQI, nonwithholding foreign partnership, or nonwithholding foreign trust of an amount subject to chapter 3 withholding to a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees must identify the payees consistent with the description in Regulations section 1.1471-3(c)(3)(iii)(B)(2)(iii).  
第 4 章预扣税声明必须包含姓名、地址、纳税人识别号（如果有）、实体类型、每个收款人的第 4 章状态、分配给每个收款人的金额以及有效的预扣税证书或足以证明每个收款人第 4 章的其他文件未包含在第 4 章非参与 FFI 预扣税率池中的收款人的身份。预扣税声明还必须标明正在接收付款的每个中介或流通实体（不包括作为另一个 QI、WP 或 WT 的账户持有人或利益持有人的任何中介或流通实体），每个此类实体的第 4 章状态和 GIIN（如果适用），以及与每个此类实体相关的第 4 章预扣税率池。将受第 3 章规定的预扣税金额分配给 NQI、非预扣税外国合伙企业或非预扣税外国信托基金至美国收款人第 4 章预扣税率池的付款必须按照条例第 1.1471-3 条（ c)(3)(iii)(B)(2)(iii)。

_**For chapter 3 purposes.**_

The withholding statement should allocate for chapter 3 purposes only the portion of the payment that was not allocated to a chapter 4 withholding rate pool or to a payee identified on a withholding statement to whom withholding was applied under chapter 4. For chapter 3 purposes, a withholding statement must include the information described below for a reportable amount.

  

_**用于第 3 章的目的。** _

就第 3 章而言，预扣税表应仅分配未分配至第 4 章预扣税率池或预扣税表中确定的根据第 4 章适用预扣税的收款人的部分付款。就第 3 章而言，预扣税声明必须包含下述可报告金额的信息。

1.  The name, address, and TIN (if any, or if required) of each person for whom documentation is provided.  
    为其提供文件的每个人的姓名、地址和纳税人识别号（如果有或需要的话）。
    
2.  The type of documentation (documentary evidence, Form W-8, or Form W-9) for every person for whom documentation has been provided, and, for a withholdable payment, that the documentation establishes the payee’s chapter 4 status to the extent required for chapter 4 purposes.  
    已为其提供文件的每个人的文件类型（文件证据、表格 W-8 或表格 W-9），并且对于可预扣付款，该文件在所需范围内确定收款人的第 4 章身份第 4 章目的。
    
3.  The status of the person for whom the documentation has been provided, such as whether the person is a U.S. exempt recipient, U.S. nonexempt recipient, or a foreign person. For a foreign person, the statement must indicate whether the person is the beneficial owner or a foreign intermediary, flow-through entity, or a U.S. branch that is not included in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool or in a pool of payees under the alternative procedures (see [_Alternative procedure_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224847 "Alternative procedure."), later).  
    已提供文件的人的身份，例如该人是否是美国豁免接收人、美国非豁免接收人或外国人。对于外国人，该声明必须表明该人是否是受益所有人或外国中介、流通实体或未包含在第 4 章预扣税率池或替代方案下的收款人池中的美国分支机构程序（参见后面的[_替代程序_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224847 "Alternative procedure.")）。
    
4.  The type of recipient the person is, based on the recipient codes used on Form 1042-S.  
    该人的收件人类型，基于表格 1042-S 上使用的收件人代码。
    
5.  Information allocating each payment, by income type, to each payee (including U.S. exempt and nonexempt recipients) for whom documentation has been provided that is not included in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool or in a pool of payees under the alternative procedures (see [_Alternative procedure_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224847 "Alternative procedure."), later).  
    按收入类型将每笔付款分配给已提供文件但未包含在第 4 章预扣税率池或替代程序下的收款人池中的每个收款人（包括美国豁免和非豁免收款人）的信息（请参阅[_替代程序）程序_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224847 "Alternative procedure.")，稍后）。
    
6.  The rate of withholding that applies to each foreign person to whom a payment is allocated.  
    适用于每个收到付款的外国人的预扣税率。
    
7.  A foreign payee's country of residence.  
    外国收款人的居住国。
    
8.  If a reduced rate of withholding is claimed under chapter 3, the basis for a reduced rate of withholding (for example, portfolio interest, treaty benefit, etc.).  
    如果根据第 3 章要求降低预扣税率，则为降低预扣税率的依据（例如投资组合利息、协定优惠等）。
    
9.  In the case of treaty benefits claimed by entities, whether the applicable limitation on benefits statement and the statement that the foreign person derives the income for which treaty benefits are claimed, have been made.  
    对于实体主张协定待遇的，是否已作出适用的优惠限制声明以及外国人取得协定待遇所得的声明。
    
10.  The name, address, and TIN (if any) and, for a withholdable payment, the chapter 4 status (if required) and GIIN (if applicable) of any other NQI, flow-through entity, or U.S. branch from which the payee will directly receive a payment.  
    收款人从其发出的任何其他 NQI、流通实体或美国分支机构的名称、地址和 TIN（如果有），以及对于可预扣付款的第 4 章状态（如果需要）和 GIIN（如果适用）直接收到付款。
    
11.  Any other information a withholding agent requests to fulfill its reporting and withholding obligations.  
    扣缴义务人为履行报告和扣缴义务而要求提供的任何其他信息。
    

**Alternative procedure.**

Under this alternative procedure, the NQI can give you the information that allocates each payment to each foreign and U.S. exempt recipient or chapter 4 withholding rate pool by January 31 following the calendar year of payment, rather than before the payment is made, as otherwise required. To take advantage of this procedure, the NQI must (a) inform you, on its withholding statement, that it is using the alternative procedure; and (b) obtain your consent. You must receive the withholding statement with all the required information (other than item 5) before the NQI makes the payment.

  

**替代程序。** 

根据此替代程序，NQI 可以在付款日历年之后 1 月 31 日之前（而不是在付款之前（如另有要求）向您提供将每笔付款分配给每个外国和美国豁免收款人或第 4 章预扣税率池的信息。要利用此程序，NQI 必须 (a) 在其预扣税声明中告知您其正在使用替代程序； (b) 征得您的同意。在 NQI 付款之前，您必须收到包含所有必需信息（第 5 项除外）的预扣税单。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_The alternative procedure cannot, however, be used for payments to U.S. nonexempt recipients other than those recipients included in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees. See_ [_Chapter 4_](#en_US_2024_publink100015493 "Chapter 4.")_, later. Therefore, an NQI must provide you with allocation information for any U.S. nonexempt recipients not included in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees before the NQI makes a payment._  
然而，替代程序不能用于向美国收款人第 4 章预扣税率池中包含的收款人以外的美国非豁免收款人付款。请参阅稍后的第 4 章。因此，在 NQI 付款之前，NQI 必须向您提供未包含在第 4 章美国收款人预扣税率池中的任何美国非豁免收款人的分配信息。.

_**Pooled withholding information for chapters 3 and 4.**_

If an NQI uses the alternative procedure, it must provide you with withholding rate pool information, as opposed to individual allocation information, before the payment of a reportable amount. The NQI must provide you with the payee specific allocation information (information allocating each payment to each payee) by January 31 following the calendar year of payment, except as otherwise permitted for chapter 4 purposes, when using this procedure.

  

_**第 3 章和第 4 章的汇总预扣税信息。** _

如果 NQI 使用替代程序，则必须在支付可报告金额之前向您提供预扣税率池信息，而不是个人分配信息。使用此程序时，NQI 必须在付款日历年之后的 1 月 31 日之前向您提供收款人特定分配信息（将每笔付款分配给每个收款人的信息），除非出于第 4 章目的另有允许。

_**Chapter 4.**_

In the case of a reportable amount that is also a withholdable payment, an NQI may include amounts allocable to a chapter 4 withholding rate pool (other than a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees) and payees subject to chapter 4 withholding for whom the NQI will provide payee-specific information in a 30% rate pool together with payees subject to chapter 3 withholding at the 30% rate. For the amount of the payment allocable to a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees, an NQI may include amounts allocable to the pool with other amounts exempt from withholding (and an NQI may allocate payments to this pool regardless of whether the payment is a withholdable payment) and may not otherwise apply these provisions for payments made to U.S. nonexempt recipients. The NQI must identify prior to the payment each chapter 4 withholding rate pool to be allocated a portion of the payment, in addition to each payee to be allocated the payments that is not included in such a pool. The NQI must then also allocate, by January 31 following the calendar year of the payment, the portion of the payment to each such pool in addition to allocating the payment to each payee that is not included in the pool.

  

_**第 4 章。** _

如果应报告金额也是应预扣付款，NQI 可能包括分配给第 4 章预扣税率池（美国收款人的第 4 章预扣税率池除外）的金额以及受第 4 章预扣税约束的收款人。 NQI 将在 30% 税率池中提供收款人特定信息，以及按 30% 税率缴纳第 3 章预扣税的收款人。对于可分配至美国收款人第 4 章预扣税率池的付款金额，NQI 可能包括可分配至该池的金额以及免予预扣税的其他金额（并且 NQI 可以将付款分配至该池，无论该付款是否为预扣税）预扣税款），并且不得以其他方式将这些规定适用于向美国非豁免收款人支付的款项。 NQI 必须在付款前确定要分配一部分付款的每个第 4 章预扣税率池，以及要分配不包含在此类池中的付款的每个收款人。然后，除了将付款分配给未包含在资金池中的每个收款人之外，NQI 还必须在付款日历年之后的 1 月 31 日之前将付款部分分配给每个此类资金池。

_**Failure to provide allocation information.**_

If an NQI fails to provide you with the payee specific allocation information for a withholding rate pool or chapter 4 withholding rate pool by January 31, you must not apply the alternative procedure to any of the NQI's withholding rate pools from that date forward. You must treat the payees as undocumented and apply the presumption rules, discussed later in [_Presumption Rules_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224878 "Presumption Rules"). An NQI is deemed to have failed to provide specific allocation information if it does not give you such information for more than 10% of any one withholding rate pool.

  

_**未能提供分配信息。** _

如果 NQI 未能在 1 月 31 日之前向您提供预扣税率池或第 4 章预扣税率池的收款人特定分配信息，则自该日起，您不得对任何 NQI 预扣税率池应用替代程序。您必须将收款人视为无证并应用推定规则，稍后将在[_推定规则_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224878 "Presumption Rules")中讨论。如果 NQI 未向您提供超过任一预扣税率池 10% 的具体分配信息，则该 NQI 将被视为未能提供具体分配信息。

However, if you receive such information by February 14, you may make the appropriate adjustments to repay any excess withholding incurred between February 1 and on or before February 14.  
但是，如果您在 2 月 14 日之前收到此类信息，您可以进行适当的调整，以偿还 2 月 1 日至 2 月 14 日或之前发生的任何超额预扣税。

If the NQI fails to allocate more than 10% of the payment to a withholding rate pool by February 14 following the calendar year of payment, you must file a Form 1042-S for each account holder in the pool on a pro-rata basis (treating a chapter 4 withholding rate pool as an account holder for this purpose and excluding U.S. exempt recipients). For example, if there are four account holders in a withholding rate pool that receive a $100 payment and the NQI fails to allocate more than $10 of the payment, you must file four Forms 1042-S, one for each account holder in the pool, showing $25 of income to each. You must also check the “Pro-rata Basis Reporting” box at the top of each form. If, however, the NQI provides allocation information for 90% or more of the payment to a withholding rate pool, the pro-rata reporting method is not required. Instead, you must file a Form 1042-S for each account holder for whom you have allocation information and report the unallocated part of the payment on a Form 1042-S issued to “unknown recipient.”  
如果 NQI 未能在付款日历年之后的 2 月 14 日之前将超过 10% 的付款分配至预扣税率池，您必须按比例为池中的每个账户持有人提交一份表格 1042-S（为此目的，将第 4 章预扣税率池视为账户持有人，但不包括美国豁免接收人）。例如，如果预扣税率池中有四名账户持有人收到了 100 美元的付款，而 NQI 未能分配超过 10 美元的付款，则您必须提交四份 1042-S 表格，池中的每个账户持有人各一份，显示每人 25 美元的收入。您还必须选中每个表格顶部的“按比例基础报告”框。但是，如果 NQI 提供预扣税率池中 90% 或以上付款的分配信息，则不需要按比例报告方法。相反，您必须为您拥有分配信息的每个账户持有人提交一份 1042-S 表格，并在发给“未知收款人”的 1042-S 表格上报告付款的未分配部分。

#### Withholding Foreign Partnerships (WPs)  
预扣外国合伙企业 (WP)

If you are making payments to a WP for chapter 3 or 4 purposes, you do not have to withhold if the WP is acting in that capacity. The WP must assume primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibility for amounts that are distributed to, or included in the distributive share of, any direct partner and may assume chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibilities for certain of its indirect partners. The WP must withhold the amount required to be withheld. A WP must provide you with a Form W-8IMY that certifies that the WP is acting in that capacity and provides all other information and certifications required by the form. The Form W-8IMY must contain the WP-EIN and GIIN (if applicable).  
如果您出于第 3 章或第 4 章的目的向 WP 付款，且该 WP 以该身份行事，则您无需扣缴款项。 WP 必须对分配给任何直接合作伙伴或包含在其分配份额中的金额承担第 3 章和第 4 章主要预扣责任，并可对其某些间接合作伙伴承担第 3 章和第 4 章预扣责任。 WP 必须预扣所需预扣的金额。 WP 必须向您提供 W-8IMY 表格，证明该 WP 正在以该身份行事，并提供该表格所需的所有其他信息和证明。 W-8IMY 表格必须包含 WP-EIN 和 GIIN（如果适用）。

A WP can be either an FFI or an NFFE. An FFI (other than a retirement fund) that is a WP must be a _[participating FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015541 "Participating FFI.")_, a _[registered deemed-compliant FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015543 "Registered deemed-compliant FFI.")_, or an FFI treated as a _[deemed-compliant FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015533 "Deemed-compliant FFI.")_ under an applicable Model 1 IGA that is subject to similar due diligence and reporting requirements with respect to its U.S. accounts as those applicable to a registered deemed-compliant FFI under Regulations section 1.1471-5(f)(1) (including the requirement to register with the IRS) (defined in the WP agreement as a “registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI”). Thus, an FFI certifying its status as a WP must provide you a Form W-8IMY that certifies to one of the chapter 4 statuses referenced in the preceding sentence when a chapter 4 status is required.  
WP 可以是 FFI 或 NFFE。作为 WP 的 FFI（退休基金除外）必须是_[参与 FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015541 "Participating FFI.")_ 、_[注册的视为合规 FFI](#en_US_2024_publink100015543 "Registered deemed-compliant FFI.")_或根据适用的模型 1 IGA 被视为_[视为合规 FFI 的](#en_US_2024_publink100015533 "Deemed-compliant FFI.")_FFI，并接受类似的尽职调查和与其美国账户有关的报告要求与适用于第 1.1471-5(f)(1) 条规定的已注册视为合规 FFI 的报告要求（包括向 IRS 注册的要求）（在 WP 协议中定义为“已注册的视为合规模型 1 IGA FFI”）。因此，当需要第 4 章状态时，证明其 WP 状态的 FFI 必须向您提供一份 W-8IMY 表格，证明上句中提到的第 4 章状态之一。

**Responsibilities of the WP.**

The WP must withhold under chapter 3 or 4 on the date it makes a distribution of a withholdable payment or an amount subject to chapter 3 withholding to a direct foreign partner based on the Form W-8 or W-9 it receives from its partners. If the partner's distributive share has not been distributed, the WP must withhold on the partner's distributive share on the earlier of the date that the partnership must mail or otherwise provide to the partner a Schedule K-1 (Form 1065) or the due date for furnishing the statement (whether or not the WP is required to furnish the statement).

  

**WP 的职责。** 

WP 必须根据从其合作伙伴处收到的 W-8 或 W-9 表，在向直接外国合作伙伴分配可预扣付款或受第 3 章规定的预扣金额之日，根据第 3 章或第 4 章进行预扣。如果合伙人的分配份额尚未分配，WP 必须在合伙企业必须向合伙人邮寄或以其他方式提供附表 K-1（表格 1065）的日期或合伙企业的到期日（以较早者为准）扣留合伙人的分配份额。提供声明（无论WP是否需要提供声明）。

The WP may determine the amount of withholding based on a reasonable estimate of the partner's distributive share of income subject to withholding for the year. The WP must correct the estimated withholding to reflect the actual distributive share on the earlier of the dates mentioned in the preceding paragraph. If that date is after the earlier of the due date (including extensions) for filing the WP's Form 1042-S or the date the WP actually issues Form 1042-S for the calendar year, the WP may withhold and report any adjustments required by correcting the information for the following calendar year.  
工作伙伴可以根据对合伙人当年应缴纳预扣税的收入分配份额的合理估计来确定预扣税金额。 WP 必须更正估计的预扣税，以反映上段提到的较早日期的实际分配份额。如果该日期晚于提交 WP 表格 1042-S 的截止日期（包括延期）或 WP 实际签发日历年表格 1042-S 的日期，则 WP 可以扣留并报告更正所需的任何调整下一个日历年的信息。

_**Form 1042 filing.**_

The WP must file Form 1042 even if no amount was withheld. In addition to the information that is required for the Form 1042, the WP must attach a statement showing the amounts of any over- or under-withholding adjustments and an explanation of those adjustments.

  

_**1042 表格归档。** _

即使没有预扣金额，WP 也必须提交 1042 表格。除了 1042 表格所需的信息外，WP 还必须附上一份声明，显示任何过高或过低的预扣税调整金额以及对这些调整的解释。

_**Form 1042-S reporting.**_

The WP can elect to report payments made to its foreign direct partners on a pooled basis for chapter 3 purposes rather than reporting payments to each direct partner in addition to reporting payments in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool to the extent the WP is permitted to do so based on its chapter 4 status. A WP can treat as its direct partners those indirect partners of the WP for which it applies joint account treatment or the agency option (described later). A WP must otherwise issue a Form 1042-S to each partner to the extent it is required to do so under the WP agreement. You may issue a single Form 1042-S for all payments you make to a WP other than payments for which the entity does not act as a WP. You may, however, have Form 1099 requirements for certain indirect partners of a WP that are U.S. nonexempt recipients.

  

_**1042-S 表格报告。** _

工作伙伴可以选择出于第 3 章的目的汇总报告向其外国直接合作伙伴支付的款项，而不是在允许工作伙伴这样做的范围内，除了在第 4 章预扣税率池中报告付款之外，还报告向每个直接合作伙伴支付的款项因此基于其第 4 章状态。 WP 可以将其应用联合账户处理或代理选项（稍后描述）的 WP 间接合作伙伴视为其直接合作伙伴。 WP 必须按照 WP 协议的要求向每个合作伙伴签发 1042-S 表格。您可以为您向 WP 支付的所有款项（该实体不充当 WP 的付款除外）签发一份表格 1042-S。但是，对于作为美国非豁免接收者的 WP 的某些间接合作伙伴，您可能有 1099 表格要求。

_**Collective refund procedures.**_

A WP may seek a refund of tax withheld under chapters 3 and 4 on behalf of its partners when the WP has not issued a Form 1042-S to the partners that received the payment that was subject to overwithholding. The partners, therefore, are not required to file claims for refund with the IRS to obtain refunds, but rather may obtain them from the WP. A WP may obtain a refund of tax withheld under chapter 4 to the extent permitted under the WP agreement.

  

_**集体退款程序。** _

如果 WP 未向收到预扣款项的合作伙伴签发 1042-S 表格，WP 可以代表其合作伙伴要求退还根据第 3 章和第 4 章扣缴的税款。因此，合作伙伴无需向 IRS 提出退款申请即可获得退款，而是可以从 WP 获得退款。在 WP 协议允许的范围内，WP 可以获得根据第 4 章扣缴的税款的退款。

_**Reporting of U.S. partners.**_

A WP must report its U.S. partners on Schedule K-1 to the extent required under the WP agreement. If the WP is an FFI, it is also required to report each of its U.S. accounts (or U.S. reportable accounts if a reporting Model 1 FFI) on Form 8966 consistent with its chapter 4 requirements or the requirements of an IGA. If the WP is an NFFE, the WP must file Form 8966 to report any partner that is an NFFE (other than an excepted NFFE) with one or more substantial U.S. owners (or, under an applicable IGA, controlling persons that are specified U.S. persons) if the NFFE is the beneficial owner of a withholdable payment received by the WP. The WP must also file a Form 8966 to report withholdable payments made to a pass-through partner for which the WP acts under the WP agreement that provides information on an account holder (or interest holder) that is an NFFE (other than an excepted NFFE) with one or more substantial U.S. owners (or, under an applicable IGA, controlling persons that are specified U.S. persons) and that is the beneficial owner of the withholdable payment received by the WP, unless the pass-through partner certifies to the WP that it is reporting on the account holder (or interest holder) pursuant to its U.S. account reporting requirements. The preceding sentence applies with respect to a pass-through partner to which the WP applies the agency option or which has partners, beneficiaries, or owners that are indirect partners of the WP.

  

_**美国合作伙伴的报告。** _

工作伙伴必须在工作伙伴协议要求的范围内按照附表 K-1 报告其美国合作伙伴。如果 WP 是 FFI，则还需要按照第 4 章要求或 IGA 的要求，在表格 8966 上报告其每个美国账户（如果是报告模式 1 FFI，则为美国应报告账户）。如果 WP 是 NFFE，则 WP 必须提交表格 8966，以报告属于 NFFE（例外 NFFE 除外）且拥有一名或多名实质美国所有者（或根据适用的 IGA，控制人为指定美国人）的任何合作伙伴) 如果 NFFE 是 WP 收到的预扣付款的受益所有人。 WP 还必须提交 8966 表格，报告向 WP 根据 WP 协议行事的传递合作伙伴支付的预扣付款，该协议提供作为 NFFE（例外 NFFE 除外）的账户持有人（或利益持有人）的信息）与一名或多名实质美国所有者（或根据适用的 IGA，控制人为指定的美国人），且该人是 WP 收到的预扣付款的受益所有人，除非转手合伙人向 WP 证明：它根据其美国账户报告要求对账户持有人（或利益持有人）进行报告。前一句适用于 WP 应用代理选项的过继合伙人，或者其合伙人、受益人或所有者是 WP 的间接合伙人的合伙人。

**Joint account treatment.**

Under special procedures provided in the WP agreement, a WP may apply joint account treatment to a partnership or trust that is a direct partner of the WP. A WP that applies the joint account option must elect to perform pool reporting for amounts subject to chapter 3 withholding that either are not withholdable payments or are withholdable payments for which no chapter 4 withholding is required and that the WP distributes to, or includes in the distributive share of, a foreign direct partner. These rules only apply to a partnership or trust that meets the following conditions.

  

**联名账户处理。** 

根据 WP 协议规定的特殊程序，WP 可以对其直接合伙人的合伙企业或信托实行联名账户处理。应用联名账户选项的 WP 必须选择对受第 3 章预扣税约束的金额执行汇总报告，这些金额要么不是可预扣付款，要么是不需要第 4 章预扣税的可预扣付款，并且 WP 分配给或包含在外国直接合作伙伴的分配份额。这些规则仅适用于满足以下条件的合伙企业或信托。

*   It is a nonwithholding foreign partnership or nonwithholding foreign trust that is either a simple or grantor trust.  
    它是非预扣税外国合伙企业或非预扣税外国信托，可以是简单信托，也可以是设保人信托。
    
*   It is a certified deemed-compliant FFI (other than a registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI, as defined in the WP agreement), an owner-documented FFI, an exempt beneficial owner, or an NFFE (other than a WP or WT).  
    它是经认证的视为合规 FFI（除注册的视为合规模型 1 IGA FFI 外，如 WP 协议中所定义）、所有者记录的 FFI、豁免受益所有人或 NFFE（除 WP 或 WT 外） ）。
    
*   It is a direct partner of the WP.  
    它是WP的直接合作伙伴。
    
*   None of its partners, beneficiaries, or owners is a flow-through entity or intermediary.  
    其合作伙伴、受益人或所有者均不是流通实体或中介机构。
    
*   None of the partnership’s or trust’s partners, beneficiaries, or owners is a U.S. person or is subject to withholding or reporting under chapter 4.  
    合伙企业或信托的合伙人、受益人或所有者均不是美国人，也无需根据第 4 章进行预扣税或报告。
    
*   It agrees to make available upon request to the WP (or the WP’s auditor) records that establish it has provided the WP with documentation for purposes of chapters 3 and 4 for all of its partners, beneficiaries, or owners.  
    它同意应要求向 WP（或 WP 的审计员）提供记录，证明其已向 WP 提供了用于其所有合作伙伴、受益人或所有者的第 3 章和第 4 章的文件。
    

For more information on applying these rules, see section 9.01 of the WP agreement in section 6 of Revenue Procedure 2017-21, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21).  
有关应用这些规则的更多信息，请参阅 2017-21 年收入程序第 6 节中的 WP 协议第 9.01 节，网址为[IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21) 。

**Agency option.**

A WP may apply the agency option to a partnership or trust under which the partnership or trust agrees to act as an agent of the WP and to apply the provisions of the WP agreement to its partners, beneficiaries, or owners. A WP that applies the agency option must elect to perform pool reporting for amounts subject to chapter 3 withholding that either are not withholdable payments or are withholdable payments for which no chapter 4 withholding is required and that the WP distributes to, or includes in the distributive share of, a foreign direct partner. A WP and a partnership or trust may only apply the agency option if the partnership or trust meets the following conditions.

  

**代理选项。** 

WP 可以将代理选项应用于合伙企业或信托，根据该选项，合伙企业或信托同意充当 WP 的代理人，并将 WP 协议的条款应用于其合伙人、受益人或所有者。应用代理选项的 WP 必须选择对受第 3 章预扣税约束的金额执行汇总报告，这些金额要么不是可预扣的付款，要么是不需要第 4 章预扣税的可预扣付款，并且 WP 分配给或包含在分配中外国直接合作伙伴的份额。只有当合伙企业或信托满足以下条件时，WP 和合伙企业或信托才可以应用代理选项。

*   It is a nonwithholding foreign partnership or nonwithholding foreign trust that is either a simple or grantor trust.  
    它是非预扣税外国合伙企业或非预扣税外国信托，可以是简单信托，也可以是设保人信托。
    
*   It is either a direct partner of the WP or an indirect partner of the WP that is a direct partner, beneficiary, or owner of a partnership or trust to which the WP also applies the agency option.  
    它可以是 WP 的直接合伙人，也可以是 WP 的间接合伙人，即 WP 也应用代理选项的合伙企业或信托的直接合伙人、受益人或所有者。
    
*   It is an FFI that is a certified deemed-compliant FFI (other than a registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI, as defined in the WP agreement), an owner-documented FFI, an NFFE, or an exempt beneficial owner.  
    FFI 是经认证的视为合规 FFI（除注册的视为合规模型 1 IGA FFI 外，如 WP 协议中所定义）、所有者记录的 FFI、NFFE 或豁免受益所有人。
    
*   None of its partners, beneficiaries, or owners is a WT, WP, participating FFI, registered deemed-compliant FFI, registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI (as defined in the WP agreement), or QI acting as an intermediary for a payment made by the WP to the partnership or trust.  
    其合作伙伴、受益人或所有者均不是 WT、WP、参与 FFI、注册视为合规 FFI、注册视为合规模型 1 IGA FFI（如 WP 协议中定义）或充当支付中介的 QI由 WP 向合伙企业或信托机构作出。
    
*   The WP may not act as a withholding foreign partnership with respect to any direct or indirect partner of the partnership or trust that is a U.S. nonexempt recipient, unless the U.S. nonexempt recipient is a partner of an owner-documented FFI or passive NFFE to which the WP applies the agency option and is included in the WP’s U.S. payee pool.  
    对于美国非豁免接收人的合伙企业或信托的任何直接或间接合伙人，WP 不得充当预扣税外国合伙企业，除非美国非豁免接收人是拥有所有者记录的 FFI 或被动 NFFE 的合伙人，并且WP 采用代理选项并包含在 WP 的美国收款人池中。
    
*   It agrees to comply with the compliance procedures described in section 8.05 of the WP agreement by providing the WP with the certification described in section 8.03 of the WP agreement and providing the WP with documentation or other information for review.  
    它同意遵守 WP 协议第 8.05 节中所述的合规程序，向 WP 提供 WP 协议第 8.03 节中所述的认证，并向 WP 提供文件或其他信息以供审查。
    
*   It agrees to comply with the documentation requirements of a WP in the WP agreement.  
    它同意遵守 WP 协议中 WP 的文件要求。
    

For more information on applying these rules, see section 9.02 of the WP agreement in section 6 of Revenue Procedure 2017-21, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21).  
有关应用这些规则的更多信息，请参阅 2017-21 年收入程序第 6 节中的 WP 协议第 9.02 节，网址为[IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21) 。

**WP acting for indirect partners.**

A WP may act as a WP with respect to an indirect partner of the WP that is not a U.S. nonexempt recipient. However, a WP may act as a WP for an indirect partner that is a U.S. nonexempt recipient if the indirect partner is included in a pass-through partner’s chapter 4 withholding rate pool of recalcitrant account holders or U.S. payees. A WP acting as a WP for an indirect partner is not required to forward to its withholding agent the documentation and the withholding statement of the pass-through partner and indirect partner that the WP would have otherwise been required to provide under the requirements of a nonwithholding foreign partnership. See [_Not acting as a WP_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224857 "Not acting as a WP."), later. However, a WP must provide the withholding agent with documentation and any other information from any pass-through partner whose direct or indirect partner, beneficiary, or owner is a U.S. nonexempt recipient unless the recipient is included in the pass-through partner’s chapter 4 withholding rate pool of recalcitrant account holders or U.S. payees.

  

**WP 代表间接合作伙伴。** 

WP 可以充当 WP 的非美国非豁免接收者的间接合作伙伴的 WP。然而，如果间接合作伙伴包含在转递合作伙伴的顽固账户持有人或美国收款人的第 4 章预扣税率池中，则 WP 可以充当美国非豁免收款人的间接合作伙伴的 WP。作为间接合作伙伴的工作伙伴，无需向其扣缴义务人转发传递伙伴和间接合作伙伴的文件和预扣税声明，而根据非扣缴义务人的要求，工作伙伴本应提供这些文件和预扣税声明。外国合伙企业。请参阅稍后不充当 WP。但是，WP 必须向扣缴义务人提供来自任何直接或间接合作伙伴、受益人或所有者是美国非豁免接收人的任何传递合作伙伴的文件和任何其他信息，除非接收人包含在传递合作伙伴的第 4 章预扣税中顽固账户持有人或美国收款人的利率池。

If a WP is making a payment that is a withholdable payment, the pass-through partner’s withholding statement must meet the requirements of Regulations section 1.1471-3(c)(3)(iii)(B). The pass-through partner’s withholding statement must include the account holders or interest holders of the pass-through partner in chapter 4 withholding rate pools (to the extent permitted), and, for an amount subject to chapter 3 withholding that is not a withholdable payment or is a withholdable payment for which chapter 4 withholding is not required, valid documentation provided by the account holders or interest holders of the pass-through partner that are not themselves QIs or flow-through entities.  
如果 WP 支付的款项属于应预扣款项，则转手合作伙伴的预扣税声明必须符合法规第 1.1471-3(c)(3)(iii)(B) 条的要求。直通合作伙伴的预扣税报表必须包括第 4 章预扣税率池中的直通合作伙伴的账户持有人或利息持有人（在允许的范围内），并且对于受第 3 章预扣税约束且不属于可预扣付款的金额或 是不需要根据第 4 章扣缴税款的可扣缴付款，由本身不属于 QI 或流通实体的账户持有人或权益持有者提供的有效文件。

For more information on applying these rules, see section 9.03 of the WP agreement in section 6 of Revenue Procedure 2017-21, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21).  
有关应用这些规则的更多信息，请参阅 2017-21 年收入程序第 6 节中的 WP 协议第 9.03 节，网址为[IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21) 。

**Not acting as a WP.**

A foreign partnership that is not acting as a WP is a nonwithholding foreign partnership. This occurs if a WP is not acting in that capacity for some or all of the amounts it receives from you.

  

**不充当 WP。** 

不作为 WP 的外国合伙企业是非预扣税的外国合伙企业。如果 WP 没有以该身份处理从您处收到的部分或全部金额，就会发生这种情况。

You must treat payments made to a nonwithholding foreign partnership as made to the partners of the partnership. The partnership must provide you with a Form W-8IMY (with Part VIII completed), a withholding statement identifying the amounts, the withholding certificates or documentary evidence of the partners, and the information shown earlier under [_Withholding statement_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224846 "Withholding statement.") under _Nonqualified Intermediary (NQI)._  
您必须将向非预扣税外国合伙企业支付的款项视为向合伙企业的合伙人支付的款项。合伙企业必须向您提供 W-8IMY 表格（已填写第 VIII 部分）、识别金额的预扣税声明、合作伙伴的预扣税证书或文件证据，以及先前在非合格中介机构 (NQI) 下的[_预扣税声明_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224846 "Withholding statement.")中显示的信息_。_

#### Withholding Foreign Trusts (WTs)  
预扣外国信托 (WT)

If you are making payments to a WT for chapter 3 or 4 purposes, you do not have to withhold if the WT is acting in that capacity. The WT must assume primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibility for amounts that are distributed to, or included in the distributive share of, any direct beneficiary or owner and may assume primary chapters 3 and 4 withholding responsibility for certain of its indirect beneficiaries or owners. The WT must withhold the amount required to be withheld. A WT must provide you with a Form W-8IMY that certifies that the WT is acting in that capacity and provides all other information and certifications required by the form. The Form W-8IMY must contain the WT-EIN and GIIN (if applicable).  
如果您出于第 3 章或第 4 章的目的向 WT 付款，且 WT 以该身份行事，则您无需扣缴款项。 WT 必须对分配给任何直接受益人或所有者或包含在其分配份额中的金额承担主要第 3 章和第 4 章的预扣责任，并可对其某些间接受益人或所有者承担主要第 3 章和第 4 章的预扣责任。 WT 必须预扣所需预扣的金额。 WT 必须向您提供 W-8IMY 表格，证明 WT 正在以该身份行事，并提供该表格所需的所有其他信息和证明。 W-8IMY 表格必须包含 WT-EIN 和 GIIN（如果适用）。

A WT can be either an FFI or an NFFE. An FFI (other than a retirement fund) that is a WT must be a participating FFI, a registered deemed-compliant FFI, or an FFI treated as a deemed-compliant FFI under an applicable Model 1 IGA that is subject to similar due diligence and reporting requirements with respect to its U.S. accounts as those applicable to a registered deemed-compliant FFI under Regulations section 1.1471-5(f)(1) (including the requirement to register with the IRS) (defined in the WT agreement as a “registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI”). Thus, you must identify the chapter 4 status of an FFI certifying its status as a WT as one of the chapter 4 statuses referenced in the preceding sentence on a Form W-8IMY when a chapter 4 status is required for chapter 4 purposes.  
WT 可以是 FFI 或 NFFE。作为 WT 的 FFI（退休基金除外）必须是参与 FFI、注册的视为合规 FFI 或根据适用的模型 1 IGA 被视为视为合规 FFI 的 FFI，并接受类似的尽职调查和与其美国账户有关的报告要求与适用于《条例》第 1.1471-5(f)(1) 条规定的已注册视为合规 FFI 的报告要求（包括向 IRS 注册的要求）（WT 协议中定义为“已注册的 FFI”）被视为符合模型 1 IGA FFI”）。因此，当第 4 章目的需要第 4 章状态时，您必须将证明其 WT 状态的 FFI 第 4 章状态识别为表格 W-8IMY 上一句中引用的第 4 章状态之一。

**Responsibilities of a WT.**

The WT must withhold on the date it makes a distribution of a withholdable payment or an amount subject to chapter 3 withholding to a direct foreign beneficiary or owner. If the beneficiary's or owner's distributive share has not been distributed, the WT must withhold on the beneficiary's or owner's distributive share on the earlier of the date that the trust must mail or otherwise provide to the beneficiary or owner the statement required under section 6048(b) or the due date for furnishing the statement (whether or not the WT is required to furnish the statement).

  

**WT 的职责。** 

WT 必须在向直接外国受益人或所有人分配可预扣付款或受第 3 章预扣税约束的金额之日预扣税款。如果受益人或所有者的分配份额尚未分配，WT 必须在信托必须邮寄或以其他方式向受益人或所有者提供第 6048(b) 条要求的声明之日（以较早者为准）扣留受益人或所有者的分配份额。 ) 或提供报表的截止日期（不论 WT 是否需要提供报表）。

The WT may determine the amount of withholding based on a reasonable estimate of the beneficiary's or owner's distributive share of income subject to withholding for the year. The WT must correct the estimated withholding to reflect the actual distributive share on the earlier of the dates mentioned in the preceding paragraph. If that date is after the earlier of the due date (including extensions) for filing the WT's Form 1042-S or the date the WT actually issues Form 1042-S for the calendar year, the WT may withhold and report any adjustments required by correcting the information for the following calendar year.  
工作组可以根据对受益人或所有者当年应扣缴收入的分配份额的合理估计来确定扣缴金额。 WT 必须更正估计的预扣税，以反映上一段提到的较早日期的实际分配份额。如果该日期晚于提交 WT 表格 1042-S 的截止日期（包括延期）或 WT 实际签发该日历年表格 1042-S 的日期（以较早者为准），则 WT 可扣留并报告更正所需的任何调整下一个日历年的信息。

_**Form 1042 filing.**_

The WT must file Form 1042 even if no amount was withheld. In addition to the information that is required for the Form 1042, the WT must attach a statement showing the amounts of any over- or under-withholding adjustments and an explanation of those adjustments.

  

_**1042 表格归档。** _

即使没有预扣金额，WT 也必须提交 1042 表格。除了 1042 表格所需的信息外，WT 还必须附上一份声明，显示任何超额或不足预扣税调整的金额以及对这些调整的解释。

_**Form 1042-S reporting.**_

The WT can elect to report payments made to its foreign direct beneficiaries or owners on a pooled basis for chapter 3 purposes rather than reporting payments made to each foreign direct beneficiary or owner in addition to reporting payments in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool to the extent the WT is permitted to do so based on its chapter 4 status. A WT can treat as its direct beneficiaries or owners those indirect beneficiaries or owners of the WT for which it applies joint account treatment or the agency option (described later). A WT must otherwise issue a Form 1042-S to each beneficiary or owner to the extent it is required to do so under the WT agreement. You may issue a single Form 1042-S for all payments you make to a WT other than payments for which the entity does not act as a WT. You may, however, have Form 1099 requirements for certain indirect beneficiaries or owners of a WT that are U.S. nonexempt recipients.

  

_**1042-S 表格报告。** _

WT 可以选择出于第 3 章的目的汇总报告向其外国直接受益人或所有者支付的款项，而不是除了在第 4 章预扣税率池中报告支付外，还报告向每个外国直接受益人或所有者支付的款项WT 根据其第 4 章的地位被允许这样做。 WT 可以将其应用联名账户处理或代理选项（稍后描述）的 WT 间接受益人或所有者视为其直接受益人或所有者。 WT 必须按照 WT 协议的要求向每个受益人或所有人签发 1042-S 表格。您可以为您向 WT 支付的所有款项（该实体不充当 WT 的付款除外）签发一份表格 1042-S。但是，您可能对属于美国非豁免接收者的某些间接受益人或 WT 所有者有 1099 表格要求。

_**Collective refund procedures.**_

A WT may seek a refund of tax withheld under chapters 3 and 4 on behalf of its beneficiaries or owners when the WT has not issued a Form 1042-S to the beneficiaries or owners that received the payment that was subject to overwithholding. The beneficiaries or owners, therefore, are not required to file claims for refund with the IRS to obtain refunds, but rather may obtain them from the WT. A WT may obtain a refund of tax withheld under chapter 4 to the extent permitted under the WT agreement.

  

_**集体退款程序。** _

如果 WT 未向收到预扣款项的受益人或所有者签发 1042-S 表，则 WT 可以代表其受益人或所有者要求退还根据第 3 章和第 4 章扣缴的税款。因此，受益人或所有者无需向 IRS 提出退款申请即可获得退款，而是可以从 WT 获得退款。在 WT 协议允许的范围内，WT 可以获得根据第 4 章扣缴的税款的退税。

_**Reporting of U.S. beneficiaries or owners.**_

If the WT is a grantor trust with U.S. owners, the WT is required to file Form 3520-A, and to provide statements to a U.S. owner, as well as each U.S. beneficiary who is not an owner and receives a distribution. If the WT is an FFI, it is required to report each of its U.S. accounts (or U.S. reportable accounts if a reporting Model 1 FFI) on Form 8966 consistent with its FATCA requirements or the requirements of an IGA. If the WT is an NFFE, the WT must file Form 8966 to report any beneficiary or owner that is an NFFE (other than an excepted NFFE) with one or more substantial U.S. owners (or, under an applicable IGA, controlling persons that are specified U.S. persons) if the NFFE is the beneficial owner of a withholdable payment received by the WT.

  

_**美国受益人或所有者的报告。** _

如果 WT 是美国所有者的设保人信托，则 WT 需要提交 3520-A 表格，并向美国所有者以及非所有者但收到分配的每个美国受益人提供报表。如果 WT 是 FFI，则需要按照 FATCA 要求或 IGA 要求，在 8966 表格上报告其每个美国账户（或美国应报告账户，如果是报告模式 1 FFI）。如果 WT 是 NFFE，则 WT 必须提交表格 8966，报告任何受益人或所有者是 NFFE（例外的 NFFE 除外），且拥有一名或多名实质性美国所有者（或者，根据适用的 IGA，指定的控制人）美国人），如果 NFFE 是 WT 收到的预扣付款的受益所有人。

The WT must also file a Form 8966 to report withholdable payments made to a pass-through beneficiary or owner for which the WT acts under the WT agreement that provides information on an account holder (or interest holder) that is an NFFE (other than an excepted NFFE) with one or more substantial U.S. owners (or, under an applicable IGA, controlling persons that are specified U.S. persons) and that is the beneficial owner of the withholdable payment received by the WT, unless the pass-through beneficiary or owner certifies to the WT that it is reporting on the account holder (or interest holder) pursuant to its U.S. account reporting requirements. The preceding sentence applies with respect to a pass-through beneficiary or owner to which the WT applies the agency option or which has partners, beneficiaries, or owners that are indirect beneficiaries or owners of the WT. In addition, if the WT is not a participating FFI, a registered deemed-compliant FFI, or a registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI and is not required to report with respect to a U.S. beneficiary of the WT on Form 3520-A, then the WT must report with respect to such beneficiary on Form 8966, as required in the WT agreement. A beneficiary for this purpose means a beneficiary that receives a distribution from the WT during the year or that is required to include an amount in gross income with respect to the WT under sections 652(a) or 662(a).  
WT 还必须提交 8966 表格，报告向 WT 根据 WT 协议行事的转手受益人或所有者支付的预扣付款，该协议提供作为 NFFE（非 NFFE）账户持有人（或利益持有人）的信息。除外 NFFE）与一名或多名实质美国所有者（或根据适用的 IGA，控制人为指定的美国人），并且是 WT 收到的预扣付款的受益所有人，除非转手受益人或所有者证明向 WT 告知其正在根据其美国账户报告要求报告账户持有人（或利益持有人）。前一句适用于 WT 应用代理选项的传递受益人或所有者，或者其合作伙伴、受益人或所有者是 WT 的间接受益人或所有者。此外，如果 WT 不是参与 FFI、注册的视为合规 FFI 或注册的视为合规模型 1 IGA FFI，并且不需要在表格 3520-A 上报告 WT 的美国受益人，那么 WT 必须按照 WT 协议的要求，在表格 8966 上报告该受益人的情况。为此目的的受益人是指在一年内从 WT 获得分配的受益人，或者根据第 652(a) 或 662(a) 条要求将一定金额计入 WT 总收入的受益人。

**Joint account treatment.**

Under special procedures provided in the WT agreement, a WT may apply joint account treatment to a partnership or trust that is a direct beneficiary or owner of the WT. A WT that applies the joint account option must elect to perform pool reporting for amounts subject to chapter 3 withholding that either are not withholdable payments or are withholdable payments for which no chapter 4 withholding is required and that the WT distributes to, or includes in the distributive share of, a foreign direct beneficiary or owner. These rules only apply to a partnership or trust that meets the following conditions.

  

**联名账户处理。** 

根据 WT 协议规定的特殊程序，WT 可以对作为 WT 直接受益人或所有者的合伙企业或信托适用联名账户待遇。应用联名账户选项的 WT 必须选择对受第 3 章预扣税约束的金额执行合并报告，这些金额要么不是可预扣的付款，要么是不需要第 4 章预扣税的可预扣付款，并且 WT 分配给或包含在外国直接受益人或所有者的分配份额。这些规则仅适用于满足以下条件的合伙企业或信托。

*   It is a nonwithholding foreign partnership or nonwithholding foreign trust that is either a simple or grantor trust.  
    它是非预扣税外国合伙企业或非预扣税外国信托，可以是简单信托，也可以是设保人信托。
    
*   It is a certified deemed-compliant FFI (other than a registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI, as defined in the WT agreement), an owner-documented FFI, an exempt beneficial owner, or an NFFE (other than a WP or WT).  
    它是经认证的视为合规 FFI（除 WT 协议中定义的已注册视为合规模型 1 IGA FFI 外）、所有者记录的 FFI、豁免受益所有人或 NFFE（除 WP 或 WT 外） ）。
    
*   It is a direct beneficiary or owner of the WT.  
    它是 WT 的直接受益人或所有者。
    
*   None of its partners, beneficiaries, or owners is a flow-through entity or intermediary.  
    其合作伙伴、受益人或所有者均不是流通实体或中介机构。
    
*   None of the partnership’s or trust’s partners, beneficiaries, or owners is a U.S. person or is subject to withholding or reporting under chapter 4.  
    合伙企业或信托的合伙人、受益人或所有者均不是美国人，也无需根据第 4 章进行预扣税或报告。
    
*   It agrees to make available upon request to the WT (or the WT’s auditor) records that establish it has provided the WT with documentation for purposes of chapters 3 and 4 for all of its partners, beneficiaries, or owners.  
    它同意根据 WT（或 WT 审计员）的要求提供记录，证明其已向 WT 提供了其所有合作伙伴、受益人或所有者用于第 3 章和第 4 章的文件。
    

For more information on applying these rules, see section 9.01 of the WT agreement found in section 7 of Revenue Procedure 2017-21, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21).  
有关应用这些规则的更多信息，请参阅 2017-21 年收入程序第 7 节中的 WT 协议第 9.01 节（可在[IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21)上获取）。

**Agency option.**

A WT may apply the agency option to a partnership or trust under which the partnership or trust agrees to act as an agent of the WT and to apply the provisions of the WT agreement to its partners, beneficiaries, or owners. A WT that applies the agency option must elect to perform pool reporting for amounts subject to chapter 3 withholding that either are not withholdable payments or are withholdable payments for which no chapter 4 withholding is required and that the WT distributes to, or includes in the distributive share of, a foreign direct beneficiary or owner. A WT and a partnership or trust may only apply the agency option if the partnership or trust meets the following conditions.

  

**代理选项。** 

WT 可以将代理选项应用于合伙企业或信托，根据该选项，合伙企业或信托同意充当 WT 的代理人，并将 WT 协议的条款应用于其合伙人、受益人或所有者。应用代理选项的 WT 必须选择对受第 3 章预扣税约束的金额执行汇总报告，这些金额要么不是可预扣的付款，要么是不需要第 4 章预扣税的可预扣付款，并且 WT 分配给或包含在分配中外国直接受益人或所有者的份额。仅当合伙企业或信托满足以下条件时，WT 和合伙企业或信托才可以应用代理选项。

*   It is a nonwithholding foreign partnership or nonwithholding foreign trust that is either a simple or grantor trust.  
    它是非预扣税外国合伙企业或非预扣税外国信托，可以是简单信托，也可以是设保人信托。
    
*   It is either a direct beneficiary or owner of the WT or an indirect beneficiary or owner of the WT that is a direct partner, beneficiary, or owner of a partnership or trust to which the WT also applies the agency option.  
    它可以是 WT 的直接受益人或所有者，也可以是 WT 的间接受益人或所有者，即 WT 也应用代理选项的合伙企业或信托的直接合伙人、受益人或所有者。
    
*   It is an FFI that is a certified deemed-compliant FFI (other than a registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI, as defined in the WT agreement), an owner-documented FFI, an NFFE, or an exempt beneficial owner.  
    FFI 是经认证的视为合规 FFI（除 WT 协议中定义的注册视为合规模型 1 IGA FFI 外）、所有者记录的 FFI、NFFE 或豁免受益所有人。
    
*   None of its partners, beneficiaries, or owners is a WT, WP, participating FFI, registered deemed-compliant FFI, registered deemed-compliant Model 1 IGA FFI (as defined in the WT agreement), or a QI acting as an intermediary for a payment made by the WT to the partnership or trust.  
    其合作伙伴、受益人或所有者均不是 WT、WP、参与 FFI、注册视为合规 FFI、注册视为合规模型 1 IGA FFI（如 WT 协议中所定义）或充当中介的 QI WT 向合伙企业或信托机构支付的款项。
    
*   The WT may not act as a withholding foreign trust with respect to any direct or indirect beneficiary or owner of the partnership or trust that is a U.S. nonexempt recipient, unless the U.S. nonexempt recipient is a beneficiary or owner of an owner-documented FFI or passive NFFE to which the WT applies the agency option and is included in the WT’s U.S. payee pool.  
    对于属于美国非豁免接收者的合伙企业或信托的任何直接或间接受益人或所有者，WT 不得充当预扣税外国信托，除非美国非豁免接收者是所有者记录的 FFI 或被动机构的受益人或所有者WT对其应用代理选项并包含在WT的美国收款人池中的NFFE。
    
*   It agrees to comply with the compliance procedures described in section 8.05 of the WT agreement by providing the WT with the certification described in section 8.03 of the WT agreement and providing the WT with documentation or other information for review.  
    它同意遵守 WT 协议第 8.05 节中所述的合规程序，向 WT 提供 WT 协议第 8.03 节中所述的认证，并向 WT 提供文件或其他信息以供审查。
    
*   It agrees to comply with the documentation requirements of a WT in the WT agreement.  
    同意遵守WT协议中WT的文件要求。
    

For more information on applying these rules, see section 9.02 of the WT agreement in section 7 of Revenue Procedure 2017-21, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21).  
有关应用这些规则的更多信息，请参阅 2017-21 年收入程序第 7 节中的 WT 协议第 9.02 节，网址为[IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21) 。

**WT acting for indirect beneficiaries or owners.**

A WT may act as a WT with respect to an indirect beneficiary or owner of the WT that is not a U.S. nonexempt recipient. However, a WT may act as a WT for an indirect beneficiary or owner that is a U.S. nonexempt recipient if the indirect beneficiary or owner is included in a pass-through beneficiary’s or owner’s chapter 4 withholding rate pool of recalcitrant account holders or U.S. payees. A WT acting as a WT for an indirect beneficiary or owner is not required to forward to its withholding agent the documentation and the withholding statement of the pass-through beneficiary or owner and indirect beneficiary or owner that the WT would have otherwise been required to provide under the requirements of a nonwithholding foreign trust. See [_Not acting as a WT_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224864 "Not acting as a WT."), later. However, a WT must provide the withholding agent with documentation and any other information from any pass-through beneficiary or owner whose direct or indirect partner, beneficiary, or owner is a U.S. nonexempt recipient unless the recipient is included in the pass-through beneficiary’s or owner’s chapter 4 withholding rate pool of recalcitrant account holders or U.S. payees. If a WT is making a payment that is a withholdable payment, the pass-through beneficiary’s or owner’s withholding statement must meet the requirements of Regulations section 1.1471-3(c)(3)(iii)(B). The pass-through beneficiary’s or owner’s withholding statement must include the account holders or interest holders of the pass-through beneficiary or owner in chapter 4 withholding rate pools (to the extent permitted), and, for an amount subject to chapter 3 withholding that is not a withholdable payment or is a withholdable payment for which chapter 4 withholding is not required, valid documentation provided by the account holders or interest holders of the pass-through beneficiary or owner that are not themselves QIs or flow-through entities.

  

**WT 代表间接受益人或所有者。** 

WT 可充当非美国非豁免接收者的间接受益人或 WT 所有者的 WT。然而，如果间接受益人或所有者属于美国非豁免收款人的间接受益人或所有者包含在顽抗账户持有人或美国收款人的传递受益人或所有者的第 4 章预扣税率池中，则 WT 可以充当美国非豁免收款人的间接受益人或所有者的 WT。作为间接受益人或所有人的 WT，无需向其扣缴义务人转发转手受益人或所有人以及间接受益人或所有人的文件和预扣税表，否则 WT 需要提供这些文件和预扣税表根据非预扣税外国信托的要求。请参阅稍后不充当 WT。但是，WT 必须向扣缴义务人提供来自任何传递受益人或所有者（其直接或间接合作伙伴、受益人或所有者是美国非豁免收款人）的文件和任何其他信息，除非收款人包含在传递受益人或所有者中。所有者的第 4 章顽抗账户持有人或美国收款人的预扣税率池。如果 WT 支付的款项属于应预扣款项，则转手受益人或所有者的预扣税声明必须符合法规第 1.1471-3(c)(3)(iii)(B) 条的要求。 传递受益人或所有者的预扣税报表必须包括第 4 章预扣税率池中的传递受益人或所有者的账户持有人或利益持有人（在允许的范围内），并且，对于受第 3 章预扣税约束的金额，不是可预扣付款，或者是不需要第 4 章预扣税的可预扣付款，由转嫁受益人或所有者的账户持有人或利益持有人（本身不是 QI 或流通实体）提供的有效文件。

For more information on applying these rules, see section 9.03 of the WT agreement in section 7 of Revenue Procedure 2017-21, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21).  
有关应用这些规则的更多信息，请参阅 2017-21 年收入程序第 7 节中的 WT 协议第 9.03 节，网址为[IRS.gov/irb/2017-06\_IRB#RP-2017-21](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-06_IRB#RP-2017-21) 。

**Not acting as a WT.**

A foreign trust that is not acting as a WT is a nonwithholding foreign trust. This occurs if a WT is not acting in that capacity for some or all of the amounts it receives from you.

  

**不充当WT。** 

不充当信托基金的外国信托是非预扣税外国信托。如果 WT 没有以该身份处理从您处收到的部分或全部金额，就会发生这种情况。

In most cases, you must treat payments made to a nonwithholding foreign trust as made to the beneficiaries of a simple trust or the owners of a grantor trust. The trust must provide you with a Form W-8IMY (with Part VIII completed), a withholding statement identifying the amounts, the withholding certificates or documentary evidence of the beneficiaries or owners, and the information shown earlier under [_Withholding statement_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224846 "Withholding statement.") under _Nonqualified Intermediary (NQI)_.  
在大多数情况下，您必须将向非预扣税外国信托支付的款项视为向简单信托的受益人或设保人信托的所有者支付的款项。信托必须向您提供 W-8IMY 表（已填写第 VIII 部分）、识别金额的预扣税声明、受益人或所有人的预扣税证书或文件证据，以及之前在_非合格中介 (NQI)_下的[_预扣税声明_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224846 "Withholding statement.")下显示的信息_）_ 。

#### Standards of Knowledge for Purposes of Chapter 3  
第 3 章的知识标准

You must withhold in accordance with the presumption rules (discussed later) if you know or have reason to know that a withholding certificate or documentary evidence provided by a payee is unreliable or incorrect to establish the payee's status for chapter 3 purposes. If you rely on an agent to obtain documentation, you are considered to know, or have reason to know, the facts that are within the knowledge of your agent for this purpose. If you receive notification from the IRS that a payee's claim of status for chapter 3 purposes is incorrect or unreliable, you may not rely upon the claim except to the extent indicated by the IRS.  
如果您知道或有理由知道收款人提供的预扣税证明或文件证据不可靠或不正确，无法根据第 3 章的目的确定收款人的身份，则您必须根据推定规则（稍后讨论）进行预扣税。如果您依赖代理人获取文件，则您被视为了解或有理由了解您的代理人为此目的所知的事实。如果您收到 IRS 的通知，称收款人针对第 3 章目的的身份声明不正确或不可靠，则您不得依赖该声明，除非 IRS 指示的范围内。

#### Reason To Know知道的理由

In general, you are considered to have reason to know that a claim of foreign status or of a reduced rate of withholding is incorrect if statements contained in the withholding certificate or other documentation, or other relevant facts of which you have knowledge, would cause a reasonably prudent person in your position to question the claims made.  
一般而言，如果预扣税证书或其他文件中包含的陈述或您所了解的其他相关事实会导致处于您位置的合理谨慎的人可以质疑所提出的主张。

For an obligation that is not a preexisting obligation (that is, an obligation, including an account, held by an individual that is outstanding on June 30, 2014, or an obligation, including an account, held by an entity that is opened, executed, or issued before January 1, 2015), you have reason to know that an account holder’s chapter 3 claim is unreliable or incorrect if any information contained in your account opening files or other account information conflicts with the account holder’s claim. For an obligation other than a preexisting obligation, you will not be considered to have reason to know that a person’s chapter 3 claim is unreliable or incorrect based on documentation collected for anti-money laundering (AML) purposes until 30 days after the obligation is executed, or 30 days after the account is opened for such person, whichever is applicable.  
对于不属于预先存在的债务的债务（即，由个人持有且于 2014 年 6 月 30 日尚未清偿的债务，包括账户，或由已开立、执行的实体持有的债务，包括账户） ，或在 2015 年 1 月 1 日之前签发），如果您的开户文件或其他账户信息中包含的任何信息与账户持有人的信息相冲突，您有理由知道账户持有人的第 3 章索赔不可靠或不正确。 宣称。对于既存义务以外的义务，在义务履行后 30 天之前，您不会被视为有理由知道某人根据为反洗钱 (AML) 目的收集的文件而提出的第 3 章索赔不可靠或不正确，或为该人开设账户后 30 天，以适用者为准。

Financial institutions, insurance companies, or brokers or dealers in securities have reason to know that documentation provided by a direct account holder is unreliable or incorrect only in the circumstances discussed next. If the documentation is considered unreliable or incorrect, you must get new documentation to support the payee’s claimed status or may rely on the original documentation if you receive the additional statements and/or documentation discussed later and are a withholding agent described above with respect to a direct account holder (defined in Regulations section 1.1441-7(b)(3)(i)). Such documentation is described in Regulations section 1.1471-3(c)(5)(i).  
金融机构、保险公司或证券经纪人或交易商有理由知道直接账户持有人提供的文件仅在下面讨论的情况下不可靠或不正确。如果该文件被认为不可靠或不正确，您必须获取新的文件来支持收款人声称的身份，或者如果您收到稍后讨论的附加声明和/或文件并且是上述有关扣缴义务人，则可以依赖原始文件。直接账户持有人（定义见《条例》第 1.1441-7(b)(3)(i) 条）。此类文件在法规第 1.1471-3(c)(5)(i) 节中进行了描述。

The circumstances, discussed next, also apply to other withholding agents. However, these withholding agents are not limited to these circumstances in determining if they have reason to know that documentation is unreliable or incorrect. These withholding agents cannot base their determination on the receipt of additional statements or documents. They need to get new documentation.  
接下来讨论的情况也适用于其他扣缴义务人。然而，这些扣缴义务人在确定他们是否有理由知道文件不可靠或不正确时，并不限于这些情况。这些扣缴义务人不能根据收到的额外报表或文件来做出决定。他们需要获得新的文档。

#### Withholding Certificates预扣证书

You have reason to know that a Form W-8 provided by a direct account holder that is a foreign person is unreliable or incorrect if:  
如果出现以下情况，您有理由知道由外国人直接账户持有人提供的 W-8 表格不可靠或不正确：

*   The Form W-8 is incomplete with respect to any item on the form that is relevant to the claims made by the account holder;  
    W-8 表中与账户持有人提出的索赔相关的任何项目不完整；
    
*   The Form W-8 contains any information that is inconsistent with the account holder's claim;  
    W-8 表包含与账户持有人的主张不一致的任何信息；
    
*   The Form W-8 lacks information necessary to establish entitlement to a reduced rate of withholding, if a reduced rate is claimed; or  
    如果申请降低预扣税率，W-8 表缺乏确定有权享受降低的预扣税率所需的信息；或者
    
*   You have information not contained on the form that is inconsistent with the claims made on the form.  
    您的表格中未包含的信息与表格中的声明不一致。
    

The rules below apply to withholding agents that are financial institutions, insurance companies, or brokers or dealers in securities.  
以下规则适用于金融机构、保险公司、证券经纪人或交易商等扣缴义务人。

**Limits on reason to know for preexisting obligations.**

With respect to a preexisting obligation (that is, an obligation, including an account, held by an individual that is outstanding on June 30, 2014, or an obligation, including an account, held by an entity that is opened, executed, or issued before January 1, 2015), if you have documented the foreign status of an account holder for purposes of chapter 3 or 61 prior to July 1, 2014, you may continue to rely on that documentation. In addition, if you make a payment to a new entity account holder that you treat as a preexisting entity account under Notice 2014-33, 2014-20 I.R.B. 1006, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2014-21\_IRB#NOT-2014-33](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2014-21_IRB#NOT-2014-33), you may apply the standards of knowledge in Regulations sections 1.1441-7(b)(5) and (b)(8), that were applicable prior to the issuance of the temporary regulations. See Notice 2014-59, 2014-44 I.R.B. 747, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2014-44\_IRB#NOT-2014-59](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2014-44_IRB#NOT-2014-59).

  

**对预先存在的义务的了解理由的限制。** 

对于预先存在的债务（即，由个人持有且在 2014 年 6 月 30 日尚未清偿的债务，包括账户，或由实体持有的已开立、执行或发行的债务，包括账户） 2015 年 1 月 1 日之前），如果您在 2014 年 7 月 1 日之前已根据第 3 章或第 61 章的规定记录了账户持有人的外国身份，您可以继续依赖该文件。此外，如果您根据通知 2014-33、2014-20 IRB 1006（可在 IRS.gov/irb/2014-21\_IRB#NOT-2014- 获取）向新的实体账户持有人付款，该账户被视为现有实体账户33，您可以应用法规第 1.1441-7(b)(5) 条和(b)(8)，在暂行条例发布之前适用。请参阅通知 2014-59、2014-44 IRB 747，可在 IRS.gov/irb/2014-44\_IRB#NOT-2014-59 上获取。

However, if you review documentation for an individual account holder claiming foreign status that contains a U.S. place of birth or if you are notified of a change in circumstances, the obligation will be treated as having a change in circumstances as of the date you review the documentation or receive the notification, and you will then have reason to know that the documentation is unreliable or incorrect. However, if you are reviewing documentation provided by an entity before January 1, 2015, you will not be required to treat the additional U.S. indicia added to Regulations section 1.1441-7(b) by the temporary regulations as a change in circumstances. See Notice 2014-59, for more information.  
但是，如果您审查了声称具有美国出生地的外国身份的个人账户持有人的文件，或者如果您被告知情况发生变化，则该义务将被视为自您审查文件之日起情况发生变化。文档或收到通知，然后您就有理由知道该文档不可靠或不正确。但是，如果您正在审查 2015 年 1 月 1 日之前实体提供的文件，则您无需将临时法规第 1.1441-7(b) 条中添加的额外美国标记视为情况变更。有关更多信息，请参阅通知 2014-59。

**Establishment of foreign status by certain withholding agents.  
某些扣缴义务人建立外国身份。** 

You have reason to know that a Form W-8BEN or W-8BEN-E is unreliable or incorrect to establish a direct account holder's status as a foreign person if:  
如果出现以下情况，您有理由知道 W-8BEN 或 W-8BEN-E 表格对于确定直接账户持有人的外国人身份不可靠或不正确：

1.  The Form W-8 has a current permanent residence address in the United States,  
    W-8 表有美国目前的永久居住地址，
    
2.  The Form W-8 has a current mailing address in the United States,  
    W-8 表格的当前邮寄地址位于美国，
    
3.  You have a current residence or current mailing address as part of your account information that is an address in the United States,  
    您的帐户信息中有一个当前居住地或当前邮寄地址，该地址是美国的地址，
    
4.  The account holder notifies you of a new residence or mailing address in the United States,  
    帐户持有人通知您在美国的新居住或邮寄地址，
    
5.  You have classified the account holder as a U.S. person in your account information, or  
    您已在您的账户信息中将账户持有人归类为美国人，或者
    
6.  You have a current telephone number for the account holder in the United States and no telephone number for the account holder outside the United States (only to the extent described in Regulations section 1.1441-7(b)(5)).  
    您拥有美国境内账户持有人的当前电话号码，但没有美国境外账户持有人的电话号码（仅限于法规第 1.1441-7(b)(5) 条中所述的范围）。
    

You may, however, rely on a Form W-8 as establishing the account holder's foreign status if any of the following apply.  
但是，如果以下任何情况适用，您可以依靠 W-8 表格来确定账户持有人的外国身份。

1.  You receive the Form W-8BEN from an individual and:  
    您收到个人发送的 W-8BEN 表格，并且：
    
    1.  You possess or obtain documentary evidence (that does not contain a U.S. address) that supports the claim of foreign status, and the individual provides you with a reasonable explanation, in writing, supporting the claim of foreign status;  
        您拥有或获得支持外国身份主张的文件证据（不包含美国地址），并且该个人向您提供合理的书面解释，支持外国身份主张；
        
    2.  If you make a payment outside the United States with respect to an offshore obligation and you possess or obtain documentary evidence establishing foreign status that does not contain a U.S. address;  
        如果您在美国境外就离岸债务进行付款，并且您拥有或获得不包含美国地址的证明外国身份的文件证据；
        
    3.  With respect to an offshore obligation, if you classify the individual as a resident of the country where the obligation is maintained and you are required to report payments to the individual annually to the tax authority of the country where the obligation is maintained and that country has a tax treaty or information exchange agreement in effect with the United States; or  
        对于离岸义务，如果您将个人归类为履行义务的国家/地区的居民，并且您需要每年向履行义务的国家/地区的税务机关报告向该个人支付的款项，并且该国家/地区已与美国有效的税务条约或信息交换协议；或者
        
    4.  You have classified the account holder as a U.S person in your account information and you possess or obtain documentary evidence evidencing citizenship in a country other than the United States.  
        您已在账户信息中将账户持有人归类为美国人，并且您拥有或获得证明美国以外国家公民身份的文件证据。
        
    
2.  You receive the Form W-8BEN-E from an entity that is not a flow-through entity and:  
    您从非流通实体的实体收到表格 W-8BEN-E，并且：
    
    1.  You have in your possession or obtain documentation establishing foreign status that substantiates that the entity is organized or created under foreign law; or  
        您拥有或获得证明外国身份的文件，证明该实体是根据外国法律组织或创建的；或者
        
    2.  With respect to an offshore obligation, if you classify the entity as a resident of the country where the obligation is maintained and you are required to report payments to the entity annually to the tax authority of the country where the obligation is maintained and that country has a tax treaty or information exchange agreement in effect with the United States.  
        对于离岸义务，如果您将实体归类为承担义务的国家/地区的居民，并且您需要每年向承担义务的国家/地区的税务机关报告向该实体支付的款项，并且该国家/地区已与美国有效的税务条约或信息交换协议。
        
    
3.  The account holder (whether an individual or an entity) has provided standing instructions to make payments with respect to an offshore obligation to an address in, or an account maintained in, the United States, unless the account holder provides a reasonable explanation, in writing, that supports its foreign status or provides documentary evidence supporting its foreign status.  
    账户持有人（无论是个人还是实体）已提供长期指示，要求向美国地址或在美国维护的账户进行离岸债务付款，除非账户持有人以书面形式提供合理解释，支持其外国身份或提供支持其外国身份的文件证据。
    
4.  If an individual account holder provides a Form W-8BEN to establish the individual’s foreign status, and you have, either an accompanying documentation or as part of your account information, an unambiguous indication of a place of birth for the individual in the United States, you may not rely on the Form W-8BEN unless you possess or obtain documentary evidence evidencing citizenship in a country other than the United States, and either (i) a copy of the individual’s Certificate of Loss of Nationality of the United States, or (ii) a reasonable written explanation for the individual’s renunciation of U.S. citizenship (or, under an applicable IGA, the reason the individual does not have a Certificate of Loss of Nationality of the United States despite relinquishing its U.S. citizenship), or the reason the individual did not obtain U.S. citizenship at birth.  
    如果个人账户持有人提供 W-8BEN 表格来确定该个人的外国身份，并且您有随附文件或作为您账户信息的一部分，明确表明该个人在美国的出生地，您不能依赖 W-8BEN 表格，除非您拥有或获得证明美国以外国家公民身份的文件证据，并且 (i) 个人丧失美国国籍证明的副本，或(ii) 对该个人放弃美国公民身份的合理书面解释（或者，根据适用的 IGA，该个人尽管放弃了美国公民身份，却没有丧失美国国籍的证明），或者个人在出生时未获得美国公民身份。
    

**Claim of reduced rate of withholding under treaty by certain withholding agents.**

You have reason to know that a Form W-8BEN or W-8BEN-E provided by a direct account holder to claim a reduced rate of withholding under a treaty is unreliable or incorrect for purposes of establishing the account holder's residency in a treaty country if:

  

**某些扣缴义务人要求根据条约降低扣缴税率。** 

您有理由知道，在以下情况下，直接账户持有人提供的用于申请根据条约降低预扣税率的 W-8BEN 或 W-8BEN-E 表格对于确定账户持有人在条约国家的居住权而言是不可靠或不正确的： :

*   The permanent residence address on the Form W-8 is not in the treaty country or the beneficial owner notifies you of a new permanent residence address that is not in the treaty country,  
    W-8 表上的永久居住地址不在条约国家或受益所有人通知您新的永久居住地址不在条约国家，
    
*   The permanent residence address on the Form W-8 is in the treaty country but the withholding certificate (or your account information) contains a mailing address that is not in the treaty country,  
    W-8 表格上的永久居住地址位于条约国家，但预扣税证明（或您的账户信息）包含不在条约国家的邮寄地址，
    
*   You have a current mailing address in your account information outside the treaty country, or  
    您的帐户信息中的当前邮寄地址位于条约国家/地区之外，或者
    
*   The account holder has standing instructions for you to pay amounts from its account to an address or an account not in the treaty country.  
    账户持有人有长期指示，要求您从其账户向条约国家以外的地址或账户付款。
    

You may, however, rely on a Form W-8 as establishing an account holder's claim of a reduced rate of withholding under a treaty if any of the following apply.  
但是，如果满足以下任何条件，您可以依靠 W-8 表格来证明账户持有人根据条约提出的降低预扣税率的主张。

1.  The permanent residence address is not in the treaty country and:  
    永久居住地址不在条约国家，并且：
    
    1.  The account holder provides a reasonable explanation for the permanent residence address outside the treaty country, or  
        账户持有人对条约国以外的永久居住地址提供合理的解释，或
        
    2.  You possess or obtain documentary evidence described in Regulations section 1.1471-3(c)(5)(i) that establishes residency in a treaty country.  
        您拥有或获得条例第 1.1471-3(c)(5)(i) 条中所述的文件证据，可证明您在条约国家的居住权。
        
    
2.  The mailing address is not in the treaty country and:  
    邮寄地址不在条约国家且：
    
    1.  You possess or obtain documentary evidence described in Regulations section 1.1471-3(c)(5)(i) (that does not contain an address outside the treaty country) supporting the beneficial owner's claim of residence in the treaty country,  
        您拥有或获得条例第 1.1471-3(c)(5)(i) 条中描述的文件证据（不包含条约国以外的地址），支持受益所有人在条约国居住的主张，
        
    2.  You possess or obtain documentation that establishes that the beneficial owner is an entity organized in a treaty country,  
        您拥有或获得证明受益所有人是在条约国家组织的实体的文件，
        
    3.  You know that the address outside the treaty country is a branch of the account holder that is a resident of the treaty country, or  
        您知道条约国以外的地址是账户持有人（条约国居民）的分支机构，或者
        
    4.  You obtain a written statement from the beneficial owner that reasonably establishes its entitlement to treaty benefits.  
        您从受益所有人处获得一份书面声明，合理地确定其享有协定优惠的权利。
        
    
3.  You have instructions to pay amounts outside the treaty country and the account holder gives you a reasonable explanation, in writing, establishing residence in the applicable treaty country or you possess or obtain documentary evidence described in Regulations section 1.1471-3(c)(5)(i) establishing the account holder’s residence in the treaty country.  
    您收到在条约国家/地区之外支付金额的指示，并且账户持有人以书面形式向您提供合理解释，证明您在适用的条约国家/地区居住，或者您拥有或获得《条例》第 1.1471-3(c)(5) 条中所述的文件证据(i) 确定账户持有人在条约国的居住地。
    

**Hold mail instruction.**

An address that is provided subject to an instruction to hold all mail to that address is not a permanent residence address such that you may not rely upon the Form W-8. However, the address can be used as a permanent residence address if the person has provided you with the documentary evidence that is permitted under Regulations section 1.1441-1(c)(38)(ii). If, after a Form W-8 is provided, a person’s permanent residence address is subsequently subject to a hold mail instruction, this is a change in circumstances requiring the person to provide the documentary evidence described in the preceding sentence in order to use the address as a permanent residence address.

  

**保留邮件说明。** 

所提供的地址须遵守保留寄往该地址的所有邮件的指示，该地址不是永久居住地址，因此您不能依赖 W-8 表格。但是，如果此人向您提供了《条例》第 1.1441-1(c)(38)(ii) 条允许的文件证据，则该地址可以用作永久居住地址。如果在提供 W-8 表格后，某人的永久居住地址随后受到保留邮件指令的约束，则情况发生变化，要求该人提供上一句中所述的文件证据才能使用该地址作为永久居住地址。

#### Documentary Evidence书面证据

You have reason to know that documentary evidence provided by a direct account holder to support a claim of foreign status is unreliable or incorrect if:  
如果出现以下情况，您有理由知道直接账户持有人提供的支持外国身份主张的文件证据不可靠或不正确：

*   The documentary evidence does not reasonably establish the identity of the person presenting the documentary evidence;  
    文件证据不能合理确定出示文件证据的人的身份；
    
*   The documentary evidence contains information that is inconsistent with the account holder's claim of a reduced rate of withholding; or  
    文件证据中包含的信息与账户持有人关于降低预扣税率的主张不一致；或者
    
*   You have account information that is inconsistent with the account holder's claim of a reduced rate of withholding, or the documentary evidence lacks information necessary to establish a reduced rate of withholding. For example, the documentary evidence does not contain, or is not supplemented by, statements regarding the derivation of the income or compliance with limitations on benefits provisions in the case of an entity claiming treaty benefits.  
    您的账户信息与账户持有人声称的降低预扣税率不一致，或者书面证据缺乏确定降低预扣税率所需的信息。例如，文件证据不包含或不补充有关收入来源的声明，或对于要求享受协定待遇的实体遵守福利规定限制的声明。
    

**Establishment of foreign status.  
外国身份的确立。** 

You have reason to know that documentary evidence is unreliable or incorrect to establish a direct account holder's status as a foreign person if any of the following apply.  
如果存在以下任何情况，您有理由知道证明直接账户持有人的外国人身份的文件证据不可靠或不正确。

*   For documentary evidence received prior to January 1, 2001, if you have actual knowledge that the account holder is a U.S. person or if you have a mailing or residence address for the account holder in the United States.  
    对于 2001 年 1 月 1 日之前收到的文件证据，如果您确实知道账户持有人是美国人，或者您有账户持有人在美国的邮寄或居住地址。
    
*   For documentary evidence received after December 31, 2000, if you do not have a permanent residence address for the account holder, if you have classified the account holder as a U.S. person in your account information, if you have a current mailing or current permanent residence address (whether or not on the documentation) for the account holder in the United States, if the account holder notifies you of a new residence or mailing address in the United States, or if you have a current telephone number for the account holder in the United States and no telephone number for the account holder outside the United States.  
    对于 2000 年 12 月 31 日之后收到的文件证据，如果您没有账户持有人的永久居住地址，如果您在账户信息中将账户持有人归类为美国人，如果您有当前邮寄地址或当前永久居住地账户持有人在美国的地址（无论是否在文件上），如果账户持有人通知您在美国有新的居住地址或邮寄地址，或者如果您有账户持有人在美国的当前电话号码美国，并且没有美国境外账户持有人的电话号码。
    
*   If the account holder is an individual and you have, either on the documentary evidence or as part of your account information, an unambiguous place of birth for the individual in the United States.  
    如果账户持有人是个人，并且您在文件证据或账户信息中拥有该个人在美国的明确出生地。
    
*   With respect to an offshore obligation, the account holder has standing instructions directing you to pay amounts from the account to an address or account maintained in the United States.  
    对于离岸义务，账户持有人有长期指示，指示您将账户中的金额支付到在美国维护的地址或账户。
    

You may, however, rely on documentary evidence as establishing an account holder's foreign status if any of the following apply.  
但是，如果以下任何情况适用，您可以依靠文件证据来确定账户持有人的外国身份。

1.  The mailing or residence address or sole telephone number is in the United States, you receive the documentary evidence from an individual, and:  
    邮寄或居住地址或唯一的电话号码位于美国，您收到来自个人的文件证据，并且：
    
    1.  You possess or obtain additional documentary evidence (that does not contain a U.S. address) supporting the claim of foreign status and a reasonable explanation, in writing, supporting the account holder's foreign status;  
        您拥有或获得支持外国身份主张的额外文件证据（不包含美国地址）以及支持账户持有人外国身份的合理书面解释；
        
    2.  You obtain a Form W-8 that contains a permanent residence address and mailing address outside the United States (or, if a mailing address is inside the United States, the account holder provides a reasonable explanation, in writing, supporting the account holder’s foreign status); or  
        您获得一份 W-8 表格，其中包含美国境外的永久居住地址和邮寄地址（或者，如果邮寄地址在美国境内，则账户持有人提供合理的书面解释，支持账户持有人的外国身份） ）；或者
        
    3.  For a payment made with respect to an offshore obligation, if you classify the individual as a resident of the country where the obligation is maintained, you are required to report a payment made to the individual annually on a tax information statement filed with that country’s tax authority as part of the resident reporting requirements, and that country has a tax information exchange agreement or income tax treaty in effect with the United States.  
        对于与离岸义务相关的付款，如果您将该个人归类为维持该义务的国家/地区的居民，则您需要每年在向该国税务局提交的税务信息声明中报告向该个人支付的付款作为居民报告要求的一部分，并且该国家/地区与美国签订了有效的税务信息交换协议或所得税条约。
        
    
2.  The mailing or residence address or sole telephone number is in the United States, you receive the documentary evidence from an entity (other than a flow-through entity), and:  
    邮寄或居住地址或唯一电话号码位于美国，您从实体（流通实体除外）收到文件证据，并且：
    
    1.  You possess or obtain documentation to substantiate that the entity is actually organized or created under the laws of a foreign country;  
        您拥有或获得证明该实体实际上是根据外国法律组织或创建的文件；
        
    2.  You obtain a valid Form W-8 that contains a permanent residence address and mailing address outside the United States (or, if a mailing address is inside the United States, the account holder provides a reasonable explanation, in writing, supporting the account holder’s foreign status); or  
        您获得有效的 W-8 表格，其中包含美国境外的永久居住地址和邮寄地址（或者，如果邮寄地址在美国境内，则账户持有人提供合理的书面解释，支持账户持有人的外国国籍）地位）;或者
        
    3.  For a payment made with respect to an offshore obligation, if you classify the entity as a resident of the country where the obligation is maintained and you are required to report a payment made to the entity annually on a tax information statement filed with that country’s tax authority as part of the resident reporting requirements, and that country has a tax information exchange agreement or income tax treaty in effect with the United States.  
        对于与离岸债务相关的付款，如果您将该实体归类为维持该债务的国家/地区的居民，并且您需要每年在向该国税务局提交的税务信息报表中报告向该实体支付的付款作为居民报告要求的一部分，并且该国家/地区与美国签订了有效的税务信息交换协议或所得税条约。
        
    
3.  You have instructions to pay amounts to an address or an account in the United States and the account holder provides you with a reasonable explanation, in writing, that supports the account holder's foreign status or a valid beneficial owner withholding certificate claiming foreign status.  
    您收到向美国境内的地址或账户付款的指示，并且账户持有人向您提供合理的书面解释，支持账户持有人的外国身份或声称外国身份的有效受益所有人预扣税证明。
    
4.  You have an unambiguous place of birth in the United States for an individual account holder and you possess or obtain documentary evidence demonstrating the individual’s citizenship in a country other than the United States and a copy of the individual’s Certificate of Loss of Nationality of the United States. Alternatively, you may treat such an individual as a foreign person if you obtain a valid beneficial owner withholding certificate that establishes the individual’s foreign status, documentary evidence evidencing citizenship in a country other than the United States, and a reasonable explanation, in writing, of the individual’s renunciation of U.S. citizenship (or, under an applicable IGA, the reason the individual does not have a Certificate of Loss of Nationality of the United States despite relinquishing U.S. citizenship) or the reason the individual did not obtain U.S. citizenship at birth.  
    个人账户持有人在美国有明确的出生地，并且您拥有或获得证明该个人在美国以外国家的公民身份的文件证据以及该个人丧失美国国籍的证明副本。或者，如果您获得了证明该个人的外国身份的有效受益所有人预扣税证明、证明美国以外国家/地区公民身份的文件证据以及合理的书面解释，则您可以将此类个人视为外国人该个人放弃美国公民身份（或者，根据适用的 IGA，该个人尽管放弃美国公民身份但没有丧失美国国籍的证明）或该个人在出生时未获得美国公民身份的原因。
    

**Claim of reduced rate of withholding under treaty.**

You have reason to know that documentary evidence provided by a direct account holder to claim a reduced rate of withholding under a treaty is unreliable or incorrect for purposes of establishing the account holder's residency in a treaty country if:

  

**根据条约要求降低预扣税率。** 

您有理由知道，在下列情况下，直接账户持有人提供的要求根据条约降低预扣税率的文件证据对于确定账户持有人在条约国家的居住权而言是不可靠或不正确的：

*   You have a mailing or residence address for the account holder that is outside the applicable treaty country,  
    您的账户持有人的邮寄或居住地址位于适用条约国家/地区之外，
    
*   You have no permanent residence for the account holder, or  
    账户持有人没有永久居留权，或者
    
*   The account holder has standing instructions for you to pay amounts from its account to an address or account not in the treaty country.  
    账户持有人有长期指示，要求您从其账户向条约国家以外的地址或账户付款。
    

You may, however, rely on documentary evidence as establishing an account holder's claim of a reduced rate of withholding under a treaty if any of the following apply.  
但是，如果满足以下任何条件，您可以依靠文件证据来证明账户持有人根据条约提出的降低预扣税率的主张。

1.  The mailing or residence address is outside the treaty country and:  
    邮寄地址或居住地址在条约国家之外，并且：
    
    1.  You possess or obtain additional documentary evidence supporting the account holder's claim of residence in the treaty country (and the documentary evidence does not contain an address outside the treaty country, a P.O. box, an in-care-of address, or the address of a financial institution),  
        您拥有或获得额外的文件证据，支持账户持有人声称在条约国居住（并且该文件证据不包含条约国以外的地址、邮政信箱、转交地址或转交地址）金融机构），
        
    2.  You possess or obtain documentary evidence that establishes that the account holder is an entity organized in a treaty country, or  
        您拥有或获得证明账户持有人是在条约国家组织的实体的文件证据，或
        
    3.  You obtain a valid Form W-8 that contains a permanent residence address and a mailing address in the applicable treaty country.  
        您获得有效的 W-8 表格，其中包含适用条约国家/地区的永久居住地址和邮寄地址。
        
    
2.  You have instructions to pay amounts outside the treaty country and the account holder gives you a reasonable explanation, in writing, establishing residence in the applicable treaty country or a valid beneficial owner withholding certificate that contains a permanent residence address and a mailing address in the applicable treaty country.  
    您收到在条约国家/地区之外支付金额的指示，并且账户持有人以书面形式向您提供了合理的解释，证明您在适用的条约国家/地区居住，或包含适用条约国家/地区的永久居住地址和邮寄地址的有效受益所有人预扣税证明。条约国。
    

#### Indirect Account Holders' Chapter 3 Status  
间接账户持有人的第三章状态
