A withholding agent that receives documentation from a payee through an NQI, a flow-through entity, or a U.S. branch of a foreign bank or insurance company subject to U.S. or state regulatory supervision or a territory financial institution (other than a U.S. branch treated as a U.S. person) has reason to know that the documentary evidence is unreliable or incorrect for purposes of a claim of foreign status or a treaty claim if a reasonably prudent person in the withholding agent's position would question the claims made. This standard requires, but is not limited to, compliance with the following rules.  
通过 NQI、流通实体或受美国或州监管的外国银行或保险公司的美国分行或领土金融机构（被视为被视为美国分行的美国分行除外）接收收款人文件的扣缴义务人如果处于扣缴义务人地位的合理谨慎的人会对所提出的主张提出质疑，则有理由知道文件证据对于外国身份主张或条约主张的目的是不可靠或不正确的。本标准要求但不限于遵守以下规则。

**Withholding statement.**

You must review the withholding statement provided with Form W-8IMY and may not rely on information in the statement to the extent the information does not support the claims made for a payee. You may not treat a payee as a foreign person if a U.S. address is provided for the payee. You may not treat a person as a resident of a country with which the United States has an income tax treaty if the address for the person is outside the treaty country.

  

**扣留声明。** 

您必须审查随 W-8IMY 表提供的预扣税声明，并且如果声明中的信息不支持为收款人提出的索赔，则不得依赖该信息。如果收款人提供了美国地址，您不得将收款人视为外国人。如果某人的地址位于与美国签订了所得税条约的国家/地区之外，则您不得将其视为该国家/地区的居民。

You may, however, treat a payee as a foreign person and may treat a foreign person as a resident of a treaty country if the withholding statement is accompanied by a valid withholding certificate and documentary evidence or a reasonable explanation is provided, by the NQI, flow-through entity, or U.S. branch supporting the payee’s foreign status or residency in a treaty country.  
但是，如果预扣税声明附有有效的预扣税证书和文件证据，或者由 NQI 提供合理的解释，您可以将收款人视为外国人，也可以将外国人视为条约国的居民，支持收款人在条约国家的外国身份或居住权的流通实体或美国分支机构。

**Withholding certificate.**

If you receive a Form W-8 for a payee in association with a Form W-8IMY, you must review each Form W-8 and verify that the information is consistent with the information on the withholding statement. If there is a discrepancy, you may rely on the Form W-8, if valid, and instruct the NQI, flow-through entity, or U.S. branch to correct the withholding statement, or, alternatively, you may apply the presumption rules, discussed later in [_Presumption Rules_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224878 "Presumption Rules"), to the payee.

  

**扣留证明。** 

如果您收到与 W-8IMY 表格相关的收款人 W-8 表格，您必须查看每份 W-8 表格并验证该信息与预扣税单上的信息是否一致。如果存在差异，您可以依赖表格 W-8（如果有效），并指示 NQI、流通实体或美国分支机构更正预扣税表，或者您也可以应用讨论的推定规则稍后在[_推定规则_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224878 "Presumption Rules")中，向收款人。

If you choose to rely on the withholding certificate, you must, in addition to instructing the NQI, flow-through entity, or U.S. branch to correct the withholding statement, instruct the NQI, flow-through entity, or U.S. branch to confirm that it does not know or have reason to know that the withholding certificate is unreliable or inaccurate.  
如果您选择依赖扣缴证明，除了指示 NQI、流通实体或美国分支机构更正扣缴声明外，您还必须指示 NQI、流通实体或美国分支机构确认不知道或没有理由知道扣缴证明不可靠或不准确。

**Documentary evidence.**

If you receive documentary evidence for a payee in association with a Form W-8IMY, you must review the documentary evidence provided by the NQI, flow-through entity, or U.S. branch to determine that there is no obvious indication that the payee is a U.S. person subject to Form 1099 reporting or that the documentary evidence does not establish the identity of the person who provided the documentation (for example, the documentary evidence does not appear to be an identification document).

  

**文件证据。** 

如果您收到与 W-8IMY 表相关的收款人的文件证据，您必须审查 NQI、流通实体或美国分支机构提供的文件证据，以确定没有明显迹象表明收款人是美国公民须接受 1099 表格报告的人，或文件证据无法确定提供文件的人的身份（例如，文件证据似乎不是身份证明文件）。

#### Standards of Knowledge for Purposes of Chapter 4  
第 4 章的知识标准

If you make a withholdable payment, you must withhold in accordance with the _[presumption rules](#en_US_2024_publink1000224878 "Presumption Rules")_ (discussed later) if you know or have reason to know that a withholding certificate or documentary evidence provided by the payee is unreliable or incorrect to establish a payee’s chapter 4 status. If you rely on an agent to obtain documentation, you are considered to know, or have reason to know, the facts that are within the knowledge of your agent for this purpose.  
如果您支付预扣付款，并且您知道或有理由知道收款人提供的预扣税证明或文件证据不可靠或不正确，无法确定收款人的第 4 章身份，则必须按照_[推定规则](#en_US_2024_publink1000224878 "Presumption Rules")_（稍后讨论）预扣税款。如果您依赖代理人获取文件，则您被视为了解或有理由了解您的代理人为此目的所知的事实。

#### Notification by the IRS美国国税局的通知

If you receive notification from the IRS that a claim of status as a U.S. person, a participating FFI, a deemed-compliant FFI, or other entity entitled to a reduced rate of withholding under chapter 4 is incorrect, you are considered to have knowledge that such a claim is incorrect beginning 30 days after you receive the notice.  
如果您收到 IRS 的通知，称美国人、参与的 FFI、被视为合规的 FFI 或根据第 4 章有权享受降低预扣税率的其他实体的身份声明不正确，则您将被视为了解：从您收到通知后 30 天开始，此类索赔是不正确的。

#### GIIN VerificationGIIN验证

If you have received a Form W-8BEN-E or Form W-8IMY from an entity payee that is claiming certain chapter 4 statuses, you must obtain and verify the entity’s GIIN against the published IRS FFI list. The IRS FFI list can be found at [IRS.gov/Businesses/Corporations/FFI-List-Resources-Page](https://www.irs.gov/Businesses/Corporations/FFI-List-Resources-Page). You must obtain and verify against the published IRS FFI list a GIIN for the following chapter 4 statuses.  
如果您从声称某些第 4 章状态的实体收款人收到了 W-8BEN-E 表格或 W-8IMY 表格，您必须根据已发布的 IRS FFI 列表获取并验证该实体的 GIIN。 IRS FFI 列表可在[IRS.gov/Businesses/Corporations/FFI-List-Resources-Page](https://www.irs.gov/Businesses/Corporations/FFI-List-Resources-Page)上找到。您必须获取并对照已发布的 IRS FFI 列表验证以下第 4 章状态的 GIIN。

*   Participating FFIs (including reporting Model 2 FFIs).  
    参与的 FFI（包括报告模型 2 FFI）。
    
*   Registered deemed-compliant FFIs (including reporting Model 1 FFIs).  
    注册被视为合规的 FFI（包括报告模式 1 FFI）。
    
*   Sponsored FFIs.赞助的 FFI。
    
*   Direct reporting NFFEs.直接报告 NFFE。
    
*   Sponsored direct reporting NFFEs.  
    赞助直接报告的 NFFE。
    
*   Certain nonreporting IGA FFIs (as described below).  
    某些非报告 IGA FFI（如下所述）。
    

If you receive a Form W-8BEN-E or Form W-8IMY from a nonreporting IGA FFI that is a trustee-documented trust with a foreign trustee, you must obtain the GIIN of a foreign trustee, but you are not required to verify the GIIN. The GIIN that the trustee must provide is the GIIN that it received when it registered as a participating FFI or reporting Model 1 FFI, not the GIIN that it received when it registered as a trustee of a trustee-documented trust.  
如果您从非报告 IGA FFI 收到表格 W-8BEN-E 或表格 W-8IMY，该机构是与外国受托人建立受托人记录的信托，则您必须获取外国受托人的 GIIN，但无需验证GIIN。受托人必须提供的 GIIN 是其注册为参与 FFI 或报告模型 1 FFI 时收到的 GIIN，而不是其注册为受托人记录信托的受托人时收到的 GIIN。

If you receive a Form W-8BEN-E or Form W-8IMY from a nonreporting IGA FFI that checks Model 2 IGA in Part XII of Form W-8BEN-E or Part XIX of Form W-8IMY (as applicable) and identifies a category of entity that is a registered deemed-compliant FFI under Annex II of an applicable Model 2 IGA, you must obtain and verify the GIIN of the nonreporting IGA FFI. Additionally, if you receive a Form W-8BEN-E or Form W-8IMY from a nonreporting IGA FFI that provides a citation to a section of the regulations for its registered deemed-compliant status in Part XII of Form W-8BEN-E or Part XIX of Form W-8IMY (as applicable), you must obtain and verify the GIIN of the nonreporting IGA FFI. You will have reason to know that such payee is not such a financial institution if the payee's name (including a name reasonably similar to the name the withholding agent has on file for the payee) and GIIN do not appear on the most recently published IRS FFI list within 90 days of the date that the claim is made.  
如果您从非报告 IGA FFI 收到表格 W-8BEN-E 或表格 W-8IMY，该 FFI 检查表格 W-8BEN-E 第 XII 部分或表格 W-8IMY 第 XIX 部分（如适用）中的模型 2 IGA，并确定如果您是适用模型 2 IGA 附件 II 下注册的视为合规 FFI 的实体类别，则您必须获取并验证非报告 IGA FFI 的 GIIN。此外，如果您从非报告 IGA FFI 收到表格 W-8BEN-E 或表格 W-8IMY，并在表格 W-8BEN-E 或第 XII 部分中引用了其已注册视为合规状态的法规部分，根据 W-8IMY 表第 XIX 部分（如适用），您必须获取并验证非报告 IGA FFI 的 GIIN。如果收款人的姓名（包括与扣缴义务人为收款人存档的姓名相当相似的姓名）和 GIIN 未出现在最近公布的 IRS FFI 上，您就有理由知道该收款人不是此类金融机构提出索赔之日起 90 天内列出。

If you receive a Form W-8BEN-E or Form W-8IMY from an entity payee and the form contains “Applied for” in the box for the GIIN, the payee must provide you its GIIN within 90 days of providing the form. A Form W-8BEN-E or Form W-8IMY from such payee that does not include a GIIN, or includes a GIIN that does not appear on the published IRS FFI list, will be invalid for chapter 4 purposes 90 days after the date the form is provided.  
如果您从实体收款人处收到表格 W-8BEN-E 或表格 W-8IMY，并且该表格的 GIIN 框中包含“已申请”，则收款人必须在提供表格后 90 天内向您提供其 GIIN。此类收款人提交的 W-8BEN-E 表格或 W-8IMY 表格如果不包含 GIIN，或包含未出现在已公布的 IRS FFI 名单上的 GIIN，则在 90 天后，出于第 4 章的目的将无效。提供表格。

The GIIN that you must confirm is the GIIN assigned to the FFI identifying its country of residence for tax purposes (or place of organization if the FFI has no country of residence), except as otherwise provided.  
您必须确认的 GIIN 是分配给 FFI 的 GIIN，用于识别其税务居住国（或组织所在地，如果 FFI 没有居住国），除非另有规定。

**Branches and disregarded entities.**

If you make a withholdable payment to a branch of, or an entity that is disregarded as an entity separate from, a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI located outside of the FFI's country of residence or organization, the GIIN you must verify is the GIIN of the branch or disregarded entity receiving the payment. You must identify a GIIN associated with a disregarded entity to the extent provided in the Instructions for Form W-8BEN-E or the Instructions for Form W-8IMY.

  

**分支机构和被忽视的实体。** 

如果您向参与 FFI 或位于 FFI 居住国或组织境外的注册视为合规 FFI 的分支机构或被视为独立实体的实体支付预扣税款，则您必须验证的 GIIN 是接收付款的分支机构或独立实体的 GIIN。您必须在表格 W-8BEN-E 说明或表格 W-8IMY 说明中规定的范围内识别与被忽视实体相关的 GIIN。

You will have reason to know that a withholdable payment is made to a branch (including a disregarded entity) of a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI that is not itself a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI when you are directed to make the payment to an address in a jurisdiction other than that of the participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI (or branch of, or disregarded entity wholly owned by, such FFI) that is identified as the FFI (or branch of, or disregarded entity wholly owned by, such FFI) that is supposed to receive the payment and for which the FFI's GIIN is not confirmed, as described in the preceding paragraphs.  
当您被指示进行以下操作时，您将有理由知道，应预扣付款是支付给参与 FFI 或注册的视为合规 FFI 的分支机构（包括非独立实体），而该分支机构本身并非参与 FFI 或注册的视为合规 FFI向参与 FFI 或被认定为 FFI（或其分支机构、或如前几段所述，该 FFI 全资拥有的实体）应收到付款，但 FFI 的 GIIN 未确认。

The preceding sentence does not apply to an FFI that is an investment entity. If an FFI (other than an investment entity) directs you to make the payment to an account held by the FFI and maintained by another financial institution, the FFI must provide to you a statement, in writing, that the FFI is not directing the payment to any branch of such FFI that is not a participating FFI or a registered deemed-compliant FFI.  
前一句不适用于作为投资实体的 FFI。如果 FFI（投资实体除外）指示您向 FFI 持有并由另一家金融机构维护的账户付款，则 FFI 必须向您提供一份书面声明，表明 FFI 并未指示付款此类 FFI 的任何分支机构（不是参与 FFI 或已注册的视为合规 FFI）。

**Sponsored, closely held investment vehicles.**

If you make a withholdable payment to a certified deemed-compliant FFI that is a sponsored, closely held investment vehicle, you must obtain a GIIN for the sponsoring entity and verify it against the published IRS FFI list.

  

**赞助的、少数人持有的投资工具。** 

如果您向经认证的视为合规 FFI（作为赞助的、紧密持有的投资工具）支付预扣税款，您必须获得赞助实体的 GIIN，并根据 IRS 发布的 FFI 名单进行验证。

#### Reason To Know知道的理由

In general, you have reason to know that a claim of chapter 4 status is unreliable or incorrect if your knowledge of relevant facts or statements contained in the withholding certificate or other documentation is such that a reasonably prudent person would question the claim being made. For an obligation other than a preexisting obligation (that is, an obligation other than an obligation, including an account, held by an individual that is outstanding on June 30, 2014, or an obligation, including an account, held by an entity that is opened, executed, or issued before January 1, 2015), you have reason to know that a claim of chapter 4 status is unreliable or incorrect if any information contained in the account opening files or other customer account files, including documentation collected for AML due diligence purposes, conflicts with the chapter 4 status being claimed. You will not have reason to know that a claim of chapter 4 status is unreliable or incorrect based on documentation collected for AML due diligence purposes until the date that is 30 days after the obligation is created.  
一般来说，如果您对预扣税证书或其他文件中包含的相关事实或陈述的了解足以让一个相当谨慎的人对所提出的索赔提出质疑，那么您就有理由知道第 4 章状态的索赔不可靠或不正确。对于既存债务以外的债务（即，个人持有的债务以外的债务，包括账户，在 2014 年 6 月 30 日尚未清偿，或实体持有的债务，包括账户） 2015 年 1 月 1 日之前开立、执行或签发），如果开户文件或其他客户账户文件（包括收集的文件）中包含任何信息，您有理由知道第 4 章状态的索赔不可靠或不正确。反洗钱尽职调查的目的，与所声称的第 4 章地位相冲突。在义务产生后 30 天之日之前，根据为反洗钱尽职调查目的收集的文件，您没有理由知道第 4 章状态的索赔不可靠或不正确。

If you have classified an entity as engaged in a particular type of business based on your records, such as through the use of a standardized industry coding system, you have reason to know that the chapter 4 status claimed by the entity is unreliable or incorrect only if the entity’s claim conflicts with the withholding agent’s classification of the entity’s business type.  
如果您根据您的记录（例如通过使用标准化行业编码系统）将某个实体归类为从事特定类型的业务，您有理由知道该实体声称的第 4 章状态只是不可靠或不正确如果主体的申报与扣缴义务人对该主体的业务类型的分类相冲突。

#### Withholding Certificates预扣证书

In general, you have reason to know that a withholding certificate from a person is unreliable or incorrect with respect to a claim of chapter 4 status if:  
一般而言，在以下情况下，您有理由知道某人的预扣税证明对于第 4 章身份的索赔不可靠或不正确：

*   The withholding certificate is incomplete with respect to any item on the certificate that is relevant to the claim made by the person;  
    对于与该人提出的索赔相关的任何项目，预扣税证明不完整；
    
*   The withholding certificate contains any information that is inconsistent with the person’s claim;  
    扣缴证明中包含与该人的主张不一致的任何信息；
    
*   You have other account information that is inconsistent with the person’s claim;  
    您有其他与该人声称不符的账户信息；
    
*   The withholding certificate lacks information necessary to establish entitlement to an exemption from withholding for chapter 4 purposes; or  
    预扣税证明缺乏必要的信息来确定根据第 4 章目的获得预扣税豁免的权利；或者
    
*   With respect to an alternative certification under an applicable IGA included with a withholding certificate, if you know or have reason to know the certification is incorrect.  
    对于预扣税证书中包含的适用 IGA 下的替代认证，如果您知道或有理由知道该认证不正确。
    

If you obtain a withholding certificate associated with a withholdable payment to a participating FFI, a registered deemed-compliant FFI, a sponsoring entity, or a sponsored FFI, you do not need to apply the standards of knowledge described earlier with respect to an account holder’s claim of foreign status if you have confirmed the FFI’s GIIN on the current published IRS FFI list within 90 days of receipt of the withholding certificate.  
如果您获得与参与 FFI、注册的视为合规 FFI、赞助实体或赞助 FFI 的预扣付款相关的预扣税证书，则您无需应用前面描述的有关账户持有人的知识标准如果您在收到预扣税证明后 90 天内在当前公布的 IRS FFI 名单上确认了 FFI 的 GIIN，则可以申请外国身份。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_A withholding certificate used for chapter 4 purposes must also include the information required for chapter 3 purposes (that is, the entity’s tax classification) with regard to a payment that is a reportable amount under Regulations section 1.1441-1(e)(3)(vi).  
用于第 4 章目的的预扣税证明还必须包括第 3 章目的所需的信息（即实体的税务分类），涉及根据条例第 1.1441-1(e)(3)(六）。_.

#### Documentary Evidence书面证据

You have reason to know that documentary evidence provided by a person is unreliable or incorrect with respect to a claim of chapter 4 status if:  
如果出现以下情况，您有理由知道某人提供的关于第 4 章身份主张的书面证据不可靠或不正确：

*   The documentary evidence does not reasonably establish the identity of the person presenting the documentary evidence,  
    文件证据不能合理地确定出示文件证据的人的身份，
    
*   The documentary evidence contains information that is inconsistent with the person’s claim as to its chapter 4 status,  
    文件证据包含的信息与该人关于其第 4 章身份的主张不一致，
    
*   You have other account information that is inconsistent with the person’s chapter 4 status, or  
    您有其他与此人的第 4 章身份不一致的帐户信息，或者
    
*   The documentary evidence lacks information necessary to establish the person’s chapter 4 status.  
    文件证据缺乏确定该人的第四章身份所需的信息。
    

For standards of knowledge applicable to specific types of documentary evidence, see Regulations section 1.1471-3.  
有关适用于特定类型文件证据的知识标准，请参阅《条例》第 1.1471-3 节。

#### Payee Documentation From Intermediaries or Flow-Through Entities  
来自中介机构或流通实体的收款人文件

**In general.**

If you receive documentation for a payee of a withholdable payment through one or more intermediaries or flow-through entities, you must, in addition to determining each such entity’s chapter 4 status when required for chapter 4 purposes, review all documentation obtained with respect to the payee. Under certain circumstances, you may rely on a withholding certificate with an electronic signature provided by an account holder that is an NQI, when you are permitted to do so under Regulations section 1.1441-1(e)(4)(i)(B). When withholding under chapter 4 is not applied based on the chapter 4 status of an intermediary or flow-through entity, you are not required to obtain documentation for a payee through an intermediary or flow-through entity that is a QI, WP, or WT, or a payee that is included in a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees.

  

**一般来说。** 

如果您通过一个或多个中介机构或流通实体收到可预扣付款收款人的文件，除了在第 4 章目的需要时确定每个此类实体的第 4 章状态之外，您还必须审查获得的与该实体相关的所有文件。收款人。在某些情况下，如果法规第 1.1441-1(e)(4)(i)(B) 条允许您这样做，您可以依赖 NQI 账户持有人提供的带有电子签名的预扣税证书。当根据中介或流通实体的第 4 章状态不适用第 4 章规定的预扣税时，您无需通过属于 QI、WP 或 WT 的中介或流通实体获取收款人的文件，或包含在第 4 章美国收款人预扣税率池中的收款人。

_**Withholding statement.**_

You must review the withholding statement provided and may not rely on information in the statement to the extent the information does not support the claims made regarding the chapter 4 status of the payee. You may not treat a person as a foreign person if a U.S. address is provided, unless the withholding statement is accompanied by a valid withholding certificate and documentary evidence establishing foreign status.

  

_**扣留声明。** _

您必须审查所提供的预扣税声明，并且如果声明中的信息不支持有关收款人第 4 章身份的索赔，则不得依赖该信息。如果提供了美国地址，您不得将某人视为外国人，除非预扣税声明附有有效的预扣税证书和证明外国身份的文件证据。

_**Withholding certificate.**_

You must review each withholding certificate, written statement (as permitted for chapter 4 purposes with respect to certain payments to entities), or documentary evidence, and must verify that the information is consistent with the information on the withholding statement. If there is a discrepancy, you may rely on the documentation provided such documentation is valid and the intermediary or flow-through entity does not indicate that the documentation is unreliable or incorrect, or, alternatively, you may apply the presumption rules. If you choose to rely on the documentation, you must instruct the intermediary or flow-through entity to correct the withholding statement and confirm that the intermediary or flow-through entity does not know or have reason to know that the documentation is unreliable or incorrect. See Regulations section 1.1471-3(d) for when a written statement is permitted for chapter 4 purposes.

  

_**扣留证明。** _

您必须审查每份预扣税证书、书面声明（根据第 4 章目的允许的有关向实体支付的某些款项的规定）或文件证据，并且必须验证该信息与预扣税声明上的信息一致。如果存在差异，您可以依赖该文件，前提是该文件有效且中介或流通实体未表明该文件不可靠或不正确，或者您也可以应用推定规则。如果您选择依赖该文件，您必须指示中介或流通实体更正预扣税表，并确认中介或流通实体不知道或有理由知道该文件不可靠或不正确。请参阅法规第 1.1471-3(d) 节，了解何时允许出于第 4 章的目的而使用书面声明。

**Documentation from participating FFIs and registered deemed-compliant FFIs.**

If you receive documentation for a payee of a withholdable payment through a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI that is an intermediary or flow-through entity receiving the payment, you may rely on the chapter 4 status provided in the withholding statement, including a chapter 4 status determined under the requirements of (and documentation or information that is publicly available that determines the chapter 4 status of the payee permitted under) an applicable IGA, provided that you have the information necessary to report on Form 1042-S, unless you have information that conflicts with the chapter 4 status provided. If underlying documentation is provided for the payee and information in the documentation or in your records conflicts with the chapter 4 status claimed, you have reason to know that the chapter 4 status claimed is unreliable or incorrect. However, you are not required to verify the information contained in the documentation that is not facially incorrect, and you are generally not required to obtain supporting documentation for the payee. You may determine the recipient code of a payee for chapter 4 purposes (for filing Form 1042-S) that is not identified on a withholding statement when you are able to do so based on other information included on or with the withholding statement or in your records with respect to the payee.

  

**来自参与 FFI 和注册的视为合规 FFI 的文件。** 

如果您通过参与 FFI 或注册的视为合规 FFI（接收付款的中介或流通实体）收到可预扣付款收款人的文件，您可以依赖预扣税表中提供的第 4 章状态，包括根据适用 IGA 的要求确定的第 4 章身份（以及确定受款人允许的第 4 章身份的公开文件或信息），前提是您拥有在 1042-S 表格上报告所需的信息，除非您的信息与第 4 章提供的状态相冲突。如果为收款人提供了基础文件，并且该文件或您的记录中的信息与所声明的第 4 章状态相冲突，则您有理由知道所声明的第 4 章状态不可靠或不正确。但是，您不需要验证文件中包含的信息表面上没有错误，并且通常不需要为收款人获取支持文件。您可以出于第 4 章的目的（用于提交表格 1042-S）确定预扣税单上未标识的收款人代码，前提是您能够根据预扣税单中包含的其他信息或您的预扣税单中包含的其他信息来确定收款人代码。有关收款人的记录。

_**Preexisting obligation of entities.**_

If you make a withholdable payment with respect to a preexisting obligation to an entity, the scope of review is limited with respect to the time in which you must determine the entity’s chapter 4 status. For more information, see Regulations section 1.1471-3(e)(4)(vii) or, if you are a reporting Model 1 FFI or a reporting Model 2 FFI, the requirements of the applicable IGA.

  

_**实体先前存在的义务。** _

如果您就先前存在的义务向某个实体支付了可预扣的付款，则审查范围将受到您必须确定该实体的第 4 章状态的时间的限制。如需了解更多信息，请参阅法规第 1.1471-3(e)(4)(vii) 节，或者，如果您是报告模式 1 FFI 或报告模式 2 FFI，请参阅适用 IGA 的要求。

#### Presumption Rules推定规则

If you cannot reliably associate a payment with valid documentation, you must apply certain presumption rules or you may be liable for tax, interest, and penalties. If you comply with the presumption rules, you are not liable for tax, interest, and penalties even if the rate of withholding that should have been applied based on the payee's actual status is different from that presumed.  
如果您无法可靠地将付款与有效文件关联起来，则必须应用某些推定规则，否则您可能需要承担税收、利息和罚款。如果您遵守推定规则，即使根据收款人的实际情况应适用的预扣税率与推定的不同，您也无需承担税收、利息和罚款。

The presumption rules apply to determine the status of the person you pay as a U.S. or foreign person and other relevant characteristics, such as whether the payee is a beneficial owner or intermediary, and whether the payee is an individual, corporation, partnership, or trust. In the case of a withholdable payment you make to an entity, you must apply the presumption rules for chapter 4 purposes to treat the entity as a nonparticipating FFI when you cannot reliably associate the payment with documentation permitted for chapter 4 purposes. You are not permitted to apply a reduced rate of chapter 3 withholding based on a payee's presumed status if documentation is required to establish a reduced rate of withholding. For example, if the payee of interest is presumed to be a foreign person, you may not apply the portfolio interest exception or a reduced rate of withholding under a tax treaty since both exceptions require documentation.  
推定规则适用于确定您付款人的身份为美国人或外国人以及其他相关特征，例如收款人是否是受益所有人或中间人，以及收款人是否是个人、公司、合伙企业或信托。对于您向实体支付的预扣付款，当您无法可靠地将付款与第 4 章允许的文件关联时，您必须应用第 4 章目的的推定规则，将该实体视为非参与 FFI。如果需要提供文件来确定降低的预扣税率，则您不得根据收款人的假定身份应用第 3 章预扣税的降低税率。例如，如果利息收款人被推定为外国人，您可能无法应用投资组合利息例外或税收协定规定的降低预扣税率，因为这两种例外都需要提供文件。

If you rely on your actual knowledge about a payee's status and withhold an amount less than that required under the presumption rules or do not report a payment that is subject to reporting under the presumption rules, you may be liable for tax, interest, and penalties. You should, however, rely on your actual knowledge if doing so results in withholding an amount greater than would apply under the presumption rules or in reporting an amount that would not be subject to reporting under the presumption rules.  
如果您依赖对收款人状况的实际了解，预扣的金额低于推定规则要求的金额，或者未报告应根据推定规则报告的付款，您可能需要缴纳税款、利息和罚款。但是，如果这样做导致扣留的金额大于推定规则下适用的金额或报告的金额不属于推定规则下报告的金额，则您应该依赖您的实际知识。

In the case of a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI that cannot report with respect to an individual account holder, the FFI must classify the account holder under the requirements (as applicable) of the FFI agreement, Regulations section 1.1471-5(f), or an applicable IGA. Whether withholding applies to payments made to such account holders classified as recalcitrant account holders (including payments to intermediaries or flow-through entities allocating payments to such account holders on an applicable withholding statement) differs under these requirements.  
如果参与 FFI 或已注册的视为合规 FFI 无法报告个人账户持有人，则 FFI 必须根据 FFI 协议、条例第 1.1471-5(f 条) 的要求（如适用）对账户持有人进行分类)，或适用的 IGA。根据这些要求，预扣税是否适用于向被归类为顽抗账户持有人的账户持有人支付的款项（包括向在适用的预扣税表上向此类账户持有人分配款项的中介机构或流通实体的付款）。

The presumption rules, in the absence of documentation, for the subject matter are discussed in the regulations section indicated on _[Chart A](#en_US_2024_publink1000224879 "Chart A. Presumption Rules in the Absence of Documentation")_.  
在没有文件的情况下，该主题的推定规则在_[图 A](#en_US_2024_publink1000224879 "Chart A. Presumption Rules in the Absence of Documentation")_所示的法规部分中讨论。

**Chart A. Presumption Rules in the Absence of Documentation  
图 A. 无文件情况下的推定规则**

  
| **For the presumption rules related to:  
对于与以下相关的推定规则：**  | **See Regulations section:请参阅法规部分：**  |
| Payee's status收款人状态 | 1.1441-1(b)(3); 1.6049-5(d); 1.1471-3(f) (chapter 4 payees)  
1.1441-1(b)(3)； 1.6049-5(d)； 1.1471-3(f)（第 4 章收款人） |
| Effectively connected income  
有效关联收入 | 1.1441-4(a)(2) |
| Partnership and its partners  
合伙企业及其合作伙伴 | 1.1441-5(d); 1.1446-1(c)(3)  
1.1441-5(d)； 1.1446-1(c)(3) |
| Estate or trust and its beneficiaries or owner  
遗产或信托及其受益人或所有者 | 1.1441-5(e)(6) |
| Foreign tax-exempt organizations (including private foundations)  
外国免税组织（包括私人基金会） | 1.1441-9(b)(3) |

 

#### Presumption Rules for Chapter 4  
第 4 章的推定规则

If you determine that you are making a withholdable payment to an entity and cannot reliably associate the payment with a valid Form W-8 or other documentation that you are permitted to rely upon and that is sufficient to determine the chapter 4 status of the entity, you are required to treat the entity payee as a nonparticipating FFI such that withholding applies. For purposes of determining whether the payment is made to an individual or an entity, or to a U.S. person or a foreign person, if you cannot reliably associate a payment with a valid Form W-8 or other documentation that you are permitted to rely upon and from which you are able to determine the payee’s status as an individual or entity, or U.S. or foreign status, you must apply the presumption rules of Regulations section 1.1441-1(b)(3)(ii) to determine the payee’s status as an individual or entity and Regulations section 1.1441-1(b)(3)(iii) to determine the payee’s U.S. or foreign status.  
如果您确定您正在向某个实体支付可预扣的付款，并且无法可靠地将付款与有效的 W-8 表格或您允许依赖且足以确定该实体的第 4 章状态的其他文件关联起来，您需要将实体收款人视为非参与 FFI，以便适用预扣税。为了确定付款是向个人还是实体、美国人还是外国人支付，如果您无法可靠地将付款与有效的 W-8 表格或您可以依赖的其他文件关联起来并且您能够从中确定收款人的身份为个人或实体，或者美国或外国身份，您必须应用法规第 1.1441-1(b)(3)(ii) 条的推定规则来确定收款人的身份为个人或实体和法规第 1.1441-1(b)(3)(iii) 条，以确定收款人的美国或外国身份。

If you are making a withholdable payment to joint payees and cannot reliably associate the payment with valid documentation from each payee and each of the payees appears to be an individual, the payment is presumed made to an unidentified U.S. person. If any of the joint payees does not appear, by its name or other information in its account file, to be an individual, then the entire payment is treated as made to a nonparticipating FFI. However, if you receive from one of the joint payees a Form W-9, the payment shall be treated as made to that payee.  
如果您向联合收款人支付预扣税款，并且无法可靠地将付款与每个收款人的有效文件关联起来，并且每个收款人似乎都是个人，则该付款将被假定为支付给身份不明的美国人。如果任何联合收款人的姓名或账户文件中的其他信息不显示为个人，则全部付款将被视为支付给非参与 FFI。但是，如果您从联合收款人之一收到 W-9 表格，则该付款应视为向该收款人支付。

#### Income Subject to Withholding  
需预扣税款的收入

This section explains how to determine if a payment is subject to chapter 3 withholding or is a withholdable payment.  
本节说明如何确定某笔付款是否需要遵守第 3 章的预扣税规定或属于可预扣税款。

#### Amounts Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding  
第 3 章规定的预扣税金额

A payment is subject to chapter 3 withholding if it is from sources within the United States, and it is fixed or determinable annual or periodical (FDAP) income. Generally, excluding gains but including certain gains from the disposal of timber, coal, and iron ore, or from the sale or exchange of patents, copyrights, and similar intangible property.  
如果付款来自美国境内，并且是固定或可确定的年度或定期 (FDAP) 收入，则需缴纳第 3 章预扣税。一般来说，不包括收益，但包括处置木材、煤炭和铁矿石，或出售或交换专利、版权和类似无形财产的某些收益。

In addition, a payment is subject to chapter 3 withholding if withholding is specifically required, even though it may not constitute U.S. source income or FDAP income. For example, corporate distributions may be subject to chapter 3 withholding even though a part of the distribution may be a return of capital or capital gain that is not FDAP income.  
此外，如果特别需要预扣税，则即使付款可能不构成美国来源收入或 FDAP 收入，也需缴纳第 3 章预扣税。例如，公司分配可能需要缴纳第 3 章预扣税，即使分配的一部分可能是资本回报或资本收益，而不是 FDAP 收入。

**Amounts not subject to chapter 3 withholding.**

The following amounts are not subject to chapter 3 withholding.

  

**不受第 3 章预扣税约束的金额。** 

以下金额无需缴纳第 3 章预扣税。

*   Portfolio interest paid on obligations that meet certain requirements. See [_Interest_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224904 "Interest"), later.  
    为满足特定要求的债务支付的投资组合利息。稍后参见[_“兴趣”_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224904 "Interest") 。
    
*   Bank deposit interest that is not effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business. See [_Interest_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224904 "Interest"), later.  
    与美国贸易或业务活动没有有效联系的银行存款利息。稍后参见[_“兴趣”_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224904 "Interest") 。
    
*   Original issue discount on certain short- term obligations. See [_Original issue discount_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224906 "Original issue discount (Income Code 30)."), later.  
    某些短期债务的原始发行折扣。稍后请参阅[_原始发行折扣_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224906 "Original issue discount (Income Code 30).")。
    
*   Nonbusiness gambling income of a nonresident alien playing blackjack, baccarat, craps, roulette, or big-6 wheel in the United States. See [_Gambling winnings_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225022 "Gambling winnings (Income Code 28)."), later.  
    非居民外国人在美国玩二十一点、百家乐、掷骰子、轮盘赌或大 6 轮盘的非商业赌博收入。稍后请参阅[_赌博奖金_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225022 "Gambling winnings (Income Code 28).")。
    
*   Amounts paid as part of the purchase price of an obligation sold between interest payment dates. See [_Interest_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224904 "Interest"), later.  
    作为利息支付日期之间出售的债务的购买价格的一部分而支付的金额。稍后参见[_“兴趣”_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224904 "Interest") 。
    
*   Original issue discount paid on the sale of an obligation other than a redemption. See [_Original issue discount_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224906 "Original issue discount (Income Code 30)."), later.  
    出售除赎回以外的债务时支付的原始发行折扣。稍后请参阅[_原始发行折扣_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224906 "Original issue discount (Income Code 30).")。
    
*   Insurance premiums paid on a contract issued by a foreign insurer subject to the excise tax under section 4371.  
    根据外国保险公司签发的合同支付的保险费须根据第 4371 条缴纳消费税。
    

*   U.S. source transportation income subject to a 4% tax on gross income.  
    美国来源的运输收入需缴纳总收入 4% 的税。
    

#### Amounts Subject to Chapter 4 Withholding  
第 4 章规定的预扣税金额

U.S. source FDAP income for purposes of chapter 4 is similar to U.S. source FDAP income for purposes of chapter 3, subject to certain modifications such as the exclusion of certain types of non-financial payments and the inclusion (as U.S. source interest) of deposit interest paid by a foreign branch of a U. S. corporation or partnership. Also, see [_Fixed or Determinable Annual or Periodical Income (FDAP)_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224892 "Fixed or Determinable Annual or Periodical (FDAP) Income "), later.  
第 4 章中的美国来源 FDAP 收入与第 3 章中的美国来源 FDAP 收入类似，但需进行某些修改，例如排除某些类型的非金融付款以及包含存款利息（作为美国来源利息）由美国公司或合伙企业的外国分支机构支付。另请参阅后面的[_固定或可确定的年度或定期收入 (FDAP)_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224892 "Fixed or Determinable Annual or Periodical (FDAP) Income") 。

A withholding agent must withhold on a payment of U.S. source FDAP income that is a withholdable payment to which an exception does not apply under chapter 4.  
扣缴义务人必须对源自美国 FDAP 收入的付款进行扣缴，该收入属于应扣缴付款，根据第 4 章不适用例外情况。

**Amounts not subject to withholding under chapter 4.**

The following amounts are not subject to withholding under chapter 4.

  

**根据第 4 章无需预扣的金额。** 

根据第 4 章，以下金额无需缴纳预扣税。

*   Interest or original issue discount from a short-term obligation.  
    短期债务的利息或原始发行折扣。
    
*   Payments made under a grandfathered obligation (for example, obligations outstanding on July 1, 2014).  
    根据祖父债务支付的款项（例如，2014 年 7 月 1 日未清偿的债务）。
    

#### Source of Income收入来源

In most cases, income is from U.S. sources if it is paid by domestic corporations, U.S. citizens or resident aliens, or entities formed under the laws of the United States or a state. Income is also from U.S. sources if the property that produces the income is located in the United States or the services for which the income is paid were performed in the United States or the income is a dividend equivalent. A payment is treated as being from sources within the United States if the source of the payment cannot be determined at the time of payment, such as fees for personal services paid before the services have been performed. Other source rules are summarized in Chart B and explained in detail in the separate discussions under [_Withholding on Specific Income_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224897 "Withholding on Specific Income"), later.  
在大多数情况下，如果收入是由国内公司、美国公民或居民外国人或根据美国或州法律成立的实体支付的，则收入来自美国。如果产生收入的财产位于美国，或者支付收入的服务是在美国提供的，或者收入是股息等价物，则收入也来自美国。如果付款时无法确定付款来源，例如在提供服务之前支付的个人服务费用，则该付款将被视为来自美国境内的来源。其他来源规则在图 B 中进行了总结，并在稍后[_针对特定收入预扣税_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224897 "Withholding on Specific Income")下的单独讨论中进行了详细解释。

In most cases, interest on an obligation of a foreign corporation or foreign partnership is foreign-source income. If the entity is engaged in a trade or business in the United States during its tax year, interest paid by such entity is treated as from U.S. sources only if the interest is paid by a U.S. trade or business conducted by the entity or is allocable to income that is treated as effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business. This applies to a foreign partnership only if it is predominantly engaged in the active conduct of a trade or business outside the United States.  
在大多数情况下，外国公司或外国合伙企业的债务利息是外国来源收入。如果该实体在其纳税年度内在美国从事贸易或业务，则仅当该实体支付的利息是由该实体进行的美国贸易或业务支付或可分配给美国时，该实体支付的利息才被视为来自美国来源。被视为与美国贸易或业务活动有效相关的收入。这仅适用于主要在美国境外积极开展贸易或业务的外国合伙企业。

**Guarantee income.**

Certain amounts paid, directly or indirectly, for the provision of a guarantee of indebtedness issued after September 27, 2010, are from U.S. sources. The amounts must be paid by one of the following.

  

**保证收入。** 

为提供 2010 年 9 月 27 日之后发行的债务担保而直接或间接支付的某些金额来自美国。金额必须由以下其中之一支付。

1.  A noncorporate U.S. resident or a U.S. corporation for the provision of a guarantee of the resident or corporation.  
    非公司美国居民或美国公司为居民或公司提供担保。
    
2.  Any foreign person for the provision of a guarantee if the payment of income is effectively connected, or treated as effectively connected, with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business.  
    如果收入支付与美国贸易或业务活动有实际联系或被视为有实际联系，则可以向任何外国人提供担保。
    

**Personal service income (for purposes of chapter 3 withholding).**

If the income is for personal services performed in the United States, it is from U.S. sources. The place where the services are performed determines the source of the income, regardless of where the contract was made, the place of payment, or the residence of the payer.

  

**个人劳务收入（用于第 3 章预扣税）。** 

如果收入是在美国提供的个人服务，则来自美国。提供服务的地点决定了收入的来源，无论合同签订地、付款地点或付款人的居住地。

However, under certain circumstances, payment for personal services performed in the United States is not considered income from sources within the United States. For information on this exception, see [_Pay for Personal Services Performed_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224965 "Pay for Personal Services Performed"), later.  
然而，在某些情况下，在美国提供的个人服务的付款不被视为来自美国境内的收入。有关此例外的信息，请参阅稍后[_支付所执行的个人服务费用_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224965 "Pay for Personal Services Performed")。

If the income is for personal services performed partly in the United States and partly outside the United States, you must make an accurate allocation of income for services performed in the United States based on the facts and circumstances. In most cases, you make this allocation on a time basis. That is, U.S. source income is the amount that results from multiplying the total amount of pay by the following fraction.  
如果收入部分是在美国境内、部分是在美国境外提供的个人服务，您必须根据事实和情况对在美国境内提供的服务的收入进行准确的分配。在大多数情况下，您会按时间进行此分配。也就是说，美国来源收入是工资总额乘以以下分数所得的金额。

  
| Number of days services are performed in the United States  
在美国提供服务的天数 |
| Total number of days of service for which compensation is paid  
支付补偿的服务总天数 |

**Multiyear compensation.**

Generally, the source of multiyear compensation is determined on a time basis over the period to which the compensation is attributable. Multiyear compensation is compensation that is included in the taxable income of a recipient in 1 tax year but that is attributable to a period that includes 2 or more tax years. The determination of the period to which the compensation is attributable, for purposes of determining its source, is based on the facts and circumstances of each case. For example, an amount of compensation that specifically relates to a period of time that includes several calendar years is attributable to the entire multiyear period. Where determining the source of multiyear compensation on a time basis is appropriate, the amount of compensation treated as from U.S. sources is figured by multiplying the total multiyear compensation by a fraction. The numerator of the fraction is the number of days (or unit of time less than a day, if appropriate) that labor or personal services were performed in the United States in connection with the project. The denominator of the fraction is the total number of days (or unit of time less than a day, if appropriate) that labor or personal services were performed in connection with the project.

  

**多年补偿。** 

一般来说，多年期补偿的来源是根据补偿所属期间的时间来确定的。多年补偿是指包含在 1 个纳税年度的受助者应税收入中但可归属于包含 2 个或更多纳税年度的期间的补偿。为了确定赔偿来源，应根据每个案件的事实和情况来确定赔偿的归属期限。例如，与包括几个日历年的时间段具体相关的补偿金额可归因于整个多年期。如果按时间确定多年补偿的来源是适当的，则将多年补偿总额乘以一个分数即可计算出视为来自美国来源的补偿金额。分数的分子是在美国提供与该项目相关的劳务或个人服务的天数（或小于一天的时间单位，如果适用）。该分数的分母是与项目相关的劳动或个人服务的总天数（或小于一天的时间单位，如果适用）。

_**Employees.**_

If the services are performed partly in the United States and partly outside the United States by an employee, the allocation of pay, other than certain fringe benefits, is determined on a time basis. The following fringe benefits are sourced on a geographical basis as shown in the following list.

  

_**雇员。** _

如果员工部分在美国境内、部分在美国境外提供服务，则除某些附加福利外，工资的分配将按时间确定。以下附加福利按地域划分，如下表所示。

*   Housing—employee's main job location.  
    住房——员工的主要工作地点。
    
*   Education—employee's main job location.  
    教育——员工的主要工作地点。
    
*   Local transportation—employee's main job location.  
    当地交通——员工的主要工作地点。
    
*   Tax reimbursement—jurisdiction imposing tax.  
    退税——征税管辖区。
    
*   Hazardous or hardship duty pay—location of pay zone.  
    危险或艰苦条件工资——工资区的位置。
    
*   Moving expense reimbursement—employee's new main job location.  
    搬家费用报销——员工新的主要工作地点。
    

For information on what is included in these benefits, see Regulations section 1.861-4(b)(2)(ii)(D).  
有关这些福利包含哪些内容的信息，请参阅法规第 1.861-4(b)(2)(ii)(D) 节。

An employee's main job location (principal place of work) is usually the place where the employee spends most of their working time. If there is no one place where most of the work time is spent, the main job location is the place where the work is centered, such as where the employee reports for work or is otherwise required to base their work.  
员工的主要工作地点（主要工作地点）通常是员工花费大部分工作时间的地方。如果没有一个地方花费大部分工作时间，则主要工作地点是工作集中的地方，例如员工报到或需要以其他方式工作的地方。

An employee can use an alternative basis based on facts and circumstances, rather than the time or geographical basis. The employee, not the employer, must demonstrate that the alternative basis more properly determines the source of the pay or fringe benefits.  
员工可以根据事实和情况使用替代基准，而不是时间或地理基准。雇员（而不是雇主）必须证明替代基准更能正确地确定工资或附加福利的来源。

_**Territorial limits.**_

Wages received for services rendered inside the territorial limits of the United States and wages of an alien seaman earned on a voyage along the coast of the United States are regarded as from sources in the United States. Wages or salaries for personal services performed in a mine or on an oil or gas well located or being developed on the continental shelf of the United States are treated as from sources in the United States.

  

_**领土限制。** _

在美国领土范围内提供服务而获得的工资以及外籍海员在美国海岸航行中获得的工资被视为源自美国。在位于或正在美国大陆架上开发的矿山或石油或天然气井中提供的个人服务的工资或薪水被视为来自美国。

Income from the performance of services directly related to the use of a vessel or aircraft is treated as derived entirely from sources in the United States if the use begins and ends in the United States. This income is subject to withholding if it is not effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business. If the use either begins or ends in the United States, see [_Transportation income_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225024 "Transportation income."), later.  
如果使用船舶或飞机在美国开始和结束，则与使用船舶或飞机直接相关的服务收入被视为完全来自美国。如果该收入与美国贸易或业务没有有效联系，则需缴纳预扣税。如果使用开始或结束于美国，请参阅稍后的[_运输收入_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225024 "Transportation income.")。

_**Crew members.**_

Income from the performance of services by a nonresident alien in connection with the individual's temporary presence in the United States as a regular member of the crew of a foreign vessel engaged in transportation between the United States and a foreign country or a U.S. territory is not income from U.S. sources.

  

_**船员。** _

非居民外国人作为从事美国与外国或美国领土之间运输的外国船只的正式船员，在美国临时居留期间提供的服务所获得的收入不属于收入来自美国的消息来源。

_**Multilevel marketing.**_

Certain companies sell products through a multilevel marketing arrangement, such that an upper-tier distributor, who has sponsored a lower-tier distributor, is entitled to a payment from the company based on certain activities of that lower-tier distributor. Generally, depending on the facts, payments from such multilevel marketing companies to independent (nonemployee) distributors (upper-tier distributors) that are based on the sales or purchases of persons whom they have sponsored (lower-tier distributors) constitute income for the performance of personal services in recruiting, training, and supporting the lower-tier distributors. The source of such income is generally based on where the services of the upper-tier distributor are performed, and may, depending on the facts, be considered multiyear compensation, with the source of income determined over the period to which such compensation is attributable.

  

_**多层次营销。** _

某些公司通过多层次营销安排销售产品，这样赞助了下层分销商的上层分销商有权根据该下层分销商的某些活动从公司获得付款。一般来说，根据实际情况，此类多层次营销公司根据其赞助的人员（下层经销商）的销售或购买情况向独立（非雇员）经销商（上层经销商）支付的款项构成绩效收入招募、培训和支持下层经销商的个人服务。此类收入的来源通常取决于上层经销商提供服务的地点，并且根据实际情况，可以被视为多年期补偿，收入来源是在此类补偿所属期间确定的。

**Scholarships, fellowships, and grants.**

Scholarships, fellowships, and grants are sourced according to the residence of the payer. Those made by entities created or domiciled in the United States are generally treated as income from sources within the United States. However, see [_Activities outside the United States_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224890 "Activities outside the United States.") next. Those made by entities created or domiciled in a foreign country are treated as income from foreign sources.

  

**奖学金、助学金和助学金。** 

奖学金、助学金和助学金的来源是根据付款人的居住地。由在美国创建或居住的实体产生的收入通常被视为来自美国境内的收入。不过，请参阅接下来的[_美国境外活动_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224890 "Activities outside the United States.")。由在外国创建或居住的实体取得的收入被视为来自外国的收入。

_**Activities outside the United States.**_

A scholarship, fellowship, grant, targeted grant, or an achievement award received by a nonresident alien for activities conducted outside the United States is treated as foreign source income.

  

_**美国境外的活动。** _

非居民外国人因在美国境外开展活动而获得的奖学金、研究金、助学金、定向助学金或成就奖被视为外国来源收入。

**Pension payments.**

The source of pension payments is determined by the part of the distribution that constitutes the compensation element (employer contributions) and the part that constitutes the earnings element (the investment income).

  

**养老金支付。** 

养老金支付的来源由构成补偿要素（雇主缴款）的分配部分和构成收入要素（投资收益）的部分决定。

The compensation element is sourced the same as compensation from the performance of personal services. The part attributable to services performed in the United States is U.S. source income, and the part attributable to services performed outside the United States is foreign source income.  
报酬要素的来源与个人服务报酬的来源相同。在美国提供的服务的部分是美国来源收入，在美国境外提供的服务的部分是外国来源收入。

Employer contributions to a defined benefit plan covering more than one individual are not made for the benefit of a specific participant, but are made based on the total liabilities to all participants. All funds held under the plan are available to provide benefits to any participant. If the payment is from such a plan, you can use the method in Revenue Procedure 2004-37, 2004-26 I.R.B. 1099, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2004-26\_IRB#RP-2004-37](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2004-26_IRB#RP-2004-37), to allocate the payment to sources within and without the United States.  
雇主对涵盖多人的设定受益计划的缴款不是为了特定参与者的利益，而是根据所有参与者的总负债进行。该计划下持有的所有资金均可为任何参与者提供福利。如果付款来自此类计划，您可以使用收入程序 2004-37、2004-26 IRB 1099（可在[IRS.gov/irb/2004-26\_IRB#RP-2004-37](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2004-26_IRB#RP-2004-37)上获取）中的方法将付款分配给美国境内和境外的来源。

The earnings part of a pension payment is U.S. source income if the trust is a U.S. trust.  
如果信托是美国信托，则养老金支付的收入部分是美国来源收入。

**Chart B. Summary of Source Rules for FDAP Income  
图 B. FDAP 收入来源规则摘要**

  
| **IF you have...如果你有...** | **THEN the source of that income is determined by...  
那么该收入的来源由...决定** |
| pay for personal services  
支付个人服务费用 | where the services are performed.  
提供服务的地点。 |
| dividends股息 | the type of corporation (U.S. or foreign).  
公司类型（美国或外国）。 |
| interest兴趣 | the residence of the payer.  
付款人的住所。 |
| rents租金 | where the property is located.  
房产所在的地方。 |
| royalties—patents, copyrights, etc.  
特许权使用费——专利、版权等。 | where the property is used.  
使用该财产的地方。 |
| royalties—natural resources  
特许权使用费——自然资源 | where the property is located.  
房产所在的地方。 |
| pensions—distributions attributable to contributions  
养恤金——可归因于缴款的分配 | where the services were performed.  
提供服务的地点。 |
| pensions—investment earnings on contributions  
养老金——缴款投资收益 | the location of pension trust.  
养老金信托的所在地。 |
| scholarships and fellowship grants  
奖学金和助学金 | in most cases, the residence of the payer.  
在大多数情况下，是付款人的居住地。 |
| guarantee of indebtedness  
债务担保 | the residence of the debtor or whether the payment is effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business.  
债务人的居住地或付款是否与美国贸易或业务有效相关。 |

 

#### Fixed or Determinable Annual or Periodical (FDAP) Income  
固定或可确定的年度或定期收入 (FDAP)

FDAP income is all income except:  
FDAP 收入是除以下各项之外的所有收入：

*   Gains from the sale of property (not including original issue discount and certain gains that are referred to in [_Amounts Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224880 "Income Subject to Withholding"), earlier); and  
    出售财产的收益（不包括原始发行折扣和之前[_第 3 章预扣税金额_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224880 "Income Subject to Withholding")中提到的某些收益）；和
    
*   Items of income excluded from gross income without regard to U.S. or foreign status of the owner of the income, such as tax-exempt municipal bond interest and qualified scholarship income.  
    不计入总收入的收入项目，无论收入所有者的美国或外国身份如何，例如免税市政债券利息和合格的奖学金收入。
    

The following items are examples of FDAP income.  
以下项目是 FDAP 收入的示例。

*   Compensation for personal services paid to an individual or a sole proprietorship.  
    支付给个人或独资企业的个人劳务报酬。
    
*   Dividends and dividend equivalent payments.  
    股息和股息等价支付。
    
*   Interest.兴趣。
    
*   Original issue discount.原版折扣。
    
*   Real estate mortgage investment conduit (REMIC) excess inclusion income.  
    房地产抵押投资管道（REMIC）超额包含收入。
    
*   Pensions and annuities.养老金和年金。
    
*   Alimony (no longer income if the divorce or separation agreement is executed after December 31, 2018, or if executed before January 1, 2019, but modified after December 31, 2018, the modification must state that section 11051 of P.L. 115-97 (TCJA) applies to the modification).  
    赡养费（如果离婚或分居协议在 2018 年 12 月 31 日之后执行，或者如果在 2019 年 1 月 1 日之前执行，但在 2018 年 12 月 31 日之后修改，则修改必须说明 PL 115-97 (TCJA) 第 11051 条）适用于修改）。
    
*   Real property income, such as rents, other than gains from the sale of real property.  
    不动产收入，例如租金，不包括出售不动产的收益。
    
*   Royalties.版税。
    
*   Taxable scholarships and fellowship grants.  
    应税奖学金和助学金。
    
*   Other taxable grants, prizes, and awards.  
    其他应税补助金、奖金和奖励。
    
*   A sales commission paid or credited monthly.  
    每月支付或存入的销售佣金。
    
*   A commission paid for a single transaction.  
    为单笔交易支付的佣金。
    
*   The distributable net income of an estate or trust that is FDAP income and must be distributed currently, or has been paid or credited during the tax year.  
    遗产或信托的可分配净收入，即 FDAP 收入，必须当前分配，或在纳税年度内已支付或贷记。
    
*   FDAP income distributed by a partnership that, or such an amount that, although not actually distributed, is includible in the gross income of a foreign partner.  
    由合伙企业分配的 FDAP 收入，或虽然未实际分配但包含在外国合伙人总收入中的金额。
    
*   Taxes, mortgage interest, or insurance premiums paid to, or for the account of, a nonresident alien landlord by a tenant under the terms of a lease.  
    租户根据租赁条款向非居民外籍房东支付的税款、抵押贷款利息或保险费，或为非居民外籍房东支付的保险费。
    
*   Publication rights.出版权。
    
*   Prizes awarded to nonresident alien artists for pictures exhibited in the United States.  
    授予在美国展出画作的非居民外籍艺术家的奖项。
    
*   Purses paid to nonresident alien boxers for prize fights in the United States.  
    向在美国参加职业拳击比赛的非居民外籍拳击手支付的奖金。
    
*   Prizes awarded to nonresident alien professional golfers in golfing tournaments in the United States.  
    在美国高尔夫锦标赛中向非居民外籍职业高尔夫球手颁发的奖项。
    

Payments for the following purposes are examples of payments that are not withholdable payments.  
用于以下目的的付款是不可预扣付款的付款示例。

*   Services (including wages and other forms of employee compensation (such as stock options)).  
    服务（包括工资和其他形式的员工报酬（例如股票期权））。
    
*   The use of property.财产的使用。
    
*   Office and equipment leases.  
    办公室和设备租赁。
    
*   Software licenses.软件许可证。
    
*   Transportation.运输。
    
*   Freight.货运。
    
*   Gambling winnings.赌博的奖金.
    
*   Awards, prizes, and scholarships.  
    奖项、奖品和奖学金。
    
*   Interest on outstanding accounts payable arising from the acquisition of goods or services.  
    因购买商品或服务而产生的应付账款利息。
    

**Periodic or lump-sum payments.**

Income can be FDAP income whether it is paid in a series of repeated payments or in a single lump sum. For example, $5,000 in royalty income would be FDAP income whether paid in 10 payments of $500 each or in one payment of $5,000.

  

**定期或一次性付款。** 

无论是通过一系列重复付款还是一次性支付，收入都可以是 FDAP 收入。例如，5,000 美元的特许权使用费收入将是 FDAP 收入，无论是分 10 次支付，每次支付 500 美元，还是一次性支付 5,000 美元。

**Insurance proceeds.**

Income derived by an insured nonresident alien from U.S. sources upon the surrender of, or at the maturity of, a life insurance policy, is FDAP income and is subject to chapter 3 withholding and is a withholdable payment. This includes income derived under a life insurance contract issued by a foreign branch of a U.S. life insurance company. The proceeds are income to the extent they exceed the cost of the policy.

  

**保险收益。** 

来自美国的受保非居民外国人在人寿保险保单退保或到期时获得的收入为 FDAP 收入，需根据第 3 章预扣税款，属于可预扣付款。这包括根据美国人寿保险公司外国分支机构签发的人寿保险合同获得的收入。收益在超过保单成本的范围内即为收入。

However, certain payments received under a life insurance contract on the life of a terminally or chronically ill individual before death (accelerated death benefits) may not be subject to tax. This also applies to certain payments received for the sale or assignment of any part of the death benefit under contract to a viatical settlement provider. For more information, see [Pub. 525](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-525).  
然而，根据绝症或慢性病个人生前人寿保险合同收到的某些付款（加速死亡抚恤金）可能无需纳税。这也适用于根据合同将死亡抚恤金的任何部分出售或转让给交通结算提供商而收到的某些付款。欲了解更多信息，请参阅[发布。第525章](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-525)

**Racing purses (for purposes of chapter 3 withholding).**

Racing purses are FDAP income and racetrack operators must withhold 30% on any purse paid to a nonresident alien racehorse owner in the absence of definite information contained in a statement filed together with a Form W-8 that the owner has not raced, or does not intend to enter, a horse in another race in the United States during the tax year. If available information indicates that the racehorse owner has raced a horse in another race in the United States during the tax year, then the statement and Form W-8 filed for that year are ineffective. The owner may be exempt from withholding of tax at 30% on the purses if the owner gives you Form W-8ECI, which provides that the income is effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business and that the income is includible in the owner's gross income.

  

**赛车钱包（用于第 3 章扣缴的目的）。** 

赛马奖金属于 FDAP 收入，如果与 W-8 表格一起提交的声明中没有明确表明马主没有参加过比赛或没有参加过比赛，则赛马场运营商必须对支付给非居民外籍赛马所有者的任何奖金预扣 30%打算在纳税年度内让一匹马参加美国的另一场比赛。如果现有信息表明赛马所有者在纳税年度内在美国参加过另一场比赛，则该年度提交的声明和 W-8 表格无效。如果所有者向您提供 W-8ECI 表格，该表格规定该收入与在美国进行的贸易或业务有实际联系，并且该收入包含在业主的总收入。

**Covenant not to compete.**

Payment received for a promise not to compete is generally FDAP income. Its source is the place where the promisor forfeited their right to act. Amounts paid to a nonresident alien for their promise not to compete in the United States are subject to chapter 3 withholding and are withholdable payments.

  

**约定不参加比赛。** 

因承诺不参加竞争而收到的付款通常是 FDAP 收入。其根源是承诺人丧失行为权的地方。因非居民外国人承诺不在美国参加比赛而向其支付的金额须遵守第 3 章规定的预扣税，属于可预扣税款。

#### Withholding on Specific Income  
特定收入预扣税

Different kinds of income are subject to different withholding requirements.  
不同种类的收入须缴纳不同的预扣税。

#### Effectively Connected Income  
有效关联收入

In most cases, when a foreign person engages in a trade or business in the United States, all income from sources in the United States connected with the conduct of that trade or business is considered effectively connected with a U.S. business. FDAP income may or may not be effectively connected with a U.S. business. For example, effectively connected income (ECI) includes rents from real property if the alien chooses to treat that income as effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business.  
在大多数情况下，当外国人在美国从事贸易或业务时，与该贸易或业务的进行有关的来自美国的所有收入都被视为与美国企业有效相关。 FDAP 收入可能会也可能不会与美国企业有有效联系。例如，有效关联收入 (ECI) 包括不动产租金，如果外国人选择将该收入视为与美国贸易或业务有效关联的话。

The factors to be considered in establishing whether FDAP income and similar amounts are effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business include:  
在确定 FDAP 收入和类似金额是否与美国贸易或业务有效联系时需要考虑的因素包括：

*   Whether the income is from assets used in, or held for use in, the conduct of that trade or business; or  
    收入是否来自用于该贸易或业务的进行或持有用于该贸易或业务的资产；或者
    
*   Whether the activities of that trade or business were a material factor in the realization of the income.  
    该贸易或业务的活动是否是实现收入的重要因素。
    

**Income from securities.**

There is a special rule determining whether income from securities is effectively connected with the active conduct of a U.S. banking, financing, or similar business.

  

**证券收入。** 

有一条特殊规则确定证券收入是否与美国银行、金融或类似业务的活跃行为有效相关。

If the foreign person's U.S. office actively and materially participates in soliciting, negotiating, or performing other activities required to arrange the acquisition of securities, the U.S. source interest or dividend income from the securities, gain or loss from their sale or exchange, income or gain economically equivalent to such amounts, or amounts received for providing a guarantee of indebtedness, is attributable to the U.S. office and is ECI.  
如果外国人的美国办事处积极且实质性地参与安排购买证券所需的招揽、谈判或进行其他活动，则美国从证券中获得利息或股息收入、出售或交换证券的收益或损失、收入或收益经济上相当于此类金额的金额，或因提供债务担保而收到的金额，归属于美国办事处，即 ECI。

**Withholding exemption.**

In most cases, you do not need to withhold tax on income for purposes of chapter 3 or 4 if you receive a Form W-8ECI on which a foreign payee represents that:

  

**扣缴豁免。** 

在大多数情况下，如果您收到的 W-8ECI 表格中外国收款人表示：

*   The foreign payee is the beneficial owner of the income;  
    外国收款人是收入的受益所有人；
    
*   The income is effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business in the United States; and  
    该收入与在美国进行的贸易或业务有实际联系；和
    
*   For purposes of chapter 3 withholding, the income is includible in the payee's gross income.  
    就第 3 章预扣税而言，该收入包含在收款人的总收入中。
    

This withholding exemption applies to income for services performed by a foreign partnership or foreign corporation (unless item (4) below applies to the corporation). The exemption does not apply, however, to:  
此预扣税豁免适用于外国合伙企业或外国公司提供服务的收入（除非以下第 (4) 条适用于该公司）。然而，豁免不适用于：

1.  Pay for personal services performed by an individual for purposes of chapter 3 (see [_Pay for Personal Services Performed_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224965 "Pay for Personal Services Performed"), later),  
    为第 3 章中个人提供的个人服务付费（参见后面的为[_所执行的个人服务付费_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224965 "Pay for Personal Services Performed")），
    
2.  Effectively connected taxable income of a partnership that is allocable to its foreign partners (see [Partnership Withholding on ECTI](#en_US_2024_publink1000225066 "Partnership Withholding on ECTI"), later),  
    有效关联的可分配给其外国合伙人的合伙企业的应税收入（请参阅稍后[关于 ECTI 的合伙企业预扣税](#en_US_2024_publink1000225066 "Partnership Withholding on ECTI")），
    
3.  Income from the disposition of a USRPI (see [_U.S. Real Property Interest_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest"), later), or  
    来自处置 USRPI 的收入（参见下文的[_美国不动产利息_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest")），或
    
4.  Payments to a foreign corporation for personal services if all of the following apply.  
    如果满足以下所有条件，则向外国公司支付个人服务费用。
    
    1.  The foreign corporation otherwise qualifies as a personal holding company for income tax purposes;  
        外国公司在所得税方面具有个人控股公司的其他资格；
        
    2.  The foreign corporation receives amounts under a contract for personal services of an individual whom the corporation has no right to designate;  
        外国公司根据个人服务合同收取该公司无权指定的个人的款项；
        
    3.  25% or more in value of the outstanding stock of the foreign corporation at some time during the tax year is owned, directly or indirectly, by or for an individual who has performed, is to perform, or may be designated as the one to perform, the services called for under the contract.  
        在纳税年度的某个时间，外国公司已发行股票价值的 25% 或以上由已经履行、将要履行或可能被指定为履行义务的个人直接或间接拥有。 ，合同要求的服务。
        
    

**Withholding exemption for purposes of chapter 4.**

Income effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business in the United States is not a withholdable payment under chapter 4 and thus is not subject to withholding for chapter 4 purposes. You do not need to withhold tax under chapter 4 if you receive a Form W-8ECI on which a foreign payee makes the representations described in _[Withholding exemptions](#en_US_2024_publink1000224900 "Withholding exemption.")_, earlier.

  

**就第 4 章而言，预扣税豁免。** 

根据第 4 章，与在美国开展贸易或业务实际相关的收入不属于可预扣税款，因此无需根据第 4 章的目的进行预扣税。如果您收到一份 W-8ECI 表格，其中外国收款人在上面做了前面_[预扣税豁免](#en_US_2024_publink1000224900 "Withholding exemption.")_中所述的陈述，则您无需根据第 4 章预扣税款。

**Notional principal contract income.**

Certain payments attributable to a notional principal contract are not subject to withholding regardless of whether a Form W-8ECI is provided. However, payments of dividend equivalents that are not effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business in the United States, pursuant to a specified notional principal contract (described later under [_Dividend equivalent payments_](#en_US_2024_publink1000246556 "Dividend equivalent payments.")) are subject to withholding.

  

**名义主合同收入。** 

无论是否提供 W-8ECI 表格，名义主合同的某些付款均无需预扣。然而，根据特定的名义主合同（稍后在[_股息等值支付_](#en_US_2024_publink1000246556 "Dividend equivalent payments.")中进行描述），与在美国进行的交易或业务没有实际联系的股息等值支付需要预扣。

Income from a notional principal contract is subject to reporting on Form 1042-S if it is effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business in the United States. You must treat the income as effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business if you pay the income to, or to the account of, a qualified business unit (a branch) of a foreign person located in the United States or a qualified business unit located outside the United States and you know, or have reason to know, the income is effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business. You do not need to treat notional principal contract income as effectively connected if you receive a Form W-8BEN-E that represents that the income is not effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business or if the payee provides a representation in a master agreement or in the confirmation on the particular notional principal contract transaction that the payee is a U.S. person or a non-U.S. branch of a foreign person.  
如果名义主合同的收入与在美国进行的贸易或业务有实际联系，则需要在 1042-S 表格上报告。如果您将收入支付给位于美国的外国人的合格业务单位（分支机构）或位于美国的合格业务单位或账户，则必须将收入视为与美国贸易或业务有效相关在美国境外，并且您知道或有理由知道该收入与在美国进行的贸易或业务有实际联系。如果您收到 W-8BEN-E 表格，表明该收入与美国贸易或业务的行为没有实际联系，或者如果收款人在主协议或特定名义主合同交易的确认书中，收款人为美国人或外国人的非美国分支机构。

**Income paid to U.S. branch of foreign bank or insurance company.**

A payment to a U.S. branch of a foreign bank or a foreign insurance company that is subject to U.S. regulation by the Federal Reserve or state insurance authorities is presumed to be effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business in the United States if you have an EIN for the branch, unless the branch provides a Form W-8BEN-E or Form W-8IMY for the income. If a U.S. branch of a foreign bank or insurance company receives income that the payer did not withhold upon because of the presumption that the income was effectively connected with the U.S. branch's trade or business, the U.S. branch is required to withhold on the income if it is in fact not effectively connected with the conduct of its trade or business in the United States. Withholding is required whether the payment was collected on behalf of other persons or on behalf of another branch of the same entity.

  

**支付给外国银行或保险公司美国分行的收入。** 

如果您满足以下条件，则向受美国联邦储备委员会或州保险机构监管的外国银行或外国保险公司的美国分行或外国保险公司的付款将被视为与在美国进行的贸易或业务有实际联系：分行的 EIN，除非分行为收入提供 W-8BEN-E 表格或 W-8IMY 表。如果外国银行或保险公司的美国分行收到付款人未扣缴的收入，因为假定该收入与美国分行的贸易或业务有实际联系，则美国分行需要扣缴该收入，如果事实上与其在美国的贸易或业务行为没有有效联系。无论付款是代表其他人还是代表同一实体的另一个分支机构收取，都需要预扣税款。

#### Income Not Effectively Connected  
收入未有效关联

This section discusses the specific types of income that are subject to chapter 3 withholding and where withholding under chapter 4 is required. The income codes contained in this section correspond to the income codes used on the 2024 Form 1042-S (discussed later).  
本节讨论需要缴纳第 3 章预扣税以及需要根据第 4 章预扣税的具体收入类型。本节中包含的收入代码与 2024 年 1042-S 表格（稍后讨论）中使用的收入代码相对应。

For purposes of chapter 3, you must withhold tax at the statutory rates shown in _[Chart C](#en_US_2024_publink1000224907 "Chart C. Withholding Tax Rates for Purposes of Chapter 3")_ unless a reduced rate or exemption under a tax treaty applies. For U.S. source gross income that is not effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business, the rate is usually 30%. In most cases, you must withhold the tax at the time you pay the income to the foreign person. See [_When to withhold_](#en_US_2024_publink100015248 "When to withhold."), earlier.  
就第 3 章而言，您必须按照_[表 C](#en_US_2024_publink1000224907 "Chart C. Withholding Tax Rates for Purposes of Chapter 3")_所示的法定税率预扣税款，除非适用税收协定规定的降低税率或豁免。对于与美国贸易或业务没有有效联系的美国来源总收入，税率通常为 30%。在大多数情况下，您必须在向外国人支付收入时预扣税款。请参阅更早的[_何时扣留_](#en_US_2024_publink100015248 "When to withhold.")。

#### Interest兴趣

Interest from U.S. sources paid to foreign payees is subject to chapter 3 withholding and is a withholdable payment (except when the interest is paid with respect to a grandfathered obligation or another exemption under chapter 4 applies). When making a payment on an interest-bearing obligation, you must withhold on the gross amount of stated interest payable on the interest payment date, even if the payment or a part of the payment may be a return of capital rather than interest.  
从美国来源支付给外国收款人的利息须缴纳第 3 章预扣税，并且属于可预扣税款（除非利息是针对祖父债务支付的，或适用第 4 章规定的其他豁免）。在支付带息债务时，您必须预扣利息支付日规定的应付利息总额，即使该付款或部分付款可能是资本返还而不是利息。

A substitute interest payment made to the transferor of a security in a securities lending transaction or a sale-repurchase transaction is treated the same as the interest on the transferred security. Use Income Code 33 to report these substitute payments.  
证券出借交易、卖出回购交易中向证券转让方支付的替代利息，与转让证券利息相同。使用收入代码 33 报告这些替代付款。

**Interest paid by U.S. obligors—general (Income Code 1).**

With specific exceptions, such as portfolio interest (for purposes of chapter 3), you must withhold on interest paid or credited on bonds, debentures, notes, open account indebtedness, governmental obligations, certain deferred payment arrangements (as provided in section 483), or other evidences of indebtedness of U.S. obligors. U.S. obligors include the U.S. Government or its agencies or instrumentalities, any U.S. citizen or resident, any U.S. corporation, and any U.S. partnership.

  

**美国债务人支付的利息——一般（收入代码 1）。** 

除特定例外情况外，例如投资组合利息（就第 3 章而言），您必须预扣债券、债券、票据、赊账债务、政府债务、某些延期付款安排（如第 483 条规定）支付或贷记的利息，或美国债务人的其他债务证据。美国债务人包括美国政府或其机构或部门、任何美国公民或居民、任何美国公司以及任何美国合伙企业。

If, in a sale of a corporation's property, payment of the bonds or other obligations of the corporation is assumed by the buyer, that buyer, whether an individual, partnership, or corporation, must deduct and withhold the taxes that would be required to be withheld by the selling corporation as if there had been no sale or transfer. Also, if interest coupons are in default, the tax must be withheld on the gross amount of interest whether or not the payment is a return of capital or the payment of income.  
如果在出售公司财产时，买方承担了公司债券或其他义务的支付，则该买方，无论是个人、合伙企业还是公司，都必须扣除并预扣需要缴纳的税款。由出售公司扣留，如同没有出售或转让一样。此外，如果息票违约，则无论支付的是资本返还还是收入支付，都必须按利息总额扣税。

A resident alien paying interest on a margin account maintained with a foreign brokerage firm must withhold from the interest whether the interest is paid directly or constructively.  
向外国经纪公司维持的保证金账户支付利息的外籍居民必须扣除利息，无论利息是直接支付还是推定支付。

Interest on bonds of a U.S. corporation paid to a foreign corporation not engaged in a trade or business in the United States is subject to withholding even if the interest is guaranteed by a foreign corporation.  
美国公司向不在美国从事贸易或业务的外国公司支付的债券利息，即使该利息由外国公司担保，也须缴纳预扣税。

Domestic corporations must withhold on interest credited to foreign subsidiaries or foreign parents.  
国内公司必须预扣贷记给外国子公司或外国母公司的利息。

For withholding under chapter 4 on the interest payments described in this section, see the definition of withholdable payments in Regulations section 1.1473-1(a).  
对于本节所述的第 4 章利息支付的预扣税，请参阅《条例》第 1.1473-1(a) 节中可预扣税款的定义。

**Original issue discount (Income Code 30).  
原始发行折扣（收入代码 30）。** 

Original issue discount paid on the redemption of an obligation is subject to chapter 3 withholding and is a withholdable payment (except when paid with respect to a grandfathered obligation). Original issue discount paid as part of the purchase price of an obligation sold or exchanged, other than in a redemption, is not subject to chapter 3 withholding unless the purchase is part of a plan the principal purpose of which is to avoid tax and the withholding agent has actual knowledge or reason to know of the plan. However, such original issue discount is a withholdable payment (except when paid with respect to a grandfathered obligation). Withholding is required by a person other than the issuer of an obligation (or the issuer's agent).  
赎回债务时支付的原始发行折扣须缴纳第 3 章预扣税，并且属于可预扣付款（除非是针对祖父债务支付的）。作为出售或交换债务的购买价格一部分支付的原始发行折扣（赎回除外）不受第 3 章预扣税的约束，除非购买是主要目的是避税和预扣税的计划的一部分代理人实际了解或有理由了解该计划。然而，此类原始发行折扣是一项可预扣的付款（除非是针对祖父债务支付的）。债务发行人（或发行人的代理人）以外的人要求预扣税。

The original issue discount that is subject to chapter 3 withholding and is a withholdable payment (except when paid with respect to a grandfathered obligation) is the taxable amount of original issue discount. The taxable amount for both chapters 3 and 4 withholding purposes is the original issue discount that accrued while the obligation was held by the foreign beneficial owner up to the time the obligation was sold or exchanged or a payment was made, reduced by any original issue discount that was previously taxed. If a payment was made, the tax due on the original issue discount may not exceed the payment reduced by the tax imposed on the part of the payment that is qualified stated interest.  
需缴纳第 3 章预扣税且属于可预扣付款的原始发行折扣（针对祖父债务支付的除外）是原始发行折扣的应税金额。第 3 章和第 4 章预扣税目的的应税金额是外国受益所有人持有债务直至债务被出售或交换或付款时累积的原始发行折扣，减去任何原始发行折扣之前已征税。如果已付款，则原始发行折扣应缴的税款不得超过对符合规定利息的付款部分征收的税款所扣除的金额。

If you cannot determine the taxable amount, you must withhold on the entire amount of original issue discount accrued from the date of issue until the date of redemption (or sale or exchange, if subject to chapter 3 withholding or a withholdable payment) determined on the basis of the most recently published [Pub. 1212](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-1212).  
如果您无法确定应税金额，则必须预扣从发行之日起直至赎回（或出售或交换，如果受第 3 章预扣或可预扣付款约束的情况下，出售或交换）期间累积的原始发行折扣的全部金额。最近发布的[Pub 的基础。 1212](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-1212) .

For more information on original issue discount, see [Pub. 550](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-550).  
有关原始发行折扣的更多信息，请参阅[Pub。第550章](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-550)

**Chart C. Withholding Tax Rates for Purposes of Chapter 3  
图 C. 第 3 章规定的预扣税率**

> **笔记。** 除非税收协定授权降低税率或免税，否则您必须按以下税率对收入支付预扣税款。总统可以对支付给外国居民或公司的收入征收更高的税率，这些外国居民或公司对美国人征收繁重或歧视性的税收。

支付给“F”、“J”、“M”或“Q”签证持有者的美国奖学金或助学金的应税部分（请参阅后面的[_奖学金和助学金_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224951 "Scholarships and Fellowship Grants Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding (Income Code 16)")） | 14% |

#### Reduced Rates of Withholding on Interest  
降低利息预扣税率

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_Notwithstanding the exception from withholding under chapter 3 on interest described under this heading, withholding may still apply under chapter 4 when the payment is a withholdable payment and an exception from withholding under chapter 4 does not apply.  
尽管本标题下所述的利息有第 3 章规定的预扣税例外情况，但当付款是可预扣税款且第 4 章规定的预扣税例外情况不适用时，仍可根据第 4 章适用预扣税。_.

Certain interest is subject to a reduced rate of, or exemption from, withholding.  
某些利息可享受预扣税减免或减免。

**Portfolio interest exempt from chapter 3 withholding.**

Interest and original issue discount that qualifies as portfolio interest is exempt from chapter 3 withholding. However, these amounts are not exempt from withholding under chapter 4 when the interest is a withholdable payment, unless an exception from chapter 4 withholding applies. To qualify as portfolio interest, the interest must be paid on obligations issued after July 18, 1984, and otherwise subject to chapter 3 withholding.

  

**投资组合利息免征第 3 章预扣税。** 

符合投资组合利息资格的利息和原始发行折扣可免于缴纳第 3 章预扣税。然而，当利息属于应预扣税款时，这些金额不能根据第 4 章免予预扣，除非适用第 4 章预扣税的例外情况。要符合投资组合利息的资格，必须为 1984 年 7 月 18 日之后发行的债务支付利息，否则须缴纳第 3 章预扣税。

### Note.

The rules for determining whether interest is portfolio interest changed for obligations issued after March 18, 2012. Before March 19, 2012, portfolio interest included interest on certain registered and nonregistered (bearer) bonds if the obligations meet the requirements described below.

For obligations issued after March 18, 2012, portfolio interest does not include interest paid on debt that is not in registered form, except for interest paid on foreign-targeted registered obligations issued before January 1, 2016, as described in [_Foreign-targeted registered obligations_](#en_US_2024_publink1000297463 "Foreign-targeted registered obligations."), later.

  

### 笔记。

对于 2012 年 3 月 18 日之后发行的债务，确定利息是否为投资组合利息的规则发生了变化。2012 年 3 月 19 日之前，如果债务满足下述要求，则投资组合利息包括某些记名和非记名（无记名）债券的利息。

对于 2012 年 3 月 18 日之后发行的债券，投资组合利息不包括非记名债务支付的利息，但 2016 年 1 月 1 日之前发行的面向外国的记名债券支付的利息除外，如[_面向外国的记名债务_](#en_US_2024_publink1000297463 "Foreign-targeted registered obligations.")中所述， 之后。

_**Obligations in registered form.**_

Portfolio interest includes interest paid on an obligation that is in registered form, and for which you have received documentation that the beneficial owner of the obligation is not a U.S. person.

  

_**登记形式的义务。** _

投资组合利息包括以记名形式支付的利息，并且您已收到该债务的受益所有人不是美国人的文件。

Generally, an obligation is in registered form if (i) the obligation is registered as to both principal and any stated interest with the issuer (or its agent) and any transfer of the obligation may be effected only by surrender of the old obligation and reissuance to the new holder, (ii) the right to principal and stated interest with respect to the obligation may be transferred only through a book entry system maintained by the issuer or its agent, or (iii) the obligation is registered as to both principal and stated interest with the issuer or its agent and can be transferred both by surrender and reissuance and through a book entry system.  
一般来说，如果 (i) 该债务的本金和任何规定的利息均已向发行人（或其代理人）登记，并且该债务的任何转让只能通过放弃旧债务并重新发行来实现，则该债务为记名形式。对于新持有人，(ii) 与该债务相关的本金和规定利息的权利只能通过发行人或其代理人维护的记账系统转移，或者 (iii) 该债务的本金和利息均已登记向发行人或其代理人表明了兴趣，并且可以可以通过交出和重新签发以及通过簿记系统进行转移。

An obligation that would otherwise be considered to be in registered form is not considered to be in registered form as of a particular time if it can be converted at any time in the future into an obligation that is not in registered form, except as otherwise provided in Notice 2012-20, 2012-13 I.R.B. 574, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2012-13\_IRB#NOT-2012-20](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2012-13_IRB#NOT-2012-20), as described in the following section.  
除非另有规定，否则本应被视为记名形式的债务，如果在未来任何时间可以转换为非记名形式的债务，则该债务在特定时间不被视为记名形式的债务。见通知 2012-20、2012-13 IRB 574，可在[IRS.gov/irb/2012-13\_IRB#NOT-2012-20](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2012-13_IRB#NOT-2012-20)上获取，如下节所述。

_**Dematerialized book-entry systems and effectively immobilized obligations.**_

An obligation will be considered to be in registered form if it is issued through either a dematerialized book entry system maintained by a clearing organization (or agent thereof) or a clearing system in which the obligation (including a global obligation in bearer form) is effectively immobilized. See [Notice 2012-20](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2012-13_IRB#NOT-2012-20), amplified by Notice 2013-43, 2013-31 I.R.B. 113, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2013-31\_IRB#NOT-2013-43](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2013-31_IRB#NOT-2013-43).

  

_**非物质化的记账系统和有效固定的义务。** _

如果债务是通过清算组织（或其代理人）维护的非物质化记账系统或债务（包括不记名形式的全球债务）有效地通过清算系统发行的，则该债务将被视为记名形式。不动了。请参阅[通知 2012-20](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2012-13_IRB#NOT-2012-20) ，并由通知 2013-43、2013-31 IRB 113 进行放大，可在[IRS.gov/irb/2013-31\_IRB#NOT-2013-43](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2013-31_IRB#NOT-2013-43)上获取。

Under dematerialized book-entry systems, bonds are required to be represented only by book entries, and no physical certificates are issued or transferred. The bonds are transferred only by book entries.  
在非物质化账簿分录系统下，债券只需由账簿分录代表，不发行或转让任何实物凭证。债券仅通过账簿分录进行转让。

An obligation will be considered to be effectively immobilized if (1) it is represented by one or more global securities in physical form that are issued to and held by a clearing organization (or by a custodian or depository acting as an agent of the clearing organization) for the benefit of purchasers and under arrangements that prohibit transfer except to a successor clearing organization subject to the same terms, and (2) beneficial interest in the underlying obligation is transferable only through a book-entry system maintained by the clearing organization or its agent.  
如果出现以下情况，一项债务将被视为有效固定： (1) 该债务由一种或多种实物形式的全球证券代表，这些证券由清算组织（或由作为清算组织代理人的托管人或存托人）发行并持有) 为了买方的利益，并根据禁止转让的安排，除非转让给受相同条款约束的继任清算组织，并且 (2) 基础债务的实益权益只能通过清算组织或其下属机构维护的记账系统进行转让代理人。

These bonds are considered to be in registered form if the holder may only obtain a physical certificate in bearer form when (1) the clearing organization that maintains the book-entry system goes out of business without a successor, (2) the issuer defaults, or (3) definitive securities are issued at the issuer’s request upon a change in tax law adverse to the issuer. See [Notice 2012-20](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2012-13_IRB#NOT-2012-20) and proposed regulations in [82 FR 43720](https://www.federalregister.gov/documents/2017/09/19/2017-19753/guidance-on-the-definition-of-registered-form), for more information on registered form requirements.  
如果持有人只能在以下情况下获得不记名形式的实物凭证，则这些债券被视为记名形式：(1) 维护记账系统的清算组织停业而没有继任者，(2) 发行人违约， (3) 当税法发生对发行人不利的变更时，应发行人的要求发行最终证券。请参阅[通知 2012-20](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2012-13_IRB#NOT-2012-20)和[82 FR 43720](https://www.federalregister.gov/documents/2017/09/19/2017-19753/guidance-on-the-definition-of-registered-form)中的拟议法规[](https://www.federalregister.gov/documents/2017/09/19/2017-19753/guidance-on-the-definition-of-registered-form)，了解有关注册表格要求的更多信息。

_**Foreign-targeted registered obligations.**_

A registered bond issued after March 18, 2012, and before January 1, 2016, will also be considered to be in registered form if it is targeted to foreign markets, and portfolio interest treatment may apply even when you do not receive documentation regarding the beneficial owner of the bond.

  

_**针对外国的注册义务。** _

2012 年 3 月 18 日之后、2016 年 1 月 1 日之前发行的记名债券，如果面向国外市场，也将被视为记名形式，即使您没有收到有关受益人的文件，也可能适用投资组合利息处理。债券的所有者。

If the registered obligation is not targeted to foreign markets, you must receive documentation on which you may rely to treat the payee as a foreign person that is the beneficial owner of the interest. A registered obligation is targeted to foreign markets if it is sold (or resold in connection with its original issuance) only to foreign persons or to foreign branches of U.S. financial institutions in accordance with procedures similar to those provided in Regulations section 1.163-5(c)(2)(i). However, the procedure that requires the obligation to be offered for sale (or resale) only outside the United States does not apply if the registered obligation is offered for sale through a public auction. Also, the procedure that requires the obligation to be delivered outside the United States does not apply if the obligation is considered registered because it may be transferred only through a book-entry system and the obligation is offered for sale through a public auction. The documentation needed depends on whether the interest is paid to a financial institution, a member of a clearing organization, or to some other foreign person. See Notice 2012-20 and Regulations section 1.871-14(e) for more information on foreign-targeted registered obligations.  
如果登记的义务不是针对国外市场，您必须收到文件，您可以据以将收款人视为外国人，即权益的受益所有人。如果注册债券仅按照类似于《条例》第 1.163-5(c) 条规定的程序出售（或与其原始发行相关的转售）给外国人或美国金融机构的外国分支机构，则该注册债券是针对外国市场的。 )(2)(i)。但是，如果已登记的债务是通过公开拍卖出售的，则要求该债务仅在美国境外出售（或转售）的程序不适用。此外，如果债务被视为已注册，则要求在美国境外交付债务的程序并不适用，因为它只能通过簿记系统进行转让，并且债务是通过公开拍卖进行出售的。所需文件取决于利息是否支付给金融机构、清算组织成员或其他外国人。有关针对外国的注册义务的更多信息，请参阅通知 2012-20 和条例第 1.871-14(e) 条。

_**Obligations not in registered form and obligations issued before March 19, 2012.**_

For obligations issued before March 19, 2012, interest on an obligation that is not in registered form (bearer obligation) is portfolio interest if the obligation is foreign targeted. A bearer obligation is foreign targeted if:
