_**未登记形式的债务和 2012 年 3 月 19 日之前签发的债务。** _

对于 2012 年 3 月 19 日之前发行的债务，如果该债务是针对外国的，则非记名债务（无记名债务）的利息为投资组合利息。在以下情况下，不记名债务是针对外国的：

*   There are arrangements to ensure that the obligation will be sold, or resold in connection with the original issue, only to a person who is not a U.S. person;  
    有安排确保该债券仅出售或转售给非美国人；
    
*   Interest on the obligation is payable only outside the United States and its territories; and  
    该债务的利息仅在美国及其领土之外支付；和
    
*   The face of the obligation contains a statement that any U.S. person who holds the obligation will be subject to limits under the U.S. income tax laws.  
    该义务的表面包含一项声明，即任何持有该义务的美国人都将受到美国所得税法的限制。
    

Documentation is not required for interest on bearer obligations to qualify as portfolio interest. In some cases, however, you may need documentation for purposes of Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding.  
不记名义务的利息无需提供文件即可符合投资组合利息的资格。但在某些情况下，您可能需要用于 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税的文件。

Interest on such obligations is not a withholdable payment under chapter 4, except when the instrument is materially modified after March 18, 2012.  
根据第 4 章，此类义务的利息不属于可预扣的付款，除非该工具在 2012 年 3 月 18 日之后发生重大修改。

**Interest that does not qualify as portfolio interest.**

Payments to certain persons and payments of contingent interest do not qualify as portfolio interest. You must withhold at the statutory rate on such payments unless some other exception, such as a treaty provision, applies and withholding under chapter 4 does not apply.

  

**不符合投资组合利息资格的利息。** 

向某些人支付的款项以及或有利息的支付不符合投资组合利息的资格。您必须按法定税率预扣此类款项，除非适用其他例外情况（例如条约规定）并且根据第 4 章规定的预扣税不适用。

_**Contingent interest.**_

Portfolio interest generally does not include contingent interest. Contingent interest is interest that is determined by reference to any of the following.

  

_**或有利息。** _

投资组合利息一般不包括或有利息。或有利息是指参考以下任一因素确定的利息。

*   Any receipts, sales, or other cash flow of the debtor or a related person.  
    债务人或相关人员的任何收据、销售或其他现金流量。
    
*   Income or profits of the debtor or a related person.  
    债务人或关联人的收入或利润。
    
*   Any change in value of any property of the debtor or a related person.  
    债务人或相关人员任何财产价值的任何变化。
    
*   Any dividend, partnership distributions, or similar payments made by the debtor or a related person.  
    债务人或相关人员支付的任何股息、合伙分配或类似款项。
    
*   Any amount that is a dividend equivalent.  
    任何相当于股息的金额。
    

The term “related person” is defined in section 871(h)(4)(B) .  
“相关人员”一词的定义见第 871(h)(4)(B) 条。

The contingent interest rule does not apply to any interest paid or accrued on any indebtedness with a fixed term that was issued:  
或有利息规则不适用于以下情况下发行的任何固定期限债务所支付或应计的任何利息：

*   On or before April 7, 1993; or  
    1993 年 4 月 7 日或之前；或者
    
*   After April 7, 1993, pursuant to a written binding contract in effect on that date and at all times thereafter before that indebtedness was issued.  
    1993 年 4 月 7 日之后，根据该日生效的具有约束力的书面合同以及该债务发行前的所有时间。
    

_**10% owners.**_

Interest paid to a foreign person that owns 10% or more of the total combined voting power of all classes of stock of a corporation, or 10% or more of the capital or profits interest in a partnership, that issued the obligation on which the interest is paid is not portfolio interest. To determine 10% ownership, see Regulations section 1.871-14(g).

  

_**10% 业主。** _

向持有公司所有类别股票总投票权 10% 或以上，或合伙企业资本或利润权益 10% 或以上的外国人支付的利息，该合伙企业发行了利息所依据的义务支付的不是投资组合利息。要确定 10% 所有权，请参阅法规第 1.871-14(g) 条。

_**Banks.**_

Except in the case of interest paid on an obligation of the United States, interest paid to a bank on an extension of credit made pursuant to a loan agreement entered into in the ordinary course of the bank's trade or business does not qualify as portfolio interest.

  

_**银行。** _

除为美国债务支付的利息外，根据银行正常贸易或业务过程中签订的贷款协议向银行提供信贷而支付的利息不符合投资组合利息的资格。

_**Controlled foreign corporations.**_

Interest paid to a controlled foreign corporation from a person related to the controlled foreign corporation is not portfolio interest.

  

_**受控外国公司。** _

与受控外国公司相关的人员向受控外国公司支付的利息不是投资组合利息。

**Reduced rate or exemption from chapter 3 withholding for interest on real property mortgages (Income Code 2).**

Certain treaties permit a reduced rate or exemption for interest paid or credited on real property mortgages. This is interest paid on any type of debt instrument that is secured by a mortgage or deed of trust on real property located in the United States, regardless of whether the mortgagor (or grantor) is a U.S. citizen or a U.S. business entity.

  

**降低不动产抵押贷款利息的税率或免除第 3 章预扣税（收入法 2）。** 

某些条约允许降低或免除不动产抵押贷款所支付或贷记的利息。这是对由美国不动产抵押或信托契约担保的任何类型债务工具支付的利息，无论抵押人（或授予人）是美国公民还是美国商业实体。

_**REMIC excess inclusions.**_

A domestic partnership must separately state a partner's allocable share of REMIC taxable income or net loss and the excess inclusion amount on Schedule K-1 (Form 1065). If the partnership allocates all or some part of its allocable share of REMIC taxable income to a foreign partner, the partner must include the partner's allocated amount in income as if that amount was received on the earlier of the following dates.

  

_**REMIC 过量夹杂物。** _

国内合伙企业必须在附表 K-1（表格 1065）上单独说明合伙人在 REMIC 应税收入或净亏损中的可分配份额以及超额包含金额。如果合伙企业将 REMIC 应税收入的全部或部分可分配份额分配给外国合伙人，则合伙人必须将合伙人的分配金额计入收入，就像该金额是在以下日期中较早的日期收到的一样。

1.  The date of distribution by the partnership.  
    合伙企业分配的日期。
    
2.  The date the foreign partner disposed of its indirect interest in the REMIC residual interest.  
    外国合作伙伴处置其在 REMIC 剩余权益中的间接权益的日期。
    
3.  The last day of the partnership's tax year.  
    合伙企业纳税年度的最后一天。
    

For purposes of item (2), the disposition may occur as a result of:  
就第 (2) 项而言，处置可能因以下原因而发生：

*   A termination of the REMIC,  
    REMIC 的终止，
    
*   A disposition of the partnership's residual interest in the REMIC,  
    合伙企业在 REMIC 中剩余权益的处置，
    
*   A disposition of the foreign partner's interest in the partnership, or  
    外国合伙人在合伙企业中的权益的处置，或
    
*   Any other reduction in the foreign partner's allocable share of the partnership's part of the REMIC net income or deduction.  
    REMIC 净收入中外国合伙人在合伙企业中的可分配份额的任何其他减少或扣除。
    

The partnership must withhold tax on the part of the REMIC amount that is an excess inclusion. Excess inclusion income is treated as income from sources in the United States and is not eligible for any reduction in withholding tax (by treaty or otherwise). It is also a withholdable payment for chapter 4 purposes.  
合伙企业必须对 REMIC 金额中超额包含的部分预扣税款。超额纳入收入被视为来自美国的收入，并且没有资格获得任何预扣税减免（通过条约或其他方式）。这也是用于第 4 章目的的预扣付款。

An excess inclusion allocated to the following foreign persons must be included in that person's income at the same time as other income from the entity is included in income.  
分配给以下外国人的超额收入必须与该实体的其他收入同时计入该人的收入。

*   Shareholder of a real estate investment trust (REIT).  
    房地产投资信托基金（REIT）的股东。
    
*   Shareholder of a regulated investment company (RIC).  
    受监管投资公司 (RIC) 的股东。
    
*   Participant in a common trust fund.  
    共同信托基金的参与者。
    
*   Patron of a subchapter T cooperative organization.  
    T 分会合作组织的赞助人。
    

The entity must withhold on the excess inclusion.  
该实体必须对超额包含部分进行扣缴。

For information on the taxation and reporting of excess inclusion income by REITs, RICs, and other pass-through entities, see Notice 2006-97, 2006-46 I.R.B. 904, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2006-46\_IRB#NOT-2006-97](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2006-46_IRB#NOT-2006-97).  
有关 REIT、RIC 和其他传递实体的超额包容性收入征税和报告的信息，请参阅通知 2006-97、2006-46 IRB 904，网址为[IRS.gov/irb/2006-46\_IRB#NOT-2006 -97](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2006-46_IRB#NOT-2006-97) 。

**Reduced rate or exemption from chapter 3 withholding for interest paid to controlling foreign corporations (Income Code 3).**

A treaty may permit a reduced rate or exemption for interest paid by a domestic corporation to a controlling foreign corporation. The interest may be on any type of debt, including open or unsecured accounts payable, notes, certificates, bonds, or other evidences of indebtedness.

  

**降低向控股外国公司支付的利息的税率或免除第 3 章预扣税（收入法 3）。** 

条约可以允许国内公司向控股外国公司支付利息的利率降低或豁免。利息可以是任何类型的债务，包括未清或无担保的应付账款、票据、证书、债券或其他债务证据。

**Reduced rate or exemption from chapter 3 withholding for interest paid by foreign corporations (Income Code 4).**

If a foreign corporation is engaged in a U.S. trade or business, any interest paid by the foreign corporation's trade or business in the United States (branch interest) is subject to chapter 3 withholding as if paid by a domestic corporation (without considering the “payer having income from abroad” exception) and is a withholdable payment. As a result, the interest paid to foreign payees is generally subject to chapter 3 withholding and withholding may apply under chapter 4 absent an applicable withholding exception. In addition, if “allocable interest” exceeds the branch interest paid, the excess interest is also subject to tax and reported on the foreign corporation's income tax return, Form 1120-F. See the [Instructions for Form 1120-F](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-1120-f) for more information.

  

**降低外国公司支付利息的税率或免除第 3 章预扣税（《收入法》第 4 章）。** 

如果外国公司从事美国贸易或业务，则该外国公司在美国的贸易或业务所支付的任何利息（分行利息）均须缴纳第 3 章预扣税，如同由国内公司支付一样（不考虑“付款人”）有来自国外的收入”例外）并且是一项可预扣的付款。因此，支付给外国收款人的利息通常须遵守第 3 章规定的预扣税，并且在没有适用的预扣税例外情况的情况下，可根据第 4 章适用预扣税。此外，如果“可分配利息”超过分行支付的利息，超出部分的利息也需要纳税，并报告在外国公司的所得税申报表（表格 1120-F）中。有关更多信息，请参阅表格 1120-F 的说明。

If there is no treaty provision that reduces the rate of withholding on branch interest, you must withhold tax under chapter 3 at the statutory rate of 30% on the interest paid by a foreign corporation's U.S. trade or business and you must withhold under chapter 4 when otherwise applicable and without regard to a treaty provision.  
如果没有降低分支机构利息预扣税率的条约规定，则您必须根据第 3 章的规定，按照 30% 的法定税率，对外国公司在美国的贸易或业务所支付的利息进行预扣税，并且在下列情况下，您必须根据第 4 章的规定进行预扣税：其他适用且不考虑条约规定的情况。

In general, payees of interest from a U.S. trade or business of a foreign corporation are entitled to reduced rates of, or exemption from, tax under a treaty in the same manner and subject to the same conditions as if they had received the interest from a domestic corporation. However, a foreign corporation that receives interest paid by a U.S. trade or business of a foreign corporation must also be a qualified resident of its country of residence to be entitled to benefits under that country's tax treaty. If the payee foreign corporation is a resident of a country that has entered into an income tax treaty since 1987 that contains a limitation on benefits article, the foreign corporation need only satisfy the limitation on benefits article in that treaty to qualify for a reduced rate of tax.  
一般来说，来自外国公司的美国贸易或业务的利息收款人有权根据条约享受减税或免税，其方式和条件与从外国公司收到利息的方式和条件相同。国内法人。然而，接收外国公司在美国的贸易或业务支付的利息的外国公司也必须是其居住国的合格居民，才有资格享受该国税收协定规定的福利。如果收款人外国公司是自 1987 年以来已签订包含福利限制条款的所得税条约的国家的居民，则该外国公司只需满足该条约中的福利限制条款就有资格享受降低税率税。

Alternatively, a payee may be entitled to treaty benefits under the payer's treaty if there is a provision in that treaty that applies specifically to interest paid by the payer foreign corporation. This provision may exempt all or a part of this interest. Some treaties provide for an exemption regardless of the payee's residence or citizenship, while others provide for an exemption according to the payee's status as a resident or citizen of the payer's country.  
或者，如果付款人条约中有专门适用于付款人外国公司支付的利息的规定，则收款人可能有权根据付款人条约享受税收协定优惠。该规定可以免除全部或部分该利息。一些条约规定豁免，无论收款人的居住地或公民身份如何，而另一些条约则根据收款人作为付款人所在国的居民或公民的身份规定豁免。

A foreign corporation that pays interest must be a qualified resident (under section 884) of its country of residence for the payer's treaty to exempt payments from tax by the foreign corporation. However, if the foreign corporation is a resident of a country that has entered into an income tax treaty since 1987 that contains a limitation on benefits article, the foreign corporation need only satisfy the limitation on benefits article in that treaty to qualify for the exemption.  
支付利息的外国公司必须是其居住国的合格居民（根据第 884 条），才能根据付款人条约免除外国公司付款的税款。然而，如果外国公司是自1987年以来签订的所得税条约包含福利限制条款的国家的居民，则外国公司只需满足该条约中的福利限制条款就有资格获得免税。

**Interest on deposits (Income Code 29).**

Foreign persons are not subject to chapter 3 withholding on interest that is not connected with a U.S. trade or business if it is from:

  

**存款利息（收入代码 29）。** 

与美国贸易或业务无关的外国人利息如果来自以下情况，则不受第 3 章规定的预扣税：

*   Deposits with persons carrying on the banking business;  
    从事银行业务的人员的存款；
    
*   Deposits or withdrawable accounts with savings institutions chartered and supervised under federal or state law as savings and loan or similar associations, such as credit unions, if the interest is or would be deductible by the institutions; or  
    根据联邦或州法律特许并受联邦或州法律监管的储蓄机构或类似协会（例如信用合作社）的存款或提款账户，如果机构可扣除利息；或者
    
*   Amounts left with an insurance company under an agreement to pay interest on them.  
    根据协议留在保险公司以支付利息的金额。
    

Deposits include certificates of deposit, open account time deposits, Eurodollar certificates of deposit, and other deposit arrangements.

You may have to file Form 1042-S to report certain payments of interest on deposits. See [_Deposit interest paid to certain nonresident alien individuals_](#en_US_2024_publink1000293394 "Deposit interest paid to certain nonresident alien individuals.") under _Returns Required_, later. You may also have to file Form 1042-S when the deposit interest is a withholdable payment to which withholding applies (or was applied) to chapter 4.

  

存款包括存款证、开户定期存款、欧洲美元存款证和其他存款安排。

您可能需要提交 1042-S 表格来报告某些存款利息支付情况。请参阅稍后在_“要求回报”_下[_向某些非居民外籍个人支付的存款利息_](#en_US_2024_publink1000293394 "Deposit interest paid to certain nonresident alien individuals.")。当存款利息是适用（或已适用）第 4 章规定的预扣税款时，您可能还需要提交 1042-S 表格。

**Obligations issued before August 10, 2010.**

Interest received from a resident alien individual or a domestic corporation is not subject to chapter 3 withholding and is not a withholdable payment if the interest meets all of the following requirements.

  

**2010 年 8 月 10 日之前发出的义务。** 

从外国居民个人或国内公司收到的利息不受第 3 章预扣税的约束，如果利息满足以下所有要求，则该利息不属于可预扣税款。

*   At least 80% of the payer’s gross income from all sources has been from active foreign business for the 3 tax years of the payer before the year in which the interest is paid, or for the applicable part of those 3 years.  
    在支付利息之前的 3 个纳税年度中，或在这 3 年的适用部分中，付款人所有来源的总收入的至少 80% 来自活跃的外国业务。
    
*   The recipient is not a related person. Use rules similar to those in section 954(d)(3) to determine if the recipient is a related person.  
    收件人不是关联人。使用类似于第 954(d)(3) 条中的规则来确定接收者是否为相关人员。
    
*   The interest is paid on an obligation issued before August 10, 2010.  
    利息是针对 2010 年 8 月 10 日之前发行的债务支付的。
    
*   The obligation has not been significantly modified since August 10, 2010.  
    自 2010 年 8 月 10 日起，该义务未发生重大修改。
    

_**Interest from foreign business arrangements.**_

In certain cases, interest received from a domestic payer, most of whose gross income is active foreign business income, is not subject to chapter 3 withholding and is not a withholdable payment.

  

_**来自外国商业安排的利息。** _

在某些情况下，从国内付款人收到的利息（其大部分总收入是活跃的海外业务收入）不受第 3 章预扣税的约束，也不属于应预扣付款。

Active foreign business income is gross income which is:  
活跃国外业务收入是总收入，即：

*   Derived from sources outside the United States, and  
    来自美国以外的来源，并且
    
*   Attributable to the active conduct of a trade or business in a foreign country or territory of the United States by the domestic payer.  
    归因于国内付款人在外国或美国领土上积极开展的贸易或业务。
    

**Corporations existing on January 1, 2011.**

Certain interest received from a domestic corporation that is an existing 80/20 company is not subject to withholding. An existing 80/20 company must meet all of the following requirements.

  

**2011 年 1 月 1 日成立的公司。** 

从现有 80/20 公司的国内公司收到的某些利息无需预扣税款。现有 80/20 公司必须满足以下所有要求。

*   It was in existence on January 1, 2011.  
    它于 2011 年 1 月 1 日存在。
    
*   For the 3 tax years beginning before January 1, 2011 (or for its years of existence if the corporation was in existence for less than 3 tax years), at least 80% of its gross income from all sources was active foreign business income.  
    在 2011 年 1 月 1 日之前开始的 3 个纳税年度（或者如果公司成立时间少于 3 个纳税年度，则为其存在年份），其所有来源的总收入中至少 80% 是活跃的国外业务收入。
    
*   It continues to meet the 80% test for every tax year beginning after December 31, 2010.  
    它继续满足 2010 年 12 月 31 日之后开始的每个纳税年度的 80% 测试。
    
*   It has not added a substantial line of business after August 10, 2010.  
    2010年8月10日之后，它没有增加实质性的业务范围。
    

**Transitional rule for active foreign business income.**

In most cases, the domestic corporation determines its active foreign business income by combining its income and the income of any subsidiary in which it owns, directly or indirectly, 50% or more of the stock. However, if the testing period includes 1 or more tax years beginning before January 1, 2011, the corporation can use only its gross income for any tax year beginning before January 1, 2011, and will meet the 80% test if the weighted average percentage of active foreign business income is more than 80%.

  

**积极外国业务收入的过渡规则。** 

在大多数情况下，国内公司通过将其收入与其直接或间接拥有 50% 或以上股份的任何子公司的收入相结合来确定其活跃的国外业务收入。但是，如果测试期包括 2011 年 1 月 1 日之前开始的 1 个或多个纳税年度，则公司只能使用 2011 年 1 月 1 日之前开始的任何纳税年度的总收入，并且如果加权平均百分比对外营业收入占比超过80%。

A foreign beneficial owner does not need to provide a Form W-8 or documentary evidence for this exception. However, documentation may be required for purposes of Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding.  
外国受益所有人无需为此例外提供 W-8 表格或文件证据。但是，出于 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税的目的，可能需要提供文件。

**Sales of bonds between interest dates.**

Amounts paid as part of the purchase price of an obligation sold or exchanged between interest payment dates is not subject to chapter 3 withholding. In addition, such a payment is not a withholdable payment. This does not apply if the sale or exchange is part of a plan the principal purpose of which is to avoid tax and you have actual knowledge or reason to know of the plan. The exemption from chapter 3 withholding and from withholdable payments applies even if you do not have any documentation from the payee. However, documentation may be required for purposes of Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding.

  

**在利息日期之间出售债券。** 

作为在利息支付日期之间出售或交换的债务的购买价格的一部分而支付的金额不受第 3 章预扣税的约束。此外，此类付款不是可预扣的付款。如果销售或交换是主要目的是避税的计划的一部分，并且您实际了解或有理由了解该计划，则此规定不适用。即使您没有收款人提供的任何文件，第 3 章预扣税和可预扣付款的豁免也适用。但是，出于 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税的目的，可能需要提供文件。

**Short-term obligations.**

Interest and original issue discount paid on an obligation that is payable 183 days or less from the date of its original issue (without regard to the period held by the taxpayer) that satisfy other requirements intended to ensure that the debt is not held by a U.S. nonexempt person are not subject to chapter 3 withholding. In addition, such a payment is not a withholdable payment. These exemptions apply even if you do not have any documentation from the payee. However, documentation may be required for purposes of Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding.

  

**短期义务。** 

对自原始发行之日起 183 天或更短时间内应付的债务（不考虑纳税人持有的期限）支付的利息和原始发行折扣，满足旨在确保该债务不是由美国持有的其他要求非豁免人士不受第 3 章规定的预扣税。此外，此类付款不是可预扣的付款。即使您没有收款人提供的任何文件，这些豁免也适用。但是，出于 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税的目的，可能需要提供文件。

**Income from U.S. Savings Bonds of residents of the Ryukyu Islands or the Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands.**

Interest from a Series E, Series EE, Series H, or Series HH U.S. Savings Bond is not subject to chapter 3 withholding if the nonresident alien individual acquired the bond while a resident of the Ryukyu Islands or the Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands.

  

**琉球群岛或太平洋岛屿托管领土居民的美国储蓄债券收入。** 

如果非居民外籍个人在琉球群岛或太平洋岛屿托管领土居民期间购买债券，则 E 系列、EE 系列、H 系列或 HH 系列美国储蓄债券的利息不受第 3 章预扣税的约束。

#### Dividends股息

The following types of dividends paid to foreign payees are generally subject to chapter 3 withholding and are generally withholdable payments such that withholding chapter 4 applies absent an exception available under chapter 4.  
支付给外国收款人的以下类型的股息通常需要缴纳第 3 章的预扣税，并且一般属于可预扣税款，因此，在没有第 4 章规定的例外情况的情况下，第 4 章的预扣税适用。

**Dividends paid by U.S. corporations—general (Income Code 6).**

This category includes all distributions of domestic corporations (other than dividends qualifying for direct dividend rate—Income Code 7).

  

**美国公司支付的股息——一般（收入代码 6）。** 

此类别包括国内公司的所有分配（符合直接股息率 - 收入代码 7 的股息除外）。

A corporation making a distribution with respect to its stock, or any intermediary making a payment of such a distribution, is required to withhold on the entire amount of the distribution at the rate applicable under chapter 3 when withholding under chapter 4 does not apply. However, a distributing corporation or intermediary may elect to not withhold on the part of the distribution that:  
如果根据第 4 章规定的预扣税不适用，则对其股票进行分配的公司或支付此类分配的任何中介机构必须按照第 3 章适用的税率预扣分配的全部金额。然而，分销公司或中介机构可以选择不对以下分销部分进行预扣：

1.  Represents a nontaxable distribution payable in stock or stock rights;  
    代表以股票或股权形式应付的免税分配；
    
2.  Represents a distribution in part or full payment in exchange for stock;  
    代表以部分或全部付款换取股票的分配；
    
3.  Is not paid out of current or accumulated earnings and profits, based on a reasonable estimate of the anticipated amount of earnings and profits for the tax year of the distribution made at a time reasonably close to the date of the distribution;  
    根据在合理接近分配日期的时间对分配纳税年度的预期收入和利润金额进行的合理估计，不从当前或累计收入和利润中支付；
    
4.  Represents a capital gain dividend (use Income Code 36) or an exempt interest dividend by a RIC; or  
    代表 RIC 的资本利得股息（使用收入代码 36）或豁免利息股息；或者
    
5.  Is subject to withholding under section 1445 (withholding of tax on dispositions of USRPIs) and the distributing corporation is a U.S. real property holding corporation or a qualified investment entity (QIE).  
    根据第 1445 条（USRPI 处置预扣税）须缴纳预扣税，且分配公司是美国房地产控股公司或合格投资实体 (QIE)。
    

The election is made by actually reducing the amount of withholding at the time the distribution is paid.  
该选择是通过在支付分配时实际减少预扣税额来进行的。

_**Dividends paid by a QIE (Income Code 24).**_

A QIE is:

  

_**由 QIE 支付的股息（收入代码 24）。** _

QIE 是：

1.  Any REIT, or任何房地产投资信托基金，或
    
2.  Any RIC that is a U.S. real property holding corporation.  
    任何美国房地产控股公司 RIC。
    

A distribution by a QIE to a nonresident alien or a foreign corporation is treated as a dividend and is not subject to withholding under section 1445 as a gain from the sale or exchange of a USRPI if:  
QIE 向非居民外国人或外国公司的分配被视为股息，并且无需根据第 1445 条作为 USRPI 销售或交换收益进行预扣，如果：

*   The distribution is on stock regularly traded on a securities market in the United States, and  
    分配对象是在美国证券市场上定期交易的股票，并且
    
*   The individual or corporation did not own more than 10% of such stock in the case of a REIT or 5% of such stock in the case of a RIC at any time during the 1-year period ending on the date of distribution.  
    在截至分配之日的 1 年期间内的任何时间，个人或公司持有的 REIT 股票不得超过 10%，RIC 的持有不得超过 5%。
    

Certain distributions by a REIT may be treated as a dividend and are not subject to withholding under section 1445 as a gain from the sale or exchange of a USRPI. See [_Qualified investment entities (QIEs)_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225101 "Qualified investment entities (QIEs).") under _U.S. Real Property Interest_, later.  
REIT 的某些分配可被视为股息，并且无需根据第 1445 条作为出售或交换 USRPI 的收益进行预扣。请参阅稍后_美国不动产权益_下的[_合格投资实体 (QIE)_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225101 "Qualified investment entities (QIEs).") 。

_**Dividends paid by a domestic corporation (an existing “80/20” company).**_

The active foreign business percentage of any dividend paid by a domestic corporation that is an existing 80/20 company is not subject to withholding. A domestic corporation is an existing 80/20 company if it satisfies all of the following.

  

_**由国内公司（现有的“80/20”公司）支付的股息。** _

现有 80/20 公司的国内公司所支付的任何股息中活跃的外国业务百分比无需预扣税款。如果满足以下所有条件，国内公司就是现有的 80/20 公司。

1.  It was in existence on January 1, 2011.  
    它于 2011 年 1 月 1 日存在。
    
2.  For the 3 tax years beginning before January 1, 2011 (or for all years of existence if it was in existence for less than 3 tax years), at least 80% of its gross income from all sources was active foreign business income. Active foreign business income is gross income that is:  
    在 2011 年 1 月 1 日之前开始的 3 个纳税年度（或者如果存在时间少于 3 个纳税年度，则为所有存在年份），其所有来源的总收入中至少 80% 是活跃的外国业务收入。活跃国外业务收入是指总收入：
    
    1.  Derived from sources outside the United States, and  
        来自美国以外的来源，并且
        
    2.  Attributable to the active conduct of a trade or business in a foreign country or territory of the United States by the corporation.  
        归因于公司在外国或美国领土上积极开展的贸易或业务。
        
    
3.  It continues to meet the 80% test for every tax year beginning after December 31, 2010.  
    它继续满足 2010 年 12 月 31 日之后开始的每个纳税年度的 80% 测试。
    
4.  It has not added a substantial line of business after August 10, 2010.  
    2010年8月10日之后，它没有增加实质性的业务范围。
    

_**Transitional rule for item (2).**_

In most cases, the domestic corporation determines its active foreign business income by combining its income and the income of any subsidiary in which it owns, directly or indirectly, 50% or more of the stock. However, if the testing period includes 1 or more tax years beginning before January 1, 2011, the corporation can use only its gross income for any tax year beginning before January 1, 2011, and will meet the 80% test if the weighted average percentage of active foreign business income is more than 80%.

  

_**第（2）项的过渡规则。** _

在大多数情况下，国内公司通过将其收入与其直接或间接拥有 50% 或以上股份的任何子公司的收入相结合来确定其活跃的国外业务收入。但是，如果测试期包括 2011 年 1 月 1 日之前开始的 1 个或多个纳税年度，则公司只能使用 2011 年 1 月 1 日之前开始的任何纳税年度的总收入，并且如果加权平均百分比对外营业收入占比超过80%。

The active foreign business percentage is found by dividing the corporation’s active foreign business income for the testing period by the corporation’s total gross income for that period. The testing period is the 3 tax years before the year in which the dividends are declared (or shorter period if the corporation was not in existence for 3 years). If the corporation has no gross income for that 3-year period, the testing period is the tax year in which the dividend is paid.  
活跃国外业务百分比是通过将测试期间公司的活跃国外业务收入除以该期间公司的总收入得出的。测试期为宣布股息当年之前的 3 个纳税年度（如果公司不存在 3 年，则测试期较短）。如果公司在该 3 年期间没有总收入，则测试期为支付股息的纳税年度。

_**Consent dividends.**_

If you receive a Form 972, Consent of Shareholder To Include Specific Amount in Gross Income, from a nonresident alien individual or other foreign shareholder who agrees to treat the amount as a taxable dividend, you must pay and report on Form 1042 and Form 1042-S any withholding tax you would have withheld if the dividend actually had been paid.

  

_**同意股息。** _

如果您收到同意将该金额视为应税股息的非居民外籍个人或其他外国股东的 972 表格《股东同意将特定金额计入总收入》，您必须支付并在 1042 表格和 1042 表格上报告如果实际支付了股息，您应扣缴的任何预扣税。

**Interest-related dividends and short-term capital gain dividends received from mutual funds.**

Certain interest-related dividends and short-term capital gain dividends paid by a mutual fund or other RIC are exempt from chapter 3 withholding.

  

**从共同基金收到的与利息相关的股息和短期资本利得股息。** 

由共同基金或其他 RIC 支付的某些与利息相关的股息和短期资本利得股息可免除第 3 章预扣税。

**Dividends qualifying for direct dividend rate (Income Code 7).**

A treaty may reduce the rate of withholding on dividends from that which generally applies under the treaty if the shareholder owns a certain percentage of the voting stock of the corporation when withholding under chapter 4 does not apply. In most cases, this preferential rate applies only if the shareholder directly owns the required percentage, although some treaties permit the percentage to be met by direct or indirect ownership. The preferential rate may apply to the payment of a deemed dividend under section 304(a)(1). Under some treaties, the preferential rate for dividends qualifying for the direct dividend rate applies only if no more than a certain percentage of the paying corporation's gross income for a certain period consists of dividends and interest other than dividends and interest from subsidiaries or from the active conduct of a banking, financing, or insurance business. A foreign person should claim the direct dividend rate by filing the appropriate Form W-8.

  

**符合直接股息率资格的股息（收入代码 7）。** 

如果股东拥有公司一定比例的有投票权的股票，而第 4 章规定的预扣税不适用，则条约可以降低根据条约一般适用的股息预扣税率。在大多数情况下，只有当股东直接拥有所需的百分比时，此优惠税率才适用，尽管有些条约允许通过直接或间接所有权来满足该百分比。优惠利率可适用于根据第 304(a)(1) 条支付视同股息。根据某些条约，符合直接股息率资格的股息优惠利率仅适用于支付公司在一定时期内的总收入中不超过一定比例的股息和利息（子公司或活跃企业的股息和利息除外）的情况。银行、金融或保险业务的开展。外国人应通过提交适当的 W-8 表格来申请直接股息率。

_**Consent dividends.**_

If you receive a Form 972 from a foreign shareholder qualifying for the direct dividend rate, you must pay and report on Form 1042 and Form 1042-S any withholding tax you would have withheld if the dividend actually had been paid.

  

_**同意股息。** _

如果您收到符合直接股息率资格的外国股东发来的 972 表格，您必须支付并在 1042 表格和 1042-S 表格上报告您在实际支付股息时应预扣的任何预扣税。

**Dividends paid by foreign corporations (Income Code 8).**

Dividends paid by a foreign corporation generally are not subject to chapter 3 withholding and are not withholdable payments. This exception does not require a Form W-8. However, a Form W-8 may be required for purposes of Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding.

  

**外国公司支付的股息（收入代码 8）。** 

外国公司支付的股息通常不受第 3 章预扣税的约束，也不属于应预扣税款。此例外情况不需要 W-8 表。但是，出于 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税的目的，可能需要提供 W-8 表格。

The payment to a foreign corporation by a foreign corporation of a deemed dividend under section 304(a)(1) is subject to chapter 3 withholding and may be a withholdable payment except to the extent it can be clearly determined to be from foreign sources.  
外国公司根据第 304(a)(1) 条向外国公司支付的视同股息须缴纳第 3 章预扣税，并且可以是应预扣税，除非可以明确确定其来自外国来源。

_**Corporation subject to branch profits tax.**_

If a foreign corporation is subject to branch profits tax for any tax year, withholding is not required on any dividends paid by the corporation out of its earnings and profits for that tax year. Dividends may be subject to withholding if they are attributable to any earnings and profits when the branch profits tax is prohibited by a tax treaty.

  

_**公司须缴纳分公司利得税。** _

如果外国公司在任何纳税年度需缴纳分公司利润税，则该公司从该纳税年度的收入和利润中支付的任何股息无需预扣税款。如果税收协定禁止征收分公司利润税，则如果股息可归因于任何收入和利润，则可能需要缴纳预扣税。

A foreign person may claim a treaty benefit on dividends paid by a foreign corporation to the extent the dividends are paid out of earnings and profits in a year in which the foreign corporation was not subject to the branch profits tax. However, you may apply a reduced rate of withholding under an income tax treaty only under rules similar to the rules that apply to treaty benefits claimed on branch interest paid by a foreign corporation. You should check the specific treaty provision.  
外国人可以就外国公司支付的股息申请税收协定优惠，只要该股息是从该外国公司免征分公司利润税的当年的收入和利润中支付的。但是，您只能按照与适用于外国公司支付的分支机构利息主张的税收协定优惠的规则相似的规则，根据所得税协定应用降低的预扣税率。您应该检查具体的条约规定。

**Dividends paid to Puerto Rican corporation.**

For chapter 3 purposes, the tax rate on dividends paid to a corporation created or organized in, or under the law of, the Commonwealth of Puerto Rico is 10%, rather than 30%, if:

  

**支付给波多黎各公司的股息。** 

就第 3 章而言，支付给在波多黎各联邦境内或根据波多黎各联邦法律创建或组织的公司的股息税率为 10%，而不是 30%，如果：

*   At all times during the tax year less than 25% in value of the Puerto Rican corporation's stock is owned, directly or indirectly, by foreign persons;  
    在纳税年度的任何时候，外国人直接或间接拥有波多黎各公司股票价值的 25% 以下；
    
*   At least 65% of the Puerto Rican corporation's gross income is effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business in Puerto Rico or the United States for the 3-year period ending with the close of the tax year of that corporation (or the period the corporation or any predecessor has been in existence, if less); and  
    波多黎各公司至少 65% 的总收入与在该公司纳税年度结束的 3 年期间（或该期间）在波多黎各或美国进行的贸易或业务有效相关。该公司或任何前身已经存在（如果较少）；和
    
*   No substantial part of the income of the Puerto Rican corporation is used, directly or indirectly, to satisfy obligations to a person who is not a bona fide resident of Puerto Rico or the United States.  
    波多黎各公司的大部分收入均不会直接或间接用于履行对非波多黎各或美国真正居民的义务。
    

No special rules apply to Puerto Rican corporations for chapter 4 purposes, but special withholding rules do apply for withholdable payments made to territory financial institutions and nonfinancial entities. See the chapter 4 regulations for information on these special requirements.  
就第 4 章而言，没有适用于波多黎各公司的特殊规则，但特殊预扣税规则确实适用于向领土金融机构和非金融实体支付的预扣税款。有关这些特殊要求的信息，请参阅第 4 章规定。

#### Dividend Equivalents股息等值

**Dividend equivalent payments.**

Dividend equivalent payments are treated as U.S. source dividends such that withholding under chapter 3 may apply. Use Income Code 34 or 40 to report dividend equivalent payments. Dividend equivalent payments are withholdable payments except when an exception applies for chapter 4 purposes.

  

**股息等值支付。** 

等值股息支付被视为美国来源股息，因此可能适用第 3 章规定的预扣税。使用收入代码 34 或 40 报告等值股息支付。股息等值付款是可预扣的付款，除非出于第 4 章的目的适用例外情况。

A dividend equivalent is a payment (as defined in Regulations section 1.871-15(c)) that, directly or indirectly, is contingent on, or determined by reference to, the payment of a dividend from U.S. sources. Dividend equivalent payments include the following payments.  
等值股息是指直接或间接取决于美国来源的股息支付或参考美国来源的股息支付而确定的支付（定义见《条例》第 1.871-15(c) 条）。等价股息支付包括以下支付。

1.  A substitute dividend made under a securities lending or sale-repurchase transaction involving a U.S. stock.  
    涉及美国股票的证券借贷或买卖回购交易中发放的替代股息。
    
2.  A payment that references the payment of a dividend from an underlying security made under a specified notional principal contract.  
    指根据特定名义主合同支付基础证券股息的付款。
    
3.  A payment that references the payment of a dividend from an underlying security made to a specified equity-linked instrument.  
    指从基础证券向特定股票挂钩工具支付的股息的付款。
    

_**Substitute dividend (Income Code 34).**_

A substitute dividend is any payment made under a securities lending or sale-repurchase transaction that (directly or indirectly) is contingent upon, or determined by reference to, the payment of a dividend from sources in the United States.

  

_**替代股息（收入代码 34）。** _

替代股息是指在证券借贷或销售回购交易中（直接或间接）根据美国来源的股息支付而支付的任何款项，或参考美国来源的股息支付而确定的任何支付。

_**Specified notional principal contracts (SNPCs) and specified equity-linked instruments (SELIs) (Income Code 40).**_

Transactions entered into on or after January 1, 2017.

  

_**特定名义主合同 (SNPC) 和特定股票挂钩工具 (SELI)（收入代码 40）。** _

2017 年 1 月 1 日或之后进行的交易。

For transactions entered into on or after January 1, 2017 (including as a result of a deemed exchange pursuant to section 1001), an SNPC or SELI is a notional principal contract (NPC), or equity linked instrument, respectively, with a delta of 0.8 or greater if it is a simple contract under Regulations section 1.871-15(a)(14)(i), or it meets the substantial equivalence test if it is a complex contract under Regulations section 1.871-15(a)(14)(ii). See Regulations section 1.871-15(g) for the delta test and Regulations section 1.871-15(h) for the substantial equivalence test.  
对于 2017 年 1 月 1 日或之后签订的交易（包括根据第 1001 条视为交换的结果），SNPC 或 SELI 分别是名义主合同 (NPC) 或股票挂钩工具，其 delta 为如果是《条例》第 1.871-15(a)(14)(i) 条下的简单合同，则为 0.8 或更高，或者如果是《条例》第 1.871-15(a)(14) 条下的复杂合同，则满足实质性等同测试(二).有关增量测试，请参阅法规第 1.871-15(g) 条；有关实质性等同测试，请参阅法规第 1.871-15(h) 条。

Notwithstanding the preceding paragraph, for transactions entered into prior to January 1, 2025, transition relief provides that, subject to an anti-abuse rule, only delta-one transactions will be treated as SNPCs and SELIs. See Notice 2022-37, 2022-37 I.R.B. 234, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2022-37\_IRB#NOT-2022-37](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2022-37_IRB#NOT-2022-37).  
尽管有前一段规定，对于 2025 年 1 月 1 日之前达成的交易，过渡救济规定，根据反滥用规则，只有 delta-1 交易才会被视为 SNPC 和 SELI。请参阅通知 2022-37、2022-37 IRB 234，可在[IRS.gov/irb/2022-37\_IRB#NOT-2022-37](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2022-37_IRB#NOT-2022-37)上获取。

NPCs entered into before January 1, 2017.  
NPC 于 2017 年 1 月 1 日之前加入。

For transactions entered into before January 1, 2017, an SNPC is any NPC if:  
对于 2017 年 1 月 1 日之前签订的交易，如果满足以下条件，则 SNPC 是任何 NPC：

*   In connection with entering into the contract, any long party to the contract transfers the underlying security to any short party to the contract;  
    在签订合同时，合同的任何多头方将标的证券转让给合同的任何空头方；
    
*   In connection with the termination of the contract, any short party to the contract transfers the underlying security to any long party to the contract;  
    随着合同的终止，合同的任何空头方将标的证券转让给合同的任何多头方；
    
*   The underlying security is not readily tradeable on an established securities market; or  
    标的证券不易在成熟的证券市场上交易；或者
    
*   In connection with entering into the contract, the underlying security is posted as collateral by any short party to the contract with any long party to the contract.  
    在签订合同时，合同的任何空头方与合同的任何多头方将标的证券作为抵押品。
    

For more information regarding dividend equivalents, see Regulations section 1.871-15 and Notice 2022-37.  
有关股息等价物的更多信息，请参阅法规第 1.871-15 条和通知 2022-37。

_**Amounts paid to qualified securities lenders (QSLs).**_

A withholding agent that makes substitute dividend payments to a QSL may apply the transition rules described in Notice 2010-46, Part III, for payments made before January 1, 2025. See Notice 2022-37.

  

_**支付给合格证券出借人 (QSL) 的金额。** _

对于 2025 年 1 月 1 日之前支付的股息，向 QSL 支付替代股息的扣缴义务人可以适用 2010-46 号公告第三部分中所述的过渡规则。参见 2022-37 号公告。

_**Amounts paid to QDDs.**_

Only an eligible entity that has entered into a QI agreement can be a QDD. An eligible entity is a home office or branch that is a QI and that is:

  

_**支付给 QDD 的金额。** _

只有签订了 QI 协议的合格实体才能成为 QDD。符合资格的实体是属于 QI 的总部或分支机构，并且：

1.  A dealer in equity derivatives that is subject to regulatory supervision as a dealer by a governmental authority in the jurisdiction in which it was organized or operates;  
    股票衍生品交易商，作为交易商受到其组织或经营所在地的政府机构的监管；
    
2.  A bank or bank holding company that is subject to regulatory supervision as a bank or bank holding company (as applicable) by a governmental authority in the jurisdiction in which it was organized or operates;  
    银行或银行控股公司作为银行或银行控股公司（如适用）受到其组织或经营所在地的政府机构的监管；
    
3.  An entity that is wholly owned (directly or indirectly) by a bank or bank holding company subject to regulatory supervision as a bank or bank holding company (as applicable) by a governmental authority in the jurisdiction in which the bank or bank holding company (as applicable) was organized or operates and that entity, in its capacity as a dealer in equity derivatives:  
    由银行或银行控股公司（如适用）全资拥有（直接或间接）的实体，受银行或银行控股公司（如适用）所在司法管辖区的政府机构的监管。适用）的组织或经营，并且该实体以股票衍生品交易商的身份：
    
    1.  Issues potential section 871(m) transactions to customers; and  
        向客户发出潜在的第 871(m) 条交易；和
        
    2.  Receives dividends with respect to stock or dividend equivalent payments pursuant to potential section 871(m) transactions that hedge potential section 871(m) transactions that it issued;  
        根据对冲其发行的潜在第 871(m) 条交易的潜在第 871(m) 条交易，接收与股票或股息等价物支付相关的股息；
        
    
4.  A foreign branch of a U.S. financial institution if the foreign branch would be described in (1), (2), or (3) had it been a separate entity; or  
    美国金融机构的外国分支机构，如果该外国分支机构是独立实体，则符合 (1)、(2) 或 (3) 中的描述；或者
    
5.  Any person otherwise acceptable to the IRS.  
    IRS 可接受的任何人。
    

A QDD is liable for tax under section 881 on its section 871(m) amount for each dividend on each underlying security. The section 871(m) amount is described in Regulations section 1.871-15(q)(3).  
QDD 须根据第 881 条对其每份基础证券的每笔股息的第 871(m) 条金额纳税。第 871(m) 条金额在条例第 1.871-15(q)(3) 条中进行了描述。

For more information on amounts paid to QDDs, see the chapter 3 regulations issued with the section 871(m) regulations. You can view the regulations at [IRS.gov/irb/2017-09\_IRB#TD-9815](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-09_IRB#TD-9815).  
有关支付给 QDD 的金额的更多信息，请参阅与第 871(m) 条法规一起发布的第 3 章法规。您可以在[IRS.gov/irb/2017-09\_IRB#TD-9815](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2017-09_IRB#TD-9815)查看法规。

#### Gains收益

You generally do not need to withhold under chapter 3 or 4 on any gain from the sale of real or personal property because it is not FDAP income. However, see [_U.S. Real Property Interest_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest"), later.  
您通常不需要根据第 3 章或第 4 章对出售不动产或动产所得的任何收益进行预扣税，因为这不是 FDAP 收入。不过，请参阅稍后的[_美国房地产利息_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest")。

**Capital gains (Income Code 9).**

You must withhold at 30%, or if applicable, a reduced treaty rate, on the gross amount of the following items.

  

**资本收益（收入代码 9）。** 

您必须对以下物品的总金额预扣 30% 的预扣税，或按照降低的协定税率（如适用）预扣税。

*   Gains on the disposal of timber, coal, or domestic iron ore with a retained economic interest, unless an election is made to treat those gains as income effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business.  
    处置木材、煤炭或国内铁矿石并保留经济利益的收益，除非选择将这些收益视为与美国贸易或业务有效相关的收入。
    
*   Gains on contingent payments received from the sale or exchange after October 4, 1966, of patents, copyrights, secret processes and formulas, goodwill, trademarks, trade brands, franchises, and other like property.  
    1966 年 10 月 4 日之后出售或交换专利、版权、秘密工艺和配方、商誉、商标、贸易品牌、特许经营权和其他类似财产而收到的或有付款收益。
    
*   Gains on certain transfers of all substantial rights to, or an undivided interest in, patents if the transfers were made before October 5, 1966.  
    专利所有实质性权利或不可分割权益的某些转让收益（如果转让是在 1966 年 10 月 5 日之前进行的）。
    
*   Certain gains from the sale or exchange of original issue discount obligations issued after March 31, 1972. For more on withholding on original issue discount obligations, see [_Interest_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224904 "Interest"), earlier.  
    出售或交换 1972 年 3 月 31 日之后发行的原始发行贴现义务的某些收益。有关预扣原始发行贴现义务的更多信息，请参阅前面的[_利息_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224904 "Interest")。
    

If you do not know the amount of the gain, you must withhold an amount necessary to ensure that the tax withheld will not be less than 30% of the recognized gain. The amount to be withheld, however, must not be more than 30% of the amount payable because of the transaction.  
如果您不知道收益金额，您必须预扣必要的金额，以确保预扣税款不低于已确认收益的30%。但扣缴金额不得超过交易应付金额的30%。

Unless you have reason to believe otherwise, you may rely upon the written statement of the person entitled to the income as to the amount of gain. The Form W-8 or documentary evidence must show the beneficial owner's basis in the property giving rise to the gain.  
除非您有理由不相信，否则您可以依赖有权获得收入的人关于收益金额的书面声明。 W-8 表格或文件证据必须显示受益所有人在产生收益的财产中的基础。

**Tax treaties.**

Many tax treaties exempt certain types of gains from U.S. income tax. Be sure to carefully check the provision of the treaty that applies before allowing an exemption from withholding.

  

**税务条约。** 

许多税收协定免除某些类型的美国所得税。在允许豁免预扣税之前，请务必仔细检查适用的条约条款。

#### Royalties版税

In general, you must withhold tax under chapter 3 on the payment of royalties from sources in the United States. However, certain types of royalties are given reduced rates or exemptions under some tax treaties. Accordingly, these different types of royalties are treated as separate categories for withholding purposes. For chapter 4 purposes, royalties are nonfinancial payments and are therefore excluded as withholdable payments.  
一般来说，您必须根据第 3 章对来自美国的特许权使用费进行预扣税。然而，根据某些税收协定，某些类型的特许权使用费可享受降低的税率或免税。因此，这些不同类型的特许权使用费被视为单独的类别以用于预扣税目的。就第 4 章而言，特许权使用费属于非财务付款，因此不属于可预扣付款。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_Most treaties have more than one withholding rate on royalties, which varies by the classification of the payment in that treaty. Be sure to check your particular treaty for the specific rate that applies to you.  
大多数条约对特许权使用费有不止一种预扣税率，该税率根据该条约中付款的分类而有所不同。请务必检查您的特定条约，了解适用于您的具体费率。_.

**Industrial royalties (Income Code 10).**

This category of income includes royalties for the use of, or the right to use, patents, trademarks, secret processes and formulas, goodwill, franchises, “know-how,” and similar rights. It may also include payments for the use of, or right to use, industrial, commercial, and scientific equipment, when this is included in the treaty definition of royalties.

  

**工业特许权使用费（收入代码 10）。** 

此类收入包括使用专利、商标、秘密工艺和配方、商誉、特许经营权、“专有技术”和类似权利的使用费或使用权。当工业、商业和科学设备包含在特许权使用费的条约定义中时，它还可能包括为使用或使用工业、商业和科学设备的权利而支付的费用。

**Motion picture or television copyright royalties (Income Code 11).**

This category refers to royalties paid for the use of motion picture and television copyrights.

  

**电影或电视版权使用费（收入代码 11）。** 

这一类别是指为使用电影和电视版权而支付的特许权使用费。

**Other royalties (for example, copyright, recording, publishing) (Income Code 12).**

This category refers to the royalties paid for the use of copyrights on books, periodicals, articles, etc., except motion picture and television copyrights.

  

**其他特许权使用费（例如版权、录音、出版）（收入代码 12）。** 

本类是指除电影、电视版权外的图书、期刊、文章等著作权的使用所支付的特许权使用费。

#### Real Property Income and Natural Resources Royalties (Income Code 14)  
不动产收入和自然资源使用费（收入代码 14）

You must withhold tax under chapter 3 on income (such as rents and royalties) from real property located in the United States and held for the production of income, unless the foreign payee elects to treat this income as effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business. If the foreign payee chooses to treat this income as effectively connected, the payee must give you _[Form W-8ECI](#en_US_2024_publink1000224832 "Form W-8ECI.")_ (discussed earlier). This real property income includes royalties from mines, wells, or other natural deposits, as well as ordinary rents for the use of real property. For chapter 4 purposes, income from real property is either a nonfinancial payment (and therefore not a withholdable payment) or is excluded as a withholdable payment because it is ECI. For withholding that applies to the disposition of USRPI, see [_U.S. Real Property Interest_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest"), later.  
您必须根据第 3 章对来自位于美国并为产生收入而持有的不动产的收入（例如租金和特许权使用费）预扣税款，除非外国收款人选择将该收入视为与美国贸易或业务有效相关。如果外国收款人选择将此收入视为实际关联收入，则收款人必须向您提供_[W-8ECI 表格](#en_US_2024_publink1000224832 "Form W-8ECI.")_（前面已讨论过）。这种不动产收入包括来自矿山、水井或其他天然矿藏的特许权使用费，以及使用不动产的普通租金。就第 4 章而言，来自不动产的收入要么是非金融付款（因此不是应预扣付款），要么因属于 ECI 而被排除在应预扣付款之外。对于适用于 USRPI 处置的预扣税，请参阅后面的[_美国不动产利息_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest")。

#### Pensions, Annuities, and Alimony (Income Code 15)  
养老金、年金和赡养费（收入代码 15）

The following rules apply to withholding on pensions, annuities, and alimony of foreign payees.  
以下规则适用于外国收款人养老金、年金和赡养费的预扣。

**Pensions and annuities.**

In most cases, you must withhold tax on the gross amount of pensions and annuities that you pay that are from sources within the United States. This includes amounts paid under an annuity contract issued by a foreign branch of a U.S. life insurance company.

  

**养老金和年金。** 

在大多数情况下，您必须对您支付的源自美国境内的养老金和年金总额预扣税款。这包括根据美国人寿保险公司外国分支机构签发的年金合同支付的金额。

Most tax treaties provide an exemption from tax on non-government pensions and annuities. See the specific treaty rules for government pensions. The exemption may not apply to lump-sum payments. See, for example, Article 17(2) of the United States–United Kingdom income tax treaty. In addition, it does not apply to payments treated as deferred compensation, which is often treated as income from employment.  
大多数税收协定都规定对非政府养老金和年金免税。请参阅政府养老金的具体条约规则。豁免可能不适用于一次性付款。例如，参见美国-英国所得税协定第 17(2) 条。此外，它不适用于被视为递延补偿的付款，而递延补偿通常被视为就业收入。

For purposes of chapter 3 withholding, in the absence of a treaty exemption, you must withhold at the statutory rate of 30% on the entire distribution that is from sources within the United States. You may, however, apply withholding at graduated rates to the part of a distribution that arises from the performance of services in the United States after December 31, 1986.  
就第 3 章预扣税而言，在没有条约豁免的情况下，您必须对来自美国境内的全部分配按 30% 的法定税率预扣税。但是，您可以按累进税率对 1986 年 12 月 31 日之后在美国提供服务所产生的分配部分进行预扣税。

Employer contributions to a defined benefit plan covering more than one individual are not made for the benefit of a specific participant, but are made based on the total liabilities to all participants. All funds held under the plan are available to provide benefits to any participant. If the distribution is from such a plan, you can use the method in Revenue Procedure 2004-37 to allocate the distribution to sources in the United States.  
雇主对涵盖多人的设定受益计划的缴款不是为了特定参与者的利益，而是根据所有参与者的总负债进行。该计划下持有的所有资金均可为任何参与者提供福利。如果分配来自此类计划，您可以使用收入程序 2004-37 中的方法将分配分配给美国的来源。

The withholding rules that apply to payments to foreign persons generally take precedence over any other withholding rules that would apply to distributions from qualified plans and other qualified retirement arrangements.  
适用于向外国人付款的预扣税规则通常优先于适用于合格计划和其他合格退休安排的分配的任何其他预扣税规则。

Foreign pension plans are exempt from applying withholding under chapter 4 when they are exempt beneficial owners under Regulations section 1.1471-6(f). A payment from a U.S. pension plan to a foreign individual beneficiary in the plan is not subject to withholding under chapter 4.  
当外国养老金计划是条例第 1.1471-6(f) 条规定的豁免受益所有人时，可豁免根据第 4 章申请预扣税。根据第 4 章，从美国养老金计划向计划中的外国个人受益人支付的款项无需缴纳预扣税。

**No withholding.**

Do not withhold tax on an annuity payment to a nonresident alien if at the time of the first payment from the plan, 90% or more of the employees eligible for benefits under the plan are citizens or residents of the United States and the payment is:

  

**没有扣留。** 

如果在计划首次付款时，有资格享受该计划福利的雇员中 90% 或以上是美国公民或居民，且付款金额为：

1.  For the nonresident's personal services performed outside the United States; or  
    非居民在美国境外提供的个人服务；或者
    
2.  For personal services by a nonresident individual present in the United States for 90 days or less during each tax year, whose pay for those services did not exceed $3,000, and the personal services were performed for:  
    对于非居民个人在每个纳税年度内在美国停留 90 天或以下的个人服务，其为这些服务支付的费用不超过 3,000 美元，并且个人服务是为以下目的提供的：
    
    1.  A nonresident alien individual, foreign partnership, or foreign corporation not engaged in a trade or business in the United States; or  
        不在美国从事贸易或业务的非居民外籍个人、外国合伙企业或外国公司；或者
        
    2.  An office or place of business of a U.S. resident or citizen which was maintained outside the United States.  
        美国居民或公民在美国境外设立的办公室或营业场所。
        
    

If the payment otherwise qualifies under these rules, but less than 90% of the employees eligible for benefits are citizens or residents of the United States, you still need not withhold tax on the payment if:  
如果付款在其他方面符合这些规则，但有资格享受福利的员工中少于 90% 是美国公民或居民，则在以下情况下您仍无需对该付款预扣税：

*   The recipient is a resident of a country that gives a substantially equal exclusion to U.S. citizens and residents, or  
    收件人是对美国公民和居民给予基本平等排除的国家的居民，或者
    
*   The recipient is a resident of a beneficiary developing country under the Trade Act of 1974.  
    收款人是 1974 年贸易法规定的受益发展中国家的居民。
    

The foreign person entitled to the payments must provide you with a Form W-8BEN that contains the TIN of the foreign person.  
有权获得付款的外国人必须向您提供包含外国人 TIN 的 W-8BEN 表格。

**Alimony payments.**

In most cases, alimony payments made by U.S. resident aliens to nonresident aliens are taxable and subject to chapter 3 withholding whether the recipients are residing abroad or are temporarily present in the United States.

  

**赡养费。** 

在大多数情况下，美国居民外国人向非居民外国人支付的赡养费均需纳税，并须缴纳第 3 章预扣税，无论受助人居住在国外还是暂时居住在美国。

Many tax treaties, however, provide for an exemption from withholding for alimony payments. See [_Tax Treaties_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties"), later, for information about treaty benefits.  
然而，许多税收协定都规定免除赡养费预扣税。有关[_税收协定优惠的信息，请参阅后面的税收协定_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties")。

Alimony payments made to a nonresident alien by a U.S. ancillary administrator of a nonresident alien estate are from foreign sources and are not subject to withholding. Alimony payments are not subject to chapter 4 withholding.  
非居民外国人财产的美国辅助管理人向非居民外国人支付的赡养费来自外国来源，无需预扣。赡养费不受第 4 章规定的预扣税约束。

### Note.

Under section 11051 of P.L. 115-97 (TCJA), alimony is no longer considered income if the divorce or separation agreement is executed after December 31, 2018, or if executed before January 1, 2019, but modified after December 31, 2018, the modification must state that section 11051 of P.L. 115-97 applies to the modification.

  

### 笔记。

根据 PL 115-97 (TCJA) 第 11051 条，如果离婚或分居协议在 2018 年 12 月 31 日之后签署，或者在 2019 年 1 月 1 日之前签署，但在 2018 年 12 月 31 日之后修改，则赡养费不再被视为收入，修改必须声明 PL 115-97 第 11051 节适用于修改。

#### Scholarships and Fellowship Grants Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding (Income Code 16)  
奖学金和助学金需缴纳第 3 章预扣税（收入代码 16）

A scholarship or fellowship grant is an amount given to an individual for study, training, or research, and which does not constitute compensation for personal services. For information about withholding on scholarship and fellowship grants that is treated as compensation for services, see [_Pay for services rendered_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224955 "Pay for services rendered."), later. Whether a fellowship grant from U.S. sources is subject to chapter 3 withholding depends on the nature of the payments and whether the recipient is a candidate for a degree. These amounts are not subject to chapter 4 withholding. See [_Scholarships, fellowships, and grants_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224889 "Scholarships, fellowships, and grants.") under _Source of Income,_ earlier.  
奖学金或研究金是给予个人用于学习、培训或研究的金额，不构成对个人服务的补偿。有关预扣被视为服务补偿的奖学金和研究金的信息，请参阅稍后[_支付所提供的服务费用_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224955 "Pay for services rendered.")。来自美国的奖学金是否需要缴纳第三章预扣税取决于付款的性质以及接受者是否是学位候选人。这些金额不受第 4 章规定的预扣税的约束。请参阅前面_收入来源_下的[_奖学金、研究金和助学金_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224889 "Scholarships, fellowships, and grants.")。

**Candidate for a degree.**

Do not withhold on a qualified scholarship from U.S. sources granted and paid to a candidate for a degree. A qualified scholarship means any amount paid to an individual as a scholarship or fellowship grant to the extent that, in accordance with the conditions of the grant, the amount is to be used for the following expenses.

  

**学位候选人。** 

请勿扣留美国来源授予并支付给学位候选人的合格奖学金。合格奖学金是指作为奖学金或研究金支付给个人的任何金额，但根据授予条件，该金额将用于以下费用。

*   Tuition and fees required for enrollment or attendance at an educational organization.  
    注册或就读教育机构所需的学杂费。
    
*   Fees, books, supplies, and equipment required for courses of instruction at the educational organization.  
    教育组织教学课程所需的费用、书籍、用品和设备。
    

The payment of a qualified scholarship to a nonresident alien is not reportable and is not subject to withholding. However, the part of a scholarship or fellowship paid to a nonresident alien which does not constitute a qualified scholarship is reportable on Form 1042-S and is subject to withholding. For example, those parts of a scholarship devoted to travel, room, and board are subject to withholding and are reported on Form 1042-S. The withholding rate is 14% on taxable scholarship and fellowship grants paid to nonresident aliens temporarily present in the United States in “F,” “J,” “M,” or “Q” nonimmigrant status. Payments made to nonresident alien individuals in any other immigration status are subject to 30% withholding.  
向非居民外国人支付的合格奖学金无需报告，也无需预扣。然而，支付给非居民外国人的奖学金或助学金中不构成合格奖学金的部分应在 1042-S 表格中报告并需扣缴。例如，奖学金中用于旅行、住宿和膳食的部分需要预扣，并在 1042-S 表格中报告。向以“F”、“J”、“M”或“Q”非移民身份暂时居住在美国的非居民外国人支付的应税奖学金和研究金的预扣税率为 14%。向具有任何其他移民身份的非居民外国人支付的款项需缴纳 30% 的预扣税。

**Nondegree candidate.**

If the person receiving the scholarship or fellowship grant is not a candidate for a degree, and is present in the United States in “F,” “J,” “M,” or “Q” nonimmigrant status, you must withhold tax at 14% on the total amount of the grant that is from U.S. sources if the following requirements are met.

  

**非学位候选人。** 

如果获得奖学金或研究金的人不是学位候选人，并且在美国以“F”、“J”、“M”或“Q”非移民身份居住，则您必须按照 14 号预扣税款如果满足以下要求，则占来自美国的赠款总额的％。

1.  The grant must be for study, training, or research in the United States.  
    补助金必须用于在美国学习、培训或研究。
    
2.  The grant must be made by:  
    补助金必须由以下人员提供：
    
    1.  A tax-exempt organization operated for charitable, religious, educational, etc. purposes;  
        以慈善、宗教、教育等为目的的免税组织；
        
    2.  A foreign government;外国政府；
        
    3.  A federal, state, or local government agency; or  
        联邦、州或地方政府机构；或者
        
    4.  An international organization, or a binational or multinational educational or cultural organization created or continued by the Mutual Educational and Cultural Exchange Act of 1961 (known as the Fulbright-Hays Act).  
        根据 1961 年《相互教育和文化交流法案》（称为《富布赖特-海斯法案》）创建或延续的国际组织或两国或多国教育或文化组织。
        
    

If the grant does not meet both (1) and (2) above, you must withhold at 30% on the amount of the grant that is from U.S. sources.  
如果补助金不满足上述 (1) 和 (2) 条件，您必须预扣来自美国的补助金金额的 30%。

**Alternate withholding procedure.**

You may choose to treat the taxable part of a U.S. source grant or scholarship as wages. The student or grantee must have been admitted into the United States on an “F,” “J,” “M,” or “Q” visa. The student or grantee will know that you are using this alternate withholding procedure when you ask for a Form W-4.

  

**替代预扣税程序。** 

您可以选择将美国来源补助金或奖学金的应税部分视为工资。学生或受资助者必须持有“F”、“J”、“M”或“Q”签证进入美国。当您索取 W-4 表时，学生或受助人将知道您正在使用此替代预扣税程序。

The student or grantee must complete Form W-4 annually following the instructions given here and forward it to you, the payer of the scholarship, or your designated withholding agent. You may rely on the information on Form W-4 unless you know or have reason to know it is incorrect. You must file a _[Form 1042-S](#en_US_2024_publink1000225054 "Form 1042-S.")_ (discussed later) for each student or grantee who gives you, or your withholding agent, a Form W-4.  
学生或受资助者必须按照此处提供的说明每年填写 W-4 表，并将其转发给您、奖学金付款人或您指定的扣缴义务人。您可以依赖 W-4 表格中的信息，除非您知道或有理由知道该信息不正确。您必须为向您或您的扣缴义务人提供表格 W-4 的每位学生或受助人提交_[表格 1042-S](#en_US_2024_publink1000225054 "Form 1042-S.")_ （稍后讨论）。

Each student or grantee who files a Form W-4 must file an annual U.S. income tax return to take the deductions claimed on that form. If the individual is in the United States during more than 1 tax year, they must attach a statement to the annual Form W-4 indicating that the individual has filed a U.S. income tax return for the previous year. If they have not been in the United States long enough to have to file a return, the individual must attach a statement to the Form W-4 saying that a timely U.S. income tax return will be filed.  
每个提交 W-4 表格的学生或受助人都必须提交年度美国所得税申报表，以获取该表格上申报的扣除额。如果个人在美国停留超过 1 个纳税年度，则必须在年度 W-4 表格中附上一份声明，表明该个人已提交上一年的美国所得税申报表。如果他们在美国停留的时间不够长，不足以提交纳税申报表，则该个人必须在 W-4 表格中附上一份声明，表明将及时提交美国所得税申报表。

The payer of the grant or scholarship must review the Form W-4 to make sure all the necessary and required information is provided. If the withholding agent knows or has reason to know that the amounts shown on the Form W-4 may be false, the withholding agent must reject the Form W-4 and withhold at the appropriate statutory rate (14% or 30%).  
助学金或奖学金的付款人必须查看 W-4 表，以确保提供所有必要和必需的信息。如果扣缴义务人知道或有理由知道表格 W-4 上显示的金额可能不实，则扣缴义务人必须拒绝表格 W-4 并按适当的法定税率（14% 或 30%）扣缴。

After receipt and acceptance of the Form W-4, the payer must withhold at the graduated rates in Pub. 15-T as if the grant or scholarship income were wages. The gross amount of the income is reduced by the total amount of any deductions on the Form W-4 and the withholding tax is figured on the rest.  
收到并接受 W-4 表格后，付款人必须按照 Pub 的累进税率预扣税款。 15-T 就好像助学金或奖学金收入是工资一样。收入总额减去 W-4 表上的任何扣除额总额，然后根据其余部分计算预扣税。

**Pay for services rendered.**

Pay for services rendered as an employee by an alien who is also the recipient of a scholarship or fellowship grant is usually subject to graduated withholding under chapter 3 according to the rules discussed later in [_Wages Paid to Employees— Graduated Withholding_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224978 "Wages Paid to Employees—Graduated Withholding"). This includes taxable amounts an individual who is a candidate for a degree receives for teaching, doing research, and carrying out other part-time employment required as a condition for receiving the scholarship or fellowship grant (that is, compensatory scholarship or fellowship income).

  

**为所提供的服务付费。** 

获得奖学金或助学金的外国人作为雇员提供的服务的报酬通常根据第 3 章的规定，根据支付给雇员的工资——分级预扣税中讨论的规则，进行分级预扣税。这包括作为获得奖学金或研究金补助金（即补偿性奖学金或研究金收入）的条件的学位候选人因教学、研究和从事其他兼职工作而获得的应税金额。

Grants given to students, trainees, or researchers which require the performance of personal services as a necessary condition for disbursing the grant do not qualify as scholarship or fellowship grants. Instead, they are compensation for personal services considered to be wages. It does not matter what term is used to describe the grant (for example, stipend, scholarship, fellowship, etc.).  
向学生、受训人员或研究人员提供的助学金，如果要求提供个人服务作为发放助学金的必要条件，则不符合奖学金或研究金的资格。相反，它们是对被视为工资的个人服务的补偿。使用什么术语来描述补助金（例如，津贴、奖学金、研究金等）并不重要。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_Withholding agents who pay grants that are in fact wages must report such grants on Forms 941 and W-2 and withhold income tax on them at the graduated rates. Withholding agents may not allow tax treaty exemptions that apply to scholarships and fellowships to be applied to grants that are really wages. It is the responsibility of the withholding agent to determine whether a grant is “wages” or a “scholarship or fellowship,” and to report and withhold on the grant accordingly. An alien student, trainee, or researcher may not claim a scholarship or fellowship treaty exemption against income that has been reported to them on Form W-2 as wages.  
支付实际上是工资补助金的扣缴义务人必须在 941 表格和 W-2 表格中报告此类补助金，并按累进税率预扣所得税。扣缴义务人可能不允许将适用于奖学金和研究金的税收协定豁免适用于真正属于工资的补助金。扣缴义务人有责任确定补助金是“工资”还是“奖学金或研究金”，并相应地报告和扣缴补助金。外国学生、实习生或研究人员不得针对 W-2 表中作为工资向其报告的收入申请奖学金或研究金条约豁免。_.

**Per diem paid by the U.S. Government.**

Per diem for subsistence paid by the U.S. Government (directly or by contract) to a nonresident alien engaged in a training program in the United States funded by the U.S. Agency for International Development are not subject to 14% or 30% withholding. This is true even if the alien is subject to income tax on those amounts.

  

**每日津贴由美国政府支付。** 

美国政府（直接或通过合同）向在美国参加由美国国际开发署资助的培训项目的非居民外国人支付的每日生活津贴不需缴纳 14% 或 30% 的预扣税。即使外国人需要就这些金额缴纳所得税，情况也是如此。

**Tax treaties.**

Many treaties contain exemptions from U.S. taxation for scholarships and fellowships. Although usually found in the student articles of the tax treaties, many of these exemptions also apply to research grants received by researchers who are not students. See [_Tax Treaties_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties"), later, for information about treaty benefits. The treaty provision usually exempts the entire scholarship or fellowship amount, regardless of whether the grant is a “qualified scholarship” under U.S. law.

  

**税务条约。** 

许多条约都包含美国对奖学金和研究金的税收豁免。虽然这些豁免通常出现在税收协定的学生文章中，但其中许多豁免也适用于非学生研究人员获得的研究资助。有关[_税收协定优惠的信息，请参阅后面的税收协定_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties")。条约条款通常会免除全部奖学金或研究金金额，无论该资助是否属于美国法律规定的“合格奖学金”。

An alien student, trainee, or researcher may claim a treaty exemption for a scholarship or fellowship by submitting Form W-8BEN to the payer of the grant. However, a scholarship or fellowship recipient who receives both wages and a scholarship or fellowship from the same institution can claim treaty exemptions on both kinds of income on Form 8233.  
外国学生、实习生或研究人员可以通过向补助金付款人提交 W-8BEN 表格来申请奖学金或研究金的条约豁免。然而，从同一机构同时获得工资和奖学金或研究金的奖学金或研究金获得者可以在 8233 表格上申请两种收入的条约豁免。

The scholarship or fellowship recipient who is claiming a treaty exemption must provide you with a foreign TIN on Form W-8BEN or, in the case of a recipient who also received wages from the same institution, a U.S. TIN on Form 8233, or you cannot allow the treaty exemption. A copy of a completed Form W-7, showing that a TIN has been applied for, can be given to you with a Form 8233. See [_Form 8233_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224967 "Form 8233."), later, under _Pay for Personal Services Performed._  
申请条约豁免的奖学金或研究金获得者必须在 W-8BEN 表格中向您提供外国 TIN，或者如果获奖者也从同一机构领取工资，则必须在 8233 表格中提供美国 TIN，否则您不能允许条约豁免。填写完毕的 W-7 表格副本（表明已申请 TIN）可与 8233 表格一起提供给您。请参阅稍后的[_8233 表格_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224967 "Form 8233.")，在_“为所执行的个人服务付费”下。_

_**Nonresident alien who becomes a resident alien.**_

In most cases, only a nonresident alien individual may use the terms of a tax treaty to reduce or eliminate U.S. tax on income from a scholarship or fellowship grant. A student (including a trainee or business apprentice) or researcher who has become a resident alien for U.S. tax purposes may not use the terms of a tax treaty due to a provision known as a “saving clause.” However, an exception to the saving clause may permit an exemption from tax to continue for scholarship or fellowship grant income even after the recipient has otherwise become a U.S. resident alien for tax purposes. In this situation, the individual must give you a Form W-9 and an attachment that includes all the following information.

  

_**非居民外国人成为居民外国人。** _

在大多数情况下，只有非居民外籍个人可以利用税收协定的条款来减少或免除美国对奖学金或研究金补助金收入征税。由于“储蓄条款”的规定，因美国税务目的而成为外籍居民的学生（包括实习生或商业学徒）或研究人员不得使用税收协定的条款。然而，储蓄条款的例外可能允许奖学金或研究金补助收入继续免税，即使接受者出于税收目的已成为美国居民外国人。在这种情况下，该个人必须向您提供 W-9 表和包含以下所有信息的附件。

*   The treaty country.条约国。
    
*   The treaty article addressing the income.  
    关于收入的条约条款。
    
*   The article number (or location) in the tax treaty that contains the saving clause and its exceptions.  
    包含保留条款及其例外情况的税收协定中的条款编号（或位置）。
    
*   The type and amount of income that qualifies for the exemption from tax.  
    符合免税资格的收入类型和金额。
    
*   Sufficient facts to justify the exemption from tax under the terms of the treaty article.  
    有足够的事实证明根据条约条款的免税是合理的。
    

**Example.**

Article 20 of the U.S.–China income tax treaty allows an exemption from tax for scholarship income received by a Chinese student temporarily present in the United States. Under the Internal Revenue Code, a student may become a resident alien for tax purposes if their stay in the United States exceeds 5 calendar years. However, the treaty allows the provisions of Article 20 to continue to apply even after the Chinese student becomes a resident alien of the United States.

  

**例子。** 

中美所得税协定第20条允许暂时居住在美国的中国学生获得的奖学金收入免税。根据《国内税收法》，如果学生在美国停留超过 5 个日历年，则出于税收目的，学生可能会成为外籍居民。然而，该条约允许第20条的规定即使在中国学生成为美国居民后继续适用。

#### Other Grants, Prizes, and Awards Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding  
受第 3 章规定扣缴的其​​他赠款、奖品和奖励

Other grants, prizes, and awards made by grantors that reside in the United States are treated as income from sources within the United States. Those made for activities conducted outside the United States by a foreign person or by grantors that reside outside the United States are treated as income from foreign sources. These provisions do not apply to salaries or other pay for services.  
居住在美国的资助者提供的其他资助、奖金和奖励被视为来自美国境内的收入。由外国人或居住在美国境外的授予人在美国境外进行的活动而获得的收入被视为来自外国的收入。这些规定不适用于工资或其他服务报酬。

**Grant.**

The purpose of a grant must be to achieve a specific objective, produce a report or other similar product, or improve or enhance a literary, artistic, musical, scientific, teaching, or other similar capacity, skill, or talent of the grantee. A grant must also be an amount which does not qualify as a scholarship or fellowship. The grantor must not intend the amount to be given to the grantee for the purpose of aiding the grantee to perform study, training, or research.

  

**授予。** 

资助的目的必须是实现特定目标，制作报告或其他类似产品，或改善或增强受资助者的文学、艺术、音乐、科学、教学或其他类似能力、技能或才能。助学金还必须是不符合奖学金或研究金资格的金额。授予者不得将向受赠者提供的金额用于帮助受赠者进行学习、培训或研究。

**Prizes and awards.**

Prizes and awards are amounts received primarily in recognition of religious, charitable, scientific, educational, artistic, literary, or civic achievement, or are received as the result of entering a contest. A prize or award is taxable to the recipient unless all of the following conditions are met.

  

**奖品和奖项。** 

奖品和奖项主要是为了表彰宗教、慈善、科学、教育、艺术、文学或公民成就而获得的金额，或者是由于参加竞赛而获得的金额。除非满足以下所有条件，否则奖品或奖励需向接受者征税。

*   The recipient was selected without any action on their part to enter the contest or proceeding.  
    收件人无需采取任何行动即可被选择参加竞赛或程序。
    
*   The recipient is not required to render substantial future services as a condition to receive the prize or award.  
    获奖者不需要提供大量的未来服务作为获得奖品或奖励的条件。
    
*   The prize or award is transferred by the payer to a governmental unit or tax-exempt charitable organization as designated by the recipient.  
    奖品或奖金由付款人转移给受奖人指定的政府单位或免税慈善组织。
    

**Targeted grants and achievement awards.**

Targeted grants and achievement awards received by nonresident aliens for activities conducted outside the United States are treated as income from foreign sources. Targeted grants and achievement awards are issued by exempt organizations or by the United States (or one of its instruments or agencies), a state (or a political subdivision of a state), or the District of Columbia for an activity (or past activity in the case of an achievement award) undertaken in the public interest.

  

**有针对性的补助金和成就奖。** 

非居民外国人因在美国境外开展的活动而获得的定向补助金和成就奖被视为来自外国的收入。有针对性的赠款和成就奖由豁免组织或美国（或其文书或机构之一）、州（或州的政治分区）或哥伦比亚特区针对某项活动（或过去的活动）颁发为公共利益而进行的成就奖。

#### Pay for Personal Services Performed  
支付所执行的个人服务费用

This section explains the rules for withholding tax from pay for personal services. You must generally withhold tax at the 30% rate on compensation you pay to a nonresident alien individual for labor or personal services performed in the United States, unless that pay is specifically exempted from withholding or subject to graduated withholding. This rule applies regardless of your place of residence, the place where the contract for service was made, or the place of payment.  
本节介绍从个人服务工资中预扣税的规则。通常，您必须按照 30% 的税率对您向非居民外籍人士在美国提供的劳务或个人服务支付的报酬进行预扣税，除非该报酬被明确免除预扣税或需分级预扣税。无论您居住在何处、签订服务合同的地点或付款地点如何，此规则均适用。

Payments for personal services are not withholdable payments under chapter 4 when they are nonfinancial payments. See Regulations section 1.1473-1(a)(4)(iii) for a description of these payments and their exclusion as withholdable payments.  
如果个人服务付款属于非金融付款，则不属于第 4 章规定的可预扣付款。请参阅法规第 1.1473-1(a)(4)(iii) 节，了解这些付款的说明以及将其排除为可预扣付款的情况。

**Illegal aliens.**

Foreign workers who are illegal aliens are subject to U.S. taxes in spite of their illegal status. U.S. employers or payers who hire illegal aliens may be subject to various fines, penalties, and sanctions imposed by U.S. Immigration and Customs Enforcement. If such employers or payers choose to hire illegal aliens, the payments made to those aliens are subject to the same tax withholding and reporting obligations that apply to other classes of aliens. Illegal aliens who are nonresident aliens and who receive income from performing independent personal services are subject to 30% withholding unless exempt under some provision of law or a tax treaty. Illegal aliens who are resident aliens and who receive income from performing dependent personal services are subject to the same reporting and withholding obligations that apply to U.S. citizens who receive the same kind of income.

  

**非法外国人。** 

作为非法外国人的外国工人尽管具有非法身份，仍需缴纳美国税款。雇用非法外国人的美国雇主或付款人可能会受到美国移民和海关执法局施加的各种罚款、处罚和制裁。如果此类雇主或付款人选择雇用非法外国人，则向这些外国人支付的款项须遵守适用于其他类别外国人的相同预扣税和报告义务。属于非居民外国人且通过提供独立个人服务获得收入的非法外国人须缴纳 30% 的预扣税，除非根据某些法律规定或税务条约获得豁免。作为居民外国人并通过提供受抚养个人服务获得收入的非法外国人，须遵守适用于获得同类收入的美国公民的相同报告和预扣税义务。

**Form 8233.**

This form is used by a nonresident alien individual to claim a tax treaty exemption from withholding on some or all compensation paid for:

  

**表格 8233。** 

非居民外籍个人可使用此表格来申请税收协定豁免，以支付以下部分或全部赔偿：

*   Independent personal services (self-employment),  
    独立个人服务（自营职业），
    
*   Dependent personal services, or  
    依赖个人服务，或
    
*   Personal services income and noncompensatory scholarship or fellowship income from the same withholding agent.  
    来自同一扣缴义务人的个人服务收入和无偿奖学金或研究金收入。
    

A withholding agent that receives Form 8233 from a nonresident alien individual claiming a tax treaty exemption must review the form, sign to indicate its acceptance, and forward the form to the IRS within 5 days of its acceptance.  
扣缴义务人收到申请税收协定豁免的非居民外籍个人的 8233 表格后，必须审查该表格，签字以表明其接受，并在接受后 5 天内将该表格转发给 IRS。

**COVID-19 medical condition travel exception.**

For tax years after December 31, 2021, individuals cannot claim the COVID-19 medical condition travel exception to exclude any days of presence in the United States for the purpose of the “substantial presence test.” This was **solely** available for the 2020 tax year. However, days of presence in the United States in 2020 that were excluded for tax year 2020 may impact the application of the “substantial presence test” for tax year 2021. For more information, including guidance for withholding agents, see the [Instructions for Form 8233](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8233).

  

**COVID-19 医疗状况旅行例外。** 

对于 2021 年 12 月 31 日之后的纳税年度，个人不能申请 COVID-19 医疗状况旅行例外，以排除出于“实质性居住测试”的目的而在美国居住的任何天数。这**仅**适用于 2020 纳税年度。然而，2020 年纳税年度被排除在外的 2020 年在美国居住天数可能会影响 2021 年纳税年度“实质居住测试”的应用。有关更多信息，包括扣缴义务人指南，请参阅[8233 表格说明](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8233)。

**Form W-4.**

This form is used by a person providing dependent personal services to claim withholding allowances, but not a tax treaty exemption. Nonresident alien individuals are subject to special instructions for completing the Form W-4. See the discussion under [_Wages Paid to Employees—Graduated Withholding_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224978 "Wages Paid to Employees—Graduated Withholding"), later.

  

**W-4 表格。** 

提供受抚养个人服务的人可以使用此表格来申请预扣津贴，但不能申请税收协定豁免。非居民外籍个人在填写 W-4 表格时须遵守特殊说明。请参阅稍后[_支付给员工的工资 - 分级预扣税_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224978 "Wages Paid to Employees—Graduated Withholding")下的讨论。

**Pay for independent personal services (Income Code 17).**

Independent personal services (a term commonly used in tax treaties) are personal services performed by an independent nonresident alien contractor as contrasted with those performed by an employee. This category of pay includes payments for professional services, such as fees of an attorney, physician, or accountant made directly to the person performing the services. It also includes honoraria paid by colleges and universities to visiting teachers, lecturers, and researchers.

Pay for independent personal services is subject to chapter 3 withholding and reporting as follows.

  

**支付独立个人服务费用（收入代码 17）。** 

独立个人服务（税务条约中常用的术语）是由独立的非居民外籍承包商提供的个人服务，与雇员提供的个人服务不同。此类报酬包括专业服务的付款，例如直接向提供服务的人员支付的律师费、医生费或会计师费。它还包括学院和大学向客座教师、讲师和研究人员支付的酬金。

独立个人服务的报酬须遵守第 3 章的预扣税和报告规定，如下所示。

_**30% rate.**_

You must withhold at the statutory rate of 30% on all payments unless the alien enters into a withholding agreement or receives a _[final payment exemption](#en_US_2024_publink1000224974 "Final payment exemption.")_ (discussed later).

  

_**30% 的税率。** _

您必须按照 30% 的法定税率预扣所有款项，除非外国人签订预扣税协议或获得_[最终付款豁免](#en_US_2024_publink1000224974 "Final payment exemption.")_（稍后讨论）。

_**Withholding agreements.**_

Pay for personal services of a nonresident alien who is engaged during the tax year in the conduct of a U.S. trade or business may be wholly or partially exempted from withholding at the statutory rate if an agreement has been reached between the Commissioner or his delegate and the alien as to the amount of withholding required. This agreement will be effective for payments covered by the agreement that are made after the agreement is executed by all parties. The alien must agree to timely file an income tax return for the current tax year.

  

_**扣留协议。** _

如果专员或其代表与税务机关达成协议，则在纳税年度内从事美国贸易或业务的非居民外国人的个人服务费用可以全部或部分免除按法定税率预扣税款。外国人所需的预扣税金额。本协议对各方签署本协议后所支付的本协议项下的款项有效。外国人必须同意及时提交当前纳税年度的所得税申报表。

_**Final payment exemption.**_

The final payment of compensation for independent personal services may be wholly or partially exempt from withholding at the statutory rate. This exemption applies to the last payment of compensation, other than wages, for personal services rendered in the United States that the alien expects to receive from any withholding agent during the tax year.

  

_**最后付款豁免。** _

独立个人劳务报酬的最终支付可以全部或部分免征法定税率的预扣税。这项豁免适用于外国人在纳税年度内预计从任何扣缴义务人处收到的在美国提供的个人服务的最后一笔补偿金（工资除外）。

To obtain the final payment exemption, the alien, or the alien's agent, must file the forms and provide the information required by the Commissioner or his delegate. This information includes, but is not limited to, the following items.  
为了获得最终付款豁免，外国人或外国人的代理人必须提交表格并提供专员或其代表要求的信息。该信息包括但不限于以下项目。

*   A statement by each withholding agent from whom amounts of gross income effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business have been received by the alien during the tax year. It must show the amount of income paid and the amount of tax withheld. The withholding agent must sign the statement and include a declaration that it is made under penalties of perjury.  
    外国人在纳税年度从其处收到的与美国贸易或业务活动实际相关的总收入金额的每个扣缴义务人的声明。它必须显示支付的收入金额和预扣税额。扣缴义务人必须签署该声明，并声明该声明是根据伪证罪处罚的。
    
*   A statement by the withholding agent from whom the final payment of compensation for personal services will be received showing the amount of final payment and the amount that would be withheld if a final payment exemption is not granted. The withholding agent must sign the statement and include a declaration that it is made under penalties of perjury.  
    将收到个人劳务报酬最终付款的扣缴义务人出具的声明，其中显示最终付款金额以及未授予最终付款豁免时将扣留的金额。扣缴义务人必须签署该声明，并声明该声明是根据伪证罪处罚的。
    
*   A statement by the alien that they do not intend to receive any other amounts of gross income effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business during the current tax year.  
    外国人的一份声明，表明他们不打算在当前纳税年度获得与美国贸易或业务活动实际相关的任何其他金额的总收入。
    
*   The amount of tax that has been withheld (or paid) under any other provision of the Internal Revenue Code or regulations for any income effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business during the current tax year.  
    根据《国内税收法》或法规的任何其他规定，针对当前纳税年度内与美国贸易或业务活动有效相关的任何收入，已预扣（或缴纳）的税额。
    
*   The amount of any outstanding tax liabilities, including any interest and penalties, from the current tax year or prior tax periods.  
    当前纳税年度或之前纳税期间的任何未偿纳税义务金额，包括任何利息和罚款。
    
*   The provision of any income tax treaty under which a partial or complete exemption from withholding may be claimed, the country of the alien's residence, and a statement of sufficient facts to justify an exemption under that treaty.  
    可以要求部分或完全免除预扣税的任何所得税条约的规定、外国人居住的国家以及证明该条约规定的豁免合理性的充分事实的声明。
    

The alien must give a statement, signed and verified by a declaration that it is made under penalties of perjury, that all the information provided is true, and that to their knowledge no relevant information has been omitted.  
外国人必须提供一份经签署和核实的声明，证明该声明是在作伪证的处罚下做出的，所提供的所有信息都是真实的，并且据其所知，没有遗漏任何相关信息。

If satisfied with the information provided, the Commissioner or his delegate will determine the amount of the alien's tentative income tax for the tax year on gross income effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business. Ordinary and necessary business expenses may be taken into account if proved to the satisfaction of the Commissioner or his delegate.  
如果对所提供的信息感到满意，专员或其代表将根据与美国贸易或业务活动实际相关的总收入确定外国人在该纳税年度的暂定所得税金额。如果专员或其代表满意的话，可以考虑普通和必要的业务费用。

The Commissioner or his delegate will provide the alien with a letter to you, the withholding agent, stating the amount of the final payment of compensation for personal services that is exempt from withholding, and the amount that would otherwise be withheld that may be paid to the alien due to the exemption. The amount of pay exempt from withholding cannot be more than $5,000. The alien must give two copies of the letter to you and must also attach a copy of the letter to their income tax return for the tax year for which the exemption is effective.  
专员或其代表将向外国人提供一封致您（扣缴义务人）的信函，说明免予扣缴的个人劳务报酬的最终支付金额，以及可能支付给扣缴义务人的个人劳务报酬的最终金额。外国人由于豁免。免予预扣税的工资金额不能超过 5,000 美元。外国人必须向您提供该信函的两份副本，并且还必须将该信函的副本附在豁免生效的纳税年度的所得税申报表中。

_**Travel expenses.**_

If you pay or reimburse the travel expenses of a nonresident alien, the payments are not reportable to the IRS and are not subject to chapter 3 withholding if the payments are made under an accountable plan, as described in Regulations section 1.62-2. This treatment applies only to that part of a payment that represents the payment of travel and lodging expenses and not to that part that represents compensation for independent personal services.

  

_**差旅费。** _

如果您支付或报销非居民外国人的旅行费用，则该款项无需向 IRS 报告，并且如果该款项是根据实报实销计划支付的，则无需缴纳第 3 章预扣税（如条例第 1.62-2 条所述）。这种处理仅适用于代表支付旅行和住宿费用的付款部分，不适用于代表独立个人服务补偿的部分。

_**Tax treaties.**_

Under some tax treaties, pay for independent personal services performed in the United States is treated as business income and taxed according to the treaty provisions for business profits.

  

_**税务条约。** _

根据某些税收协定，在美国提供的独立个人服务的报酬被视为营业收入，并根据营业利润的协定规定纳税。
