Under other tax treaties, pay for independent personal services performed in the United States is exempt from U.S. income tax only if the independent nonresident alien contractor performs the services during a period of temporary presence in the United States (usually not more than 183 days) and is a resident of the treaty country.  
根据其他税收协定，只有当独立非居民外籍承包商在美国临时居留期间（通常不超过 183 天）提供服务时，在美国提供的独立个人服务的费用才可免征美国所得税，并且是条约国的居民。

Independent nonresident alien contractors use Form 8233 to claim an exemption from withholding under a tax treaty. For more information, see [_Form 8233_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224967 "Form 8233."), earlier.  
独立非居民外籍承包商使用 8233 表格申请税收协定下的预扣税豁免。如需了解更多信息，请参阅之前的[_8233 表格_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224967 "Form 8233.")。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/taxtip.gif)
_Form 8233 should be used to claim a treaty benefit based on a business profits provision or an independent personal services provision.  
表格 8233 应用于申请基于商业利润条款或独立个人服务条款的税收协定优惠。_.

Often, you must withhold under the statutory rules on payments made to a treaty country resident contractor for services performed in the United States. This is because the factors on which the treaty exemption is based may not be determinable until after the close of the tax year. The contractor must then file a U.S. income tax return (Form 1040-NR) to recover any overwithheld tax by providing the IRS with proof that they are entitled to a treaty exemption.  
通常，您必须根据法定规则，针对在美国提供服务而向条约国常驻承包商支付的款项进行扣缴。这是因为协定豁免所依据的因素可能要到纳税年度结束后才能确定。然后，承包商必须提交美国所得税申报表（表格 1040-NR），向 IRS 提供其有权享受条约豁免的证明，以追回任何超扣税款。

#### Wages Paid to Employees—Graduated Withholding  
支付给员工的工资——分级扣缴

Salaries, wages, bonuses, or any other pay for personal services (referred to collectively as wages) paid to nonresident alien employees are subject to graduated withholding in the same way as for U.S. citizens and residents if the wages are effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business.  
支付给非居民外籍雇员的薪水、工资、奖金或任何其他个人服务报酬（统称为工资），如果工资与以下行为有实际联系，则应按照与美国公民和居民相同的方式进行分级预扣税：美国贸易或业务。

_**Note.**_

Any wages paid to a nonresident alien for personal services performed as an employee for an employer are generally not subject to the 30% withholding if the wages are subject to graduated withholding.

  

_**笔记。** _

如果非居民外国人作为雇主雇员提供个人服务而支付给非居民外国人的任何工资，如果工资需要分级预扣税，则一般不需缴纳 30% 的预扣税。

Also, the 30% withholding does not apply to pay for personal services performed as an employee for an employer if it is effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business and is specifically exempted from the definition of wages. Chapter 4 withholding does not apply to these payments. See [_Pay that is not wages_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224983 "Pay that is not wages."), later.  
此外，如果雇员为雇主提供的个人服务与美国贸易或商业行为有实际联系，并且明确不受工资定义的约束，则 30% 的预扣税不适用于支付。第 4 章预扣税不适用于这些付款。稍后请参阅[_不是工资的 Pay_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224983 "Pay that is not wages.") 。

**Special rule for certain agricultural workers.**

The 30% withholding does not apply to pay for personal services performed by a foreign agricultural worker in the United States on an H-2A visa. However, if the total wages are $600 or more and the worker does not give you a TIN, you may need to backup withhold. You may withhold at graduated rates if the employee asks you to by giving you a completed Form W-4.

  

**针对某些农业工人的特殊规则。** 

30% 的预扣税不适用于支付持有 H-2A 签证在美国的外国农业工人提供的个人服务的费用。但是，如果总工资为 600 美元或以上，并且工人没有给您 TIN，您可能需要预扣税款。如果员工要求您提供填写完整的 W-4 表格，您可以按累进税率预扣税款。

Pay for personal services that is not subject to withholding is not subject to reporting on Form 1042-S. If the compensation is more than $600, report it on Form W-2 (if the employee gave you a TIN) or on Form 1099-NEC, Nonemployee Compensation (if the employee did not give you a TIN). See the [Instructions for Forms 1099-MISC and 1099-NEC](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-1099-nec) for more information.  
无需缴纳预扣税的个人服务费用无需在 1042-S 表格上报告。如果赔偿超过 600 美元，请在 W-2 表（如果员工给您提供了 TIN）或 1099-NEC 表“​​非雇员赔偿”（如果员工没有给您提供 TIN​​）上报告。有关更多信息，请参阅[表格 1099-MISC 和 1099-NEC 的说明](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-1099-nec)。

For more information on withholding on foreign agricultural workers, go to IRS.gov and enter “agricultural workers” in the search box.  
有关外国农业工人预扣税的更多信息，请访问 IRS.gov 并在搜索框中输入“农业工人”。

**Employer–employee relationship.**

For pay for personal services to qualify as wages, there must be an employer–employee relationship.

  

**雇主与雇员的关系。** 

为了使个人服务报酬符合工资标准，必须存在雇主与雇员的关系。

Under the common law rules, every individual who performs services subject to the will and control of an employer, both as to what shall be done and how it shall be done, is an employee. It does not matter that the employer allows the employee considerable discretion and freedom of action, as long as the employer has the legal right to control both the method and the result of the services.  
根据普通法规则，每个在雇主意愿和控制下提供服务的个人（无论是做什么还是如何做）都是雇员。只要雇主有合法权利控制服务的方法和结果，雇主允许雇员有相当大的自由裁量权和行动自由并不重要。

If an employer–employee relationship exists, it does not matter what the parties call the relationship. It does not matter if the employee is called a partner, coadventurer, agent, or independent contractor. It does not matter how the pay is measured, how the individual is paid, or what the payments are called. Nor does it matter whether the individual works full time or part time.  
如果存在雇主与雇员关系，双方如何称呼这种关系并不重要。员工是否被称为合伙人、共同冒险者、代理人或独立承包商并不重要。薪酬如何衡量、如何向个人支付或这些付款的名称并不重要。个人是全职还是兼职工作也并不重要。

The existence of the employer–employee relationship under the usual common law rules will be determined, in doubtful cases, by an examination of the facts of each case.  
在有疑问的情况下，将通过对每个案件的事实进行审查来确定普通法规则下雇主与雇员关系的存在。

_**Employee.**_

An employee generally includes any individual who performs services if the relationship between the individual and the person for whom the services are performed is the legal relationship of employer and employee. This includes an individual who receives a supplemental unemployment pay benefit that is treated as wages.

  

_**员工。** _

雇员通常包括任何提供服务的个人，如果该个人与接受服务的人之间的关系是雇主和雇员的法律关系。这包括领取被视为工资的补充失业救济金的个人。

_**No distinction is made between classes of employees.**_

Superintendents, managers, and other supervisory personnel are employees. In most cases, an officer of a corporation is an employee, but a director acting in this capacity is not. An officer who does not perform any services, or only minor services, and neither receives nor is entitled to receive any pay is not considered an employee.

  

_**员工类别之间没有区别。** _

主管、经理和其他监督人员都是雇员。在大多数情况下，公司的高级职员是雇员，但以这种身份行事的董事则不是。不提供任何服务或仅提供次要服务、既不接受也无权接受任何报酬的官员不被视为雇员。

_**Employer.**_

An employer is any person or organization for whom an individual performs or has performed any service, of whatever nature, as an employee. The term “employer” includes not only individuals and organizations in a trade or business, but organizations exempt from income tax, such as religious and charitable organizations, educational institutions, clubs, social organizations, and societies. It also includes the governments of the United States, the States, Puerto Rico, and the District of Columbia, as well as their agencies, instrumentalities, and political subdivisions.

  

_**雇主。** _

雇主是指个人作为雇员为其提供或已经提供任何性质的任何服务的任何个人或组织。 “雇主”一词不仅包括从事贸易或商业活动的个人和组织，还包括免征所得税的组织，例如宗教和慈善组织、教育机构、俱乐部、社会组织和社团。它还包括美国、美国、波多黎各和哥伦比亚特区政府及其机构、部门和政治部门。

Two special definitions of employer that may have considerable application to nonresident aliens are:  
雇主的两个特殊定义可能对非居民外国人有很大的应用：

*   An employer includes any person paying wages for a nonresident alien individual, foreign partnership, or foreign corporation not engaged in trade or business in the United States (including Puerto Rico as if a part of the United States), and  
    雇主包括为不在美国（包括波多黎各，如同美国的一部分）从事贸易或业务的非居民外国人、外国合伙企业或外国公司支付工资的任何人，以及
    
*   An employer includes any person who has control of the payment of wages for services that are performed for another person who does not have that control.  
    雇主包括对为不具有这种控制权的另一人提供的服务的工资支付有控制权的任何人。
    

For example, if a trust pays wages, such as certain types of pensions, supplemental unemployment pay, or retired pay, and the person for whom the services were performed has no legal control over the payment of the wages, the trust is the employer.  
例如，如果信托支付工资，例如某些类型的养老金、补充失业金或退休工资，并且接受服务的人对工资的支付没有法律控制权，则信托就是雇主。

These special definitions have no effect upon the relationship between an alien employee and the actual employer when determining whether the pay received is considered to be wages.  
在确定收到的工资是否被视为工资时，这些特殊定义对外籍雇员与实际雇主之间的关系没有影响。

If an employer–employee relationship exists, the employer ordinarily must withhold the income tax from wage payments by using the percentage method or wage bracket tables as shown in Pub. 15-T.  
如果存在雇主与雇员关系，雇主通常必须使用百分比法或工资等级表从工资支付中预扣所得税，如 Pub. 15-T。

**Pay that is not wages.**

Employment for which the pay is not considered wages (for graduated income tax withholding) includes, but is not limited to, the following items.

  

**支付的不是工资。** 

工资不被视为工资（用于分级所得税预扣）的就业包括但不限于以下项目。

*   Agricultural labor if the total cash wages paid to an individual worker during the year is less than $150 and the total paid to all workers during the year is less than $2,500. But even if the total amount paid to all workers is $2,500 or more, wages of less than $150 per year paid to a worker are not subject to income tax withholding if certain conditions are met. For these conditions, see [Pub. 51 (Circular A)](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-51).  
    农业劳动力，如果当年支付给单个工人的现金工资总额少于 150 美元，且当年支付给所有工人的现金工资总额少于 2,500 美元。但即使支付给所有工人的总金额为 2,500 美元或以上，如果满足某些条件，每年支付给工人的工资低于 150 美元也无需预扣所得税。对于这些条件，请参阅[Pub。 51（通告A）](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-51) 。
    
*   Services of a household nature performed in or about the private home of an employer, or in or about the clubrooms or house of a local college club, fraternity, or sorority. A local college club, fraternity, or sorority does not include an alumni club or chapter and may not be operated primarily as a business enterprise. Examples of these services include those performed as a cook, janitor, housekeeper, governess, gardener, or houseparent.  
    在雇主的私人住宅内或周围，或者在当地大学俱乐部、兄弟会或联谊会的俱乐部房间或房屋内或周围进行的家庭性质的服务。当地大学俱乐部、兄弟会或联谊会不包括校友俱乐部或分会，并且不能主要作为商业企业运营。这些服务的例子包括作为厨师、看门人、管家、家庭女教师、园丁或家庭家长提供的服务。
    
*   Certain services performed outside the course of the employer's trade or business for which cash payment is less than $50 for the calendar quarter.  
    在雇主的贸易或业务过程之外提供的某些服务，在日历季度内支付的现金少于 50 美元。
    
*   Services performed as an employee of a foreign government, without regard to citizenship, residence, or where services are performed. These include services performed by ambassadors, other diplomatic and consular officers and employees, and nondiplomatic representatives. They do not include services for a U.S. or Puerto Rican corporation owned by a foreign government.  
    作为外国政府雇员提供的服务，无论公民身份、居住地或提供服务的地点如何。其中包括大使、其他外交和领事官员和雇员以及非外交代表提供的服务。它们不包括为外国政府拥有的美国或波多黎各公司提供的服务。
    
*   Services performed within or outside the United States by an employee or officer (regardless of citizenship or residence) of an international organization designated under the International Organizations Immunities Act.  
    由根据《国际组织豁免法》指定的国际组织的雇员或官员（无论公民身份或居住地）在美国境内或境外提供的服务。
    
*   Services performed by a duly ordained, commissioned, or licensed minister of a church, but only if performed in the exercise of the ministry and not as an employee of the United States, a U.S. territory, or a foreign government, or any of their political subdivisions. These also include services performed by a member of a religious order in carrying out duties required by that order.  
    由正式任命、委托或获得许可的教会牧师提供的服务，但前提是在履行职责时提供服务，而不是以美国、美国领土或外国政府或其任何政治机构的雇员身份提供服务细分。其中还包括宗教团体成员在履行该团体要求的职责时提供的服务。
    
*   Tips paid to an employee if they are paid in any medium other than cash or, if in cash, they amount to less than $20 in any calendar month in the course of employment.  
    向雇员支付的小费，如果以现金以外的任何方式支付，或者如果以现金支付，则在受雇期间的任何日历月内小费金额少于 20 美元。
    

_**Services performed outside the United States.**_

Compensation paid to a nonresident alien (other than a resident of Puerto Rico, discussed later) for services performed outside the United States is not considered wages and is not subject to withholding.

  

_**在美国境外提供的服务。** _

向非居民外国人（波多黎各居民除外，稍后讨论）支付的在美国境外提供服务的报酬不被视为工资，也无需预扣税款。

_**Special instructions for Form W-4.**_

A nonresident alien subject to wage withholding must give the employer a completed Form W-4 to enable the employer to figure how much income tax to withhold.

  

_**W-4 表的特别说明。** _

需缴纳工资预扣税的非居民外籍人士必须向雇主提供填妥的 W-4 表格，以便雇主计算应预扣多少所得税。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_A nonresident alien cannot claim exemption from withholding on Form W-4. Use Form 8233 to claim a tax treaty exemption from withholding. See_ _[Form 8233](#en_US_2024_publink1000224967 "Form 8233.")__, earlier._  
非居民外国人不能在 W-4 表上申请预扣税豁免。使用 8233 表格申请税收协定豁免预扣税。请参阅之前的 8233 表格。.

In completing Form W-4, nonresident aliens should use the following instructions instead of the instructions on Form W-4.  
在填写 W-4 表时，非居民外籍人士应使用以下说明，而不是 W-4 表上的说明。

1.  Check “Single or Married filing separately” on Step 1(c) (regardless of actual marital status).  
    勾选步骤 1(c) 中的“单身或已婚单独申报”（无论实际婚姻状况如何）。
    
2.  Write “Nonresident Alien” or “NRA” in the space below Step 4(c).  
    在步骤 4(c) 下面的空白处写下“非居民外国人”或“NRA”。
    

For more information, see [Notice 1392](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-notice-1392).  
有关详细信息，请参阅[通知 1392](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-notice-1392) 。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/taxtip.gif)
_Nonresident alien employees are not required to request an additional withholding amount, but they can choose to have an additional amount withheld.  
非居民外籍雇员无需申请额外预扣金额，但他们可以选择额外预扣金额。_.

**Determining amount to withhold.**

Employers are required to add an amount to the wages of a nonresident alien employee solely for the purpose of calculating income tax withholding. The specific amounts depend on the payroll period. These amounts can be found in _Withholding Adjustment for Nonresident Alien Employees_ in the _Introduction_ of [Pub. 15-T](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-15-t). This adjustment does not apply to students and business apprentices from India.

  

**确定扣留金额。** 

雇主必须在非居民外籍雇员的工资中添加一定金额，仅用于计算所得税预扣税。具体金额取决于工资发放期间。这些金额可以在《酒吧_介绍_》中的_非居民外籍雇员预扣税调整_中找到[。 15-T](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-15-t) 。这一调整不适用于来自印度的学生和商业学徒。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_Do not include the additional amount on the employee's Form W-2, Wage and Tax Statement.  
请勿将额外金额纳入员工的 W-2 表、工资和税表中。_.

**Reporting requirements for wages and withheld taxes paid to nonresident aliens.**

The employer must report the amount of wages and deposits of withheld income and social security and Medicare taxes by filing Form 941. Household employers should see [Pub. 926](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-926), for information on reporting and paying employment taxes on wages paid to household employees.

  

**向非居民外国人支付的工资和预扣税的报告要求。** 

雇主必须通过提交表格 941 报告工资和预扣收入存款以及社会保障和医疗保险税。家庭雇主应参阅[Pub. 926](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-926) ，了解有关向家庭雇员支付的工资报告和缴纳就业税的信息。

_**Form W-2.**_

The employer must also report on Form W-2 the wages subject to chapter 3 withholding and the withheld taxes. You must give copies of this form to the employee. If the employee submits Form 8233 to claim exemption from withholding under a tax treaty, the wages are reported on Form 1042-S and not in box 1 of Form W-2. Wages exempt under a tax treaty may still be reported in the state and local wages boxes of Form W-2 if such wages are subject to state and local taxation. For more information, see the instructions for these forms.

  

_**W-2 表格。** _

雇主还必须在 W-2 表上报告需缴纳第 3 章预扣税的工资和预扣税。您必须将此表格的副本提供给员工。如果员工提交 8233 表以申请根据税收协定免予预扣税，则工资将在表 1042-S 上报告，而不是在表 W-2 的方框 1 中报告。如果根据税收协定免税的工资需要缴纳州和地方税，则仍可在表格 W-2 的州和地方工资栏中报告此类工资。有关更多信息，请参阅这些表格的说明。

**Trust fund recovery penalty.**

If you are a person responsible for withholding, accounting for, or depositing or paying employment taxes, and willfully fail to do so, you can be held liable for a penalty equal to the full amount of the unpaid trust fund tax, plus interest. A responsible person for this purpose can be an officer of a corporation, a partner, a sole proprietor, or an employee of any form of business. A trustee or agent with authority over the funds of the business can also be held responsible for the penalty.

  

**信托基金追回罚金。** 

如果您是负责预扣、记账、存入或缴纳就业税的人，但故意不这样做，您可能会被处以相当于未缴信托基金税全额加上利息的罚款。为此目的的负责人可以是公司的高级管理人员、合伙人、独资经营者或任何形式企业的雇员。有权管理企业资金的受托人或代理人也可能要承担处罚责任。

“Willfully” in this case means voluntarily, consciously, and intentionally. You are acting willfully if you pay other expenses of the business instead of the withholding taxes.  
这里的“故意”是指自愿、自觉、故意。如果您支付企业的其他费用而不是预扣税，则您的行为属于故意行为。

**Social security and Medicare tax.**

In most cases, the employer must also withhold Federal Insurance Contributions Act (FICA) tax and file Form 941. In certain cases, wages paid to students and railroad and agricultural workers are exempt from FICA tax. Wages paid to nonresident alien students, teachers, researchers, trainees, and other nonresident aliens in “F-1,” “J-1,”“ M-1,” or “Q” nonimmigrant status are not subject to FICA. See [Pub. 15-T](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-15-t) for the rules on withholding.

  

**社会保障和医疗保险税。** 

在大多数情况下，雇主还必须预扣联邦保险缴款法 (FICA) 税并提交 941 表格。在某些情况下，支付给学生、铁路和农业工人的工资免征 FICA 税。支付给具有“F-1”、“J-1”、“M-1”或“Q”非移民身份的非居民外籍学生、教师、研究人员、实习生和其他非居民外籍人士的工资不受 FICA 约束。参见[酒吧。 15-T](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-15-t)预扣税规则。

In addition to withholding Medicare tax at 1.45%, you must withhold a 0.9% Additional Medicare Tax from wages you pay in excess of $200,000 in a calendar year. See [Pub.15](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-15) for more information.  
除了按 1.45% 预扣医疗保险税外，您还必须从您在一个日历年支付的超过 200,000 美元的工资中预扣 0.9% 的附加医疗保险税。更多信息请参见[Pub.15](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-15) 。

**Federal unemployment tax (FUTA).**

The employer must pay FUTA tax and file Form 940. Only the employer pays this tax; it is not deducted from the employee's wages. In certain cases, wages paid to students and railroad and agricultural workers are exempt from FUTA tax. For more information, see the [Instructions for Form 940](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-940).

Wages paid to nonresident alien students, teachers, researchers, trainees, and other nonresident aliens in “F-1,” “J-1,” “M-1,” or “Q” nonimmigrant status are not subject to FUTA tax.

  

**联邦失业税（FUTA）。** 

雇主必须缴纳 FUTA 税并提交 940 表格。只有雇主缴纳此税；它不从雇员的工资中扣除。在某些情况下，支付给学生、铁路和农业工人的工资可免征 FUTA 税。如需了解更多信息，请参阅[940 表格说明](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-940)。

支付给具有“F-1”、“J-1”、“M-1”或“Q”非移民身份的非居民外籍学生、教师、研究人员、实习生和其他非居民外籍人士的工资无需缴纳 FUTA 税。

**Pay for dependent personal services (Income Code 18).**

Dependent personal services are personal services performed in the United States by a nonresident alien individual as an employee rather than as an independent contractor.

Pay for dependent personal services is subject to chapter 3 withholding and reporting as follows.

  

**支付受抚养个人服务费用（收入代码 18）。** 

受抚养个人服务是非居民外国人作为雇员而不是独立承包商在美国提供的个人服务。

受抚养个人服务费用须遵守第 3 章规定的预扣税和报告如下。

_**Graduated rates.**_

Ordinarily, you must withhold on pay (wages) for dependent personal services using graduated rates. The nonresident alien must complete Form W-4, as discussed earlier under [_Special instructions for Form W-4_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224986 "Special instructions for Form W-4."), and you must report wages and income tax withheld on Form W-2. However, you do not have to withhold if any of the following four exceptions applies.

  

_**毕业率。** _

通常，您必须使用累进税率预扣受抚养个人服务的工资（工资）。非居民外籍人士必须填写 W-4 表（如前面在[_表 W-4 的特别说明_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224986 "Special instructions for Form W-4.")中所述），并且您必须在表 W-2 上报告预扣的工资和所得税。但是，如果以下四种例外情况之一适用，您不必扣留。

_**Exception 1.**_

Compensation paid for labor or personal services performed in the United States is deemed not to be income from sources within the United States and is exempt from U.S. income tax if:

  

_**例外1。** _

在美国境内提供的劳动或个人服务所支付的报酬被视为不是来自美国境内的收入，并且在以下情况下可免征美国所得税：

1.  The labor or services are performed by a nonresident alien temporarily present in the United States for a period or periods not exceeding a total of 90 days during the tax year;  
    劳动或服务由非居民外国人在纳税年度内暂时居住在美国一段时间或总计不超过 90 天的情况下执行；
    
2.  The total pay does not exceed $3,000; and  
    工资总额不超过3000美元；和
    
3.  The pay is for labor or services performed as an employee of, or under a contract with:  
    该工资是针对作为以下人员或根据与以下人员签订的合同所提供的劳动或服务而支付的：
    
    1.  A nonresident alien individual, foreign partnership, or foreign corporation that is not engaged in a trade or business in the United States; or  
        不在美国从事贸易或业务的非居民外国人、外国合伙企业或外国公司；或者
        
    2.  A U.S. citizen or resident alien individual, a domestic partnership, or a domestic corporation, if the labor or services are performed for an office or place of business maintained in a foreign country or in a territory of the United States by this individual, partnership, or corporation.  
        美国公民或外籍居民个人、国内合伙企业或国内公司，如果该个人、合伙企业为在外国或美国境内设立的办事处或营业场所提供劳务或服务，或公司。
        
    

If the total pay is more than $3,000, the entire amount is income from sources in the United States and is subject to U.S. tax.  
如果总工资超过 3,000 美元，则全部金额都是来自美国的收入，并需缴纳美国税。

Also, compensation paid for labor or services performed in the United States by a nonresident alien in connection with the individual's temporary presence in the United States as a regular member of the crew of a foreign vessel engaged in transportation between the United States and a foreign country or a U.S. territory is not income from sources within the United States.  
此外，非居民外国人作为从事美国和外国之间运输的外国船只的正式船员暂时居住在美国，在美国提供的劳动或服务而支付的补偿或美国领土不是来自美国境内的收入。

_**Exception 2.**_

Compensation paid by a foreign employer to a nonresident alien for the period the alien is temporarily present in the United States on an “F,” “J,” or “Q” visa is exempt from U.S. income tax. For this purpose, a foreign employer means:

  

_**例外2。** _

外国雇主向持有“F”、“J”或“Q”签证的非居民外国人临时居留美国期间支付的报酬免征美国所得税。为此目的，外国雇主是指：

*   A nonresident alien individual, foreign partnership, or foreign corporation; or  
    非居民外国人、外国合伙企业或外国公司；或者
    
*   An office or place of business maintained in a foreign country or in a U.S. territory by a domestic corporation, a domestic partnership, or an individual U.S. citizen or resident.  
    由国内公司、国内合伙企业或美国公民或居民个人在外国或美国境内设立的办事处或营业场所。
    

You can exempt the payment from withholding if you can reliably associate the payment with a Form W-8BEN containing the TIN of the payee.  
如果您能够可靠地将付款与包含收款人 TIN 的 W-8BEN 表格关联起来，则您可以免除预扣付款。

_**Exception 3.**_

Compensation paid to certain residents of Canada or Mexico who enter or leave the United States at frequent intervals is not subject to withholding. These aliens must either:

  

_**例外3。** _

向经常进出美国的某些加拿大或墨西哥居民支付的报酬无需预扣。这些外国人必须：

*   Perform duties in transportation services (such as a railroad, bus, truck, ferry, steamboat, aircraft, or other type) between the United States and Canada or Mexico; or  
    履行美国与加拿大或墨西哥之间运输服务（例如铁路、公共汽车、卡车、渡轮、汽船、飞机或其他类型）的职责；或者
    
*   Perform duties connected with an international project, relating to the construction, maintenance, or operation of a waterway, viaduct, dam, or bridge crossed by, or crossing, the boundary between the United States and Canada or the boundary between the United States and Mexico.  
    履行与国际项目相关的职责，涉及跨越美国和加拿大边界或美国和墨西哥边界的水道、高架桥、水坝或桥梁的建设、维护或运营。
    

To qualify for the exemption from withholding during a tax year, a Canadian or Mexican resident must give the employer a statement with the employee's name, address, and identification number, and certifying that the resident:  
为了有资格在纳税年度内获得预扣税豁免，加拿大或墨西哥居民必须向雇主提供一份包含雇员姓名、地址和身份证号码的声明，并证明该居民：

*   Is not a U.S. citizen or resident;  
    不是美国公民或居民；
    
*   Is a resident of Canada or Mexico, whichever applies; and  
    是加拿大或墨西哥的居民（以适用者为准）；和
    
*   Expects to perform the described duties during the tax year in question.  
    预计在相关纳税年度履行所述职责。
    

The statement can be in any form, but it must be dated and signed by the employee and must include a written declaration that it is made under penalties of perjury.  
该声明可以采用任何形式，但必须注明日期并由员工签名，并且必须包含一份书面声明，表明该声明是在作伪证的处罚下做出的。

_**Canadian and Mexican residents employed entirely within the United States.**_

Neither the transportation service exception nor the international projects exception applies to the pay of a resident of Canada or Mexico who is employed entirely within the United States and who commutes from a home in Canada or Mexico to work in the United States. If an individual works at a fixed point or points in the United States (such as a factory, store, office, or designated area or areas), the wages for services performed as an employee for an employer are subject to graduated withholding.

  

_**完全在美国境内受雇的加拿大和墨西哥居民。** _

运输服务例外和国际项目例外均不适用于完全在美国境内受雇且从加拿大或墨西哥的家中通勤到美国工作的加拿大或墨西哥居民的工资。如果个人在美国的一个或多个固定点（例如工厂、商店、办公室或指定区域）工作，则作为雇员为雇主提供的服务的工资需要进行分级预扣税。

_**Exception 4.**_

Compensation paid for services performed in Puerto Rico by a nonresident alien who is a resident of Puerto Rico for an employer (other than the United States or one of its agencies) is not subject to withholding.

  

_**例外4。** _

作为波多黎各居民的非居民外国人为雇主（美国或其机构之一除外）在波多黎各提供的服务支付的报酬无需预扣。

Compensation paid for either of the following types of services is not subject to withholding if the alien does not expect to be a resident of Puerto Rico during the entire tax year.  
如果外国人预计在整个纳税年度内不会成为波多黎各居民，则为以下任一类型的服务支付的报酬无需预扣税款。

*   Services performed outside the United States but not in Puerto Rico by a nonresident alien who is a resident of Puerto Rico for an employer other than the United States or one of its agencies.  
    由身为波多黎各居民的非居民外国人在美国境外但不在波多黎各为美国或其机构之一以外的雇主提供的服务。
    
*   Services performed outside the United States by a nonresident alien who is a resident of Puerto Rico, as an employee of the United States or any of its agencies.  
    由身为波多黎各居民的非居民外国人作为美国或其任何机构的雇员在美国境外提供的服务。
    

To qualify for the exemption from withholding for any tax year, the employee must give the employer a statement showing the employee's name and address and certifying that the employee:  
要获得任何纳税年度的预扣税豁免资格，雇员必须向雇主提供一份声明，显示雇员的姓名和地址，并证明雇员：

*   Is not a citizen or resident of the United States, and  
    不是美国公民或居民，并且
    
*   Is a resident of Puerto Rico who does not expect to be a resident for that entire tax year.  
    是波多黎各居民，但预计不会在整个纳税年度成为居民。
    

The statement must be signed and dated by the employee and contain a written declaration that it is made under penalties of perjury.  
该声明必须由员工签名并注明日期，并包含一份书面声明，表明该声明是根据伪证罪处罚的。

_**Tax treaties.**_

Pay for dependent personal services under some tax treaties is exempt from U.S. income tax only if both the employer and the employee are treaty country residents and the nonresident alien employee performs the services while temporarily living in the United States (usually for not more than 183 days). Other treaties provide for exemption from U.S. tax on pay for dependent personal services if the employer is any foreign resident and the employee is a treaty country resident and the nonresident alien employee performs the services while temporarily in the United States. See [_Tax Treaties_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties"), later, for information about treaty benefits.

  

_**税务条约。** _

仅当雇主和雇员均为条约国居民且非居民外籍雇员在美国临时居住（通常不超过 183 天）期间提供服务时，根据某些税收协定支付的受抚养个人服务费用才可免征美国所得税）。其他条约规定，如果雇主是任何外国居民，雇员是条约国居民，并且非居民外籍雇员在美国临时提供服务，则美国对受抚养个人服务的工资免税。有关[_税收协定优惠的信息，请参阅后面的税收协定_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties")。

**Pay for teaching (Income Code 19).**

This category is given a separate income code number because some tax treaties exempt a teacher from tax for a limited number of years. Pay for teaching means payments to a nonresident alien professor, teacher, or researcher by a U.S. university or other accredited educational institution for teaching or research work at the institution.

  

**支付教学费用（收入代码 19）。** 

此类别有一个单独的收入代码编号，因为某些税收协定允许教师在有限的年限内免税。教学报酬是指美国大学或其他认可的教育机构向非居民外籍教授、教师或研究员支付在该机构从事教学或研究工作的费用。

_**Graduated rates.**_

Graduated withholding of income tax usually applies to all wages, salaries, and other pay for teaching and research paid by a U.S. educational institution during the period the nonresident alien is teaching or performing research at the institution.

  

_**毕业率。** _

所得税分级预扣通常适用于非居民外国人在美国教育机构任教或从事研究期间支付的所有工资、薪水和其他教学和研究费用。

_**Social security and Medicare tax.**_

A nonresident alien temporarily in the United States on an “F-1,” “J-1,” “M-1,” or “Q-1” visa is not subject to social security and Medicare taxes on pay for services performed to carry out the purpose for which the alien was admitted to the United States. Social security and Medicare taxes should not be withheld or paid on this amount.

  

_**社会保障和医疗保险税。** _

持有“F-1”、“J-1”、“M-1”或“Q-1”签证暂时居住在美国的非居民外国人无需缴纳社会保障税和医疗保险税。实现外国人被允许进入美国的目的。不应就此金额预扣或缴纳社会保障税和医疗保险税。

**Example.**

A nonresident alien is issued a visa to teach for a university. While in the United States, they take a part-time job working for a chemical company. The wages earned while teaching at the university are exempt from social security and Medicare taxes. The wages earned at the chemical company are subject to social security and Medicare taxes.

  

**例子。** 

非居民外国人获得在大学任教的签证。在美国期间，他们在一家化学公司做兼职。在大学教书期间赚取的工资免征社会保障税和医疗保险税。化学公司赚取的工资需缴纳社会保障税和医疗保险税。

If an alien is considered a resident alien, as discussed earlier, that pay is subject to social security and Medicare taxes even though the alien is still in one of the nonimmigrant statuses mentioned above. This rule also applies to FUTA (unemployment) taxes paid by the employer. Teachers, researchers, and other employees temporarily present in the United States on other nonimmigrant visas or in refugee or asylee immigration status are fully liable for social security and Medicare taxes unless an exemption applies from one of the totalization agreements in force between the United States and several other nations.  
如果外国人被视为居民外国人，如前所述，即使该外国人仍处于上述非移民身份之一，该工资仍需缴纳社会保障税和医疗保险税。该规则也适用于雇主缴纳的 FUTA（失业）税。持有其他非移民签证或难民或政治庇护移民身份暂时居住在美国的教师、研究人员和其他雇员应对社会保障税和医疗保险税承担全部责任，除非美国和美国之间有效的总和协议之一适用豁免。其他几个国家。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/compute.gif)
     _The Social Security Administration (SSA) publishes the complete texts and explanatory pamphlets of the totalization agreements, which are available by calling 410-965-7306 or by going to_ [SSA.gov/international/totalization\_agreements.html](http://www.ssa.gov/international/totalization_agreements.html)  
_社会保障管理局 (SSA) 发布了总计协议的完整文本和解释小册子，可通过拨打 410-965-7306 或访问_[SSA.gov/international/totalization\_agreements.html](http://www.ssa.gov/international/totalization_agreements.html)获取。[](http://www.ssa.gov/international/totalization_agreements.html)_._.

_**Tax treaties.**_

Under most tax treaties, pay for teaching or research is exempt from U.S. income tax and from withholding for a specified period of time when paid to a professor, teacher, or researcher who was a resident of the treaty country immediately prior to entry into the United States and who is not a citizen of the United States. The U.S. educational institution paying the compensation must report the amount of compensation paid each year that is exempt from tax under a tax treaty on Form 1042-S. See [_Tax Treaties_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties"), later, for information about treaty benefits. The employer should also report the compensation in the state and local wages boxes of Form W-2 if the wages are subject to state and local taxes, or in the social security and Medicare wages boxes of Form W-2 if the wages are subject to social security and Medicare taxes.

Claimants must give you either Form W-8BEN or Form 8233, as applicable, to obtain these treaty benefits.

  

_**税务条约。** _

根据大多数税收协定，向在进入美国之前是协定国居民的教授、教师或研究人员支付的教学或研究费用可免征美国所得税，并在指定期限内免予预扣。州以及非美国公民。支付补偿的美国教育机构必须在 1042-S 表格上报告每年根据税收协定免税支付的补偿金额。有关[_税收协定优惠的信息，请参阅后面的税收协定_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties")。如果工资需缴纳州和地方税，雇主还应在表 W-2 的州和地方工资栏中申报补偿；如果工资需缴纳州和地方税，雇主还应在表 W-2 的社会保障和医疗保险工资栏中申报补偿。社会保障和医疗保险税。

索赔人必须向您提供表格 W-8BEN 或表格 8233（如果适用）才能获得这些条约优惠。

**Pay during studying and training (Income Code 20).**

This category refers to pay (as contrasted with remittances, allowances, or other forms of scholarships or fellowship grants—see [_Scholarships and Fellowship Grants Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224951 "Scholarships and Fellowship Grants Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding (Income Code 16)"), earlier) for personal services performed while a nonresident alien is temporarily in the United States as a student, trainee, or apprentice, or while acquiring technical, professional, or business experience.

  

**学习和培训期间的工资（收入代码 20）。** 

此类别是指非居民外国人暂时在美国期间提供的个人服务的报酬（与汇款、津贴或其他形式的奖学金或助学金相比——请参阅[_前面第 3 章预扣税款规定的奖学金和助学金_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224951 "Scholarships and Fellowship Grants Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding (Income Code 16)")）。学生、实习生或学徒，或在获得技术、专业或商业经验时。

_**Graduated rates.**_

Wages, salaries, or other compensation paid to a nonresident alien student, trainee, or apprentice for labor or personal services performed in the United States are subject to graduated withholding.

  

_**毕业率。** _

向在美国提供劳动或个人服务的非居民外国学生、实习生或学徒支付的工资、薪金或其他报酬须缴纳分级预扣税。

_**Social security and Medicare tax.**_

A nonresident alien temporarily in the United States on an “F-1,” “J-1,” “M-1,” or “Q-1” visa is not subject to social security and Medicare taxes on pay for services performed to carry out the purpose for which the alien was admitted to the United States. Social security and Medicare taxes should not be withheld or paid on this amount. This exemption from social security and Medicare taxes also applies to employment performed under Curricular Practical Training and Optional Practical Training, on or off campus, by foreign students in “F-1,” “J-1,” “M-1,” or “Q” status as long as the employment is authorized by the U.S. Citizenship and Immigration Services.

  

_**社会保障和医疗保险税。** _

持有“F-1”、“J-1”、“M-1”或“Q-1”签证暂时居住在美国的非居民外国人无需缴纳社会保障税和医疗保险税。实现外国人被允许进入美国的目的。不应就此金额预扣或缴纳社会保障税和医疗保险税。社会保障税和医疗保险税的豁免也适用于外国学生在“F-1”、“J-1”、“M-1”或“校内或校外”根据课程实践培训和可选实践培训进行的就业只要就业得到美国公民及移民服务局的授权，即为“Q”身份。

**Example.**

A nonresident alien is admitted to the United States to study surveying. As part of the course, they apprentice to a surveyor. The nonresident also works part-time at a restaurant to supplement their income. The wages earned as an apprentice are not subject to social security and Medicare taxes. The wages and tips earned at the restaurant are subject to social security and Medicare taxes.

  

**例子。** 

非居民外国人被允许进入美国学习测量。作为课程的一部分，他们向测量员当学徒。非居民还在餐厅兼职以贴补收入。作为学徒赚取的工资无需缴纳社会保障税和医疗保险税。在餐厅赚取的工资和小费需缴纳社会保障税和医疗保险税。

If an alien is considered a resident alien, as discussed earlier, that pay is subject to social security and Medicare taxes even though the alien is still in one of the nonimmigrant statuses mentioned above. This rule also applies to FUTA (unemployment) taxes paid by the employer.  
如果外国人被视为居民外国人，如前所述，即使该外国人仍处于上述非移民身份之一，该工资仍需缴纳社会保障税和医疗保险税。该规则也适用于雇主缴纳的 FUTA（失业）税。

Any student who is enrolled and regularly attending classes at a school may be exempt from social security, Medicare, and FUTA taxes on pay for services performed for that school. See Pub.15.  
任何在学校注册并定期上课的学生均可免除为该学校提供的服务支付的社会保障税、医疗保险税和 FUTA 税。参见Pub.15。

_**Tax treaties.**_

Certain tax treaties provide a limited exemption from U.S. income tax and from withholding on compensation paid to nonresident alien students or trainees during training in the United States for a limited period. In addition, some treaties provide an exemption from tax and withholding for compensation paid by the U.S. Government or its contractor to a nonresident alien student or trainee who is temporarily present in the United States as a participant in a program sponsored by the U.S. Government. See [_Tax Treaties_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties"), later, for information about treaty benefits. However, a withholding agent who is a U.S. resident, a U.S. Government agency, or its contractor must report the amount of pay on Form 1042-S.

Claimants must give you either Form W-8BEN or Form 8233, as applicable, to obtain these treaty benefits.

  

_**税务条约。** _

某些税收协定提供有限的美国所得税豁免，以及对在美国培训期间向非居民外国学生或受训人员支付的补偿的预扣。此外，一些条约还规定美国政府或其承包商向作为美国政府资助项目的参与者暂时留在美国的非居民外国学生或实习生支付的补偿可免税和预扣税。有关[_税收协定优惠的信息，请参阅后面的税收协定_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties")。但是，身为美国居民、美国政府机构或其承包商的扣缴义务人必须在 1042-S 表格中报告付款金额。

索赔人必须向您提供表格 W-8BEN 或表格 8233（如果适用）才能获得这些条约优惠。

#### Artists and Athletes(Income Codes 42 and 43)  
艺术家和运动员（收入代码 42 和 43）

Because many tax treaties contain a provision for pay to artists and athletes, a separate category is assigned these payments for chapter 3 withholding purposes. This category includes payments made for performances by public entertainers (such as theater, motion picture, radio, or television artists, or musicians) or athletes.  
由于许多税收协定都包含向艺术家和运动员付款的规定，因此出于第 3 章预扣税的目的，为这些付款分配了一个单独的类别。此类别包括为公共演艺人员（例如戏剧、电影、广播或电视艺术家或音乐家）或运动员的表演支付的费用。

Use Income Code 42 to report payments to nonresident alien athletes and entertainers (NRAAEs) who have not signed a central withholding agreement (CWA), discussed later. Use Income Code 43 to report payments to artists and athletes who have signed a CWA.  
使用收入代码 42 报告向未签署中央预扣税协议 (CWA) 的非居民外籍运动员和艺人 (NRAAE) 支付的款项（稍后讨论）。使用收入代码 43 报告向签署 CWA 的艺术家和运动员支付的款项。

**Income Code 42.**

You must withhold tax at a 30% rate on payments to artists and athletes for services performed as independent contractors. See [_Pay for independent personal services_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224969 "Pay for independent personal services (Income Code 17)."), earlier, for more information. You must withhold tax at graduated rates on payments to artists and athletes for services performed as employees. See [_Pay for dependent personal services_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224997 "Pay for dependent personal services (Income Code 18)."), earlier, for more information. However, in any situation where the nature of the relationship between the payer of the income and the artist or athlete is not ascertainable, you should withhold at a rate of 30%.

  

**收入代码 42。** 

对于作为独立承包商提供的服务向艺术家和运动员支付的费用，您必须按 30% 的税率预扣税款。有关详细信息，请参阅前面的[_独立个人服务付费_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224969 "Pay for independent personal services (Income Code 17).")。您必须按照累进税率对艺术家和运动员作为雇员提供的服务的报酬预扣税款。有关详细信息，请参阅前面的[_“为受抚养个人服务付费”_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224997 "Pay for dependent personal services (Income Code 18).") 。然而，在收入支付者与艺术家或运动员之间关系性质无法确定的任何情况下，您应按 30% 的税率预扣税款。

**Income Code 43.**

NRAAEs who perform or participate in events in the United States can request a CWA for a lower rate of withholding. A CWA is an agreement entered into by the athlete or entertainer, a designated withholding agent, and the IRS. Under no circumstances will a CWA reduce taxes withheld to less than the anticipated amount of income tax liability.

We’ve temporarily waived the income requirement for which form to use when applying for a CWA. Form 13930-A is currently unavailable. While the waiver is in effect, individuals with income below $10,000 can apply for a CWA using Form 13930, Instructions on How to Apply for a Central Withholding Agreement PDF. For more information on how to apply for a CWA, see Form 13930.

For more information on the CWA program, go to [IRS.gov/Individuals/International-Taxpayers/Central-Withholding-Agreements](https://www.irs.gov/Individuals/International-Taxpayers/Central-Withholding-Agreements).

  

**收入代码 43。** 

在美国举办或参加活动的 NRAAE 可以申请 CWA 以获得较低的预扣税率。 CWA 是由运动员或演艺人员、指定扣缴义务人以及 IRS 签订的协议。在任何情况下，CWA 都不会将预扣税款减少至低于预期的所得税负债金额。

我们暂时免除了申请 CWA 时使用哪种表格的收入要求。 13930-A 表格目前不可用。在豁免生效期间，收入低于 10,000 美元的个人可以使用 13930 表格《如何申请中央预扣税协议说明》PDF 申请 CWA。有关如何申请 CWA 的更多信息，请参阅表格 13930。

有关 CWA 计划的更多信息，请访问[IRS.gov/Individuals/International-Taxpayers/Central-Withholding-Agreements](https://www.irs.gov/Individuals/International-Taxpayers/Central-Withholding-Agreements) 。

**Tax treaties.**

Under many tax treaties, compensation paid to public entertainers or athletes for services performed in the United States is exempt from U.S. income tax if the artist or athlete derives receipts for the tax year concerned, including expenses reimbursed to them or borne on their behalf, not in excess of $10,000, or in more recent treaties, $20,000. See [_Tax Treaties_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties"), later, for information about treaty benefits.

  

**税务条约。** 

根据许多税收协定，如果艺术家或运动员在相关纳税年度获得收入，包括向他们报销或代表他们承担的费用，则支付给在美国提供服务的公共演艺人员或运动员的报酬可免征美国所得税。超过 10,000 美元，或者在最近的条约中为 20,000 美元。有关[_税收协定优惠的信息，请参阅后面的税收协定_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225127 "Tax Treaties")。

Employees and independent contractors may claim an exemption from withholding under a tax treaty by filing Form 8233. Often, however, you will have to withhold at the statutory rates on the total payments to the entertainer or athlete. This is because the exemption may be based upon factors that cannot be determined until after the end of the year.  
员工和独立承包商可以通过提交 8233 表格，根据税收协定要求免除预扣税。但是，您通常必须按法定税率预扣向演艺人员或运动员支付的总款项。这是因为豁免可能基于一些直到年底之后才能确定的因素。

#### Other Income其他收入

For the discussion of Income Codes 24, 25, and 26, see [_U.S. Real Property Interest_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest"), later. For the discussion of Income Code 27, see [_Publicly Traded Partnerships_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225085 "Publicly Traded Partnership Distributions (PTP Distributions)"), later.  
有关收入代码 24、25 和 26 的讨论，请参阅稍后的[_美国不动产利息_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest")。有关收入代码 27 的讨论，请参阅后面的[_公开交易合伙企业_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225085 "Publicly Traded Partnership Distributions (PTP Distributions)")。

**Gambling winnings (Income Code 28).**

In general, nonresident aliens are subject to chapter 3 withholding at 30% on the gross proceeds from gambling won in the United States if that income is not effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business and is not exempted by treaty. The tax withheld and winnings are reportable on Forms 1042 and 1042-S. Chapter 4 withholding does not apply to these proceeds.

  

**赌博奖金（收入代码 28）。** 

一般而言，如果非居民外国人在美国赢得的赌博总收入与美国贸易或业务没有实际联系且未获得条约豁免，则需缴纳第 3 章规定的 30% 预扣税。预扣税款和奖金需在 1042 和 1042-S 表格中报告。第 4 章的预扣税不适用于这些收益。

No tax is imposed on nonbusiness gambling income a nonresident alien wins playing blackjack, baccarat, craps, roulette, or big-6 wheel in the United States. A Form W-8BEN is not required to obtain the exemption from withholding, but a Form W-8BEN may be required for purposes of Form 1099 reporting and backup withholding. Gambling income that is not subject to chapter 3 withholding is not subject to reporting on Form 1042-S.  
非居民外国人在美国玩二十一点、百家乐、掷骰子、轮盘赌或大 6 轮盘赢得的非商业赌博收入不征税。获得预扣税豁免不需要 W-8BEN 表格，但为了 1099 表格报告和备用预扣税，可能需要 W-8BEN 表格。不受第 3 章预扣税约束的赌博收入无需在 1042-S 表格上报告。

Nonresident aliens are taxed at graduated rates on net gambling income won in the United States that is effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business.  
非居民外国人对在美国赢得的与美国贸易或业务有效相关的净赌博收入按累进税率纳税。

_**Tax treaties.**_

Gambling income of residents (as defined by treaty) of the following foreign countries is not taxable by the United States: Austria, Belgium, Bulgaria, Czech Republic, Denmark, Finland, France, Germany, Hungary, Iceland, Ireland, Italy, Japan, Latvia, Lithuania, Luxembourg, Netherlands, Russia, Slovak Republic, Slovenia, South Africa, Spain, Sweden, Tunisia, Turkey, Ukraine, and the United Kingdom.

  

_**税务条约。** _

以下国家/地区的居民（根据条约的定义）的赌博收入无需缴纳美国税：奥地利、比利时、保加利亚、捷克共和国、丹麦、芬兰、法国、德国、匈牙利、冰岛、爱尔兰、意大利、日本、拉脱维亚、立陶宛、卢森堡、荷兰、俄罗斯、斯洛伐克共和国、斯洛文尼亚、南非、西班牙、瑞典、突尼斯、土耳其、乌克兰和英国。

Gambling income of residents of Malta is taxed at 10%.  
马耳他居民的赌博收入按 10% 征税。

Claimants must give you a Form W-8BEN (with a U.S. or foreign TIN) to claim treaty benefits on gambling income that is not effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business. See [_U.S. or Foreign TINs_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225029 "U.S. or Foreign TINs"), later, for when you can accept a Form W-8BEN without a TIN.  
索赔人必须向您提供 W-8BEN 表格（带有美国或外国 TIN），以针对与美国贸易或业务没有实际联系的赌博收入申请税收协定优惠。请参阅稍后的[_美国或外国 TIN_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225029 "U.S. or Foreign TINs") ，了解何时可以接受没有 TIN 的 W-8BEN 表格。

**Transportation income.**

U.S. source gross transportation income (USSGTI), as defined in section 887, is not subject to 30% gross withholding tax, and chapter 4 withholding does not apply to this income. Transportation income is income from the use of a vessel or aircraft, whether owned, hired, or leased, or from the performance of services directly related to the use of a vessel or aircraft. U.S. source gross transportation income includes 50% of all transportation income from transportation that either begins or ends in the United States. USSGTI does not include transportation income of a foreign corporation taxable in a U.S. territory. The recipient of USSGTI must pay tax on it annually at the rate of 4% on Section I of Form 1120-F, unless the income is effectively connected with the conduct of a U.S. trade or business and is reportable on Section II of Form 1120-F. Special rules apply to determine if a foreign corporation's USSGTI is effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business.

  

**运输收入。** 

根据第 887 条的定义，美国来源的总运输收入 (USSGTI) 无需缴纳 30% 的总预扣税，并且第 4 章预扣税不适用于该收入。运输收入是指使用船舶或飞机（无论是自有、租用还是租赁）产生的收入，或者是来自提供与使用船舶或飞机直接相关的服务的收入。美国来源总运输收入包括始发于或结束于美国的所有运输收入的 50%。 USSGTI 不包括在美国境内应税的外国公司的运输收入。 USSGTI 的接收者必须每年按照 1120-F 表格第一部分的 4% 税率纳税，除非该收入与美国贸易或业务活动有实际联系，并且需要在 1120-F 表格第二部分进行报告。 F。适用特殊规则来确定外国公司的 USSGTI 是否与美国贸易或业务有有效联系。

_**Canadian truck and rail income.**_

Under Article VIII (Transportation) of the U.S.–Canada treaty, any U.S. source income derived by a Canadian company engaged in the operation of trucks or a railway as a common carrier or contract carrier, and attributable to the transportation of property between Canada and the United States, is exempt from tax in the United States, provided the company is otherwise eligible for treaty benefits. Payments for the use of trucks (including trailers) or railway rolling stock, or from the use, maintenance, or rental of containers (including trailers and related equipment for the transport of containers) used to transport property between Canada and the United States are also exempt from U.S. tax, provided the company is otherwise eligible for treaty benefits. Canadian companies must file Form 1120-F and Form 8833 to claim an exemption from tax for profits from their operating income. Canadian corporations are subject to chapter 3 withholding on rental payments for the use of such equipment in the United States and may claim an exemption on Form W8-BEN-E.

  

_**加拿大卡车和铁路收入。** _

根据美加条约第八条（运输），加拿大公司作为公共承运人或合同承运人从事卡车或铁路运营，并可归因于加拿大与加拿大之间的财产运输而获得的任何来自美国的收入。美国，如果公司有资格享受条约优惠，则在美国免税。使用卡车（包括拖车）或铁路机车车辆的费用，或者用于在加拿大和美国之间运输财产的集装箱（包括拖车和用于运输集装箱的相关设备）的使用、维护或租赁的费用也包括在内。如果公司有资格享受税收协定优惠，则可免缴美国税款。加拿大公司必须提交 1120-F 表格和 8833 表格，以申请营业收入利润免税。加拿大公司因在美国使用此类设备而需缴纳第 3 章租金预扣税，并可通过 W8-BEN-E 表格申请豁免。

_**Foreign freight charges or rental of equipment used outside the United States.**_

Payments for transportation of property, whether by ship, air, or truck, solely between points outside the United States or rental of tangible property in connection with transportation solely for use between points outside the United States is not U.S. source income and not subject to chapter 3 withholding.

  

_**国外运费或在美国境外使用的设备的租金。** _

仅在美国境外地点之间通过船舶、航空或卡车运输财产而支付的费用，或仅在美国境外地点之间使用的与运输相关的有形财产租赁费用，不属于美国来源收入，且不受章节约束3 扣缴。

**Payments to certain expatriates.**

Certain payments to nonresident aliens who are covered expatriates under section 877A(g)(1) are subject to withholding at 30%. In general, nonresident aliens are covered expatriates if they were U.S. citizens or long-term residents who renounced their citizenship or ceased to be long-term residents for U.S. tax purposes after June 16, 2008, and satisfied other tests for average annual net income tax or net worth. For more information on the definition of covered expatriates, see the Instructions for Form 8854.

  

**向某些外籍人士付款。** 

根据第 877A(g)(1) 条规定，向非居民外籍人士支付的某些款项需缴纳 30% 的预扣税。一般而言，如果非居民外籍人士是美国公民或长期居民，但在 2008 年 6 月 16 日之后出于美国纳税目的放弃公民身份或不再是长期居民，并且满足平均年净所得税的其他测试，则非居民外籍人士将受到外籍人士的保障或净资产。有关受保外籍人士定义的更多信息，请参阅 8854 表格的说明。

A covered expatriate should have provided you with Form W-8CE notifying you of their covered expatriate status and the fact that they may be subject to special tax rules with respect to certain items. For more information, see the Instructions for Form W-8CE.  
受保障的外籍人士应向您提供 W-8CE 表格，通知您其受保障的外籍人士身份以及他们可能需要遵守某些项目的特殊税收规则的事实。如需了解更多信息，请参阅 W-8CE 表格说明。

_**Eligible deferred compensation items (Income Code 38).**_

In general, you must withhold tax at a 30% rate on any payment of an eligible deferred compensation item paid to a covered expatriate. The amount subject to tax is the amount of the payment that would have been included in the nonresident alien's U.S. gross income if they had continued to be taxed as a U.S. citizen or resident.

  

_**符合资格的递延补偿项目（收入代码 38）。** _

一般来说，您必须对支付给受保外籍人士的任何合格递延补偿项目按 30% 的税率预扣税款。应纳税金额是指如果非居民外国人继续作为美国公民或居民纳税，则应计入其美国总收入的付款金额。

_**Distributions from a nongrantor trust (Income Code 39).**_

In general, you must withhold tax at a 30% rate on any direct or indirect distribution from a nongrantor trust. The amount subject to tax is the part of the distribution that would have been included in the nonresident alien's U.S. gross income if they had continued to be taxed as a U.S. citizen or resident. If the nonresident alien was not a beneficiary of the nongrantor trust on the day before they gave up their U.S. citizenship or long-term residence, you do not have to withhold tax. See section 7 of Notice 2009-85, 2009-45 I.R.B. 598, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2009-45\_IRB#NOT-2009-85](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2009-45_IRB#NOT-2009-85).

  

_**来自非授予人信托的分配（收入代码 39）。** _

一般来说，您必须对非授予人信托的任何直接或间接分配按 30% 的税率预扣税款。纳税金额是分配的一部分，如果非居民外国人继续作为美国公民或居民纳税，则该部分将计入其美国总收入中。如果非居民外国人在放弃美国公民身份或长期居留权的前一天不是非授予人信托的受益人，则您无需预扣税款。请参阅通知 2009-85、2009-45 IRB 598 的第 7 节，可在[IRS.gov/irb/2009-45\_IRB#NOT-2009-85](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2009-45_IRB#NOT-2009-85)上获取。

**Guarantee of indebtedness (Income Code 41).**

An amount paid to a foreign payee for the provision of a guarantee of indebtedness issued after September 27, 2010, may be subject to chapter 3 withholding. The amounts must be paid by one of the following.

  

**债务担保（收入法典 41）。** 

为提供 2010 年 9 月 27 日之后签发的债务担保而向外国收款人支付的金额可能需要缴纳第 3 章预扣税。金额必须由以下其中之一支付。

1.  A noncorporate U.S. resident.  
    非公司美国居民。
    
2.  A domestic corporation.国内法人。
    
3.  Any foreign person if the amount paid is connected with income that is effectively connected, or treated as effectively connected, with a U.S. trade or business.  
    任何外国人，如果支付的金额与与美国贸易或业务有实际联系或被视为有效联系的收入有关。
    

An indirect payment includes a payment by a foreign bank to a foreign corporation for the foreign corporation's guarantee of indebtedness owed to the foreign bank by the foreign corporation's domestic subsidiary, where the cost of the guarantee fee is passed on to the domestic subsidiary through additional interest charged on the indebtedness.  
间接支付是指外国银行为外国公司境内子公司欠外国银行债务提供担保而向外国公司支付的款项，其中担保费成本通过额外利息转嫁给境内子公司被追究债务责任。

The amounts described above for a guarantee of indebtedness are withholdable payments, such that chapter 4 withholding may apply absent an exclusion from withholding under chapter 4.  
上述债务担保金额属于应预扣付款，因此，如果没有第 4 章规定的预扣税除外，则可以适用第 4 章预扣税。

**Other income (Income Code 23).**

Use this category to report U.S. source FDAP income that is not reportable under any of the other income categories. Examples of income that may be reportable under this category are commissions, insurance proceeds, patronage distributions, prizes, and racing purses.

  

**其他收入（收入代码 23）。** 

使用此类别报告在任何其他收入类别下均不可报告的美国来源 FDAP 收入。在此类别下可报告的收入示例包括佣金、保险收益、赞助分配、奖品和赛车奖金。

As discussed earlier under [_Amounts Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding_](#en_US_2024_publink100015523 "Amounts Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding"), every kind of FDAP income from U.S. sources that is not effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business is subject to chapter 3 withholding unless the income is specifically exempt under the Internal Revenue Code or a tax treaty. You must generally withhold at the 30% rate on this income. As a payment of U.S. source FDAP is generally a withholdable payment, you should review Regulations section 1.1473-1(a) (definition of withholdable payment) to determine if the payment is excluded from the definition of a withholdable payment.  
正如前面[_第 3 章规定的预扣税金额_](#en_US_2024_publink100015523 "Amounts Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding")中所讨论的，来自美国且与美国贸易或业务没有实际联系的每一种 FDAP 收入均须缴纳第 3 章预扣税，除非该收入根据《国内税收法》或税收特别豁免条约。您通常必须按 30% 的税率对该收入进行预扣税。由于美国来源 FDAP 的付款通常是可预扣付款，因此您应查看法规第 1.1473-1(a) 条（可预扣付款的定义），以确定该付款是否被排除在可预扣付款的定义之外。

#### Foreign Governments and Certain Other Foreign Organizations  
外国政府和某些其他外国组织

Investment income earned by a foreign government is not included in the gross income of the foreign government and is not subject to chapter 3 withholding. The term foreign government means an integral part of a foreign government or an entity that is controlled by a foreign government. See Temporary Regulations section 1.892-2T. Investment income means income from investments in the United States in stocks, bonds, or other domestic securities, financial instruments held in the execution of governmental financial or monetary policy, and interest on money deposited by a foreign government in banks in the United States. A foreign government must provide a Form W-8EXP or, in the case of a payment made outside the United States to an offshore account, documentary evidence to obtain this exemption. Investment income paid to a foreign government is subject to reporting on Form 1042-S.  
外国政府赚取的投资收益不计入外国政府总收入，也不需缴纳第三章扣缴税款。 “外国政府”一词是指外国政府的组成部分或受外国政府控制的实体。请参阅临时规定第 1.892-2T 节。投资收入是指在美国投资于股票、债券或其他国内证券、为执行政府财政或货币政策而持有的金融工具以及外国政府存入美国银行的资金产生的利息收入。外国政府必须提供 W-8EXP 表，或者如果在美国境外向离岸账户付款，则必须提供文件证据才能获得此豁免。支付给外国政府的投资收入须按照 1042-S 表格进行报告。

The following types of income received by a foreign government are subject to chapter 3 withholding.  
外国政府收到的以下类型的收入须缴纳第 3 章预扣税。

1.  Income (including investment income) received from the conduct of a commercial activity or from sources other than those stated above.  
    通过商业活动或上述以外的来源获得的收入（包括投资收入）。
    
2.  Income received from a controlled commercial entity (including gain from the disposition of any interest in a controlled commercial entity) and income received by a controlled commercial entity.  
    从受控商业实体收到的收入（包括处置受控商业实体的任何权益所获得的收益）以及由受控商业实体收到的收入。
    
    If the foreign government is a partner in a partnership carrying on a trade or business in the United States, the ECTI allocable to the foreign government is considered derived from a controlled commercial activity and is subject to withholding under section 1446.  
    如果外国政府是在美国开展贸易或业务的合伙企业的合伙人，则分配给外国政府的 ECTI 被视为源自受控商业活动，并应根据第 1446 条进行预扣税。
    
3.  Gain derived from the disposition of a USRPI. Withholding on these gains is discussed later under [_U.S. Real Property Interest_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest").  
    从 USRPI 处置中获得的收益。稍后在[_美国不动产利息_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest")中讨论对这些收益的扣缴。
    

For chapter 4 purposes, payments to a foreign government (other than earnings inuring to the benefit of a private person) are not payments to which chapter 4 withholding applies unless the payment is made to a controlled entity of the foreign government that is engaged in a commercial financial activity. See Regulations section 1.1471-6(h) for a description of a commercial financial activity. See Regulations section 1.1471-3(d)(9) for the documentation required to establish an entity’s chapter 4 status as a foreign government. Similar rules apply for chapter 4 purposes to a payment to a foreign central bank of issue.  
就第 4 章而言，向外国政府付款（受益于私人利益的收入除外）不属于第 4 章预扣税适用的付款，除非该付款是向从事某项活动的外国政府受控实体支付的。商业金融活动。有关商业金融活动的描述，请参阅法规第 1.1471-6(h) 节。请参阅法规第 1.1471-3(d)(9) 节，了解确立实体作为外国政府的第 4 章地位所需的文件。类似的规则适用于第 4 章目的的向外国发行央行的付款。

A government of a U.S. territory is exempt from U.S. tax on all U.S. source income. This income is not subject to chapter 3 withholding, and chapter 4 withholding does not apply to income paid to a government of a U.S. territory. See Regulations section 1.1471-3(d)(9) for the documentation required to establish an entity’s chapter 4 status as a government of a U.S. territory. These governments should use Form W-8EXP to claim this exemption for both chapters 3 and 4 purposes (as required).  
美国领土政府对所有来自美国的收入免征美国税。该收入不受第 3 章预扣税的约束，第 4 章预扣税不适用于支付给美国领土政府的收入。请参阅法规第 1.1471-3(d)(9) 节，了解确立实体作为美国领土政府的第 4 章地位所需的文件。这些政府应使用 W-8EXP 表格来申请第 3 章和第 4 章目的的豁免（根据要求）。

**International organizations.**

International organizations are exempt from U.S. tax on all U.S. source income. Income paid to an international organization (within the meaning of section 7701(a)(18)) is not subject to chapter 3 withholding. International organizations are not required to provide a Form W-8 or documentary evidence to receive the exemption if the name of the payee is one that is designated as an international organization by executive order.

  

**国际组织。** 

国际组织的所有来自美国的收入均免征美国税。支付给国际组织的收入（第 7701(a)(18) 条含义内）无需缴纳第 3 章预扣税。如果收款人的名称是行政命令指定为国际组织的名称，则国际组织无需提供 W-8 表格或文件证据即可获得豁免。

Payments made to an international organization, as defined for chapter 4 purposes, are not payments to which chapter 4 withholding applies. An international organization for purposes of chapter 4 means any entity described in section 7701(a)(18). The term also includes any intergovernmental or supranational organization that is comprised primarily of foreign governments, that is recognized as an intergovernmental or supranational organization under certain foreign laws, or that has in effect a headquarters agreement with a foreign government, and whose income does not inure to the benefit of private persons. See Regulations section 1.1471-3(d)(9) for the documentation required to establish an entity’s chapter 4 status as an international organization.  
根据第 4 章的定义，向国际组织支付的款项不属于适用第 4 章预扣税的付款。第 4 章中的国际组织是指第 7701(a)(18) 条中描述的任何实体。该术语还包括主要由外国政府组成的任何政府间或超国家组织，根据某些外国法律被承认为政府间或超国家组织，或者与外国政府签订了有效的总部协议，并且其收入不属于政府间或超国家组织。为了私人的利益。请参阅《条例》第 1.1471-3(d)(9) 节，了解确立实体作为国际组织的第 4 章地位所需的文件。

**Foreign tax-exempt organizations.**

A foreign organization that is a tax-exempt organization under section 501(c) is not subject to a withholding tax on amounts that are not income includible under section 512 as unrelated business taxable income. In addition, withholdable payments made to a tax-exempt organization under section 501(c) are not payments to which chapter 4 withholding applies.

  

**外国免税组织。** 

根据第 501(c) 条属于免税组织的外国组织，对于不属于第 512 条规定的无关业务应税收入的收入，无需缴纳预扣税。此外，根据第 501(c) 条向免税组织支付的应预扣付款不属于第 4 章预扣税适用的付款。

However, if a foreign organization is a foreign private foundation, it is subject to a 4% withholding tax on all U.S. source investment income. For a foreign tax-exempt organization to claim an exemption from withholding under chapter 3 or 4 because of its tax-exempt status under section 501(c), or to claim withholding at a 4% rate, it must provide you with a Form W-8EXP. However, if a foreign organization is claiming an exemption from withholding under an income tax treaty, or the income is unrelated business taxable income, the organization must provide a Form W-8BEN-E or W-8ECI. Income paid to foreign tax-exempt organizations is subject to reporting on Form 1042-S. If the organization is a partner in a partnership carrying on a trade or business in the United States, the ECI allocable to the organization is subject to withholding under section 1446.  
然而，如果外国组织是外国私人基金会，则需对所有来自美国的投资收入缴纳4%的预扣税。对于外国免税组织，如果因其根据第 501(c) 条享有免税地位而根据第 3 章或第 4 章申请预扣税豁免，或要求按 4% 的税率申请预扣税，则该组织必须向您提供表格 W -8EXP。但是，如果外国组织根据所得税条约要求豁免预扣税，或者收入是不相关的营业应税收入，则该组织必须提供 W-8BEN-E 或 W-8ECI 表格。支付给外国免税组织的收入需在 1042-S 表格上报告。如果该组织是在美国开展贸易或业务的合伙企业的合伙人，则可分配给该组织的 ECI 须根据第 1446 条进行预扣。

**Foreign financial institutions.**

For payments made to a reporting Model 1 FFI or reporting Model 2 FFI, see the applicable IGA for definitions of entities described under this heading. You may generally rely on documentation provided by such an FFI to treat an entity as described under this heading (included under the class of a nonreporting IGA FFI). See the [Instructions for Form W-8BEN-E](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-w-8-ben-e).

  

**外资金融机构。** 

对于向报告模型 1 FFI 或报告模型 2 FFI 进行的付款，请参阅适用的 IGA 以了解本标题下描述的实体定义。您通常可以依赖此类 FFI 提供的文件来处理本标题下描述的实体（包括在非报告 IGA FFI 类别下）。请参阅[表格 W-8BEN-E 的说明](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-w-8-ben-e)。

#### U.S. or Foreign TINs美国或外国 TIN

As the withholding agent, in many cases you must request that the payee provide you with its U.S. TIN. You must in such a case include the payee's TIN on forms, statements, and other tax documents. The payee's TIN may be any of the following.  
作为扣缴义务人，在许多情况下，您必须要求收款人向您提供其美国 TIN。在这种情况下，您必须在表格、报表和其他税务文件中包含收款人的纳税人识别号。收款人的 TIN 可以是以下任意一种。

*   An individual may have a social security number (SSN). If the individual does not have and is eligible for an SSN, go to [SSA.gov/ssnumber/](https://www.ssa.gov/ssnumber/) for more information. The SSA will tell the individual if they are eligible to get an SSN.  
    个人可能有社会安全号码 (SSN)。如果该个人没有且有资格获得 SSN，请访问[SSA.gov/ssnumber/](https://www.ssa.gov/ssnumber/)了解更多信息。 SSA 将告知个人是否有资格获得 SSN。
    
*   An individual may have an IRS individual taxpayer identification number (ITIN). If the individual does not have and is not eligible for an SSN, they must apply for an ITIN by using [Form W-7](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-w-7).  
    个人可能拥有 IRS 个人纳税人识别号 (ITIN)。如果个人没有且没有资格申请 SSN，则必须使用[W-7 表格](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-w-7)申请 ITIN。
    
*   Any person other than an individual, and any individual who is an employer or who is engaged in a U.S. trade or business as a sole proprietor, must have an employer identification number (EIN). Use [Form SS-4](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-ss-4) to get an EIN.  
    除个人以外的任何人，以及作为雇主或作为独资经营者从事美国贸易或业务的任何个人，都必须拥有雇主识别号 (EIN)。使用[表格 SS-4](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-ss-4)获取 EIN。
    

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_Under certain circumstances, a financial institution may be required to get a GIIN for purposes of chapter 4. See_ [Global Intermediary Identification Numbers](#en_US_2024_publink100016877 "Global Intermediary Identification Numbers (GIINs)")_, later. See the Instructions for_ [Form 8957](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8957) _for information on whether a GIIN is needed._  
在某些情况下，出于第 4 章的目的，金融机构可能需要获得 GIIN。请参阅稍后的全球中介机构识别号。有关是否需要 GIIN 的信息，请参阅表格 8957 的说明。.

A U.S. or foreign TIN (as applicable) must generally be on a withholding certificate if the beneficial owner is claiming any of the following.  
如果受益所有人提出以下任何要求，美国或外国 TIN（如适用）通常必须包含在预扣税证书上。

*   Tax treaty benefits (see [_Exceptions to TIN requirement_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225030 "Exceptions to U.S. TIN requirement."), later).  
    税收协定优惠（请参阅后面的[_TIN 要求的例外情况_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225030 "Exceptions to U.S. TIN requirement.")）。
    
*   Income is effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business.  
    收入与美国贸易或业务有效相关。
    
*   Exemption for certain annuities (see [_Pensions, Annuities, and Alimony_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224947 "Pensions, Annuities, and Alimony (Income Code 15)"), earlier).  
    某些年金的豁免（参见前面的[_养老金、年金和赡养费_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224947 "Pensions, Annuities, and Alimony (Income Code 15)")）。
    
*   Exemption based on exempt organization or private foundation status.  
    基于豁免组织或私人基金会地位的豁免。
    

A foreign TIN may also be required for certain account holders (see [_Foreign TIN requirement for account holders_](#en_US_2024_publink100015526 "Foreign TIN requirement for account holders."), later). In addition, a U.S. TIN must be on a withholding certificate from a person claiming to be any of the following.  
某些账户持有人可能还需要外国 TIN（请参阅下文[_对账户持有人的外国 TIN 要求_](#en_US_2024_publink100015526 "Foreign TIN requirement for account holders.")）。此外，美国纳税人识别号 (TIN) 必须包含在自称属于以下任一人员的预扣税证书上。

*   QI.问。
    
*   QSL.QSL。
    
*   Withholding foreign partnership.  
    扣留外国合伙企业。
    
*   Withholding foreign trust.  
    扣留外国信托。
    
*   An organization claiming an exemption or reduced rate of withholding based solely on a claim of tax-exempt status under section 501(c) or private foundation status (unless only the 4-percent tax under section 4948(a) applies to the private foundation).  
    仅根据第 501(c) 条规定的免税地位或私人基金会地位主张豁免或降低预扣税率的组织（除非第 4948(a) 条规定的 4% 税仅适用于私人基金会） 。
    
*   U.S. branch of a foreign person treated as a U.S. person (see Regulations section 1.1441-1(b)(2)(iv)), and a U.S. branch of an FFI acting as an intermediary that is not treated as a U.S person.  
    被视为美国人的外国人的美国分支机构（参见条例第 1.1441-1(b)(2)(iv) 条），以及充当中介但不被视为美国人的 FFI 美国分支机构。
    
*   U.S. person.美国人。
    

**Exceptions to U.S. TIN requirement.**

A foreign person does not have to provide a U.S. TIN to claim a reduced rate of withholding under a tax treaty if the requirements for the following exceptions are met. Instead of requesting a U.S. TIN from a foreign payee, you may request a foreign TIN issued by the payee’s country of residence except when the payee is a nonresident alien individual claiming an exemption from withholding on Form 8233.

  

**美国 TIN 要求的例外情况。** 

如果满足以下例外情况的要求，外国人无需提供美国 TIN 即可根据税收协定申请降低的预扣税率。您可以请求由收款人居住国签发的外国纳税人识别号，而不是向外国收款人申请美国纳税人识别号，除非收款人是在 8233 表格上申请豁免预扣税的非居民外籍个人。

*   Income from marketable securities (discussed earlier under [_Beneficial Owners_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224825 "Beneficial Owners")).  
    来自有价证券的收入（之前在[_受益所有人_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224825 "Beneficial Owners")下讨论过）。
    
*   Unexpected payment to an individual in the case of a payment made by a U.S. financial institution to an account maintained at a U.S. office (discussed next).  
    当美国金融机构向美国办事处的账户付款时，向个人意外付款（接下来讨论）。
    

_**Unexpected payment.**_

A Form W-8BEN or a Form 8233 provided by a nonresident alien to get treaty benefits does not need a U.S. TIN if you, the withholding agent, meet all the following requirements.

  

_**意外付款。** _

如果您（扣缴义务人）满足以下所有要求，则非居民外国人为获得协定福利而提供的 W-8BEN 表格或 8233 表格不需要美国 TIN。

*   You are an acceptance agent.  
    您是承兑代理人。
    
*   You can request an ITIN for a payee on an expedited basis.  
    您可以快速为收款人申请 ITIN。
    
*   You are required to make an unexpected payment to the nonresident alien.  
    您需要向非居民外国人支付一笔意外付款。
    
*   You cannot get the ITIN because the IRS is not issuing ITINs at the time you make the payment or at any earlier time after you know you have to make the payment.  
    您无法获得 ITIN，因为 IRS 不会在您付款时或您知道必须付款后的任何早期时间签发 ITIN。
    
*   You cannot reasonably delay making the unexpected payment.  
    您不能合理地延迟支付意外付款。
    
*   You submit a completed Form W-7 for the payee, with a certification that you have reviewed the required documentation and have no actual knowledge or reason to know that the documentation is not complete or accurate, to the IRS during the first business day after you made the payment.  
    您在提交后的第一个工作日内向 IRS 提交一份完整的收款人 W-7 表格，并证明您已审阅了所需文件，并且没有实际知识或理由知道该文件不完整或不准确。已付款。
    

An acceptance agent is a person who, under a written agreement with the IRS, is authorized to help alien individuals and other foreign persons get ITINs or EINs. For information on the application procedures for becoming an acceptance agent, go to [IRS.gov/Individuals/New-ITIN-Acceptance-Agent-Program-Changes](https://www.irs.gov/individuals/new-itin-acceptance-agent-program-changes).  
受理代理人是根据与 IRS 签订的书面协议，被授权帮助外国人和其他外国人获得 ITIN 或 EIN 的人。有关成为受理代理人的申请程序的信息，请访问[IRS.gov/Individuals/New-ITIN-Acceptance-Agent-Program-Changes](https://www.irs.gov/individuals/new-itin-acceptance-agent-program-changes) 。

### Note.

All acceptance agents will be required to adhere to new quality standards established and monitored by the IRS.

  

### 笔记。

所有验收机构都必须遵守美国国税局制定和监控的新质量标准。

A payment is unexpected if you or the beneficial owner could not have reasonably anticipated the payment during a time when an ITIN could be obtained. This could be due to the nature of the payment or the circumstances in which the payment is made. A payment is not considered unexpected solely because the amount of the payment is not fixed.  
如果您或受益所有人在可以获得 ITIN 期间无法合理预期付款，则该付款属于意外付款。这可能是由于付款的性质或付款的情况所致。付款不会仅仅因为付款金额不固定而被视为意外付款。

**Example.**

Mary, a citizen and resident of Ireland, visits the United States and wins $5,000 playing a slot machine in a casino. Under the treaty with Ireland, the winnings are not subject to U.S. tax. Mary claims the treaty benefits by providing a Form W-8BEN to the casino upon winning at the slot machine. However, she does not have an ITIN or foreign TIN. The casino is an acceptance agent that can request an ITIN on an expedited basis.

Situation 1. Assume that Mary won the money on Sunday. Since the IRS does not issue ITINs on Sunday, the casino can pay $5,000 to Mary without withholding U.S. tax. The casino must, on the following Monday, fax a completed Form W-7 for Mary, including the required certification, to the IRS for an expedited ITIN.

Situation 2. Assume that Mary won the money on Monday. To pay the winnings without withholding U.S. tax, the casino must apply for and get an ITIN for Mary because an expedited ITIN is available from the IRS at the time of the payment.

  

**例子。** 

玛丽是爱尔兰公民和居民，她访问美国并在赌场玩老虎机赢得了 5,000 美元。根据与爱尔兰签订的条约，奖金无需缴纳美国税。玛丽在老虎机获胜后向赌场提供 W-8BEN 表格，从而获得条约优惠。但是，她没有 ITIN 或外国 TIN。赌场是受理代理，可以快速申请 ITIN。

情况 1. 假设玛丽在周日赢了钱。由于国税局周日不会发放 ITIN，因此赌场可以向玛丽支付 5,000 美元，而无需预扣美国税。赌场必须在下周一将玛丽填写完整的 W-7 表格（包括所需的证明）传真至 IRS，以获取加急 ITIN。

情况 2. 假设玛丽星期一赢了钱。要在不预扣美国税的情况下支付奖金，赌场必须为玛丽申请并获取 ITIN，因为付款时 IRS 可以提供加急 ITIN。

**Foreign TIN requirement for account holders.**

If you are a U.S. office or branch of a depository institution, custodial institution, investment entity, or specified insurance company (each as defined in Regulations section 1.1471-5(e)) documenting an account holder (as defined in Regulations section 1.1471-5(a)(3)) of an account that is a financial account (as defined in Regulations section 1.1471-5(b)), you must obtain the account holder’s TIN for its jurisdiction of tax residence (foreign TIN) on a Form W-8 that is a beneficial owner withholding certificate in order for the form to not be invalid for a payment of U.S. source income reportable on Form 1042-S, unless:

  

**账户持有人的外国 TIN 要求。** 

如果您是存款机构、托管机构、投资实体或指定保险公司（均按《条例》第 1.1471-5(e) 条的定义）的美国办事处或分支机构，并记录账户持有人（如《条例》第 1.1471-5 条的定义） (a)(3)) 的账户为金融账户（定义见条例第 1.1471-5(b) 条），您必须通过表格 W 获取账户持有人的税务居住地管辖区的 TIN（外国 TIN） -8 是受益所有人预扣税证明，以便该表格对于在表格 1042-S 上报告的美国来源收入的支付不无效，除非：

*   The account holder is a resident of a jurisdiction that is not listed in section 3 of Revenue Procedure 2021-32, 2021-42 I.R.B. 465, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2021-42\_IRB#REV-PROC-2021-32](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2021-42_IRB#REV-PROC-2021-32), which may be further updated in future published guidance;  
    账户持有人是未在收入程序 2021-32、2021-42 IRB 465（可在[IRS.gov/irb/2021-42\_IRB#REV-PROC-2021-32](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2021-42_IRB#REV-PROC-2021-32)上获取）第 3 节中列出的司法管辖区的居民，其中可能会在未来发布的指南中进一步更新；
    
*   The account holder is a resident in a jurisdiction that has been identified by the IRS on a list of jurisdictions that do not issue foreign TINs. See [IRS.gov/businesses/corporations/list-of-jurisdictions-that-do-not-issue-foreign-tins](https://www.irs.gov/businesses/corporations/list-of-jurisdictions-that-do-not-issue-foreign-tins);  
    账户持有人是美国国税局在不签发外国纳税人识别号码的司法管辖区列表中确定的司法管辖区的居民。请参阅[IRS.gov/businesses/corporations/list-of-jurisdictions-that-do-not-issue-foreign-tins](https://www.irs.gov/businesses/corporations/list-of-jurisdictions-that-do-not-issue-foreign-tins) ；
    
*   The account holder is a government, international organization, foreign central bank of issue, or resident of a U.S. territory; or  
    账户持有人是政府、国际组织、外国发行中央银行或美国领土居民；或者
    
*   The account holder obtains a reasonable explanation for why the account holder has not been issued a foreign TIN, including by checking the applicable box on the applicable Form W-8 indicating that the account holder is not legally required to obtain an FTIN from the account holder’s jurisdiction of residence (including if the jurisdiction does not issue TINs).  
    账户持有人获得合理解释，解释为什么账户持有人没有获得外国 TIN，包括勾选适用表格 W-8 上的适用框，表明法律上不要求账户持有人从账户持有人的账户获取 FTIN。居住管辖区（包括该管辖区不签发 TIN 的情况）。
    

A reasonable explanation that an account holder does not have a foreign TIN must address why the account holder was not issued a foreign TIN to the extent provided in the instructions for the applicable Form W-8. If an account holder provides an explanation other than the one described in the instructions for the applicable Form W-8, you must determine whether the explanation is reasonable.  
关于账户持有人没有外国 TIN 的合理解释必须说明为什么账户持有人没有按照适用的 W-8 表格说明中规定的范围获得外国 TIN。如果账户持有人提供的解释与适用的 W-8 表格说明中所述的解释不同，您必须确定该解释是否合理。

#### Global Intermediary Identification Numbers (GIINs)  
全球中介机构识别码 (GIIN)

If you make a withholdable payment to an entity claiming certain chapter 4 statuses, you may be required to obtain and verify the entity’s GIIN against the published IRS FFI list within 90 days to rely on such a claim. See [_GIIN Verification_](#en_US_2024_publink100015505 "GIIN Verification") under _Standards of Knowledge for Purposes of Chapter 4_, earlier, for which chapter 4 statuses require a GIIN.  
如果您向声称某些第 4 章身份的实体支付了预扣税款，您可能需要在 90 天内根据公布的 IRS FFI 列表获取并验证该实体的 GIIN，以依赖此类索赔。请参阅前面_第 4 章目的知识标准下的_[_GIIN 验证_](#en_US_2024_publink100015505 "GIIN Verification")，第 4 章状态需要 GIIN。

#### Depositing Withheld Taxes  
存入预扣税款

This section discusses the rules for depositing income tax withheld on FDAP income, including tax withheld pursuant to chapter 4. The deposit rules discussed here do not apply to the following items.  
本节讨论 FDAP 收入预扣所得税的存款规则，包括根据第 4 章扣缴的税款。此处讨论的存款规则不适用于以下项目。

*   Taxes on pay subject to graduated withholding, as discussed earlier. (See [Form 941](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-941) for the deposit rules.)  
    如前所述，工资税需缴纳分级预扣税。 （有关存款规则，请参阅[表格 941。](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-941) ）
    
*   Tax withheld on pensions and annuities subject to graduated withholding or the 10% tax on nonperiodic distributions. (See [Form 945](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-945) for the deposit rules.)  
    养老金和年金的预扣税需进行分级预扣或非定期分配的 10% 税。 （有关存款规则，请参阅[表格 945。](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-945) ）
    
*   Tax withheld on a foreign partner's allocable share of ECTI of a partnership, other than a publicly traded partnership. See [_Partnership Withholding on ECTI_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225066 "Partnership Withholding on ECTI"), later.  
    对外国合伙人在合伙企业（上市合伙企业除外）的 ECTI 中的可分配份额进行预扣的税款。请参阅稍后[_关于 ECTI 的合作伙伴预扣税_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225066 "Partnership Withholding on ECTI")。
    
*   Tax withheld on dispositions of USRPI by foreign persons. See [_U.S. Real Property Interest_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest"), later.  
    外国人处置 USRPI 时扣缴的税款。参见稍后的[_美国不动产利息_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest")。
    
*   Taxes on household employees. See [Schedule H](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-schedule-h-form-1040) (Form 1040) to report social security and Medicare taxes, and any income tax withheld, on wages paid to a nonresident alien household employee.  
    对家庭雇员征税。请参阅[附表 H](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-schedule-h-form-1040) （表格 1040）报告向非居民外籍家庭雇员支付的工资的社会保障税和医疗保险税以及任何预扣所得税。
    

#### When Deposits Are Required  
何时需要存款

A deposit required for any period occurring in 1 calendar year must be made separately from a deposit for any period occurring in another calendar year. A deposit of this tax must be made separately from a deposit of any other type of tax, but you need not identify whether the deposit is of tax withheld under chapter 3 or 4.  
一个日历年中任何期间所需的存款必须与另一个日历年中任何期间的存款分开。该税款的押金必须与任何其他类型税款的押金分开，但您无需确定该押金是否属于第 3 章或第 4 章规定的预扣税款。

The amount of tax you are required to withhold determines the frequency of your deposits. For more information, see _Deposit Requirements_ in the Instructions for Form 1042.  
您需要预扣的税额决定了您存款的频率。如需了解更多信息，请参阅 1042 表格说明中的_存款要求_。

**Escrow in lieu of deposit.**

Under certain circumstances, a withholding agent may be permitted to set aside a withheld amount in escrow rather than depositing the tax. A participating FFI that withholds tax on a withholdable payment not otherwise subject to chapter 3 withholding or backup withholding under section 3406 made to a recalcitrant account holder of a dormant account may, in lieu of depositing the tax withheld, set aside the amount withheld in escrow until the date that the account ceases to be a dormant account. In such case, the tax withheld becomes due 90 days following the date that the account ceases to be a dormant account if the account holder does not provide the required documentation, or becomes refundable to the account holder if the account holder provides documentation establishing that withholding does not apply.

  

**托管代替存款。** 

在某些情况下，扣缴义务人可以被允许将预扣金额存入托管，而不是存入税款。参与 FFI 对休眠账户的顽抗账户持有人不受第 3 章预扣税或根据第 3406 节规定的备用预扣税的预扣付款进行预扣税，可以将预扣税款存入托管，以代替存入预扣税款直到该帐户不再是休眠帐户之日。在这种情况下，如果账户持有人未提供所需文件，则预扣税款将于账户不再为休眠账户之日后 90 天到期；如果账户持有人提供证明预扣税款的文件，预扣税款将退还给账户持有人不适用。

A withholding agent that withholds tax under chapter 3 on certain payments that include an undetermined amount of income may retain 30% of the payment to hold in escrow in accordance with Regulations section 1.1441-3(d). Similarly, if a withholding agent is unable to determine whether the payment is a withholdable payment because the source or character of the payment is unknown, the withholding agent may retain 30% of the payment to hold in escrow for chapter 4 purposes in accordance with Regulations section 1.1471-2(a)(5).  
根据第 3 章对包含未确定收入金额的某些付款扣缴税款的扣缴义务人可以根据条例第 1.1441-3(d) 条保留 30% 的付款进行托管。同样，如果扣缴义务人因付款来源或性质不明而无法确定该付款是否为应扣缴付款，则扣缴义务人可以根据条例第 4 章的目的保留该付款的 30% 进行托管。第 1.1471-2(a)(5) 节。

**Electronic deposit requirement.**

You must deposit all withheld taxes under chapter 3 or 4 by electronic funds transfer. In most cases, electronic funds transfers are made using the Electronic Federal Tax Payment System (EFTPS). If you do not want to use EFTPS, you can arrange for your tax professional, financial institution, or other trusted third party to make deposits on your behalf. You may also arrange for your financial institution to initiate a same-day wire payment on your behalf. EFTPS is a free service provided by the Department of Treasury. Services provided by your tax professional, financial institution, or other third party may have a fee. For more information about EFTPS or to enroll in EFTPS, visit [EFTPS.gov](http://www.eftps.gov) or call 800-555-4477. Additional information about EFTPS is also available in Pub. 966.

  

**电子存款要求。** 

您必须通过电子资金转帐存入第 3 章或第 4 章规定的所有预扣税款。在大多数情况下，电子资金转账是使用联邦电子纳税系统 (EFTPS) 进行的。如果您不想使用 EFTPS，您可以安排您的税务专业人士、金融机构或其他值得信赖的第三方代表您存款。您还可以安排您的金融机构代表您发起当日电汇付款。 EFTPS 是财政部提供的一项免费服务。您的税务专业人士、金融机构或其他第三方提供的服务可能会收费。有关 EFTPS 的更多信息或注册 EFTPS，请访问[EFTPS.gov](http://www.eftps.gov)或致电 800-555-4477。有关 EFTPS 的其他信息也可在 Pub 中找到。 966.

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/taxtip.gif)
_Qualified business taxpayers that request an EIN will automatically be enrolled in EFTPS. They will receive information on how to activate their account.  
申请 EIN 的合格企业纳税人将自动注册 EFTPS。他们将收到有关如何激活帐户的信息。_.

### Note.

All payments should be stated in U.S. dollars and should be made in U.S. dollars.

  

### 笔记。

所有付款均应以美元列明并以美元支付。

**Penalty for failure to make deposits on time.**
