If you fail to make a required deposit within the time prescribed, a penalty is imposed on the underpayment (the excess of the required deposit over any actual timely deposit for a period). You can avoid the penalty if you can show that the failure to deposit was for reasonable cause and not because of willful neglect. Also, the IRS may waive the penalty if certain requirements are met.

  

**未能按时存款的处罚。** 

如果您未能在规定的时间内缴纳规定的存款，将对少缴的款项（规定的存款超过一段时间内实际及时存款的部分）处以罚款。如果您能证明未能存款是出于合理原因而非故意疏忽，则可以避免处罚。此外，如果满足某些要求，国税局可能会免除罚款。

_**Depositing on time.**_

For deposits made by EFTPS to be on time, you must initiate the deposit by 8 p.m. Eastern time the day before the date the deposit is due. If you use a third party to make deposits on your behalf, they may have different cutoff times.

  

_**按时存款。** _

为了按时通过 EFTPS 进行存款，您必须在存款到期日前一天东部时间晚上 8 点之前发起存款。如果您使用第三方代表您存款，他们可能有不同的截止时间。

_**Penalty rate.**_

If the deposit is:

  

_**处罚率。** _

如果存款是：

*   1 to 5 days late, the penalty is 2% of the underpayment;  
    逾期1至5天，罚款为少缴金额的2%；
    
*   6 to 15 days late, the penalty is 5%; or  
    迟到6至15天，罚款5%；或者
    
*   16 or more days late, the penalty is 10%.  
    迟到16天或以上，罚款10%。
    

However, if the deposit is not made within 10 days after the IRS issues the first notice demanding payment, the penalty is 15%.  
但是，如果在 IRS 发出第一次要求付款的通知后 10 天内未缴纳押金，则罚款为 15%。

If you owe a penalty for failing to deposit tax for more than one deposit period, and you make a deposit, your deposit is applied to the most recent period to which the deposit relates unless you designate the deposit period or periods to which your deposit is to be applied. You can make this designation only during a 90-day period that begins on the date of the penalty notice. The notice contains instructions on how to make this designation.  
如果您因在超过一个存款期未能缴纳税款而受到处罚，并且您进行了存款，则您的存款将适用于该存款相关的最近一个时期，除非您指定了您的存款所涉及的一个或多个存款期。来应用。您只能在自处罚通知之日起的 90 天内做出此指定。该通知包含有关如何进行此指定的说明。

#### Adjustment for Overwithholding  
预扣税调整

What to do if you overwithheld tax depends on when you discover the overwithholding.  
如果您超额预扣税款该怎么办取决于您何时发现超额预扣税款。

**Overwithholding discovered by March 15 of the following calendar year.**

If you discover that you overwithheld tax under chapter 3 or 4 by March 15 of the following calendar year, you may use the undeposited amount of tax to make any necessary adjustments between you and the recipient of the income. However, if the undeposited amount is not enough to make any adjustments, or if you discover the overwithholding after the entire amount of tax has been deposited, you can use either the reimbursement procedure or the set-off procedure to adjust the overwithholding.

  

**次年 3 月 15 日之前发现的超额预扣税款。** 

如果您发现您在下一个日历年的 3 月 15 日之前根据第 3 章或第 4 章超额预扣了税款，您可以使用未存入的税款在您和收入接收者之间进行任何必要的调整。但是，如果未存入的金额不足以进行调整，或者在全额存入税款后发现预扣税款，您可以使用报销程序或抵扣程序来调整预扣税额。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/taxtip.gif)
_If March 15 is a Saturday, Sunday, or legal holiday, the next business day is the final date for these actions.  
如果 3 月 15 日是星期六、星期日或法定节假日，则下一个工作日是这些操作的最终日期。_.

For more information on the reimbursement procedure and set-off procedure, and what to do if you discover the overwithholding after March 15 of the following calendar year, see _Adjustment for Overwithholding_ in the Instructions for Form 1042.  
有关报销程序和抵销程序的更多信息，以及如果您在下一个日历年 3 月 15 日之后发现超扣税款该怎么办，请参阅 1042 表格说明中的_超扣税款调整_。

#### Returns Required需要退货

Every withholding agent, whether U.S. or foreign, must file Forms 1042 and 1042-S to report:  
每个扣缴义务人，无论是美国还是外国，都必须提交 1042 和 1042-S 表格来报告：

*   Amounts subject to chapter 3 withholding paid to foreign persons (including persons presumed to be foreign), even if no amount is deducted and withheld from the payment under chapter 3, and  
    向外国人（包括推定为外国人）支付的受第 3 章预扣税款约束的金额，即使没有从第 3 章规定的付款中扣除和预扣税款，以及
    
*   Payments to which chapter 4 withholding is applied or which are allocated on an applicable withholding statement provided by a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI to a chapter 4 withholding rate pool of U.S. payees (chapter 4 reportable amounts).  
    适用第 4 章预扣税的付款或根据参与 FFI 或注册的视为合规 FFI 提供的适用预扣税表分配给美国收款人第 4 章预扣税率池的付款（第 4 章应报告金额）。
    

Do not use Forms 1042 and 1042-S to report tax withheld on the following.  
请勿使用表格 1042 和 1042-S 报告以下各项的预扣税款。

*   Wages, salaries, or other compensation reported on Form W-2 (see [_Wages Paid to Employees—Graduated Withholding_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224978 "Wages Paid to Employees—Graduated Withholding"), earlier, under _Pay for Personal Services Performed_).  
    W-2 表中报告的工资、薪金或其他报酬（请参阅之前的[_“支付给员工的工资 - 分级预扣税_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224978 "Wages Paid to Employees—Graduated Withholding")”下的_“为所提供的个人服务付费”_ ）。
    
*   Any part of a U.S. or foreign partnership's (other than a publicly traded partnership) ECTI allocable to a foreign partner (see [_Partnership Withholding on ECTI_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225066 "Partnership Withholding on ECTI"), later).  
    美国或外国合伙企业（公开交易的合伙企业除外）ECTI 中可分配给外国合伙人的任何部分（请参阅后面[_关于 ECTI 的合伙企业预扣税_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225066 "Partnership Withholding on ECTI")）。
    
*   Dispositions of USRPIs by foreign persons (see [_U.S. Real Property Interest_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest"), later).  
    外国人对 USRPI 的处置（见下文的[_美国不动产权益_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest")）。
    
*   Pensions, annuities, and certain other deferred income reported on Form 1099.  
    养老金、年金和某些其他递延收入在 1099 表格中报告。
    
*   Income, social security, and Medicare taxes on wages paid to a household employee reported on Schedule H (Form 1040).  
    向家庭雇员支付的工资的所得税、社会保障税和医疗保险税在附表 H（表格 1040）中报告。
    
*   Amounts subject to backup withholding under section 3406, including withholdable payments that are reportable payments and that are paid to a recalcitrant account holder of a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI that has elected on its withholding statement for withholding under section 3406 to apply instead of withholding under chapter 4.  
    根据第 3406 条规定需缴纳备用预扣税的金额，包括属于应报告付款的应预扣付款，以及支付给参与 FFI 或已在其预扣税声明中选择根据第 3406 条规定进行预扣税的注册视为合规 FFI 的顽抗账户持有人的预扣付款第 4 章规定的预扣税。
    

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/duedate.gif)
_Forms 1042 and 1042-S must be filed by March 15 of the year following the calendar year in which the income subject to reporting was paid. If March 15 falls on a Saturday, Sunday, or legal holiday, the due date is the next business day.  
1042 和 1042-S 表格必须在支付需申报收入的日历年的次年 3 月 15 日之前提交。如果3月15日恰逢周六、周日或法定节假日，则截止日期为下一个工作日。_.

**Form 1042.**

Every U.S. and foreign withholding agent that is required to file a Form 1042-S must also file an annual return on Form 1042. You must file Form 1042 even if you were not required to withhold any income tax under chapter 3 on the payment, or if the payment is a chapter 4 reportable amount.

  

**1042 表格。** 

每个需要提交 1042-S 表格的美国和外国扣缴义务人还必须提交 1042 表年度申报表。即使您不需要根据第 3 章的付款预扣任何所得税，您也必须提交 1042 表格，或者如果付款是第 4 章的应报告金额。

Form 1042 is now available for e-filing, which is required beginning for the 2023 year for a withholding agent that is a financial institution, a partnership with more than 100 partners, or for withholding agents that are filing 10 or more information returns for the calendar year. For general information about e-filing, see Pub. 4163 and the Instructions for Form 1042.  
1042 表格现可用于电子申报，从 2023 年开始，对于金融机构、合伙企业超过 100 个的扣缴义务人，或者为纳税人提交 10 份或以上信息申报表的扣缴义务人，需要使用该表格。历年。有关电子申请的一般信息，请参阅 Pub。 4163 和 1042 表格说明。

You are encouraged to e-file Form 1042. However, you may file a paper Form 1042 with the:  
我们鼓励您以电子方式提交 1042 表格。但是，您也可以通过以下方式提交纸质 1042 表格：

  
| ![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/envelope.gif)

Address you may need

 |   
Ogden Service Center奥格登服务中心  
P.O. Box 409101邮政信箱 409101  
Ogden, UT 84409奥格登, UT 84409 |

**Form 1042-S.**

Every U.S. and foreign withholding agent must file a Form 1042-S for amounts subject to chapter 3 withholding and chapter 4 reportable amounts unless an exception applies. You may be required to e-file Form 1042–S. Go to [IRS.gov/InfoReturn](https://www.irs.gov/filing/e-file-information-returns) for e-file options.

  

**1042-S 表格。** 

每位美国和外国扣缴义务人都必须提交 1042-S 表，以了解第 3 章规定的预扣税额和第 4 章规定的应报告金额，除非有例外情况。您可能需要以电子方式提交 1042-S 表格。请访问[IRS.gov/InfoReturn](https://www.irs.gov/filing/e-file-information-returns)了解电子报税选项。

A separate Form 1042-S is required for each recipient of income to whom you made payments during the preceding calendar year regardless of whether you withheld or were required to withhold tax. However, if you make a withholdable payment to an NQI or a flow-through entity that is allocable to a chapter 4 withholding rate pool, as indicated on a withholding statement upon which you may rely with respect to the payment allocable to such a pool, you should complete a separate Form 1042-S for each chapter 4 withholding rate pool (that is, pool of recalcitrant account holders, pool of nonparticipating FFIs, pool of payees that are U.S. persons), treating the intermediary or flow-through entity as the recipient (and the applicable pool as the chapter 4 status of the recipient). You need not issue a Form 1042-S to each recipient included in such pool. You must use a separate Form 1042-S for each type of income that you paid to the same recipient. See [_Statements to recipients_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225061 "Statements to recipients."), later.  
无论您是否预扣税款或被要求预扣税款，您在上一日历年中向其付款的每个收入接收者都需要单独填写 1042-S 表格。但是，如果您向可分配给第 4 章预扣税率池的 NQI 或流通实体支付了预扣税款，如您在分配给此类池的付款时可以依赖的预扣税声明中所示，您应该为每个第 4 章预扣税率池（即顽抗账户持有人池、非参与 FFI 池、美国人收款人池）填写单独的表格 1042-S，将中介或流通实体视为收件人（以及适用的池作为收件人的第 4 章状态）。您无需向此类池中的每个接收者发放表格 1042-S。对于支付给同一收款人的每种类型的收入，您必须使用单独的 1042-S 表格。请参阅稍后[_给收件人的声明_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225061 "Statements to recipients.")。

You must furnish a Form 1042-S for each recipient even if you did not withhold tax because you repaid the tax withheld to the recipient or because the income payment was exempt from tax under the Internal Revenue Code or under a U.S. income tax treaty (except for a withholdable payment that is not a chapter 4 reportable amount).  
即使您没有预扣税款，您也必须为每个收款人提供 1042-S 表格，因为您向收款人偿还了预扣税款，或者因为根据《国内税收法》或美国所得税条约，收入付款可以免税（除非对于不属于第 4 章应报告金额的预扣付款）。

You can use a substitute Form 1042-S if it meets the requirements listed in Pub. 1179. Paper substitutes that totally conform to the format and size of the official form may be used without prior approval from the IRS. See [Pub. 1179](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-1179) for more information.  
如果符合 Pub.10 中列出的要求，您可以使用替代表格 1042-S。 1179. 可以使用完全符合正式表格格式和尺寸的纸张替代品，无需事先获得国税局批准。参见[酒吧。 1179](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-publication-1179)了解更多信息。

If you are reporting amounts withheld by another withholding agent, Form 1042-S requests the name and EIN of the withholding agent that withheld the tax to the extent required in the Instructions for Form 1042-S.  
如果您要报告由其他扣缴义务人扣缴的金额，表格 1042-S 会要求您提供按照表格 1042-S 说明中要求的范围扣缴税款的扣缴义务人的名称和 EIN。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_If you file a substitute for Copy A with the IRS that does not conform to the specifications in Pub. 1179, you may be subject to a penalty for failing to file a correct return. See_ [Penalties](#en_US_2024_publink100015229 "Penalties")_, later._  
如果您向 IRS 提交的副本 A 的替代品不符合 Pub 中的规范。 1179，您可能会因未能提交正确的申报表而受到处罚。请参阅稍后的处罚。.

_**Joint owners.**_

If there are joint owners of the withholdable payment, see _Payments directly to beneficial owners_ under _Payments to Recipients_ in the Instructions for Form 1042-S.

  

_**共同所有者。** _

如果预扣付款有共同所有人，请参阅 1042-S 表格说明中_“向收款人付款_”下的_“直接向受益所有人付款”_ 。

_**E-filing.**_

For information about Form 1042-S e-filing requirements for withholding agents or their agents, and partnerships with a Form 1042-S filing requirement, including the threshold return limits, see _Electronic Reporting_ in the Instructions for [Form 1042-S](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-1042-s).

  

_**电子归档。** _

有关扣缴义务人或其代理人的 1042-S 表格电子申报要求以及符合 1042-S 表格申报要求的合作伙伴关系（包括申报表阈值限额）的信息，请参阅[1042-S 表格](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-1042-s)说明中的_电子报告_。

For additional information and instructions on e-filing Forms 1042-S, get Pub. 1187 or go to [IRS.gov/InfoReturn](https://www.irs.gov/filing/e-file-information-returns) for e-file options.  
有关电子提交表格 1042-S 的更多信息和说明，请访问 Pub。 1187 或访问[IRS.gov/InfoReturn](https://www.irs.gov/filing/e-file-information-returns)了解电子报税选项。

**Form 1042-T.**

If you are not required to e-file and Form 1042-S is filed on paper, it must be filed with Form 1042-T. You may need to file more than one Form 1042-T. See the instructions for [Form 1042-T](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-1042-t) for more information.

  

**1042-T 表格。** 

如果您不需要以电子方式提交，而 1042-S 表格以纸质形式提交，则必须与 1042-T 表格一起提交。您可能需要提交多份 1042-T 表格。有关更多信息，请参阅[表格 1042-T](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-1042-t)的说明。

**Deposit interest paid to certain nonresident alien individuals.**

Interest earned by residents of certain foreign countries is subject to information reporting. Deposit interest of $10 or more paid to any nonresident alien individual who is a resident of a foreign country with which the United States has agreed to exchange tax information pursuant to an income tax treaty or other convention or bilateral agreement, must be reported on Form 1042-S.

  

**支付给某些非居民外国人的存款利息。** 

某些外国居民赚取的利息需要进行信息报告。向美国同意根据所得税条约或其他公约或双边协议交换税务信息的外国居民的任何非居民外籍个人支付 10 美元或以上的存款利息，必须在 1042 表格中报告-S。

[Revenue Procedure 2021-32](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2021-42_IRB#REV-PROC-2021-32) identifies those countries for which reporting of deposit interest is required with respect to a resident of any such country.  
[收入程序 2021-32](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2021-42_IRB#REV-PROC-2021-32)确定了需要报告此类国家居民存款利息的国家。

### Note.

You may elect to report interest paid to any nonresident alien.

  

### 笔记。

您可以选择报告向任何非居民外国人支付的利息。

**Statements to recipients.**

You must furnish a statement to each recipient for whom you are filing a Form 1042-S by the due date for filing Forms 1042 and 1042-S with the IRS. You may use a copy of the official Form 1042-S for this purpose. Any substitute forms must comply with the rules set out in Pub. 1179. You must furnish a separate substitute Form 1042-S for each type of income or payment. The withholding agent must ensure that any substitute Form 1042-S copies B, C, and D, which are furnished to the recipient, conforms in format and size to the official Form 1042-S and contains the exact same information as the copy filed with the IRS or e-filed. However, the size of a substitute Form 1042-S, copies B, C, and D, may be adjusted if the substitute form is presented on a landscape-oriented page instead of portrait. Only one Form 1042-S may be submitted per page, regardless of orientation.

  

**给收件人的声明。** 

您必须在向 IRS 提交 1042 和 1042-S 表格的截止日期之前向您为其提交 1042-S 表格的每位接收人提供一份声明。为此，您可以使用正式表格 1042-S 的副本。任何替代表格必须符合 Pub 中规定的规则。 1179. 您必须为每种类型的收入或付款提供单独的替代表格 1042-S。扣缴义务人必须确保向接收人提供的任何替代表格 1042-S 副本 B、C 和 D 的格式和大小符合正式表格 1042-S，并且包含与提交给收件人的副本完全相同的信息。国税局 (IRS) 或电子报税。但是，如果替代表格以横向页面而不是纵向页面呈现，则可以调整替代表格 1042-S 副本 B、C 和 D 的尺寸。无论方向如何，每页只能提交一份 1042-S 表格。

#### Form 89668966 表格

A withholding agent that makes a withholdable payment to a passive NFFE with one or more substantial U.S. owners (or, in the case of a reporting Model 2 FFI, controlling persons of such an entity) or an owner-documented FFI with a specified U.S. person owning certain equity or debt interests in the FFI must report the payment and each such substantial U.S. owner (or controlling person, as applicable) or specified U.S. person owner of the passive NFFE or owner-documented FFI, respectively, on Form 8966 (in addition to reporting the payment and tax (if any) on Forms 1042 and 1042-S when the payment is an amount subject to chapter 3 withholding). An exception to the requirement to report on Form 8966 applies when the payment is made to an account reported by an FFI as a U.S. account under the FFI’s applicable chapter 4 requirements or the requirements of an applicable IGA.  
向拥有一名或多名美国大股东（或者在报告模式 2 FFI 的情况下，控制此类实体的人员）的被动 NFFE 或拥有指定美国人的拥有者记录的 FFI 支付应扣税款的扣缴义务人拥有 FFI 的某些股权或债务权益的人必须在 8966 表格上分别报告付款情况以及被动 NFFE 或所有者记录的 FFI 的每个此类主要美国所有者（或控制人，如适用）或指定美国人所有者（当付款是受第 3 章预扣税约束的金额时，除了在表格 1042 和 1042-S 上报告付款和税款（如果有）之外）。当付款支付至 FFI 根据适用的第 4 章要求或适用的 IGA 的要求而被 FFI 报告为美国账户的账户时，适用 8966 表格报告要求的例外情况。

Form 8966 must be filed by March 31 of the year following the calendar year in which the payment is made. An automatic 90-day extension of time to file [Form 8966](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8966) may be requested. To request an automatic 90-day extension of time to file Form 8966, file [Form 8809-I](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8809-i). See the Instructions for Form 8809-I for where to file that form. You should request an extension as soon as you are aware that an extension is necessary, but no later than the due date for filing Form 8966. Under certain hardship conditions, the IRS may grant an additional 90-day extension to file Form 8966. To request an additional 90-day extension of time to file Form 8966, file a second Form 8809-I before the end of the initial extended due date.  
8966 表必须在付款日历年的次年 3 月 31 日之前提交。可能会请求自动将[8966 表格的](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8966)提交时间延长 90 天。要请求自动将 8966 表格的提交时间延长 90 天，请提交[8809-I 表格](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8809-i)。请参阅表格 8809-I 的说明，了解提交该表格的位置。一旦您意识到有必要延期，您应该立即申请延期，但不得迟于提交 8966 表格的截止日期。在某些困难情况下，IRS 可能会额外批准 90 天的延期以提交 8966 表格。请求将提交表格 8966 的时间再延长 90 天，并在最初的延长到期日结束之前提交第二份表格 8809-I。

**E-filing requirement for Form 8966.**

For information about the Form 8966 e-filing requirements, including the threshold return limits, for financial institutions and all other entities with a Form 8966 filing requirement, see _Electronic filing requirement_ and _How to file electronically_ in the [Instructions for Form 8966](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8966).

  

**8966 表格的电子提交要求。** 

有关 8966 表格电子申报要求的信息，包括金融机构和具有 8966 表格申报要求的所有其他实体的阈值回报限额，请参阅[8966 表格说明](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8966)中的_电子申报要求_和_如何以电子方式申报_。

#### Extensions of Time To File  
延长归档时间

You can request extensions of time to file Forms 1042 and 1042-S with the IRS and additional extensions to furnish Forms 1042-S to recipients.  
您可以请求延长向 IRS 提交 1042 和 1042-S 表格的时间，并请求延长向收件人提供 1042-S 表格的时间。

**Extension to file Form 1042.**

You can get an automatic 6-month extension of time to file Form 1042 by filing [Form 7004](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-7004). File Form 7004 on or before the due date of Form 1042. Form 7004 does not extend the time for payment of tax.

  

**提交表格 1042 的扩展。** 

您可以通过提交[表格 7004](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-7004)获得自动将提交表格 1042 的时间延长 6 个月。在表格 1042 到期日或之前提交表格 7004。表格 7004 不会延长纳税时间。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_Form 7004 extends only the due date for filing the returns with the IRS. It does not extend the due date for furnishing statements to recipients.  
7004 表格仅延长向 IRS 提交纳税申报表的截止日期。它不会延长向收件人提供报表的截止日期。_.

**Extension to file Form 1042-S with the IRS.**

You can get an automatic 30-day extension of time to file Form 1042-S by filing [Form 8809](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8809). You should request an extension as soon as you are aware that an extension is necessary, but no later than the due date for filing Form 1042-S.

  

**向 IRS 提交 1042-S 表格的延期。** 

通过填写[8809 表格，](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8809)您可以自动将 1042-S 表格的提交时间延长 30 天。一旦您意识到有必要延期，您应该立即申请延期，但不得晚于提交表格 1042-S 的截止日期。

You may request one additional extension of 30 days by submitting a second Form 8809 before the end of the first extension period. Requests for an additional extension are not automatically granted. When requesting the additional extension, include a copy of the filed Form 8809. The IRS will send you a letter of explanation approving or denying your request for an additional extension. See the instructions for [Form 8809](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8809) for more information.  
您可以在第一个延期期结束前提交第二份 8809 表格，请求再延期 30 天。额外延期的请求不会自动获得批准。请求额外延期时，请附上已提交的 8809 表格副本。IRS 将向您发送一封解释信，批准或拒绝您的额外延期请求。有关更多信息，请参阅[8809 表格](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8809)的说明。

### Note:

If you have questions about Form 8809, call the Technical Operations (TSO) toll free at 866-455-7438 or 304-263-8700 (not toll free). Persons with a hearing or speech disability with access to TTY/TDD equipment can call 304-579-4827 (not toll free).

  

### 笔记：

如果您对 8809 表格有疑问，请拨打免费电话 866-455-7438 或 304-263-8700（非免费）联系技术运营 (TSO)。有听力或语言障碍且可以使用 TTY/TDD 设备的人士可以拨打 304-579-4827（非免费电话）。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_If you are requesting extensions of time to file for more than one withholding agent or payer, you must submit the extension request electronically.  
如果您请求延长向多个扣缴义务人或付款人申报的时间，您必须以电子方式提交延期请求。_.

**Extension to furnish statements to recipients.**

You may request an extension of time to furnish the statements to recipients by faxing a letter to:

  

**向收件人提供声明的扩展。** 

您可以通过传真至以下地址来请求延长向收件人提供报表的时间：

Internal Revenue Service Technical Services Operation  
国税局技术服务运营  
Attn: Extension of Time Coordinator  
收件人：延长时间协调员  
Fax: 866-477-0572传真：866-477-0572  
(International: 304-589-4151)  
（国际：304-589-4151）

The letter must include the following:  
该信函必须包括以下内容：

*   Payer name,付款人姓名，
    
*   Payer TIN,付款人 TIN，
    
*   Payer address,付款人地址，
    
*   Type of return (for example, Form 1042-S),  
    申报表类型（例如，表格 1042-S），
    
*   A statement that your extension request is for providing statements to recipients,  
    一份声明，表明您的延期请求是为了向收件人提供声明，
    
*   Reason for delay, and延迟原因，以及
    
*   The signature of the payer or authorized agent.  
    付款人或授权代理人的签名。
    

Your request must be received no later than the date on which the statements are due to the recipients. If your request for an extension is approved, you will generally be granted a maximum of 30 extra days (15 days for Forms W-2) to furnish the recipient statements.  
您的请求必须在账单到期日送达收件人之日之前收到。如果您的延期请求获得批准，您通常将获得最多 30 天的额外时间（表格 W-2 为 15 天）来提供收件人报表。

#### Penalties处罚

If you do not file a correct and complete Form 1042 or Form 1042-S with the IRS on time or if you do not provide a correct and complete Form 1042-S to the recipient on time, you may be subject to a penalty.  
如果您未按时向 IRS 提交正确且完整的 1042 表格或 1042-S 表格，或者未按时向收件人提供正确且完整的 1042-S 表格，您可能会受到处罚。

**Failure to file Form 1042.**

The penalty for not filing Form 1042 when due (including extensions) is usually 5% of the unpaid tax for each month or part of a month the return is late, but not more than 25% of the unpaid tax.

  

**未能提交 1042 表格。** 

未按时提交 1042 表格（包括延期）的罚款通常为每个月或迟交一个月的部分时间未缴税款的 5%，但不超过未缴税款的 25%。

**Failure to file correct Form 1042-S.**

A penalty may be imposed for failure to file a complete and correct Form 1042-S when due (including extensions).

  

**未能提交正确的 1042-S 表格。** 

如果未能在到期时提交完整且正确的 1042-S 表格（包括延期），可能会受到处罚。

For more information on the penalty for failure to timely file a correct Form 1042-S with the IRS, see _Penalties_ in the 2024 [Instructions for Form 1042-S](https://www.irs.gov/instructions/i1042s#en_US_2022_publink64278ad0e2303) .  
有关未能及时向 IRS 提交正确的 1042-S 表格的处罚的更多信息，请参阅 2024 年[表格 1042-S 说明](https://www.irs.gov/instructions/i1042s#en_US_2022_publink64278ad0e2303)中的_处罚_。

**Failure to furnish Form 1042-S to recipient.**

For more information on the penalty for failure to timely furnish Form 1042-S to a recipient, see _Penalties_ in the 2024 Instructions for Form 1042-S.

  

**未能向收件人提供 1042-S 表格。** 

有关未能及时向收件人提供 1042-S 表的处罚的更多信息，请参阅 2024 年 1042-S 表说明中的_处罚_。

**Penalty for intentional disregard of requirements to file or furnish returns.**

If you intentionally disregard the requirement to file Form 1042-S when due, to furnish Form 1042-S to the recipient when due, or to report correct information, the penalty is the greater of $630 or 10% of the total amount of the items that must be reported, with no maximum penalty.

  

**故意无视提交或提供申报表要求的处罚。** 

如果您故意忽视按时提交 1042-S 表格、按时向收件人提供 1042-S 表格或报告正确信息的要求，则罚款为 630 美元或物品总金额的 10%，以较高者为准必须报告，且没有最高处罚。

_**Failure to e-file.**_

If you are required to e-file Form 1042-S but you fail to do so, and you do not have an approved waiver, penalties may apply unless you establish reasonable cause for your failure.

  

_**电子归档失败。** _

如果您被要求以电子方式提交 1042-S 表格，但您没有这样做，并且您没有获得批准的豁免，则可能会受到处罚，除非您提出了失败的合理原因。

For more information on failure to e-file, see _Penalties_ in the 2024 Instructions for Form 1042-S.  
有关未能通过电子方式提交的更多信息，请参阅 1042-S 表格 2024 年说明中的_处罚_。

#### Partnership Withholding on ECTI  
ECTI 合作伙伴预扣税

Under section 1446(a), a partnership (foreign or domestic) that has income effectively connected with a U.S. trade or business (or income treated as effectively connected) must pay a withholding tax on the ECTI that is allocable to its foreign partners. A publicly traded partnership or nominee for a publicly traded partnership distribution must withhold tax on actual distributions of ECI. See _[Publicly Traded Partnership Distributions (PTP Distributions)](#en_US_2024_publink1000225085 "Publicly Traded Partnership Distributions (PTP Distributions)")_, later. Chapter 4 withholding does not apply to this income.  
根据第 1446(a) 条，拥有与美国贸易或业务有效关联的收入（或被视为有效关联的收入）的合伙企业（外国或国内）必须为可分配给其外国合伙人的 ECTI 缴纳预扣税。公开交易合伙企业或公开交易合伙企业分配的提名人必须对 ECI 的实际分配预扣税款。请参阅稍后_[公开交易的合作伙伴分配（PTP 分配）](#en_US_2024_publink1000225085 "Publicly Traded Partnership Distributions (PTP Distributions)")_ 。第 4 章预扣税不适用于该收入。

This withholding tax does not apply to income that is not effectively connected with the partnership's U.S. trade or business. That income may be subject to [Chapter 3 withholding tax](#en_US_2024_publink100015523 "Amounts Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding"), as discussed earlier in this publication.  
该预扣税不适用于与合伙企业在美国的贸易或业务没有有效联系的收入。正如本出版物前面所讨论的，该收入可能需要缴纳[第 3 章预扣税](#en_US_2024_publink100015523 "Amounts Subject to Chapter 3 Withholding")。

#### Who Must Withhold谁必须扣留

The partnership, or a withholding agent for the partnership, must pay the withholding tax. A partnership that must pay the withholding tax but fails to do so may be liable for the payment of the tax and any penalties and interest.  
合伙企业或合伙企业的扣缴义务人必须缴纳预扣税。必须缴纳预扣税但未缴纳的合伙企业可能需要缴纳税款以及任何罚款和利息。

The partnership must determine whether a partner is a foreign partner. A foreign partner can be a nonresident alien individual, foreign corporation, foreign partnership, foreign estate or trust, foreign tax-exempt organization, or foreign government.  
合伙企业必须确定合伙人是否为外国合伙人。外国合伙人可以是非居民外籍个人、外国公司、外国合伙企业、外国遗产或信托、外国免税组织或外国政府。

**U.S. partner.**

A partner that is a U.S. person should provide Form W-9 to the partnership.

  

**美国合作伙伴。** 

美国人合伙人应向合伙企业提供 W-9 表格。

A partnership may rely on a partner's certification of nonforeign status and assume that a partner is not a foreign partner unless the form:  
合伙企业可以依赖合伙人的非外国身份证明，并假定合伙人不是外国合伙人，除非以下形式：

*   Does not give the partner's name, U.S. TIN, and address; or  
    不提供合作伙伴的姓名、美国纳税人识别号和地址；或者
    
*   Is not signed under penalties of perjury and dated.  
    未签署，否则将受到伪证罪处罚并注明日期。
    

The partnership must keep the certification for as long as it may be relevant to the partnership's liability for tax under section 1446.  
只要该证明可能与第 1446 条规定的合伙企业的纳税义务相关，合伙企业就必须保留该证明。

The partnership may not rely on the certification if it has actual knowledge or has reason to know that any information on the form is incorrect or unreliable.  
如果合伙企业实际了解或有理由知道表格上的任何信息不正确或不可靠，则不得依赖该认证。

If a partnership does not receive a Form W-9 (or similar documentation), the partnership must presume that the partner is a foreign person.  
如果合伙企业未收到 W-9 表（或类似文件），则合伙企业必须推定合伙人是外国人。

#### Foreign Partner国外合作伙伴

A partner that is a foreign person should provide the appropriate Form W-8 (as shown in _[Chart D](#en_US_2024_publink1000225070 "Chart D. Documentation for Foreign Partners*")_) to the partnership.  
外国人合伙人应向合伙企业提供适当的 W-8 表格（如_[图表 D](#en_US_2024_publink1000225070 "Chart D. Documentation for Foreign Partners*")_所示）。

Partners who have otherwise provided Form W-8 to a partnership for purposes of section 1441 or 1442, as discussed earlier, can use the same form for purposes of section 1446(a) if they meet the requirements discussed earlier under [_Documentation_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224819 "Documentation"). However, a foreign simple trust that has provided documentation for its beneficiaries for purposes of section 1441 must provide a Form W-8 on its own behalf for purposes of section 1446.  
如前所述，出于第 1441 条或第 1442 条的目的，以其他方式向合伙企业提供了表格 W-8 的合伙人，如果满足前面在[_文件_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224819 "Documentation")中讨论的要求，则可以出于第 1446(a) 条的目的使用相同的表格。然而，为了第 1441 条的目的，已为其受益人提供文件的外国简单信托必须为第 1446 条的目的代表其自己提供 W-8 表格。

The partnership may not rely on the certification if it has actual knowledge or has reason to know that any information on the form is incorrect or unreliable.  
如果合伙企业实际了解或有理由知道表格上的任何信息不正确或不可靠，则不得依赖该认证。

The partnership must keep the certification for as long as it may be relevant to the partnership's liability for section 1446 tax.  
只要证明可能与合伙企业的第 1446 条税款责任相关，合伙企业就必须保留该证明。

**Chart D. Documentation for Foreign Partners\*  
图 D. 外国合作伙伴的文件\***

  
| **IF you are a...如果你是一个...** | **THEN provide to the partnership Form...  
然后向合作伙伴提供表格...** |
| nonresident alien非居民外国人 | W-8BEN. |
| foreign corporation外国公司 | W-8BEN-E. |
| foreign partnership外国合伙企业 | W-8IMY. |
| foreign government外国政府 | W-8EXP. |
| foreign grantor trust\*\*外国设保人信托\*\* | W-8IMY. |
| certain foreign trust or foreign estate  
某些外国信托或外国财产 | W-8BEN. |
| foreign tax-exempt organization (including a private foundation)  
外国免税组织（包括私人基金会） | W-8EXP. |
| nominee被提名人 | W-8 used by beneficial owner.  
W-8 由受益所有人使用。 |
| \* A partnership may substitute its own form for the official version of Form W-8 to ascertain the identity of its partners.  
\* 合伙企业可以用自己的表格代替正式版本的 W-8 表格，以确定其合伙人的身份。 |
| \*\* A domestic grantor trust must provide a statement as shown in Regulations section 1.1446-1(c)(2)(ii)(E), and documentation for its grantor.  
\*\* 国内授予人信托必须提供《条例》第 1.1446-1(c)(2)(ii)(E) 条中所示的声明及其授予人的文件。 |

 

#### Amount of Withholding Tax  
预扣税金额

The amount a partnership must withhold is based on its effectively connected taxable income that is allocable to its foreign partners for the partnership's tax year. However, see [_Publicly Traded Partnerships_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225085 "Publicly Traded Partnership Distributions (PTP Distributions)"), later.  
合伙企业必须预扣的金额基于其在合伙企业纳税年度分配给其外国合伙人的有效关联应税收入。不过，请参阅稍后的[_公开交易合伙企业_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225085 "Publicly Traded Partnership Distributions (PTP Distributions)")。

**Reduction of withholding.**

The foreign partner's share of the partnership's gross ECI is reduced by the following.

  

**减少预扣税。** 

外国合伙人在合伙企业总 ECI 中所占的份额按以下比例减少。

*   The partner's share of partnership deductions connected to that income for the year.  
    合伙人在与当年收入相关的合伙企业扣除额中所占的份额。
    
*   The partner's tax treaty benefits related to that income (see _[Chart D. Documentation for Foreign Partners](#en_US_2024_publink1000225070 "Chart D. Documentation for Foreign Partners*")_ for documentation).  
    合作伙伴与该收入相关的税收协定优惠（有关文件，请参阅_[表 D. 外国合作伙伴的文件](#en_US_2024_publink1000225070 "Chart D. Documentation for Foreign Partners*")_）。
    

The partnership may reduce the foreign partner's share of partnership gross ECI by the following.  
合伙企业可以按以下方式减少外国合伙人在合伙企业总 ECI 中所占的份额。

1.  State and local income taxes the partnership withholds and pays on behalf of the partner on current-year effectively connected taxable income allocated to the partner.  
    合伙企业代表合伙人就分配给合伙人的当年实际关联应税收入代扣代缴的州和地方所得税。
    
2.  The foreign partner's partner-level deductions and losses that the partner certifies to the partnership as:  
    外国合伙人向合伙企业证明的合伙人级别的扣除和损失为：
    
    1.  Carried forward from a prior year,  
        从上一年结转，
        
    2.  Properly allocated to gross ECI of the partner's trade or business in the United States, and  
        正确分配至合作伙伴在美国的贸易或业务的总 ECI，以及
        
    3.  Reasonably expected to be available and claimed on the partner's U.S. income tax return.  
        合理预期可在合作伙伴的美国所得税申报表上申报并申报。
        
    

To certify the deductions and losses, a partner must submit to the partnership Form 8804-C.  
为了证明扣除和损失，合伙人必须向合伙企业提交表格 8804-C。

If the partner's investment in the partnership is the only activity producing ECI and the section 1446 tax is less than $1,000, no withholding is required. The partner must provide Form 8804-C to the partnership to receive the exemption from withholding.  
如果合伙人对合伙企业的投资是产生 ECI 的唯一活动，并且第 1446 条税额低于 1,000 美元，则无需预扣税。合伙人必须向合伙企业提供 8804-C 表格才能获得预扣税豁免。

A foreign partner may submit a Form 8804-C to a partnership at any time during the partnership's year and prior to the partnership's filing of its Form 8804. An updated certificate is required when the facts or representations made in the original certificate have changed or a status report is required.  
外国合伙人可以在合伙企业一年内以及在合伙企业提交 8804 表之前的任何时间向合伙企业提交 8804-C 表。当原始证书中的事实或陈述发生变化或发生变化时，需要更新证书。需要状态报告。

For more information, see the [Instructions for Form 8804-C](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8804-c).  
如需了解更多信息，请参阅[8804-C 表格说明](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8804-c)。

**Tax rate.**

The withholding tax rate on a partner's share of ECTI is 37% for noncorporate partners and 21% for corporate partners. However, the partnership may withhold at the highest rate applicable to a particular type of income allocated to a partner provided the partnership received the appropriate documentation. See Regulations section 1.1446-3(a)(2)(ii).

  

**税率。** 

对于非公司合作伙伴，合作伙伴在 ECTI 中所占份额的预扣税率为 37%，对于公司合作伙伴，预扣税率为 21%。然而，如果合伙企业收到了适当的文件，合伙企业可以按照适用于分配给合伙人的特定类型收入的最高税率进行预扣。请参阅法规第 1.1446-3(a)(2)(ii) 节。

**Installment payments.**

A partnership must make installment payments of withholding tax on its foreign partners' share of effectively connected taxable income whether or not distributions are made during the partnership's tax year. The amount of a partnership's installment payment is the sum of the installment payments for each of its foreign partners. The amount of each installment payment can be figured by using [Form 8804-W](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8804-w).

  

**分期付款。** 

合伙企业必须为其外国合伙人在有效关联的应税收入中所占的份额分期缴纳预扣税，无论是否在合伙企业的纳税年度内进行分配。合伙企业的分期付款金额为各外国合伙人分期付款的总和。每期分期付款的金额可以使用[表格 8804-W](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8804-w)计算。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/duedate.gif)
  **Date payments are due.** _Payments of withholding tax must be made during the partnership's tax year in which the ECTI is derived. A partnership must pay the IRS a part of the annual withholding tax for its foreign partners by the 15th day of the 4th, 6th, 9th, and 12th months of its tax year for U.S. income tax purposes. Any additional amounts due are to be paid with Form 8804, the annual partnership withholding tax return, discussed later._  
付款到期日。预扣税的缴纳必须在产生 ECTI 的合伙企业纳税年度内缴纳。出于美国所得税目的，合伙企业必须在其纳税年度的第 4、6、9 和 12 个月的 15 日之前向 IRS 为其外国合伙人缴纳部分年度预扣税。任何额外应付金额均需通过 8804 表格（稍后讨论的年度合伙企业预扣税申报表）支付。.

A foreign partner's share of withholding tax paid by a partnership is treated as distributed to the partner on the earliest of:  
外国合伙人在合伙企业中所缴纳的预扣税份额被视为在以下时间（以最早者为准）分配给合伙人：

*   The day on which the tax was paid by the partnership,  
    合伙企业缴纳税款的日期，
    
*   The last day of the partnership's tax year for which the tax was paid, or  
    合伙企业纳税年度的最后一天，或者
    
*   The last day on which the partner owned an interest in the partnership during that year.  
    合伙人当年拥有合伙企业权益的最后一天。
    

The amount treated as distributed to the partner resulting from an installment payment is generally treated as an advance or draw under Regulations section 1.731-1(a)(1)(ii) to the extent of the partner's share of income for the partnership year.  
根据《条例》第 1.731-1(a)(1)(ii) 条，因分期付款而分配给合伙人的金额通常被视为预付款或提款，以合伙人在合伙企业年度的收入份额为限。

**Notification to partners.**

In most cases, a partnership must notify each foreign partner of the tax withheld on its behalf within 10 days of the installment payment date. No particular form is required for this notification. For more information on the substance of the notification and exceptions, see Regulations section 1.1446-3(d)(1)(i).

  

**通知合作伙伴。** 

在大多数情况下，合伙企业必须在分期付款日期后 10 天内将代表其扣缴的税款通知每个外国合伙人。此通知不需要特定的表格。有关通知实质内容和例外情况的更多信息，请参阅法规第 1.1446-3(d)(1)(i) 节。

**Real property transfers.**

If a domestic partnership disposes of a USRPI, gain or loss from the sale allocable to a foreign partner is treated as effectively connected to the conduct of a U.S. trade or business and is included in ECTI. The partnership or withholding agent must withhold following the rules discussed here for section 1446(a) withholding. A domestic partnership's compliance with these rules satisfies the requirements for withholding on the disposition of _[U.S. real property interests](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest")_ (discussed later).

  

**不动产转让。** 

如果国内合伙企业处置 USRPI，则分配给外国合伙人的销售收益或损失将被视为与美国贸易或业务活动有效相关，并包含在 ECTI 中。合伙企业或扣缴义务人必须按照此处讨论的第 1446(a) 节扣缴税款规则扣缴税款。国内合伙企业遵守这些规则即可满足处置_[美国不动产权益](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest")_的预扣税要求（稍后讨论）。

If a foreign partnership disposes of a U.S. property interest, the transferee must withhold under section 1445(a), although gain or loss from the sale is also treated as effectively connected to the conduct of a U.S. trade or business and is included in ECTI. The foreign partnership may credit the amount withheld under section 1445(a) that is allocable to foreign partners against its tax liability under section 1446.  
如果外国合伙企业处置美国财产权益，受让人必须根据第 1445(a) 条扣缴税款，尽管出售所得的收益或损失也被视为与美国贸易或业务活动有效相关并包含在 ECTI 中。外国合伙企业可以将根据第 1445(a) 条扣缴的可分配给外国合伙人的金额抵扣其根据第 1446 条规定的纳税义务。

**Transfers of interests in partnerships engaged in the conduct of a U.S. trade or bussines.**

If a domestic partnership transfers a direct or indirect interest in another partnership engaged in the conduct of a U.S. trade or business, gain or loss from the sale allocable to a foreign partner that is treated under section 864(c)(8) as effectively connected to the conduct of a U.S. trade or business is included in ECTI.

  

**从事美国贸易或业务的合伙企业的利益转让。** 

如果国内合伙企业转让从事美国贸易或业务的另一合伙企业的直接或间接权益，则出售收益或损失可分配给根据第 864(c)(8) 条视为有效关联的外国合伙人ECTI 涵盖了美国贸易或业务的开展。

If a foreign partnership transfers an interest in another partnership for a gain and section 864(c)(8) treats any portion of that gain as effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business in the United States, then the partnership will be withheld upon under section 1446(f)(1). The foreign partnership may credit the amount withheld under section 1446(f)(1) that is allocable to foreign partners against its tax liability under section 1446(a).  
如果外国合伙企业转让另一合伙企业的权益以获取收益，并且第 864(c)(8) 条将该收益的任何部分视为与在美国进行的贸易或业务有效相关，则该合伙企业将被扣缴根据第 1446(f)(1) 条。外国合伙企业可以将根据第 1446(f)(1) 条规定分配给外国合伙人的预扣金额抵免其根据第 1446(a) 条规定的纳税义务。

#### Reporting and Paying the Tax  
申报和纳税

Three forms are required for reporting and paying over tax withheld on ECTI allocable to foreign partners. This does not apply to publicly traded partnerships, discussed later.  
报告和支付分配给外国合作伙伴的 ECTI 预扣税需要三份表格。这不适用于公开交易的合伙企业，稍后讨论。

**Form 8804.**

The withholding tax liability of the partnership for its tax year is reported on Form 8804. Form 8804 is also a transmittal form for Forms 8805.

  

**表格 8804。** 

合伙企业在其纳税年度的预扣税责任在表格 8804 上报告。表格 8804 也是表格 8805 的传输表格。

Any additional withholding tax owed for the partnership's tax year is paid (in U.S. currency) with Form 8804.  
合伙企业纳税年度所欠的任何额外预扣税均通过 8804 表格缴纳（以美元）。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/duedate.gif)
_File_ [Form 8804](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8804) _by the 15th day of the 3rd month after the close of the partnership's tax year. If you need more time to file Form 8804, file Form 7004 to request an extension of time to file. Form 7004 does not extend the time to pay the tax._  
在合伙企业纳税年度结束后第三个月的 15 日之前提交 8804 表格。如果您需要更多时间提交 8804 表格，请提交 7004 表格以请求延长提交时间。 7004 表不会延长纳税时间。.

**Form 8805.**

This form is used to show the amount of ECTI and any withholding tax payments allocable to a foreign partner for the partnership's tax year. At the end of the partnership's tax year, [Form 8805](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8805) must be sent to each foreign partner on whose behalf tax under section 1446 was withheld or whose Form 8804-C the partnership considered, whether or not any withholding tax is paid. It must be delivered to the foreign partner by the due date of the partnership return (including extensions). A copy of Form 8805 for each foreign partner must also be attached to Form 8804 when it is filed. Also attach the most recent Form 8804-C, discussed earlier, to the Form 8805 filed for the partnership's tax year in which the [Form 8804-C](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8804C) was considered.

  

**8805 表格。** 

此表格用于显示 ECTI 金额以及在合伙企业纳税年度分配给外国合伙人的任何预扣税款。在合伙企业的纳税年度结束时，必须将 8805 表格发送给代表其根据第 1446 条扣缴税款的每个外国合伙人，或合伙企业考虑其 8804-C 表格，无论是否缴纳任何预扣税。它必须在合伙企业申报表（包括延期）到期日之前交付给外国合伙人。提交 8804 表格时，每个外国合伙人还必须附上 8805 表格的副本。还要将前面讨论过的最新 8804-C 表格附加到为考虑 8804-C 表格的合伙企业纳税年度提交的 8805 表格中。

A copy of Form 8805 must be attached to the foreign partner's U.S. income tax return to take a credit on its Form 1040-NR or Form 1120-F.  
外国合作伙伴的美国所得税申报表必须附有 8805 表的副本，以便在其 1040-NR 表或 1120-F 表上获得抵免。

**Form 8813.**

This form is used to make payments of withheld tax to the U.S. Treasury. Payments must be made in U.S. currency by the payment dates (see [_Date payments are due_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225075), earlier). See the Instructions for Form 8804-C for when you must attach a copy of that form to [Form 8813](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8813).

  

**表格 8813。** 

该表格用于向美国财政部缴纳预扣税。必须在付款日期之前以美元付款（请参阅[_付款到期日_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225075)，较早）。请参阅表格 8804-C 的说明，了解何时必须将该表格的副本附加到[表格 8813](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8813)中。

**Penalties.**

A penalty may be imposed for failure to file Form 8804 when due (including extensions). It is generally the same as the penalty for not filing Form 1042, discussed earlier under _Failure to file Form 1042._

  

**处罚。** 

如果未能按时提交 8804 表格（包括延期），可能会受到处罚。它通常与未提交 1042 表格的处罚相同，如前面_未提交 1042 表格所述。_

A penalty may be imposed for failure to file Form 8805 when due (including extensions) or for failure to provide complete and correct information. The amount of the penalty depends on when you file a correct Form 8805. The penalty for each Form 8805 is generally the same as the penalty for not filing Form 1042-S. For more information, see _Penalties_ in the 2024 Instructions for Form 1042-S.  
如果未能按时提交 8805 表格（包括延期）或未能提供完整且正确的信息，可能会受到处罚。罚款金额取决于您何时提交正确的 8805 表格。每份 8805 表格的罚款通常与未提交 1042-S 表格的罚款相同。有关更多信息，请参阅 1042-S 表格 2024 年说明中的_处罚_。

If you fail to provide a complete and correct Form 8805 to each partner when due (including extensions), a penalty may be imposed. The amount of the penalty depends on when you provide the correct Form 8805. The penalty for each Form 8805 is generally the same as the penalty for not providing a correct and complete Form 1042-S. For more information, see _Penalties_ in the 2024 Instructions for Form 1042-S.  
如果您未能在到期时（包括延期）向每个合作伙伴提供完整且正确的 8805 表格，可能会受到处罚。罚款金额取决于您何时提供正确的 8805 表格。每份 8805 表格的罚款通常与未提供正确且完整的 1042-S 表格的罚款相同。有关更多信息，请参阅 1042-S 表格 2024 年说明中的_处罚_。

_**Exception.**_

No penalty is imposed if you meet certain requirements. The rules are the same as for Form 1042-S. However, if a filer intentionally disregards the requirement to file Form 8805 when due, to furnish Form 8805 to the recipient when due, or to report correct information, the penalty for each Form 8805 (or statement to recipient) may be higher.

  

_**例外。** _

如果您满足某些要求，则不会受到处罚。规则与表格 1042-S 相同。但是，如果申报人故意忽视在到期时提交 8805 表格、在到期时向收件人提供 8805 表格或报告正确信息的要求，则每份 8805 表格（或向收件人提供的声明）的处罚可能会更高。

For more information, see _Penalties_ in the 2024 Instructions for Form 1042-S.  
有关更多信息，请参阅 1042-S 表格 2024 年说明中的_处罚_。

**Identification numbers.**

A partnership that has not been assigned a U.S. EIN must obtain one. If a number has not been assigned by the due date of the first withholding tax payment, the partnership should enter the date the number was applied for on Form 8813 when making its payment. As soon as the partnership receives its EIN, it must immediately provide that number to the IRS.

  

**识别号码。** 

尚未分配美国 EIN 的合伙企业必须获得一个。如果在首次预扣税缴纳到期日之前尚未分配号码，合伙企业应在付款时在 8813 表格中输入申请该号码的日期。合伙企业收到 EIN 后，必须立即向 IRS 提供该号码。

To ensure proper crediting of the withholding tax when reporting to the IRS, the partnership must include each partner's U.S. TIN on Form 8805. If there are partners in the partnership without identification numbers, the partnership should inform them of the need to get a number. See [_U.S. or Foreign TINs_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225029 "U.S. or Foreign TINs"), earlier.  
为了确保在向 IRS 报告时正确扣除预扣税，合伙企业必须在 8805 表格中包含每个合伙人的美国纳税人识别号。如果合伙企业中有合伙人没有身份证号码，合伙企业应告知他们需要获取号码。请参阅前面的[_美国或外国 TIN_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225029 "U.S. or Foreign TINs") 。

#### Publicly Traded Partnership Distributions (PTP Distributions)  
公开交易的合作伙伴分配（PTP 分配）

A PTP that has ECTI must pay withholding tax under section 1446(a) on any distributions of that income made to its foreign partners. A PTP must use Forms 1042 and 1042-S (Income Code 27) to report withholding from PTP distributions. The rate of withholding is 37% for noncorporate partners and 21% for corporate partners under section 1446(a).  
拥有 ECTI 的 PTP 必须根据第 1446(a) 条就向其外国合作伙伴分配的任何收入缴纳预扣税。 PTP 必须使用表格 1042 和 1042-S（收入代码 27）报告 PTP 分配中的预扣税款。根据第 1446(a) 条，非公司合伙人的预扣税率为 37%，公司合伙人的预扣税率为 21%。

A publicly traded partnership (PTP) is any partnership an interest in which is regularly traded on an established securities market or is readily tradable on a secondary market. These rules do not apply to a PTP treated as a corporation under section 7704.  
公开交易合伙企业 (PTP) 是指其权益在成熟的证券市场上定期交易或易于在二级市场上交易的任何合伙企业。这些规则不适用于根据第 7704 条被视为公司的 PTP。

**Foreign partner.**

The partnership determines whether a partner is a foreign partner using the rules discussed earlier under [_Foreign Partner_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225069 "Foreign Partner").

  

**国外合作伙伴。** 

合伙企业使用前面讨论的外国[_合伙人下的规则来确定合伙人是否为外国_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225069 "Foreign Partner")合伙人。

**Nominee.**

The withholding agent under section 1446(a) can be the PTP or a nominee. Starting in 2023, a nominee for section 1446(a) purposes is a person receiving a PTP distribution on behalf of a foreign person and that is a domestic person, a U.S. branch of a foreign corporation that is treated as a U.S. person, or a QI that assumes primary withholding responsibility for the distribution. See Regulations section 1.1446-4(b)(3) (describing nominees and their withholding requirements). For purposes of section 1446(a) withholding, a nominee generally determines whether a partner is a foreign partner under the same requirements applicable to a PTP. See [_Foreign partner_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225086 "Foreign partner."), directly above. A nominee for a PTP distribution must, in addition to withholding on the distribution to the extent required under section 1446(a), withhold on amounts attributable to the distribution that are subject to withholding under chapters 3 and 4, in addition to withholding under section 1446(f) on an amount realized on the distribution. See _[Ordering rules](#en_US_2024_publink1000225089 "Ordering rules.")_ and _[Section 1446(f): PTP Interests](#en_US_2024_publink1000115526 "Section 1446(f): PTP Interests")_, later. A nominee determines each amount subject to withholding on a PTP distribution based on a qualified notice issued by the PTP making the distribution or, in the absence of a qualified notice (or when a qualified notice does not specify each amount attributable to the distribution), based on the withholding default rule in section 1.1446-4(d).

  

**提名人。** 

第 1446(a) 条规定的扣缴义务人可以是 PTP 或指定人。从 2023 年开始，第 1446(a) 条的提名人是代表外国人接收 PTP 分配的人，该人是国内人士、被视为美国人的外国公司的美国分支机构，或QI 承担分配的主要预扣责任。请参阅法规第 1.1446-4(b)(3) 节（描述提名人及其预扣税要求）。就第 1446(a) 条预扣税而言，提名人通常会根据适用于 PTP 的相同要求来确定合伙人是否为外国合伙人。请参阅上方的外国合作伙伴。 PTP 分配的提名人除了根据第 1446(a) 条的要求对分配进行预扣之外，还必须根据第 3 章和第 4 章的规定预扣分配中应予预扣的金额。 1446(f) 关于分配实现的金额。请参阅稍后的订购规则和第 1446(f) 节：PTP 权益。被提名人根据进行分配的 PTP 发出的合格通知确定 PTP 分配中应预扣的每笔金额，或者在没有合格通知的情况下（或当合格通知未指定可归属于分配的每笔金额时），基于第 1.1446-4(d) 节中的预扣默认规则。

A PTP or a nominee for a PTP distribution is not generally required to withhold on the distribution, however, when it pays the distribution to a nominee for the distribution. In such a case, the PTP or nominee is required to report the nominee to which it pays the distribution as the recipient for Form 1042-S reporting. If a PTP or nominee pays a PTP distribution to an NQI, however, the PTP or nominee must generally determine its withholding based on a withholding statement and partner documentation provided by the NQI with respect to the distribution. An NQI for this purpose includes a U.S. branch that is not acting a U.S. person for a PTP distribution. See the Instructions for Form W-8IMY for additional information on payments of PTP distributions made to NQIs. If a PTP or nominee for a PTP distribution pays the distribution to a QI not acting as a nominee for the distribution, the PTP or nominee can determine its withholding based on withholding rate pool information provided by the QI or partner information provided by a QI that acts as a disclosing QI. See Revenue Procedure 2022-43 for information on the withholding and other requirements of QIs acting as nominees or as disclosing QIs for PTP distributions (starting January 1, 2023). See the Instructions for Form 1042-S for the reporting of a PTP distribution paid to an account holder of a disclosing QI and when a nominee for a PTP distribution is required to report information about the PTP making a distribution on a Form 1042-S.  
然而，当 PTP 或 PTP 分配的提名人向分配的提名人支付分配时，通常不需要预扣分配税。在这种情况下，PTP 或被提名人必须将其支付分配的被提名人报告为 1042-S 表格报告的接收者。然而，如果 PTP 或被提名人向 NQI 支付 PTP 分配，则 PTP 或被提名人通常必须根据 NQI 提供的与分配有关的预扣税声明和合作伙伴文件来确定其预扣税。用于此目的的 NQI 包括不代表美国人进行 PTP 分发的美国分支机构。有关向 NQI 支付 PTP 分配的更多信息，请参阅表格 W-8IMY 的说明。如果 PTP 或 PTP 分配的提名人向不作为分配提名人的 QI 支付分配，PTP 或提名人可以根据 QI 提供的预扣税率池信息或 QI 提供的合作伙伴信息确定其预扣税款，充当披露性 QI。请参阅收入程序 2022-43，了解有关作为提名人或 PTP 分配的 QI 披露的 QI 的预扣税和其他要求的信息（自 2023 年 1 月 1 日开始）。请参阅表格 1042-S 的说明，了解向披露 QI 的账户持有人支付的 PTP 分配的报告，以及何时要求 PTP 分配的提名人在表格 1042-S 上报告有关进行分配的 PTP 的信息。

**Distributions subject to withholding.**

The partnership or nominee must withhold tax on any actual distributions of money or property to foreign partners. The amount of the distribution includes the amount of any tax under section 1446(a) required to be withheld. In the case of a partnership that receives a partnership distribution from another partnership (a tiered partnership), the distribution also includes the tax withheld from that distribution.

  

**分配须予扣缴。** 

合伙企业或被提名人必须就向外国合伙人实际分配的任何金钱或财产预扣税款。分配金额包括根据第 1446(a) 条要求预扣的任何税款。如果合伙企业从另一个合伙企业（分层合伙企业）接收合伙企业分配，则该分配还包括从该分配中预扣的税款。

If the distribution is in property other than money, the partnership cannot release the property until it has enough funds to pay over the withholding tax.  
如果分配的是金钱以外的财产，则合伙企业在有足够的资金支付预扣税之前不能释放该财产。

A PTP or nominee that complies with these withholding requirements satisfies the requirements discussed later under [_U.S. Real Property Interest_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest"). Distributions subject to withholding include:  
符合这些预扣税要求的 PTP 或被提名人就满足了稍后在[_美国不动产权益_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225090 "U.S. Real Property Interest")下讨论的要求。需预扣税款的分配包括：

*   Amounts subject to withholding under section 1445(e)(1) on distributions pursuant to an election under Regulations section 1.1445-5(c)(3), and  
    根据第 1445(e)(1) 条规定，根据条例第 1.1445-5(c)(3) 条规定进行的分配，需预扣的金额，以及
    
*   Amounts not subject to withholding under section 1445 because the distributee is a partnership or is a foreign corporation that has made an election to be treated as a domestic corporation.  
    由于受让人是合伙企业或选择被视为国内公司的外国公司，因此无需根据第 1445 条预扣税款。
    

_**Ordering rules.**_

Partnership distributions are considered to be paid out of the following types of income in the order listed.

  

_**订购规则。** _

合伙分配被视为按所列顺序从以下类型的收入中支付。

1.  Amounts attributable to income described in section 1441 or 1442 that are not effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business in the United States and are subject to withholding under Regulations section 1.1441-2(a).  
    第 1441 或 1442 条中所述收入的金额，与在美国进行的贸易或业务没有实际联系，并且根据条例第 1.1441-2(a) 条规定需预扣税款。
    
2.  Amounts attributable to income described in section 1441 or 1442 that are not effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business in the United States and are not subject to withholding under Regulations section 1.1441-2(a).  
    第 1441 或 1442 条中所述收入的金额，与在美国进行的贸易或业务没有实际联系，并且不受条例第 1.1441-2(a) 条规定的预扣税。
    
3.  Amounts attributable to income effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business in the United States and not subject to withholding under Regulations section 1.1446-1 through 1.1446-6.  
    与在美国进行贸易或业务实际相关的收入所产生的金额，并且不受条例第 1.1446-1 至 1.1446-6 条规定的预扣税的限制。
    
4.  Amounts subject to withholding under Regulations section 1.1446-1 through 1.1446-6.  
    根据条例第 1.1446-1 至 1.1446-6 条规定需预扣的金额。
    
5.  Other amounts not listed above.  
    上面未列出的其他金额。
    

**Depositing taxes a PTP withholds under section 1446.**

The general rules for making payments of taxes withheld under section 1446(a) do not apply to PTP distributions. Instead, apply the rules discussed earlier, under [_Depositing Withheld Taxes_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225033 "Depositing Withheld Taxes").

  

**PTP 根据第 1446 条扣缴的存款税。** 

根据第 1446(a) 条缴纳预扣税款的一般规则不适用于 PTP 分配。相反，请应用之前在[_存入预扣税项_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225033 "Depositing Withheld Taxes")下讨论的规则。

#### Section 1446(f) Withholding  
第 1446(f) 条 预扣税

Section 13501 of the TCJA added section 1446(f) effective for transfers of partnership interests occurring on or after January 1, 2018. It generally requires that a transferee of an interest in a partnership withhold 10% of the amount realized on the disposition if any portion of the gain (if any) would be treated under section 864(c)(8) as effectively connected with the conduct of a trade or business within the United States. A transfer can occur when a partnership distribution results in gain under section 731. Under section 1446(f)(4), if the transferee fails to withhold any required amount, the partnership must deduct and withhold from distributions to the transferee the amount that the transferee failed to withhold (plus interest).  
TCJA 第 13501 条添加了第 1446(f) 条，该条对 2018 年 1 月 1 日或之后发生的合伙企业权益转让有效。它通常要求合伙企业权益的受让人预扣处置中实现的金额的 10%（如果有）根据第 864(c)(8) 条，该部分收益（如有）将被视为与在美国境内进行的贸易或业务有效相关。当合伙企业分配产生第 731 条规定的收益时，即可发生转让。根据第 1446(f)(4) 条，如果受让人未能预扣任何所需金额，则合伙企业必须从向受让人分配的金额中扣除并预扣该金额。受让人未能扣留（加利息）。

Notice 2018-08, 2018-07 I.R.B. 352, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2018-07\_IRB#NOT-2018-08](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2018-07_IRB#NOT-2018-08), temporarily suspended the application of section 1446(f) to the disposition of certain PTP interests.  
通知 2018-08、2018-07 IRB 352（可在[IRS.gov/irb/2018-07\_IRB#NOT-2018-08](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2018-07_IRB#NOT-2018-08)获取）暂时中止了第 1446(f) 条对某些 PTP 权益处置的适用。

Notice 2018-29, 2018-16 I.R.B. 495, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2018-16\_IRB#NOT-2018-29](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2018-16_IRB#NOT-2018-29), provides interim guidance regarding withholding of U.S. tax related to transfers of interests in partnerships, other than PTPs, under section 1446(f). It also temporarily suspended withholding under section 1446(f)(4).  
公告 2018-29、2018-16 IRB 495（可在[IRS.gov/irb/2018-16\_IRB#NOT-2018-29](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2018-16_IRB#NOT-2018-29)获取）提供了有关预扣与合伙企业（PTP 除外）权益转让相关的美国税款的临时指南，第1446(f)条。它还根据第 1446(f)(4) 条暂时中止了预扣税。

On May 7, 2019, the Department of Treasury and the IRS issued proposed regulations under section 1446(f) (84 FR 21198) for transfers of both non-PTP and PTP interests. During the period that Notice 2018-29 applies, instead of applying the rules described in the Notice, taxpayers and other affected persons may choose to apply Regulations sections 1.1446(f)-1, 1.1446(f)-2, and 1.1446(f)-5 of the proposed regulations in their entirety to all transfers as if they were final regulations.  
2019 年 5 月 7 日，财政部和国税局根据第 1446(f) 条 (84 FR 21198) 发布了关于非 PTP 和 PTP 权益转让的拟议法规。在 2018-29 号通知适用期间，纳税人和其他受影响人员可以选择应用条例第 1.1446(f)-1、1.1446(f)-2 和 1.1446(f) 条，而不是应用通知中所述的规则。 -5 的拟议法规全部适用于所有转让，就好像它们是最终法规一样。

On November 30, 2020, the Department of Treasury and the IRS issued final regulations under section 1446(f) in T.D. 9926 (85 FR 76910) for transfers of both non-PTP and PTP interests. The final regulations require any transferee to withhold a tax equal to 10% of the amount realized on any transfer of a partnership interest (other than certain PTP interests) under section 1446(f)(1), unless an exception to withholding applies. These regulations generally apply to transfers that occur on or after January 29, 2021. However, in accordance with Notice 2021-51, 2021-36 I.R.B. 361, the rules related to withholding under section 1446(f)(4) and to transfers of PTP interests apply to transfers occurring on or after January 1, 2023. Additionally, the final regulations revised certain provisions in Regulations section 1.1446-4 for withholding under section 1446(a) on PTP distributions. Also in accordance with Notice 2021-51, these revisions apply to PTP distributions made on or after January 1, 2023. Notices 2018-8 and 2018-29 apply to transfers that occur before the effective date of the final regulations or, as previously described, taxpayers may apply the proposed regulations to transfers of non-PTP interests during this time.  
2020 年 11 月 30 日，财政部和 IRS 根据 TD 9926 (85 FR 76910) 第 1446(f) 条发布了关于非 PTP 和 PTP 权益转让的最终规定。最终法规要求任何受让人根据第 1446(f)(1) 条扣缴相当于任何合伙权益（某些 PTP 权益除外）转让所实现金额 10% 的税款，除非适用扣缴例外情况。这些规定通常适用于 2021 年 1 月 29 日或之后发生的转让。但是，根据通知 2021-51、2021-36 IRB 361、与第 1446(f)(4) 条规定的预扣税以及转让相关的规则PTP 利息适用于 2023 年 1 月 1 日或之后发生的转让。此外，最终法规修订了法规部分中的某些规定1.1446-4 根据第 1446(a) 条关于 PTP 分配的预扣税。另外，根据通知 2021-51，这些修订适用于 2023 年 1 月 1 日或之后进行的 PTP 分配。通知 2018-8 和 2018-29 适用于在最终法规生效日期之前或如前所述发生的转让，纳税人可以在此期间将拟议的规定应用于非 PTP 利益的转让。

#### Section 1446(f): Non-PTP Interests  
第 1446(f) 条：非 PTP 利益

**Exceptions to withholding on transfers of non-PTP interests.  
非 PTP 权益转让的预扣税例外情况。** 

A transferee, including a partnership when the partner is a distributee, is not required to withhold on the transfer of a non-PTP interest if it properly relies on one of the following six certifications, the requirements of which are more fully described in the referenced regulations. A transferee may not rely on a certification if it has actual knowledge that the certification is incorrect or unreliable. A partnership that is a transferee because it makes a distribution may not rely on its books and records if it knows, or has reason to know, that the information is incorrect or unreliable. A certification must provide the name and address of the person providing it, be signed under penalties of perjury, and generally include the taxpayer identification number of the transferor. See Regulations sections 1.1446(f)-1(c)(2)(i) and 1.1446(f)-2(b)(1). Also, separate rules apply if the transfer results from a partnership distribution. Only the certification in exception six must be submitted to the IRS.  
受让人（包括合作伙伴（当合伙人是受让人时的合伙企业））如果正确依赖以下六种认证之一，则无需在非 PTP 权益的转让中预扣税款，其要求在参考文献中进行了更全面的描述法规。如果受让人实际知道认证不正确或不可靠，则不得依赖该认证。因进行分配而成为受让人的合伙企业，如果其知道或有理由知道信息不正确或不可靠，则不得依赖其账簿和记录。证明必须提供提供者的姓名和地址，签署后将受到伪证罪的处罚，并且通常包括转让人的纳税人识别号。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-1(c)(2)(i) 和 1.1446(f)-2(b)(1) 节。此外，如果转让是由合伙分配产生的，则适用单独的规则。只有例外六中的证明必须提交给 IRS。

The certifications in several of the exceptions are based on a **determination date**. The determination date must be one of the following: (a) the date of the transfer; (b) any date no more than 60 days before the date of the transfer; or (c) if the transferor is not a controlling partner, as defined in Regulations section 1.1446(f)-1(b)(2), the later of (i) the first day of the partnership’s taxable year in which the transfer occurs, or (ii) the date before the transfer of the partnership’s most recent capital account revaluation event. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-1(c)(4).  
一些例外情况中的认证是基于**确定日期的**。确定日期必须是以下日期之一： (a) 转让日期； (b) 转让日期之前不超过 60 天的任何日期； (c) 如果转让人不是法规第 1.1446(f)-1(b)(2) 条中定义的控股合伙人，则 (i) 转让发生的合伙企业纳税年度的第一天（以较晚者为准） ，或 (ii) 合伙企业最近一次资本账户重估事件转移之前的日期。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-1(c)(4) 条。

1.  **Certification of non-foreign status.**The transferor provides a certification of non-foreign status signed under penalties of perjury that states that the transferor is not a foreign person, and provides the transferor’s name, TIN, and address. A certificate of non-foreign status includes a Form W-9. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(b)(2).  
    **非外国人身份证明。** 转让人提供一份非外国人身份证明，该证明签署后将受到伪证处罚，表明转让人不是外国人，并提供转让人的姓名、纳税人识别号和地址。非外国人身份证明包括 W-9 表格。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-2(b)(2) 条。
    
2.  **Certification of no realized gain.** The transferor provides a certification that there was no realized gain on the transfer of the partnership interest (including no ordinary income arising from the application of section 751 and Regulations section 1.751-1) as of the determination date. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(b)(3).  
    **未实现收益的证明。** 转让人提供证明，证明截至确定日期，合伙企业权益转让没有实现收益（包括没有因适用第 751 条和《条例》第 1.751-1 条而产生的普通收入）。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-2(b)(3) 条。
    
3.  **Certification of less than 10% effectively connected gain.** The partnership provides a certification stating that:  
    **有效连接增益低于 10% 的认证。** 该合作伙伴提供了一份证明，声明：
    
    1.  On the deemed sale of the partnership assets in the manner described in Regulations section 1.864(c)(8)-1(c) as of the determination date either: the partnership would have no effectively connected gain (or the net amount of its effectively connected gain would be less than 10% of the total net gain) on all its assets; or the transferor’s distributive share of net effectively connected gain resulting from the deemed sale would be less than 10% of the transferor’s distributive share of the total net gain; or  
        自确定之日起，按照《条例》第 1.864(c)(8)-1(c) 条所述方式视同出售合伙企业资产：该合伙企业将没有有效关联收益（或其有效收益净额）。其所有资产的关联收益将低于总净收益的 10%；或转让方在视同出售产生​​的实际关联净收益中的分配份额将低于转让方在总净收益中的分配份额的10%；或者
        
    2.  The partnership was not engaged in a trade or business within the United States at any time during the taxable year of the partnership until the date of transfer. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(b)(4).  
        在合伙企业纳税年度的任何时间，直到转让之日，该合伙企业均未在美国境内从事贸易或业务。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-2(b)(4) 条。
        
    
4.  **Certification of Less Than 10% effectively connected income.** The transferor provides a certification that:  
    **有效关联收入低于 10% 的认证。** 转让方提供以下证明：
    
    1.  The transferor was a partner in the partnership for the transferor’s immediately prior tax year (for which it has already received a Schedule K-1) and the 2 preceding tax years (the look back period) and had a distributive share of gross income from the partnership in each of these years;  
        转让人在转让人的前一个纳税年度（已收到附表 K-1）和前 2 个纳税年度（回顾期）是合伙企业的合伙人，并且在转让人的总收入中享有分配份额每年的合作伙伴关系；
        
    2.  The transferor’s distributive share of gross ECI from the partnership, and any persons related to the transferor, as reported on a Schedule K-1 (Form 1065) or other statement required by the partnership, was less than $1 million for each of the tax years during the look back period;  
        根据附表 K-1（表格 1065）或合伙企业要求的其他报表中的报告，转让人从合伙企业以及与转让人相关的任何人中分配的 ECI 总额在每个纳税年度均少于 100 万美元在回顾期间；
        
    3.  The transferor’s distributive share of partnership gross ECI, as reported on a Schedule K-1 or K-3 (Form 1065) or other statement required by the partnership, for each year during the look-back period, was less than 10% of its total distributive share of partnership gross income; and  
        在回顾期内，转让人在合伙企业总 ECI 中的分配份额（如附表 K-1 或 K-3（表格 1065）或合伙企业要求的其他声明中所报告的），在回顾期内每年低于其合伙企业总 ECI 的 10%。合伙企业总收入的总分配份额；和
        
    4.  For each year during the look-back period, the transferor’s distributive share of partnership ECI or gain (or losses properly allocated and apportioned to that income) has been timely reported on a federal income tax return of the transferor (or if the transferor was a partnership, its direct or indirect nonresident alien and foreign corporate partners) and any tax due with respect to such amounts have been timely paid, provided the return was required to be filed when the transferor furnishes the certification. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(b)(5).  
        在回顾期内的每一年，转让人在合伙企业 ECI 或收益（或正确分配并分摊到该收入的损失）中的分配份额已及时报告在转让人的联邦所得税申报表上（或者如果转让人是合伙企业、其直接或间接的非居民外国人和外国公司合伙人）以及与此类金额相关的任何应缴税款均已及时缴纳，前提是转让人提供证明时需要提交纳税申报表。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-2(b)(5) 条。
        
    
5.  **Certification of nonrecognition.** The transferor provides a certification that it is not required to recognize any gain or loss with respect to the transfer by reason of the operation of a nonrecognition provision of the Internal Revenue Code. The certification must briefly describe the transfer and provide the relevant law and facts relating to the certification. This exception does not apply if only a portion of the gain is not recognized. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(b)(6).  
    **不认可证明。** 转让方提供证明，证明其无需因《国内税收法》不承认条款的实施而确认与转让相关的任何收益或损失。证明必须简要描述转让并提供与证明有关的相关法律和事实。如果仅部分收益未被确认，则此例外情况不适用。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-2(b)(6) 条。
    
6.  **Certification that an income tax treaty applies.**The transferor provides a certification using Form W-8BEN or W-8BEN-E, as applicable, or applicable substitute form that meets the requirements under Regulations section 1.1446-1(c)(5) that the transferor is not subject to tax on any gain from the transfer pursuant to an income tax treaty. The transferor may not provide this certification if any portion of the gain is subject to tax. The form should contain the information necessary to support the claim for treaty benefits. Within 30 days after the date of the transfer, the transferee must mail certain information, plus a copy of the certificate, to the IRS, at the address in the Instructions for Form 8288. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(b)(7).  
    **证明所得税协定适用。** 转让人使用表格 W-8BEN 或 W-8BEN-E（如适用）或符合条例第 1.1446-1(c)(5) 条要求的适用替代表格提供证明，证明转让人无需就任何税项缴税。根据所得税协定从转让中获得的收益。如果收益的任何部分需要纳税，转让方不得提供此证明。该表格应包含支持条约优惠主张所需的信息。转让之日起 30 天内，受让人必须将某些信息以及证书副本邮寄至 IRS，地址位于表格 8288 说明中。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-2(b) 条（7）。
    

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_See the discussion, later, regarding certification of maximum tax lability if a nonrecognition provision applies to only a portion of the gain realized on the transfer or only a portion of the gain on the transfer is not subject to tax pursuant to an income tax treaty.  
请参阅稍后关于最大纳税义务证明的讨论，如果不承认条款仅适用于转让中实现的收益的一部分，或者根据所得税条约仅部分转让收益不需纳税。_.

A non-PTP making a distribution to a partner may generally rely on any of the above exceptions, with certain additional considerations:  
非 PTP 向合作伙伴进行分配通常可能依赖上述任何例外情况，但需要考虑一些额外因素：

*   In Exception 2, the no realized gain exception, a distributing partnership generally may rely on its books and records or on a certification from the distributee partner.  
    在例外 2（未实现收益例外）中，分销合伙企业通常可以依赖其账簿和记录或分销合作伙伴的证明。
    
*   In Exception 4, the less than 10% ECI exception, a distributing partnership may generally rely on its books and records but must also obtain a representation from the distributee partner stating that the distributee partner satisfies the reporting and tax payment requirements with respect to the partnership’s ECI for the look-back period.  
    在例外 4（低于 10% ECI 的例外）中，分配合伙企业通常可以依赖其账簿和记录，但还必须获得受分配合伙人的陈述，表明受分配合伙人满足合伙企业的报告和纳税要求。回顾期的 ECI。
    

**Determining the amount to withhold.**

In general, the transferee must withhold 10% of the amount realized. The amount realized includes the cash paid, the fair market value of property transferred, plus the assumption of and relief from liabilities, and liabilities to which the partnership interest is subject. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(c)(2)(i). If certain requirements are met, the transferee may rely on a certification of the amount of the transferor's share of partnership liabilities reported on the most recent Schedule K-1 (Form 1065) issued by the partnership or a certification from a partnership that provides the amount of the transferor's share of partnership liabilities as of the determination date. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(c)(2)(ii) and (iii).

  

**确定扣留金额。** 

一般来说，受让方必须预扣变现金额的10%。变现金额包括支付的现金、转让财产的公平市场价值、加上承担和免除的负债以及合伙权益所承担的负债。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-2(c)(2)(i) 条。如果满足某些要求，受让人可以依赖合伙企业签发的最新附表 K-1（表格 1065）上报告的转让人在合伙企业负债中所占份额的金额证明，或合伙企业提供的提供该金额的证明截至确定日期，转让人在合伙企业负债中的份额。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-2(c)(2)(ii) 和 (iii) 条。

_**Modified amount realized.**_

If a foreign partnership is the transferor, separate rules may apply to determine a modified amount realized. The modified amount realized is determined by multiplying the amount realized by the aggregate percentage computed as of the determination date. The aggregate percentage is the percentage of the gain (if any) arising from the transfer that would be allocated to any presumed foreign taxable persons. For this purpose, a presumed foreign taxable person is any person that has not provided a certificate of non-foreign status, as previously described in the Exception 1 to withholding, or a certification that pursuant to a tax treaty no portion of the foreign taxable person’s gain is subject to tax. The certification the transferor foreign partnership provides does not need to be submitted to the IRS. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(c)(2)(iv).

  

_**修改后的实现金额。** _

如果外国合伙企业是转让人，则可能适用单独的规则来确定修改后的变现金额。修改后的实现金额是通过将实现金额乘以截至确定日期计算的总百分比来确定的。总百分比是分配给任何推定外国纳税人的转让收益（如果有）的百分比。为此目的，推定外国应税人是指未提供非外国身份证明（如前述预扣税例外 1 中所述）的任何人，或未根据税收协定提供外国应税人的任何部分的证明的人。收益需缴税。转让方外国合伙企业提供的证明无需提交给美国国税局。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-2(c)(2)(iv) 条。

_**Lack of money or property or lack of knowledge regarding liabilities.**_

Under certain circumstances, the amount the transferee must withhold equals the entire amount realized, rather than 10% of the amount realized, but the amount realized is determined without regard to any decrease in the transferor’s share of partnership liabilities. These circumstances are if:

  

_**缺乏金钱或财产或缺乏有关责任的知识。** _

在某些情况下，受让人必须预扣的金额等于变现金额的全部，而不是变现金额的 10%，但变现金额的确定不考虑转让人在合伙企业负债中所占份额的任何减少。这些情况是如果：

1.  The amount otherwise required to be withheld would exceed the amount realized determined without regard to the decrease in the transferor’s share of partnership liabilities; or  
    否则需要预扣的金额将超过在不考虑转让人在合伙企业负债中所占份额减少的情况下确定的实现金额；或者
    
2.  The transferee is unable to determine the amount realized because it does not have actual knowledge of the transferor’s share of partnership liabilities (and has not received or cannot rely on a certification of the transferor’s share of partnership liabilities received from the transferor (including the most recent Schedule K-1) or a certification of the transferor’s share of liabilities received from the partnership). See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(c)(3)(ii).  
    受让人无法确定实现的金额，因为它并不实际了解转让人在合伙企业负债中的份额（并且没有收到或不能依赖从转让人处收到的转让人在合伙企业负债中的份额的证明（包括最近的附表 K-1) 或转让人从合伙企业收到的负债份额的证明)。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-2(c)(3)(ii) 条。
    

_**Certification of maximum tax liability.**_

A transferor that meets certain requirements can certify its maximum tax liability to the transferee. The maximum tax liability is the amount of the transferor’s effectively connected gain multiplied by the applicable percentage under Regulations section 1.1446-3(a)(2). The applicable percentage for foreign corporations is the highest rate of tax under section 11(b) and for non-corporations is the highest rate of tax under section 1. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(c)(4) for further information. The certificate does not need to and should not be submitted to the IRS for approval.

  

_**最大纳税义务证明。** _

满足一定要求的转让方可以向受让方证明其最大纳税义务。最高纳税义务为转让方实际关联收益乘以《条例》第 1.1446-3(a)(2) 条规定的适用百分比。外国公司的适用百分比是第 11(b) 条规定的最高税率，非公司适用的百分比是第 1 条规定的最高税率。有关更多信息，请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-2(c)(4) 条信息。该证书不需要也不应该提交给国税局批准。

_**Effect of withholding on transferor.**_

A transferee’s withholding of tax under section 1446(f)(1) does not relieve a foreign person from filing a U.S. tax return with respect to the transfer. Further, it does not relieve a nonresident alien individual or foreign corporation subject to tax on gain by reason of section 864(c)(8) from paying with the return any tax due that has not been fully satisfied through withholding.

  

_**预扣税对转让人的影响。** _

受让人根据第 1446(f)(1) 条扣缴税款并不能免除外国人就转让提交美国纳税申报表的义务。此外，它并不能免除根据第 864(c)(8) 条规定应缴纳收益税的非居民外籍个人或外国公司在纳税申报表中缴纳尚未通过预扣税完全缴纳的应付税款。

**Transfers of partnership interests subject to withholding under sections 1445(e)(5) and 1446(f)(1).**

The transfer of a partnership interest may be subject to withholding under section 1445(e)(5) or Regulations section 1.1445-11T(d)(1) if 50% or more of the value of the partnership’s gross assets consist of USRPI, and 90% or more of the value of its gross assets consist of USRPI plus any cash or cash equivalents. The transfer of a partnership interest may also be subject to withholding under section 1446(f)(1) and Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2 if the partnership also holds other property used in the conduct of a trade or business within the United States. If both sections 1445(e)(5) and 1446(f)(1) could apply to the same transfer, generally the transfer is subject to the payment and reporting requirements of section 1445 only, and not section 1446(f)(1). However, if the transferor has applied for a withholding certificate under the last sentence of Regulations section 1.1445-11T(d)(1), the transferee must withhold the greater of the amounts required under section 1445(e)(5) or 1446(f)(1). A transferee that has complied with the withholding requirements under either section 1445(e)(5) or 1446(f)(1), as described under this paragraph, will be deemed to satisfy its withholding requirement.

  

**根据第 1445(e)(5) 和 1446(f)(1) 条规定，合伙企业权益的转让须缴纳预扣税。** 

如果合伙企业总资产价值的 50% 或以上由 USRPI 构成，则合伙企业权益的转让可能需要根据第 1445(e)(5) 条或条例第 1.1445-11T(d)(1) 条进行预扣税，并且其总资产价值的 90% 或以上由 USRPI 加上任何现金或现金等价物组成。如果合伙企业还持有用于在美国境内开展贸易或业务的其他财产，则合伙企业权益的转让也可能需要根据第 1446(f)(1) 条和条例第 1.1446(f)-2 条缴纳预扣税。如果第 1445(e)(5) 条和第 1446(f)(1) 条均适用于同一项转让，则该转让通常仅受第 1445 条的付款和报告要求的约束，而不受第 1446(f)(1 条)的约束）。然而，如果转让人已根据《条例》第 1.1445-11T(d)(1) 条的最后一句申请了预扣证明，受让人必须预扣第 1445(e)(5) 条或第 1446( f)(1)。如本段所述，已遵守第 1445(e)(5) 或 1446(f)(1) 条规定的预扣税要求的受让人将被视为满足其预扣税要求。

**Forms for paying and reporting section 1446(f)(1) withholding.**

To meet the withholding, payment, and reporting requirements under section 1446(f)(1) for transfers of interests in partnerships other than PTPs, taxpayers must use Forms 8288 and 8288-A and follow the instructions for those forms.

  

**支付和报告第 1446(f)(1) 条预扣税的表格。** 

为了满足第 1446(f)(1) 条中关于 PTP 以外的合伙企业权益转让的预扣、付款和报告要求，纳税人必须使用表格 8288 和 8288-A 并遵循这些表格的说明。

The time for filing Forms 8288 and 8288-A to report section 1446(f)(1) withholding is the same as for section 1445 withholding. The same rules for filing Forms 8288 and 8288-A by transferees withholding tax under section 1445 apply to transferees withholding tax under section 1446(f)(1). The same rules for claiming a credit for withholding of tax under section 1445 apply to transferors receiving Form 8288-A claiming credit for withholding under section 1446(f)(1). The rules relating to Forms 8288 and 8288-A discussed in this paragraph are described, later, under _U.S. Real Property Interest, [Reporting and Paying the Tax](#en_US_2024_publink1000225110 "Reporting and Paying the Tax")_ and in the [Instructions for Form 8288](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8288).  
提交表格 8288 和 8288-A 以报告第 1446(f)(1) 节预扣税的时间与第 1445 节预扣税的时间相同。根据第 1445 条规定由受让人预扣税提交 8288 和 8288-A 表格的相同规则也适用于根据第 1446(f)(1) 条规定的受让人预扣税。根据第 1445 条申请预扣税款抵免的相同规则适用于收到 8288-A 表格并根据第 1446(f)(1) 条申请预扣税款抵免的转让人。本段中讨论的与表格 8288 和 8288-A 相关的规则将在稍后的_美国不动产利息、[报告和纳税](#en_US_2024_publink1000225110 "Reporting and Paying the Tax")_以及[表格 8288 的说明](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-8288)中进行描述。

**Transferee reporting to partnership.**

No later than 10 days after the transfer, a transferee (other than a partnership that is a transferee because it made a distribution) must certify to the partnership the extent to which it has satisfied its withholding obligation. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(d)(2) for the documentation required for making this certification.

  

**受让人向合伙企业汇报。** 

转让后 10 天内，受让人（因进行分配而成为受让人的合伙企业除外）必须向合伙企业证明其已履行预扣义务的程度。有关进行此认证所需的文件，请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-2(d)(2) 节。

**Partnership’s requirement to withhold under section 1446(f)(4) on distributions to transferee.**

Section 1446(f)(4) requires a partnership to withhold on distributions to a transferee on any amount that the transferee failed to properly withhold under section 1446(f)(1), plus any interest on this amount. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3. These rules apply to transfers occurring on or after January 1, 2023. See Notice 2021-51, 2021-36 I.R.B. 361, available at [IRS.gov/irb/2021-36\_IRB#NOT-2021-51](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2021-36_IRB).

  

**合伙企业根据第 1446(f)(4) 条关于向受让人分配的预扣税的要求。** 

第 1446(f)(4) 条要求合伙企业扣留受让人未能根据第 1446(f)(1) 条适当扣留的任何金额，以及该金额的任何利息。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3 节。这些规则适用于 2023 年 1 月 1 日或之后发生的转移。请参阅通知 2021-51、2021-36 IRB 361，可在[IRS.gov/irb/2021-36\_IRB#NOT-2021-51](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2021-36_IRB)上获取。

**Requirement to withhold.**

If a transferee fails to withhold any amount required by Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2 in connection with the transfer of a partnership interest, the partnership must withhold from the distributions it makes to the transferee. Generally, a partnership may rely on the certification described in Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(d)(2) that it receives from the transferee to determine whether a transferee has withheld the amount required by Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2, unless it knows, or has reason to know, that the certification is incorrect or unreliable. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(a)(1).

  

**要求扣留。** 

如果受让人未能根据《条例》第 1.1446(f)-2 条的规定扣留与合伙企业权益转让相关的任何金额，则合伙企业必须从其向受让人分配的款项中扣留。一般来说，合伙企业可以依靠从受让人处收到的《条例》第 1.1446(f)-2(d)(2) 条中所述的证明来确定受让人是否已预扣《条例》第 1.1446(f)-2 条要求的金额，除非它知道或有理由知道该认证不正确或不可靠。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3(a)(1) 节。

If the partnership receives, within 10 days from the transfer, a certification from the transferee stating that an exception to withholding applies or establishing that the transferee has withheld the amount required to be withheld under Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2, then the partnership generally is not required to withhold under Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(a)(1). See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(b)(1). However, a partnership is required to withhold under section 1446(f)(4) if it receives notification from the IRS that the transferee has provided incorrect information on the certification. This may occur when the IRS determines that the transferee has provided incorrect information on the certification regarding the amount realized or the amount withheld, or that the transferee failed to pay the amounts reported as withheld to the IRS. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(a)(2).  
如果合伙企业在转让后 10 天内收到受让人出具的证明，表明适用预扣税例外情况或证明受让人已预扣了《条例》第 1.1446(f)-2 条规定的预扣金额，则合伙企业根据条例第 1.1446(f)-3(a)(1) 条，一般不需要扣缴。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3(b)(1) 条。然而，如果合伙企业收到 IRS 的通知，称受让人提供了不正确的证明信息，则根据第 1446(f)(4) 条，合伙企业必须扣缴税款。当 IRS 确定受让人提供了有关变现金额或预扣金额的证明信息不正确时，或者受让人未能支付向 IRS 报告的预扣金额时，可能会发生这种情况。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3(a)(2) 条。

A partnership that is a transferee because it makes a distribution subject to section 1446(f)(1) is not required to withhold under section 1446(f)(4). However, the partnership remains liable for its failure to withhold in its capacity as a transferee. A publicly traded partnership is not required to withhold on distributions made to a transferee under section 1446(f)(4). See Regulations sections 1.1446(f)-3(b)(2) and (3).  
因合伙企业根据第 1446(f)(1) 条进行分配而成为受让人的合伙企业无需根据第 1446(f)(4) 条扣缴税款。然而，合伙企业仍因其作为受让人的身份未能扣缴税款而承担责任。公开交易的合伙企业无需对根据第 1446(f)(4) 条向受让人进行的分配预扣税款。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3(b)(2) 和 (3) 节。

**Withholding rules.**
