A partnership that does not receive, or cannot rely on, a timely certification from a transferee stating that an exception to withholding applies or that the proper amount has been withheld must begin withholding on distributions made to the transferee on the later of the date that is 30 days after the transfer or the date that is 15 days after the partnership acquires actual knowledge of the transfer. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(c)(1)(i).

  

**扣留规则。** 

如果合伙企业没有收到或不能依赖受让人及时证明适用预扣税的例外情况或已预扣适当金额的合伙企业，则必须开始对向受让人分配的分配进行预扣税，以较晚者为准。转让后 30 天或合伙企业实际了解转让后 15 天之日。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3(c)(1)(i) 条。

The partnership must withhold on the entire amount of each distribution made to the transferee until it may rely on a certification from the transferee that states that an exception to withholding applies or that provides the information necessary to determine the amount required to be withheld. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(c)(1)(ii). The partnership may rely on this certification to determine its withholding obligation regardless of whether it is provided within the time prescribed in Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(d)(2). Once the partnership receives a certification from the transferee, the partnership must withhold 10% of the amount realized on the transfer, reduced by any amount already withheld by the transferee, plus any computed interest. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(c)(2)(i).  
合伙企业必须预扣向受让人的每次分配的全部金额，直到它可以依赖受让人提供的证明，证明适用预扣税的例外情况或提供确定需要预扣的金额所需的信息。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3(c)(1)(ii) 条。合伙企业可以依据此证明来确定其预扣税义务，无论该证明是否在条例第 1.1446(f)-2(d)(2) 条规定的时间内提供。一旦合伙企业收到受让人的证明，合伙企业必须预扣转让实现金额的 10%，减去受让人已预扣的任何金额，再加上任何计算的利息。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3(c)(2)(i) 条。

A partnership that is required to withhold under Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(a)(1) may not take into account any adjustment procedures that would otherwise affect the amount required to be withheld under Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(c)(2)(i). See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(c)(2)(i)(A). Thus, for example, a partnership may not reduce the amount that it is required to withhold under the procedures described in Regulations section 1.1446(f)-2(c)(4) (adjusting the amount subject to withholding based on a transferor’s maximum tax liability). For example, if a partnership is required to withhold $30 under section 1441 on a $100 distribution, the maximum amount required to be withheld on that distribution under section 1446(f)(4) is $70.  
根据条例第 1.1446(f)-3(a)(1) 条要求扣缴的合伙企业不得考虑任何可能影响条例第 1.1446(f)-2( c)(2)(i)。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3(c)(2)(i)(A)​​ 条。因此，举例来说，合伙企业不得减少根据条例第 1.1446(f)-2(c)(4) 条所述程序所需预扣的金额（根据转让人的最高税额调整预扣金额）责任）。例如，如果合伙企业根据第 1441 条要求对 100 美元的分配预扣 30 美元，则根据第 1446(f)(4) 条要求对该分配预扣的最高金额为 70 美元。

A partnership that does not receive or cannot rely on a certification from the transferee must withhold the full amount of each distribution made to the transferee until the partnership receives a certification that it can rely on. However, any amount required to be withheld on a distribution under any other withholding provision in the Code is not required to be withheld under section 1446(f)(4). See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(c)(3). Nevertheless, the partnership may stop withholding if the transferee disposes of all of its interest in the partnership, unless the partnership has actual knowledge that any successor to the transferee is related to the transferee or the transferor from which the transferee acquired the interest.  
未收到或不能依赖受让人证明的合伙企业必须扣留向受让人的每次分配的全部金额，直到合伙企业收到可以信赖的证明。然而，根据《守则》中任何其他预扣税条款要求在分配中预扣的任何金额，无需根据第 1446(f)(4) 条进行预扣。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3(c)(3) 节。然而，如果受让人处置其在合伙企业中的所有权益，合伙企业可以停止扣缴，除非合伙企业实际知道受让人的任何继承人与受让人或受让人从其获得权益的转让人有关系。

**Computation of interest.**

The amount of interest required to be withheld is the amount of interest that would be required to be paid under section 6601 and Regulations section 301.6601-1 if the amount that should have been withheld by the transferee was considered an underpayment of tax. Interest is payable between the date that is 20 days after the date of the transfer and the date on which the transferee’s withholding tax liability due under section 1446(f)(1) is satisfied. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(c)(2)(ii).

  

**利息计算。** 

如果受让方应预扣的金额被认为少缴税款，则需要预扣的利息金额是根据第 6601 条和条例第 301.6601-1 条要求支付的利息金额。利息应在转让之日起 20 天后至受让人根据第 1446(f)(1) 条履行预扣税义务之日之间支付。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3(c)(2)(ii) 条。

**Forms and filing dates.**

A partnership required to withhold under section 1446(f)(4) must report and pay the tax withheld using Forms 8288 and 8288-C. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(d). The time for filing Forms 8288 and 8288-C to report section 1446(f)(4) withholding is the same as for section 1445 withholding.

  

**表格和提交日期。** 

根据第 1446(f)(4) 条要求预扣税款的合伙企业必须使用表格 8288 和 8288-C 报告并缴纳预扣税款。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3(d) 条。提交表格 8288 和 8288-C 以报告第 1446(f)(4) 节预扣税的时间与第 1445 节预扣税的时间相同。

**Buyer/transferee claiming refund of section 1446(f)(4) withholding.**

A transferee may claim a refund for an excess amount if it has been overwithheld upon under section 1446(f)(4). An excess amount is the amount of tax and interest withheld that exceeds the transferee's withholding tax liability plus any interest owed by the transferee with respect to such liability. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-3(e). The transferee may also be liable for any applicable penalties or additions to tax. A transferee must complete Part V of Form 8288 and attach Form(s) 8288-C it received from the partnership when making a claim for refund of section 1446(f)(4) withholding. If a transferee that has not yet completed and filed Part III of Form 8288 with respect to a transfer and is now claiming a refund for amounts withheld under section 1446(f)(4), the transferee must complete Part III when filing Part V of Form 8288.

  

**买方/受让人要求退还第 1446(f)(4) 条的预扣税。** 

如果根据第 1446(f)(4) 条超额预扣，受让人可以要求退款。超额金额是指预扣税款和利息超过受让人的预扣税义务加上受让人就该义务所欠的任何利息的金额。请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-3(e) 条。受让人还可能需要承担任何适用的罚款或附加税款。受让人在申请退还第 1446(f)(4) 条预扣税款时，必须填写 8288 表格第五部分，并附上从合伙企业收到的 8288-C 表格。如果受让人尚未填写并提交有关转让的 8288 表格第 III 部分，并且现在要求退还根据第 1446(f)(4) 条扣缴的金额，则受让人必须在提交 8288 表格第 V 部分时填写第 III 部分8288 表格。

#### Section 1446(f): PTP Interests  
第 1446(f) 条：PTP 利益

For purposes of section 1446(f), a broker is generally required to withhold on an amount realized from the transfer of a PTP interest that it effects for the transferor of the interest. A broker is generally required to withhold at a 10% rate on an amount realized paid to the transferor. However, certain exceptions to withholding may apply under Regulations section 1.1446(f)-4(b), which include exceptions for a transferor providing a certification of non-foreign status, a certification from a transferor claiming an exemption from tax on any gain from the transfer under an income tax treaty, or a certification of the transferor’s status as a dealer in securities stating that any gain from the transfer is effectively connected with a trade or business in the U.S. without regard to section 864(c)(8). Additionally, for an amount realized paid to a transferor that is a foreign partnership, a broker may rely on a claim for a modified amount realized made by the partnership on a valid Form W-8IMY and determine its withholding taking into account a certification of non-foreign status or claim for treaty benefits provided for a partner in the partnership that meets the requirements of Regulations section 1.1446(f)-4(b)(2) or (5). See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-4(c)(2)(ii) for further information on a modified amount realized. For an amount realized paid to a transferor that is a grantor trust, a broker may similarly determine its withholding taking into account any withholding exception applicable to a grantor or owner in the trust.  
就第 1446(f) 条而言，经纪人通常需要对因 PTP 利息转让而为利息转让人带来的影响所实现的金额进行预扣。经纪人通常需要按 10% 的税率预扣支付给转让人的变现金额。然而，根据条例第 1.1446(f)-4(b) 条，某些预扣税例外情况可能适用，其中包括转让人提供非外国人身份证明、转让人要求对任何收益免税的证明的例外情况。根据所得税条约进行的转让，或转让人作为证券交易商的身份证明，表明转让所得的任何收益与美国的贸易或业务有效相关，而不考虑第 864(c)(8) 条。此外，对于支付给外国合伙企业转让人的变现金额，经纪人可以依据合伙企业在有效的 W-8IMY 表格上提出的修改变现金额的索赔，并在考虑非合伙企业证明的情况下确定其预扣税款。 - 为符合条例第 1.1446(f)-4(b)(2) 或 (5) 条要求的合伙企业中的合伙人提供的外国身份或税收协定优惠要求。有关已实现修改金额的更多信息，请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-4(c)(2)(ii) 节。对于支付给授予人信托的转让人的变现金额，经纪人可以类似地确定其预扣税，同时考虑适用于信托中的授予人或所有者的任何预扣税例外情况。

A broker is also required to withhold under section 1446(f) an amount realized from the transfer of a PTP interest that it pays to a broker that is an NQI, a QI (other than a QI assuming primary withholding responsibility for the amount realized), or U.S. branch or territory financial institution that is not treated as a U.S. person for the amount realized. In the case of an amount realized paid to an NQI (including a U.S. branch or territory financial institution not treated as a U.S. person), a broker is required to withhold at the 10% percent rate under section 1446(f). See the Instructions for Form W-8IMY for additional information on amount realized paid to NQIs. In the case of an amount realized paid to a QI not assuming primary withholding responsibility for the amount, a broker may withhold based on either withholding rate pool information provided by the QI or information on the transferors of the PTP interest when the QI acts as a disclosing QI.  
根据第 1446(f) 条，经纪人还必须预扣其向 NQI、QI 经纪人（对实现金额承担主要预扣责任的 QI 除外）转让 PTP 利息而实现的金额。 ，或在实现金额方面不被视为美国人的美国分行或地区金融机构。如果变现金额支付给 NQI（包括不被视为美国人的美国分支机构或领土金融机构），经纪人必须根据第 1446(f) 条按 10% 的税率预扣税款。有关支付给 NQI 的实际金额的更多信息，请参阅 W-8IMY 表格的说明。如果向 QI 支付的变现金额不承担该金额的主要预扣责任，经纪人可以根据 QI 提供的预扣税率池信息或当 QI 充当 PTP 利息转让方的信息进行预扣。披露QI。

Regardless of whether an amount realized is paid to a transferor of a PTP interest through a broker, a broker is not required to withhold under section 1446(f) when it may rely on a qualified notice from the PTP that states the applicability of the “10% exception” to withholding. See Regulations section 1.1446(f)-4(b)(3) for further information on this exception, which applies to a PTP with less than 10% effectively connected gain (or that is otherwise not engaged in a trade or business in the United States).  
无论实现的金额是否通过经纪人支付给 PTP 利息转让人，当经纪人可以依赖 PTP 发出的合格通知，说明“预扣税有“10% 的例外”。有关此例外的更多信息，请参阅法规第 1.1446(f)-4(b)(3) 条，该例外适用于实际关联收益低于 10% 的 PTP（或未在美国从事贸易或业务的 PTP）。州）。

An amount realized from the sale of a PTP interest is the amount of gross proceeds paid or credited from the sale. In the case of a PTP distribution, an amount realized on the distribution is limited to an amount described in Regulations section 1.1446(f)-4(c)(2)(iii).  
出售 PTP 利息实现的金额是指出售时支付或记入的总收益金额。在 PTP 分配的情况下，分配实现的金额仅限于条例第 1.1446(f)-4(c)(2)(iii) 条中描述的金额。

For when an amount realized is reportable on Form 1042-S and other requirements for reporting amounts realized on Form 1042-S, see Regulation section 1.1461-1(c)(2)(i) and the Instructions for Form 1042-S. Also see the instructions for Form 1042-S for the reporting of an amount realized paid to an NQI, or to a QI (including when the QI acts as a disclosing QI for the amount realized). See Revenue Procedure 2022-43 for the withholding and reporting requirements of QIs with respect to amounts realized paid to their account holders (including QIs acting as disclosing QIs), effective starting January 1, 2023.  
对于何时应在表格 1042-S 上报告变现金额以及在表格 1042-S 上报告变现金额的其他要求，请参阅法规第 1.1461-1(c)(2)(i) 节和表格 1042-S 的说明。另请参阅表格 1042-S 的说明，了解支付给 NQI 或 QI 的已实现金额（包括 QI 作为已实现金额的披露 QI 的情况）。请参阅收入程序 2022-43，了解 QI 向其账户持有人支付的变现金额（包括充当披露 QI 的 QI）的预扣和报告要求，自 2023 年 1 月 1 日起生效。

#### U.S. Real Property Interest  
美国房地产权益

The disposition of a USRPI by a foreign person (the transferor) is subject to income tax withholding under section 1445. If you are the transferee, you must find out if the transferor is a foreign person. If the transferor is a foreign person and you fail to withhold, you may be held liable for the tax.  
外国人（转让人）处置 USRPI 需根据第 1445 条缴纳所得税。如果您是受让人，则必须查明转让人是否为外国人。如果转让人是外国人而您未能预扣税款，您可能需要缴纳税款。

**Foreign person.**

A foreign person is a nonresident alien individual, or a foreign corporation that has not made an election under section 897(i) to be treated as a domestic corporation, foreign partnership, foreign trust, or foreign estate. It does not include a resident alien individual or, in certain cases, a qualified foreign pension fund. See _[Retirement and pension funds](#en_US_2024_publink100047770 "Retirement and pension funds.")_, later.

  

**外国人。** 

外国人是指非居民外国人，或未根据第 897(i) 条选择被视为国内公司、外国合伙企业、外国信托或外国财产的外国公司。它不包括外国居民个人，或在某些情况下，不包括合格的外国养老基金。请参阅稍后的_[退休金和养老基金](#en_US_2024_publink100047770 "Retirement and pension funds.")_。

**Transferor.**

A transferor is any foreign person that disposes of a USRPI by sale, exchange, gift, or any other transfer. A transfer includes distributions to shareholders of a corporation and beneficiaries of a trust or estate.

  

**转让者。** 

转让人是指通过出售、交换、赠与或任何其他转让方式处置 USRPI 的任何外国人。转让包括向公司股东和信托或遗产受益人的分配。

The owner of a disregarded entity, not the entity, is treated as the transferor of the property transferred by the disregarded entity.  
被忽视实体的所有者（而非该实体）被视为该被忽视实体转让的财产的转让人。

**Transferee.**

A transferee is any person, foreign or domestic, that acquires a USRPI by purchase, exchange, gift, or any other transfer.

  

**受让人。** 

受让人是指通过购买、交换、赠与或任何其他转让方式获得 USRPI 的任何人，无论是外国人还是国内人。

**USRPI defined.**

A USRPI is an interest, other than as a creditor, in real property (including an interest in a mine, well, or other natural deposit) located in the United States or the USVI, as well as certain personal property that is associated with the use of real property (such as farming machinery). It also means any interest, other than as a creditor, in any domestic corporation unless it is established that the corporation was at no time a U.S. real property holding corporation during the shorter of the period during which the interest was held, or the 5-year period ending on the date of disposition (applicable periods).

  

**USRPI 定义。** 

USRPI 是指除作为债权人以外，位于美国或美属维尔京群岛的不动产（包括矿山、油井或其他天然矿藏的权益）以及与该不动产相关的某些个人财产的权益。使用不动产（例如农业机械）。它还指除作为债权人之外，在任何国内公司中的任何权益，除非可以确定该公司在持有权益期间（以较短者为准）期间从未是美国房地产控股公司，或 5-截至处置日期的年度（适用期间）。

An interest in a corporation is not a USRPI if:  
在以下情况下，公司权益不属于 USRPI：

1.  Such corporation did not hold any USRPI on the date of disposition,  
    该公司在处置之日没有持有任何 USRPI，
    
2.  All the USRPI held by such corporation at any time during the shorter of the applicable periods were disposed of in transactions in which the full amount of any gain was recognized, and  
    该公司在适用期间较短的任何时间持有的所有 USRPI 均在交易中处置，其中任何收益均已全额确认，并且
    
3.  Such corporation and any predecessor of such corporation was not a RIC or a REIT during the shorter of the applicable periods during which the interest was held.  
    在持有权益的适用期间中较短的期间内，该公司及其任何前身都不是 RIC 或 REIT。
    

_**Exception for publicly traded stock.**_

If, at any time during the calendar year, any class of stock of a domestic corporation is regularly traded on an established securities market, an interest in such corporation will not be treated as a USRPI if the beneficial owner did not own more than 5% of the total fair market value of that class of interests, or 10% of the total fair market value of that class of interests in the case of a REIT, at any time during the shorter of the applicable periods. Certain constructive ownership rules apply for purposes of determining whether any person meets the above ownership threshold of any class of stock. See section 897(c)(6)(C) for more information on the constructive ownership rules.

  

_**公开交易股票的例外。** _

如果在一年中的任何时间，国内公司的任何类别的股票在成熟的证券市场上定期交易，且受益所有人所持股份不超过 5%，则该公司的权益将不会被视为 USRPI该类别权益的总公平市场价值的 10%，或如果是 REIT，则为该类别权益总公平市场价值的 10%，在适用期间较短的任何时间。某些推定所有权规则适用于确定任何人是否符合上述任何类别股票的所有权门槛。有关推定所有权规则的更多信息，请参阅第 897(c)(6)(C) 条。

**Amount to withhold.**

The transferee must deduct and withhold a tax on the total amount realized by the foreign person on the disposition. The rate of withholding is generally 15%.

  

**扣留金额。** 

受让人必须根据外国人在处置中实现的总金额扣除并预扣税款。预扣税率一般为15%。

The amount realized is the sum of:  
实现的金额是以下各项的总和：

*   The cash paid, or to be paid (principal only);  
    已支付或待支付的现金（仅限本金）；
    
*   The fair market value of other property transferred, or to be transferred; and  
    已转让或待转让的其他财产的公平市场价值；和
    
*   The amount of any liability assumed by the transferee or to which the property is subject immediately before and after the transfer.  
    受让人承担的任何责任的金额或财产在转让之前和之后所承担的任何责任的金额。
    

If the property transferred was owned jointly by U.S. and foreign persons, the amount realized is allocated between the transferors based on the capital contribution of each transferor.  
如果转让的财产由美国人和外国人共同拥有，则变现金额根据每个转让人的出资额在转让人之间分配。

**Residences.**

This rule applies when the property disposed of is acquired by the transferee for use by the transferee as a residence. If the amount realized on such disposition does not exceed $300,000, no withholding is required. Otherwise, the transferee must generally withhold 10% of the amount realized by a foreign person. The rate of withholding is 15% when the amount realized is in excess of $1,000,000.

  

**住宅。** 

当所处置的财产由受让人购买以供受让人用作住宅时，适用本规则。如果此类处置实现的金额不超过 300,000 美元，则无需预扣税款。否则，受让人通常必须预扣外国人变现金额的 10%。当变现金额超过 1,000,000 美元时，预扣税率为 15%。

_**Foreign corporations.**_

A foreign corporation that distributes a USRPI must withhold a tax equal to 21% of the gain it recognizes on the distribution to its shareholders.

  

_**外国公司。** _

分配 USRPI 的外国公司必须预扣相当于其向股东分配收益的 21% 的税款。

_**Domestic corporations.**_

A domestic corporation must withhold tax on the fair market value of the property distributed to a foreign shareholder if:

  

_**国内企业。** _

在以下情况下，国内公司必须对分配给外国股东的财产的公平市场价值预扣税款：

*   The shareholder's interest in the corporation is a USRPI, and  
    股东在公司中的权益是 USRPI，并且
    
*   The property distributed is either in redemption of stock or in liquidation of the corporation.  
    分配的财产要么用于赎回股票，要么用于公司的清算。
    

The corporation must generally withhold 15% of the amount realized by a foreign person.  
公司通常必须预扣外国人变现金额的 15%。

_**U.S. real property holding corporations.**_

A distribution from a domestic corporation that is a U.S. real property holding corporation (USRPHC) is generally subject to chapter 3 withholding and withholding under the USRPI provisions. This also applies to a corporation that was a USRPHC at any time during the shorter of the period during which the USRPI was held, or the 5-year period ending on the date of disposition. A USRPHC can satisfy both withholding provisions if it withholds under one of the following procedures.

  

_**美国房地产控股公司。** _

来自美国房地产控股公司 (USRPHC) 的国内公司的分配通常须遵守第 3 章预扣税和 USRPI 规定的预扣税。这也适用于在 USRPI 持有期间或截至处置之日结束的 5 年期间中的较短期间内的任何时间作为 USRPHC 的公司。如果 USRPHC 根据以下程序之一进行扣缴，则可以满足这两项扣缴规定。

*   Apply chapter 3 withholding on the full amount of the distribution, whether or not any part of the distribution represents a return of basis or capital gain. If a reduced tax rate applies under an income tax treaty, see Regulations section 1.1441-3T(c)(4)(i)(A) for the minimum withholding rate that may be applicable.  
    对全部分配金额适用第 3 章预扣税，无论分配的任何部分是否代表基础回报或资本收益。如果根据所得税协定适用降低税率，请参阅法规第 1.1441-3T(c)(4)(i)(A)​​ 条了解可能适用的最低预扣税率。
    
*   Apply chapter 3 withholding to the part of the distribution that the USRPHC estimates is a dividend. Then, withhold 15% on the remainder of the distribution (or on a smaller amount if a withholding certificate is obtained and the amount of the distribution that is a return of capital is established).  
    将第 3 章预扣税适用于 USRPHC 估计为股息的分配部分。然后，对分配的剩余部分预扣 15%（如果获得了预扣证明并且确定了作为资本回报的分配金额，则预扣较小的金额）。
    

The same procedure must be used for all distributions made during the year. A different procedure may be used each year.  
一年内进行的所有分配都必须采用相同的程序。每年可能会使用不同的程序。

_**Partnerships.**_

If a domestic or foreign partnership with any foreign partners disposes of a USRPI at a gain, the gain is treated as ECI and is generally subject to the rules explained earlier under _[_Partnership Withholding on ECTI_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225066 "Partnership Withholding on ECTI")_. A foreign partnership that disposes of a USRPI may credit the taxes withheld by the transferee against the tax liability determined under the partnership withholding on ECTI rules.

  

_**伙伴关系。** _

如果与任何外国合作伙伴的国内或外国合伙企业通过处置 USRPI 获得收益，则该收益将被视为 ECI，并且通常须遵守前面在_[_ECTI 上的合伙企业预扣税_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225066 "Partnership Withholding on ECTI")_中解释的规则。处置 USRPI 的外国合伙企业可以将受让人预扣的税款抵扣根据 ECTI 规则的合伙企业预扣税确定的纳税义务。

If a foreign person disposes of an interest in a partnership in which 50% or more of the value of the gross assets consist of USRPI and 90% or more of the value of the gross assets consist of USRPI plus any cash or cash equivalents, the transferee of the partnership interest must deduct and withhold 15% of the amount realized on the disposition.  
如果外国人处置合伙企业的权益，其中总资产价值的 50% 或以上由 USRPI 组成，且总资产价值的 90% 或以上由 USRPI 加上任何现金或现金等价物组成，则合伙权益的受让人必须扣除并预扣处置所实现金额的 15%。

_**Trusts and estates.**_

You are a withholding agent if you are a trustee, fiduciary, or executor of a trust or estate having one or more foreign beneficiaries. You must establish a USRPI account. You enter in the account all gains and losses realized during the tax year of the trust or estate from dispositions of USRPI. You must withhold 21% on any distribution to a foreign beneficiary that is attributable to the balance in the real property interest account on the day of the distribution. A distribution from a trust or estate to a beneficiary (foreign or domestic) will be treated as attributable first to any balance in the USRPI account and then to other amounts.

  

_**信托和遗产。** _

如果您是拥有一名或多名外国受益人的信托或遗产的受托人、受托人或执行人，您就是扣缴义务人。您必须建立一个 USRPI 帐户。您在账户中输入信托或遗产纳税年度中因 USRPI 处置而实现的所有收益和损失。对于分配给外国受益人的分配当天房地产利息账户余额的任何分配，您必须预扣 21%。从信托或遗产到受益人（国外或国内）的分配将被视为首先归属于 USRPI 账户中的任何余额，然后归属于其他金额。

A trust with more than 100 beneficiaries may elect to withhold from each distribution 21% of the amount attributable to the foreign beneficiary's proportionate share of the current balance of the trust's real property interest account. This election does not apply to publicly traded trusts or REITs. For more information about this election, see Regulations section 1.1445-5(c).  
受益人超过 100 名的信托可以选择从每次分配中扣除外国受益人在信托房地产利息账户当前余额中所占比例份额金额的 21%。此选择不适用于公开交易的信托或房地产投资信托基金。有关本次选举的更多信息，请参阅《条例》第 1.1445-5(c) 节。

**Publicly traded partnership and trust interests.**

If any class of interest in a partnership or a trust is regularly traded on an established securities market, any interest in such a partnership or trust will be treated as an interest in a publicly traded corporation and will be subject to the rules applicable to those interests.

  

**公开交易的合伙企业和信托权益。** 

如果合伙企业或信托中的任何类别的权益定期在成熟的证券市场上交易，则此类合伙企业或信托中的任何权益将被视为上市公司的权益，并将受到适用于这些权益的规则的约束。

**Qualified investment entities (QIEs).**

Special rules apply to QIEs. A QIE is:

  

**合格投资实体（QIE）。** 

特殊规则适用于 QIE。 QIE 是：

1.  A REIT, or房地产投资信托基金，或
    
2.  A RIC that is a U.S. real property holding corporation.  
    RIC 是一家美国房地产控股公司。
    

_**Look-through rule for QIEs.**_

In most cases, any distribution from a QIE to a nonresident alien, foreign corporation, or other QIE that is attributable to the QIE's gain from the sale or exchange of a USRPI is treated as gain recognized by the nonresident alien, foreign corporation, or other QIE from the sale or exchange of a USRPI.

  

_**QIE 的查找规则。** _

在大多数情况下，QIE 向非居民外国人、外国公司或其他 QIE 进行的任何分配（归因于 QIE 从 USRPI 销售或交换中获得的收益）均被视为非居民外国人、外国公司或其他 QIE 认可的收益。 QIE 来自 USRPI 的销售或交换。

A distribution by a QIE to a nonresident alien or foreign corporation that is treated as gain from the sale or exchange of a USRPI by the shareholder is subject to withholding at 21%.  
QIE 向非居民外国人或外国公司的分配，如果被视为股东出售或交换 USRPI 的收益，则需缴纳 21% 的预扣税。

Certain exceptions apply to the look-through rule for distributions by QIEs. Any distribution by a QIE with respect to stock regularly traded on an established securities market in the United States is not treated as gain from the sale or exchange of a USRPI if the shareholder did not own more than 5% of that stock (or more than 10% of that stock in the case of REITs) at any time during the 1-year period ending on the date of the distribution. A distribution by a REIT generally is not treated as gain from the sale or exchange of a USRPI if the shareholder is a qualified shareholder (as described in section 897(k)(3)). These distributions may be included in the shareholder's gross income as a dividend from the QIE, not as long-term capital gain.  
某些例外情况适用于 QIE 分配的查找规则。如果股东持有该股票不超过 5%（或不超过就 REIT 而言，为该股票的 10%），在截至分配之日的一年期间内的任何时间。如果股东是合格股东（如第 897(k)(3) 条所述），则 REIT 的分配通常不被视为出售或交换 USRPI 的收益。这些分配可能作为 QIE 的股息而非长期资本收益计入股东的总收入。

_**Disposition of REIT stock.**_

Disposition of stock in a REIT that is held directly (or indirectly through one or more partnerships) by a qualified shareholder may not be subject to withholding. See section 897(k)(2) for more information.

  

_**房地产投资信托基金股票的处置。** _

合格股东直接（或通过一个或多个合伙企业间接）持有的房地产投资信托基金股票的处置可能无需缴纳预扣税。请参阅第 897(k)(2) 节了解更多信息。

_**Domestically controlled QIE.**_

The sale of an interest in a domestically controlled QIE is not the sale of a USRPI. The entity is domestically controlled if at all times during the testing period less than 50% in value of its stock was held, directly or indirectly, by foreign persons. The testing period is the shorter of (a) the 5-year period ending on the date of disposition, or (b) the period during which the entity was in existence.

  

_**国内控股的QIE。** _

出售国内控制的 QIE 权益并非出售 USRPI。如果在测试期间任何时候外国人直接或间接持有其股票价值低于 50%，则该实体属于国内控制。测试期是 (a) 截至处置之日的 5 年期间，或 (b) 实体存在期间中较短的一个。

For the purpose of determining whether a QIE is domestically controlled, the following rules apply.  
判断QIE是否受境内控制时，适用以下规则。

1.  A person holding less than 5% of any class of stock of a QIE which is regularly traded on an established securities market in the United States at all times during the testing period will be treated as a U.S. person unless the QIE has actual knowledge that such person is not a U.S. person.  
    在测试期间，持有 QIE 任何类别股票的 5% 以下且在美国成熟证券市场上始终定期交易的人士将被视为美国人，除非 QIE 实际知道该股票的持有量低于 5%。该人不是美国人。
    
2.  Any stock in a QIE that is held by another QIE will be treated as held by a foreign person if:  
    在以下情况下，一个 QIE 中由另一个 QIE 持有的任何股票将被视为由外国人持有：
    
    1.  Any class of stock of such other QIE is regularly traded on an established securities market, or  
        此类其他 QIE 的任何类别的股票在成熟的证券市场上定期交易，或
        
    2.  Such other QIE is a RIC that issues certain redeemable securities.  
        此类其他 QIE 是发行某些可赎回证券的 RIC。
        
    
    Notwithstanding the above, the stock of the QIE will be treated as held by a U.S. person if such other QIE is domestically controlled.  
    尽管有上述规定，如果其他 QIE 是国内控制的，则该 QIE 的股票将被视为由美国人持有。
    
3.  Stock in a QIE that is held by any other QIE not described above will be treated as held by a U.S. person in proportion to the stock ownership of such other QIE which is (or is treated as) held by a U.S. person.  
    上述未提及的任何其他 QIE 持有的 QIE 股票将被视为由美国人持有，比例与美国人持有（或被视为）的该其他 QIE 的股权比例相同。
    

If a foreign shareholder in a domestically controlled QIE disposes of an interest in the QIE in an applicable wash sale transaction, special rules apply. See section 897 for more information.  
如果境内控制的 QIE 的外国股东在适用的洗售交易中处置 QIE 的权益，则适用特殊规则。有关详细信息，请参阅第 897 节。

**Retirement and pension funds.**

A qualified foreign pension fund or any entity wholly owned by such qualified foreign pension fund will not be treated as a foreign person for dispositions of USRPI or distributions received from a REIT or certain RICs described in section 897(h)(4)(A)(ii). Qualified foreign pension funds are described in section 897(l)(2).

  

**退休和养老基金。** 

合格外国养老基金或该合格外国养老基金全资拥有的任何实体在处置 USRPI 或从 REIT 或第 897(h)(4)(A) 条所述的某些 RIC 收到的分配时，不会被视为外国人(二).第 897(l)(2) 节描述了合格的外国养老基金。

**Additional information.**

For additional information on the withholding rules that apply to corporations, trusts, estates, and qualified investment entities, see section 1445 and the related regulations. For additional information on the withholding rules that apply to partnerships, see the previous discussion.

  

**附加信息。** 

有关适用于公司、信托、遗产和合格投资实体的预扣税规则的更多信息，请参阅第 1445 节和相关法规。有关适用于合伙企业的预扣税规则的更多信息，请参阅之前的讨论。

**Exceptions.**

You do not have to withhold if any of the following apply.

  

**例外情况。** 

如果存在以下任何情况，您无需扣留。

1.  You (the transferee) acquire the property for use as a residence and the amount realized (sales price) is not more than $300,000. You or a member of your family must have definite plans to reside at the property for at least 50% of the number of days the property is used by any person during each of the first two 12-month periods following the date of transfer. When counting the number of days the property is used, do not count the days the property will be vacant. For this exception, the transferee must be an individual.  
    您（受让人）购买该房产用作住宅，且变现金额（销售价格）不超过 300,000 美元。您或您的家庭成员必须有明确的计划，在转让日期后的前两个 12 个月期间内，每个人在该房产中居住的​​时间至少占任何人使用该房产天数的 50%。在计算房产的使用天数时，不要计算房产的空置天数。对于这种例外，受让人必须是个人。
    
2.  The property disposed of is an interest in a domestic corporation and any class of stock of the corporation is regularly traded on an established securities market. However, this exception does not apply to certain dispositions of substantial amounts of non-publicly traded interests in publicly traded corporations.  
    所处置的财产是国内公司的权益，并且该公司的任何类别的股票都在成熟的证券市场上定期交易。然而，此例外不适用于上市公司中大量非公开交易权益的某些处置。
    
3.  The disposition is of an interest in a domestic corporation and that corporation furnishes you a certification stating, under penalties of perjury, that the interest is not a USRPI. In most cases, the corporation can make this certification only if either of the following is true.  
    该处置涉及一家国内公司的权益，该公司向您提供一份证明，证明该权益不是 USRPI，否则将受到伪证处罚。在大多数情况下，只有满足以下任一条件，公司才能进行此认证。
    
    *   During the previous 5 years (or, if shorter, the period the interest was held by its present owner), the corporation was not a USRPHC.  
        在过去 5 年（或者，如果更短，则为现任所有者持有权益的期间），该公司不是 USRPHC。
        
    *   As of the date of disposition, the interest in the corporation is not a USRPI by reason of section 897(c)(1)(B). The certification must be dated not more than 30 days before the date of transfer.  
        截至处置之日，根据第 897(c)(1)(B) 条，公司权益不属于 USRPI。证明的日期不得早于转让日期前 30 天。
        
    
4.  The transferor gives you a certification stating, under penalties of perjury, that the transferor is not a foreign person and containing the transferor's name, U.S. TIN, and home address (or office address, in the case of an entity). A certificate of non-foreign status includes a Form W-9 and for qualified foreign pension funds, or entities wholly owned by qualified foreign pension funds, Form W-8 EXP.  
    转让人向您提供一份证明，证明转让人不是外国人，并包含转让人的姓名、美国 TIN 和家庭住址（如果是实体，则为办公地址），否则将受伪证罪处罚。非外国人身份证明包括表格 W-9，对于合格的外国养老基金或由合格的外国养老基金全资拥有的实体，包括表格 W-8 EXP。
    
    The transferor can give the certification to a qualified substitute. The qualified substitute gives you a statement, under penalties of perjury, that the certification is in the possession of the qualified substitute. For this purpose, a qualified substitute is (a) the person (including any attorney or title company) responsible for closing the transaction, other than the transferor's agent, and (b) the transferee's agent.  
    转让人可以将证明授予合格的替代者。合格的替代者向您提供一份声明，证明该证书由合格的替代者持有，否则将受伪证罪处罚。为此目的，合格替代人是 (a) 负责完成交易的人员（包括任何律师或产权公司），转让人的代理人除外，以及 (b) 受让人的代理人。
    
5.  You receive a withholding certificate from the IRS that excuses withholding. See [_Withholding Certificates_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225116 "Withholding Certificates"), later.  
    您会收到美国国税局 (IRS) 签发的预扣税证明，证明您可以免除预扣税。请参阅稍后的[_预扣证书_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225116 "Withholding Certificates")。
    
6.  The transferor gives you written notice that no recognition of any gain or loss on the transfer is required because of a nonrecognition provision in the Internal Revenue Code or a provision in a U.S. tax treaty. You must file a copy of the notice by the 20th day after the date of transfer with:  
    转让方向您发出书面通知，表明由于《国内税收法》中的不确认条款或美国税务条约中的条款，无需确认转让中的任何收益或损失。您必须在转让日期后 20 天之前将通知副本提交给：
    
    Ogden Service Center奥格登服务中心  
    P.O. Box 409101邮政信箱 409101  
    Ogden, UT 84409奥格登, UT 84409
    
7.  The amount the transferor realizes on the transfer of a USRPI is zero.  
    转让人在转让 USRPI 时实现的金额为零。
    
8.  The property is acquired by the United States, a U.S. state or territory, a political subdivision, or the District of Columbia.  
    该财产由美国、美国的州或领地、政治分区或哥伦比亚特区收购。
    
9.  The grantor realizes an amount on the grant or lapse of an option to acquire a USRPI. However, you must withhold on the sale, exchange, or exercise of that option.  
    授予人通过授予或失效获取 USRPI 的选择权来实现一定金额。但是，您必须扣留该期权的出售、交换或行使。
    
10.  The disposition is of an interest in a publicly traded partnership or trust. However, this exception does not apply to certain dispositions of substantial amounts of non-publicly traded interests in publicly traded partnerships or trusts.  
    该处置涉及公开交易的合伙企业或信托的权益。然而，此例外不适用于公开交易的合伙企业或信托中大量非公开交易权益的某些处置。
    

_**Late filing of certifications or notices.**_

If you become aware that you have failed to timely file certain certifications or notices, you still may be able to file them. See Revenue Procedure 2008-27, 2008-21 I.R.B. 1014 available at [IRS.gov/irb/2008-21\_IRB#RP-2008-27](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2008-21_IRB#RP-2008-27).

  

_**逾期提交证明或通知。** _

如果您发现自己未能及时提交某些证明或通知，您仍然可以提交它们。请参阅税收程序 2008-27、2008-21 IRB 1014，网址为[IRS.gov/irb/2008-21\_IRB#RP-2008-27](https://www.irs.gov/irb/2008-21_IRB#RP-2008-27) 。

Complete the required certification or notice and file it with the appropriate person or the IRS. Also include the following.  
完成所需的证明或通知，并将其提交给适当的人员或国税局。还包括以下内容。

*   A statement at the top of the document(s) that it is “FILED PURSUANT TO Revenue Procedure 2008-27.”  
    文件顶部的声明，表明该文件“根据 2008-27 年收入程序归档”。
    
*   An explanation describing why the failure was due to reasonable cause. Within the explanation, provide that you filed with, or obtained from, an appropriate person the required certification or notice.  
    描述失败原因的解释。在说明中，请提供您向适当人员提交或从适当人员处获取所需的证明或通知。
    

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/envelope.gif)
_The completed certification or notice attached to the explanation must be sent to:  
附有解释的完整证明或通知必须发送至：_.

Ogden Service Center奥格登服务中心  
P.O. Box 409101邮政信箱 409101  
Ogden, UT 84409.奥格登，UT 84409。

.

_**Certifications.**_

The certifications in items (3) and (4) are not effective if you (or the qualified substitute) have actual knowledge, or receive a notice from an agent (or substitute), that they are false. This also applies to the qualified substitute's statement under item (4).

  

_**认证。** _

如果您（或合格的替代者）实际知道或收到代理人（或替代者）的通知，证明第（3）和（4）项中的证明是虚假的，则这些证明无效。这也适用于第（4）项中合格替补人员的声明。

If you (or the substitute) are required by regulations to furnish a copy of the certification (or statement) to the IRS and you (or the substitute) fail to do so in the time and manner prescribed, the certification (or statement) is not effective.  
如果法规要求您（或替代人）向 IRS 提供证明（或声明）副本，而您（或替代人）未能按照规定的时间和方式提供，则该证明（或声明）将被视为无效。没有效果。

_**Liability of agent or qualified substitute.**_

If you (or the substitute) receive a certification discussed in item (3) or (4) or a statement in item (4), and the agent, or substitute, has actual knowledge that the certification (or statement) is false, or in the case of (3), that the corporation is a foreign corporation, the agent (or substitute) must notify you, or the agent (or substitute) will be held liable for the tax. The agent's (or substitute's) liability is limited to the compensation the agent (or substitute) gets from the transaction.

  

_**代理人或合格替代者的责任。** _

如果您（或替代者）收到第 (3) 或 (4) 项中讨论的证明或第 (4) 项中的声明，并且代理人或替代者实际知道该证明（或声明）是虚假的，或者在第(3)种情况下，该公司是外国公司，代理人（或替代人）必须通知您，否则代理人（或替代人）将承担纳税责任。代理人（或替代人）的责任仅限于代理人（或替代人）从交易中获得的补偿。

An agent is any person who represents the transferor or transferee in any negotiation with another person (or another person's agent) relating to the transaction, or in settling the transaction. A person is not treated as an agent if the person only performs one or more of the following acts related to the transaction.  
代理人是代表转让人或受让人与他人（或他人的代理人）就交易进行任何谈判或解决交易的任何人。如果一个人仅执行以下一项或多项与交易相关的行为，则该人不被视为代理人。

*   Receipt and disbursement of any part of the consideration.  
    任何部分对价的收取和支付。
    
*   Recording of any document.  
    任何文件的记录。
    
*   Typing, copying, and other clerical tasks.  
    打字、复印和其他文书工作。
    
*   Obtaining title insurance reports and reports concerning the condition of the property.  
    获取产权保险报告和有关财产状况的报告。
    
*   Transmitting documents between the parties.  
    在双方之间传输文件。
    

#### Reporting and Paying the Tax  
申报和纳税

Transferees must use Forms 8288 and 8288-A to report and pay over any tax withheld on the acquisition of USRPI. These forms must also be used by corporations, estates, and QIEs that must withhold tax on distributions and other transactions involving USRPI. You must include the U.S. TIN of both the transferor and the transferee on the forms.  
受让人必须使用 8288 和 8288-A 表格来报告并支付因收购 USRPI 而预扣的任何税款。这些表格还必须由必须对涉及 USRPI 的分配和其他交易预扣税的公司、遗产和 QIE 使用。您必须在表格中包含转让人和受让人的美国 TIN。

For partnerships disposing of USRPI, the manner of reporting and paying over the tax withheld is the same as discussed earlier under [_Partnership Withholding on ECTI_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225066 "Partnership Withholding on ECTI").  
对于处置 USRPI 的合伙企业，报告和缴纳预扣税款的方式与之前在[_ECTI 的合伙企业预扣税项_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225066 "Partnership Withholding on ECTI")下讨论的方式相同。

Publicly traded trusts must use Forms 1042 and 1042-S to report and pay over tax withheld on distributions from dispositions of USRPI.  
公开交易的信托必须使用 1042 和 1042-S 表格来报告和支付 USRPI 处置分配的预扣税款。

QIEs must use Forms 1042 and 1042-S for a distribution to a nonresident alien or foreign corporation that is treated as a dividend, as discussed earlier under [_Qualified investment entities (QIEs)_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225101 "Qualified investment entities (QIEs).").  
QIE 必须使用 1042 和 1042-S 表格向非居民外国人或外国公司进行分配，该分配被视为股息，如前面[_合格投资实体 (QIE)_](#en_US_2024_publink1000225101 "Qualified investment entities (QIEs).")中所述。

**Form 8288.**

The tax withheld on the acquisition of a USRPI from a foreign person is reported and paid over using Form 8288. Form 8288 also serves as the transmittal form for copies A and B of Form 8288-A.

  

**8288 表格。** 

从外国人处获得 USRPI 时所扣缴的税款使用 8288 表格进行报告和缴纳。8288 表格还可作为 8288-A 表格副本 A 和 B 的传输表格。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/duedate.gif)
_In most cases, you must file Form 8288 by the 20th day after the date of the transfer.  
在大多数情况下，您必须在转让日期后的 20 天之前提交 8288 表格。_.

If an application for a _[withholding certificate](#en_US_2024_publink1000225116 "Withholding Certificates")_ (discussed later) is submitted to the IRS before or on the date of a transfer and the application is still pending with the IRS on the date of transfer, the correct withholding tax must be withheld, but does not have to be reported and paid over immediately. The amount withheld (or lesser amount, as determined by the IRS) must be reported and paid over within 20 days following the day on which a copy of the withholding certificate or notice of denial is mailed by the IRS.  
如果在转让之前或转让之日向 IRS 提交了_[预扣税证明](#en_US_2024_publink1000225116 "Withholding Certificates")_申请（稍后讨论），并且该申请在转让之日仍待 IRS 处理，则必须预扣正确的预扣税，但不必须立即报告并付款。预扣金额（或由 IRS 确定的较小金额）必须在 IRS 邮寄预扣证明副本或拒绝通知之日起 20 天内报告并支付。

If the principal purpose of applying for a withholding certificate is to delay paying over the withheld tax, the transferee will be subject to interest and penalties. The interest and penalties will be assessed for the period beginning on the 21st day after the date of transfer and ending on the day the payment is made.  
如果申请预扣税凭证的主要目的是延迟缴纳预扣税款，受让人将需要缴纳利息和罚款。利息和罚款将从转账日期后的第 21 天开始到付款之日结束。

**Form 8288-A.**

The withholding agent must prepare a Form 8288-A for each person from whom tax has been withheld. Attach copies A and B of Form 8288-A to Form 8288. Keep copy C for your records.

  

**表格 8288-A。** 

扣缴义务人必须为每个被扣缴税款的人准备一份 8288-A 表格。将表格 8288-A 的副本 A 和 B 附加到表格 8288。保留副本 C 供您记录。

The IRS will stamp copy B and send it to the person subject to withholding. That person must file a U.S. income tax return and attach the stamped Form 8288-A to receive credit for any tax withheld.  
IRS 将在副本 B 上盖章并将其发送给需缴纳预扣税的人。该人必须提交美国所得税申报表并附上盖章的 8288-A 表格才能获得任何预扣税款的抵免。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_A stamped copy of Form 8288-A will not be provided to the transferor if the transferor's TIN is not included on that form. The IRS will send a letter to the transferor requesting the TIN and providing instructions for how to get a TIN. When the transferor provides the IRS with a TIN, the IRS will provide the transferor with a stamped copy B of Form 8288-A.  
如果转让人的 TIN 未包含在表格 8288-A 中，则不会向转让人提供盖章的表格副本。 IRS 将致函转让人，索取 TIN 并提供如何获取 TIN 的说明。当转让人向 IRS 提供 TIN​​ 时，IRS 将向转让人提供 8288-A 表的盖章副本 B。_.

**Form 1099-S.**

In most cases, the real estate broker or other person responsible for closing the transaction must report the sale of the property to the IRS using Form 1099-S. For more information about Form 1099-S, see the [Instructions for Form 1099-S](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-1099-s) and the [General Instructions for Certain Information Returns](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-1099).

  

**1099-S 表格。** 

在大多数情况下，房地产经纪人或其他负责完成交易的人员必须使用 1099-S 表格向 IRS 报告房产出售情况。有关 1099-S 表格的更多信息，请参阅[1099-S 表格说明](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-1099-s)和[某些信息申报表的一般说明](https://www.irs.gov/forms-pubs/about-form-1099)。

#### Withholding Certificates预扣证书

The amount that must be withheld from the disposition of a USRPI can be adjusted by a withholding certificate issued by the IRS. The transferee, the transferee's agent, or the transferor may request a withholding certificate. The IRS will generally act on these requests within 90 days after receipt of a complete application including the TINs of all the parties to the transaction. A transferor that applies for a withholding certificate must notify the transferee, in writing, that the certificate has been applied for on the day of or the day before the transfer.  
处置 USRPI 时必须预扣的金额可以通过 IRS 签发的预扣税证书进行调整。受让人、受让人的代理人或转让人可以要求提供预扣税证明。 IRS 通常会在收到完整申请（包括交易各方的 TIN）后 90 天内对这些请求采取行动。转让人申请扣缴证明的，应当在转让当日或者前一日书面通知受让人已申请扣缴证明。

A withholding certificate may be issued due to:  
扣缴证明可能因以下原因而被签发：

1.  A determination by the IRS that reduced withholding is appropriate because either:  
    美国国税局 (IRS) 决定减少预扣税是适当的，因为：
    
    1.  The amount that must be withheld would be more than the transferor's maximum tax liability, or  
        必须预扣的金额将超过转让人的最高纳税义务，或
        
    2.  Withholding of the reduced amount would not jeopardize collection of the tax;  
        预扣减少的金额不会影响税收；
        
    
2.  The exemption from U.S. tax of all gain realized by the transferor; or  
    转让方实现的所有收益免征美国税；或者
    
3.  An agreement for the payment of tax providing security for the tax liability, entered into by the transferee or transferor.  
    由受让人或转让人签订的纳税协议，为纳税义务提供担保。
    

Applications for withholding certificates are divided into six basic categories. This categorizing provides for specific information that is needed to process the applications. The six categories are:  
扣缴证明申请分为六个基本类别。这种分类提供了处理申请所需的特定信息。这六个类别是：

1.  Applications based on a claim that the transferor is entitled to nonrecognition treatment or is exempt from tax,  
    基于转让人有权享受不承认待遇或免税的主张的申请，
    
2.  Applications based solely on a calculation of the transferor's maximum tax liability,  
    仅基于转让人最大纳税义务计算的申请，
    
3.  Applications under special installment sales rules,  
    特别分期销售规则下的申请，
    
4.  Applications based on an agreement for the payment of tax with conforming security,  
    基于具有合格担保的纳税协议的申请，
    
5.  Applications for blanket withholding certificates, and  
    申请一揽子预扣税证书，以及
    
6.  Applications on any other basis.  
    任何其他基础上的应用程序。
    

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/files.gif)
_The applicant must make available to the IRS, within the time prescribed, all information required to verify that representations relied upon in accepting the agreement are accurate, and that the obligations assumed by the applicant will be performed pursuant to the agreement. Failure to provide requested information promptly will usually result in rejection of the application, unless the IRS grants an extension of the target date.  
申请人必须在规定的时间内向国税局提供所有所需信息，以验证接受协议时所依据的陈述是准确的，并且申请人将根据协议履行其所承担的义务。未能及时提供所要求的信息通常会导致申请被拒绝，除非国税局同意延长目标日期。_.

**Categories (1), (2), and (3).**

Use Form 8288-B to apply for a withholding certificate. Follow the instructions for the form.

  

**类别 (1)、(2) 和 (3)。** 

使用 8288-B 表格申请预扣税证明。请按照表格的说明进行操作。

**Categories (4), (5), and (6).  
类别（4）、（5）和（6）。** 

Do not use Form 8288-B for applications under categories (4), (5), and (6). For these categories, follow the instructions given here and under the specific category.  
请勿将 8288-B 表格用于类别 (4)、(5) 和 (6) 下的申请。对于这些类别，请按照此处和特定类别下给出的说明进行操作。

All applications for withholding certificates must use the following format. The information must be provided in paragraphs labeled to correspond with the numbers and letters set forth below. If the information requested does not apply, place “N/A” in the relevant space.  
所有扣缴证明申请必须使用以下格式。信息必须在标记为与下面列出的数字和字母相对应的段落中提供。如果所要求的信息不适用，请在相关空白处填写“不适用”。

1.  Information on the application category:  
    申请类别信息：
    
    1.  State which category (4, 5, or 6) describes the application,  
        说明哪个类别（4、5 或 6）描述了该应用程序，
        
    2.  If a category (4) application:  
        如果类别 (4) 应用程序：
        
        1.  State whether the proposed agreement secures (A) the transferor's maximum tax liability, or (B) the amount that would otherwise have to be withheld; and  
            说明拟议协议是否保证 (A) 转让人的最大纳税义务，或 (B) 否则必须预扣的金额；和
            
        2.  State whether the proposed agreement and security instrument conform to the standard formats.  
            说明拟议的协议和安全文书是否符合标准格式。
            
        
    
2.  Information on the transferee or transferor:  
    受让方或转让方信息：
    
    1.  State the name, address, and TIN of the person applying for the withholding certificate (if this person does not have a TIN and is eligible for an ITIN, they can apply for the ITIN by attaching the application to a completed Form W-7 and forwarding the package to the address given in the Form W-7 instructions);  
        说明申请预扣税证明的人员的姓名、地址和 TIN（如果此人没有 TIN 但有资格获得 ITIN，他们可以通过将申请表附加到填妥的 W-7 表格中来申请 ITIN，并且将包裹转发至 W-7 表格说明中给出的地址）；
        
    2.  State whether that person is the transferee or transferor; and  
        说明该人是受让人还是转让人；和
        
    3.  State the name, address, and TIN of all other transferees and transferors of the USRPI for which the withholding certificate is sought.  
        说明要求扣缴证明的 USRPI 所有其他受让人和转让人的姓名、地址和 TIN。
        
    
3.  Information on the USRPI for which the withholding certificate is sought. State the:  
    有关寻求预扣税证明的 USRPI 的信息。说明：
    
    1.  Type of interest (such as interest in real property, in associated personal property, or in a domestic U.S. real property holding corporation);  
        权益类型（例如不动产、相关个人财产或美国国内不动产控股公司的权益）；
        
    2.  Contract price;合同价；
        
    3.  Date of transfer;转让日期；
        
    4.  Location and general description (if an interest in real property);  
        位置和一般描述（如果对不动产感兴趣）；
        
    5.  Class or type and amount of the interest in a U.S. real property holding corporation; and  
        美国房地产控股公司的权益类别或类型及金额；和
        
    6.  Whether in the 3 preceding tax years (1) U.S. income tax returns were filed relating to the USRPI and, if so, when and where those returns were filed and, if not, why returns were not filed, and (2) U.S. income taxes were paid relating to the USRPI and, if so, the amount of tax paid.  
        是否在之前的 3 个纳税年度中 (1) 提交了与 USRPI 相关的美国所得税申报表，如果是，提交这些申报表的时间和地点，如果没有，为什么没有提交申报表，以及 (2) 美国所得税是否已支付与 USRPI 相关的费用，如果是，则支付的税额。
        
    
4.  Provide full information concerning the basis for the issuance of the withholding certificate. Although the information to be included in this section of the application will vary from case to case, the rules shown under the specific category provide general guidelines for the inclusion of appropriate information for that category.  
    提供有关签发扣缴证明依据的完整信息。尽管应用程序这一部分中包含的信息因具体情况而异，但特定类别下显示的规则为包含该类别的适当信息提供了一般准则。
    

The application must be signed by the individual, a responsible officer in the case of a corporation, a general partner in the case of a partnership, or a trustee, executor, or equivalent fiduciary in the case of a trust or estate, or a duly authorized agent (with a copy of the power of attorney, such as Form 2848, attached). The person signing the application must verify under penalties of perjury that all representations are true, correct, and complete to that person's knowledge and belief. If the application is based in whole or in part on information provided by another party to the transaction, that information must be supported by a written verification signed under penalties of perjury by that party and attached to the application.  
申请必须由个人、公司的负责人、合伙企业的普通合伙人、信托或遗产的受托人、遗嘱执行人或同等受托人或正式的受托人签署。授权代理人（附有授权书副本，例如表格 2848）。签署申请的人必须核实所有陈述均据该人所知和所信是真实、正确和完整的，否则将受伪证罪处罚。如果申请全部或部分基于交易另一方提供的信息，则该信息必须得到该方签署的书面验证的支持，否则将受到伪证罪处罚，并附在申请中。

Send applications to the:  
将申请发送至：

  
| ![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/envelope.gif)

Address you may need

 |   
Ogden Service Center奥格登服务中心  
P.O. Box 409101邮政信箱 409101  
Ogden, UT 84409奥格登, UT 84409 |

**Category (4) applications.**

If the application is based on an agreement for the payment of tax, the application must include:

  

**类别（4）应用。** 

如果申请基于纳税协议，则申请必须包括：

*   Information establishing the transferor's maximum tax liability, or the amount that otherwise has to be withheld;  
    确定转让人最大纳税义务或必须预扣金额的信息；
    
*   A signed copy of the agreement proposed by the applicant; and  
    申请人提出的协议的签名副本；和
    
*   A copy of the security instrument proposed by the applicant.  
    申请人提出的担保文书副本。
    

Either the transferee or the transferor may enter into an agreement for the payment of tax. The agreement is a contract between the IRS and any other person and consists of two necessary elements. Those elements are:  
受让方和转让方可以签订纳税协议。该协议是国税局与任何其他人之间的合同，由两个必要要素组成。这些要素是：

*   A detailed description of the rights and obligations of each, and  
    每个权利和义务的详细描述，以及
    
*   A security instrument or other form of security acceptable to the Commissioner or his delegate.  
    专员或其代表可接受的担保文书或其他形式的担保。
    

For more information on the agreement for the payment of tax, including a sample agreement, see section 5 of Revenue Procedure 2000-35, 2000-35 I.R.B. 211, available at [IRS.gov/pub/irs-irbs/irb00-35.pdf](https://www.irs.gov/pub/irs-irbs/irb00-35.pdf).  
有关纳税协议的更多信息，包括协议样本，请参阅《收入程序 2000-35》、《2000-35 IRB 211》第 5 节，网址为[IRS.gov/pub/irs-irbs/irb00-35.pdf](https://www.irs.gov/pub/irs-irbs/irb00-35.pdf) 。

There are four major types of security acceptable to the IRS. They are:  
美国国税局可以接受四种主要的安全类型。他们是：

*   Bond with surety or guarantor,  
    与保证人或担保人的债券，
    
*   Bond with collateral,有抵押品的债券，
    
*   Letter of credit, and信用证，以及
    
*   Guarantee (corporate transferors).  
    担保（公司转让人）。
    

The IRS may, in unusual circumstances and at its discretion, accept any additional form of security that it finds to be adequate.  
在特殊情况下，美国国税局可以自行决定接受其认为足够的任何额外形式的担保。

For more information on acceptable security instruments, including sample forms of these instruments, see section 6 of Revenue Procedure 2000-35.  
有关可接受的担保工具的更多信息，包括这些工具的样本表格，请参阅《收入程序 2000-35》第 6 节。

**Category (5) applications.**

A blanket withholding certificate may be issued if the transferor holding the USRPI provides an irrevocable letter of credit or a guarantee and enters into a tax payment and security agreement with the IRS. A blanket withholding certificate excuses withholding concerning multiple dispositions of those property interests by the transferor or the transferor's legal representative during a period of no more than 12 months.

  

**第(5)类应用。** 

如果持有 USRPI 的转让人提供不可撤销的信用证或担保，并与 IRS 签订纳税和担保协议，则可以签发一揽子预扣税凭证。一揽子预扣税证明可以免除转让人或其法定代表人在不超过 12 个月的时间内多次处置这些财产权益的预扣税。

For more information, see section 9 of Revenue Procedure 2000-35.  
欲了解更多信息，请参阅《收入程序 2000-35》第 9 节。

**Category (6) applications.**

These are nonstandard applications and may be of the following types.

  

**第(6)类应用。** 

这些是非标准应用程序，可能属于以下类型。

_**Agreement for payment of tax with nonconforming security.**_

An applicant seeking to enter into an agreement for the payment of tax but wanting to provide a nonconforming type of security must include the following in the application.

  

_**使用不合格担保的纳税协议。** _

寻求签订纳税协议但希望提供不合格类型担保的申请人必须在申请中包含以下内容。

1.  The information required for _[category (4) applications](#en_US_2024_publink1000225121 "Category (4) applications.")_, discussed earlier.  
    前面讨论过的_[类别 (4) 申请](#en_US_2024_publink1000225121 "Category (4) applications.")_所需的信息。
    
2.  A description of the nonconforming security proposed by the applicant.  
    对申请人提出的不合格证券的描述。
    
3.  A memorandum of law and facts establishing that the proposed security is valid and enforceable and that it adequately protects the government's interest.  
    一份法律备忘录和事实，证明所提议的担保是有效的、可执行的，并且充分保护了政府的利益。
    

_**Other nonstandard applications.**_

An application for a withholding certificate not previously described must explain in detail the proposed basis for the issuance of the certificate and set forth the reasons justifying the issuance of a certificate on that basis.

  

_**其他非标准应用。** _

申请之前未描述的预扣税证书必须详细解释拟签发证书的依据，并说明依据该依据签发证书的理由。

#### Amendments to Applications  
申请的修改

An applicant for a withholding certificate may amend an otherwise complete application by sending an amending statement to the address shown earlier in _[Withholding Certificates](#en_US_2024_publink1000225116 "Withholding Certificates")_. There is no particular form required, but the amending statement must provide the following information.  
预扣税证书的申请人可以通过向_[预扣税证书](#en_US_2024_publink1000225116 "Withholding Certificates")_前面所示的地址发送修改声明来修改原本完整的申请。没有特定的表格要求，但修改声明必须提供以下信息。

*   The name, address, and TIN of the person providing the amending statement specifying whether that person is the transferee or transferor.  
    提供修改声明的人的姓名、地址和纳税人识别号，指明该人是受让人还是转让人。
    
*   The date of the original application for a withholding certificate that is being amended.  
    原始申请正在修改的预扣税证书的日期。
    
*   A brief description of the real property interest for which the original application for a withholding certificate was provided.  
    原始预扣税申请所涉及的不动产权益的简要说明。
    
*   The basis for the amendment including any change in the facts supporting the original application for a withholding certificate and any change in the terms of the withholding certificate.  
    修改依据包括原扣缴证明申请事实的变更以及扣缴证明条款的变更。
    

The statement must be signed and accompanied by a penalties of perjury statement.  
该声明必须签署并附有伪证处罚声明。

If an amending statement is provided, the time in which the IRS must act upon the application is extended by 30 days. If the amending statement substantially changes the original application, the time for acting upon the application is extended by 60 days. If an amending statement is received after the withholding certificate has been signed, but before it has been mailed to the applicant, the IRS will have a 90-day extension of time in which to act.  
如果提供修改声明，IRS 必须对申请采取行动的时间将延长 30 天。如果修改声明对原申请有实质性改变，则对申请采取行动的时间延长60天。如果在预扣税证书签署后但在邮寄给申请人之前收到修改声明，IRS 将有 90 天的延期时间采取行动。

#### Definitions定义

**Chapter 4 withholding rate pool.**

A “chapter 4 withholding rate pool” means a pool of payees that are nonparticipating FFIs provided on a chapter 4 withholding statement (as described in Regulations section 1.1471-3(c)(3)(iii)(B)(3)) to which a withholdable payment is allocated. The term also means a pool of payees provided on an FFI withholding statement (as described in Regulations section 1.1471-3(c)(iii)(B)(2)) to which a withholdable payment is allocated to (a) a pool of payees consisting of each class of recalcitrant account holders described in Regulations section 1.1471-4(d)(6) (or with respect to an FFI that is a QI, a single pool of recalcitrant account holders), including a separate pool of account holders to which the escrow procedures for dormant accounts apply; or (b) a pool of payees that are U.S. persons as described in Regulations section 1.1471-3(c)(3)(iii)(B)(2) (including such a pool allocated to a reportable amount on a withholding statement provided solely for chapter 3 purposes).

  

**第四章 预扣税率池。** 

“第 4 章预扣税率池”是指第 4 章预扣税声明中提供的非参与 FFI 的收款人池（如条例第 1.1471-3(c)(3)(iii)(B)(3) 节所述），以其中分配了可预扣的付款。该术语还指 FFI 预扣税声明中提供的一组收款人（如条例第 1.1471-3(c)(iii)(B)(2) 条所述），其中预扣付款被分配给 (a) 一组收款人由《条例》第 1.1471-4(d)(6) 条中描述的各类顽固账户持有人组成（或对于属于 QI 的 FFI，单一池顽抗账户持有人），包括适用休眠账户托管程序的单独账户持有人池； (b) 条例第 1.1471-3(c)(3)(iii)(B)(2) 条中所述的美国人收款人池（包括在预扣税表上分配给可报告金额的此类池子，前提是仅用于第 3 章的目的）。

**Deemed-compliant FFI.**

A “deemed-compliant FFI” means an FFI that is treated, pursuant to section 1471(b)(2) and Regulations section 1.1471-5(f), as meeting the requirements of section 1471(b). The term “deemed-compliant FFI” includes a nonreporting IGA FFI (as defined in Regulations section 1.1471-1(b)(83)).

  

**视为合规的 FFI。** 

“被视为合规的 FFI”是指根据第 1471(b)(2) 条和法规第 1.1471-5(f) 条被视为满足第 1471(b) 条要求的 FFI。 “视为合规 FFI”一词包括非报告 IGA FFI（如《条例》第 1.1471-1(b)(83) 节中所定义）。

**Dividend equivalents.**

Generally, a “dividend equivalent” is any payment that references the payment of a dividend from an underlying security pursuant to a securities lending or sale-repurchase transaction, SNPC, or specified ELI. This applies without regard to whether there is an actual distribution of cash or property.

  

**股息等值。** 

一般来说，“等价股息”是指根据证券借贷或销售回购交易、SNPC 或指定 ELI 从基础证券支付股息的任何付款。无论是否实际分配现金或财产，这都适用。

**Exempt beneficial owner.**

An “exempt beneficial owner” is any person described in Regulations sections 1.1471-6(b) through (g) and includes any person treated as an exempt beneficial owner under an applicable Model 1 IGA or Model 2 IGA.

  

**豁免受益所有人。** 

“豁免受益所有人”是指条例第 1.1471-6(b) 至 (g) 条中描述的任何人，包括根据适用的模型 1 IGA 或模型 2 IGA 被视为豁免受益所有人的任何人。

**Financial institution (FI).**

A “financial institution” (FI) is any institution that is a depository institution, custodial institution, investment entity, insurance company (or holding company of an insurance company) that issues cash value insurance or annuity contracts, or a holding company or treasury center that is part of an expanded affiliated group of certain FFIs, and includes a financial institution, as defined under an applicable Model 1 IGA or Model 2 IGA. See Regulations section 1.1471-5(e)(1).

  

**金融机构 (FI)。** 

“金融机构”（FI）是指发行现金价值保险或年金合同的存款机构、托管机构、投资实体、保险公司（或保险公司的控股公司）、控股公司或财务中心的任何机构属于某些 FFI 扩大附属集团的一部分，并包括适用的模型 1 IGA 或模型 2 IGA 中定义的金融机构。请参阅法规第 1.1471-5(e)(1) 节。

**Foreign financial institution (FFI).**

Except as otherwise provided for certain foreign branches of a U.S. financial institution or territory financial institutions, a “foreign financial institution” (FFI) means a financial institution that is a foreign entity. The term “FFI” also includes a foreign branch of a U.S. financial institution with a QI agreement in effect.

  

**外国金融机构 (FFI)。** 

除非对美国金融机构或领土金融机构的某些外国分支机构另有规定，“外国金融机构”（FFI）是指外国实体的金融机构。 “FFI”一词还包括具有有效 QI 协议的美国金融机构的外国分支机构。

**Model 1 IGA.**

A “Model 1 IGA” means an agreement between the United States or the Treasury Department and a foreign government or one or more foreign agencies to implement FATCA through reporting by financial institutions to such foreign government or agency thereof, followed by automatic exchange of the reported information with the IRS. For a list of jurisdictions treated as having an IGA in effect, go to [Treasury.gov/Resource-Center/Tax-Policy/Treaties/Pages/FATCA.aspx](https://www.treasury.gov/resource-center/tax-policy/treaties/Pages/FATCA.aspx).

  

**模型 1 IGA。** 

“模型 1 IGA”是指美国或财政部与外国政府或一个或多个外国机构之间达成的一项协议，通过金融机构向该外国政府或其机构报告，然后自动交换报告来实施 FATCA。向 IRS 提供信息。有关被视为拥有有效 IGA 的司法管辖区列表，请访问[Treasury.gov/Resource-Center/Tax-Policy/Treaties/Pages/FATCA.aspx](https://www.treasury.gov/resource-center/tax-policy/treaties/Pages/FATCA.aspx) 。

**Model 2 IGA.**

A “Model 2 IGA” means an agreement or arrangement between the United States or the Treasury Department and a foreign government or one or more foreign agencies to implement FATCA through reporting by financial institutions directly to the IRS in accordance with the requirements of the FFI agreement, as modified by an applicable Model 2 IGA, supplemented by the exchange of information between such foreign government or agency thereof and the IRS. For a list of jurisdictions treated as having an IGA in effect, go to [Treasury.gov/Resource-Center/Tax-Policy/Treaties/Pages/FATCA.aspx](https://www.treasury.gov/resource-center/tax-policy/treaties/Pages/FATCA.aspx).

  

**模型 2 IGA。** 

“模型 2 IGA”是指美国或财政部与外国政府或一个或多个外国机构之间通过金融机构根据 FFI 协议的要求直接向 IRS 报告来实施 FATCA 的协议或安排，经适用的模型 2 IGA 修改，并通过该外国政府或其机构与 IRS 之间的信息交换进行补充。有关被视为拥有有效 IGA 的司法管辖区列表，请访问[Treasury.gov/Resource-Center/Tax-Policy/Treaties/Pages/FATCA.aspx](https://www.treasury.gov/resource-center/tax-policy/treaties/Pages/FATCA.aspx) 。

**Non-financial foreign entity (NFFE).**

A “non-financial foreign entity” (NFFE) is a foreign entity that is not a financial institution. An NFFE includes a territory NFFE, as defined in Regulations section 1.1471-1(b)(132), and a foreign entity treated as an NFFE pursuant to a Model 1 IGA or Model 2 IGA.

  

**非金融外国实体 (NFFE)。** 

“非金融外国实体”（NFFE）是指非金融机构的外国实体。 NFFE 包括法规第 1.1471-1(b)(132) 条中定义的境内 NFFE，以及根据模型 1 IGA 或模型 2 IGA 被视为 NFFE 的外国实体。

**Nonparticipating FFI.**

A “nonparticipating FFI” is an FFI other than a participating FFI, a deemed-compliant FFI, or an exempt beneficial owner.

  

**非参与 FFI。** 

“非参与 FFI”是指除参与 FFI、视为合规 FFI 或豁免受益所有人之外的 FFI。

**Participating FFI.**

A “participating FFI” is an FFI that has agreed to comply with the requirements of an FFI agreement with respect to all branches of the FFI, other than a branch that is a reporting Model 1 FFI or a U.S. branch. The term "participating FFI" also includes a reporting Model 2 FFI and a QI branch of a U.S. financial institution, unless such branch is a reporting Model 1 FFI.

  

**参与的 FFI。** 

“参与 FFI”是指同意遵守 FFI 协议中有关 FFI 的所有分支机构（报告模式 1 FFI 分支机构或美国分支机构除外）的要求的 FFI。 “参与 FFI”一词还包括报告模型 2 FFI 和美国金融机构的 QI 分支机构，除非此类分支机构是报告模型 1 FFI。

**Passive NFFE.**

A “passive NFFE” is an NFFE that is not an excepted NFFE. With respect to a reporting Model 2 FFI filing a Form 8966 to report its accounts and payees, a passive NFFE is an NFFE that is not an active NFFE (as described in the applicable IGA).

  

**被动 NFFE。** 

“被动 NFFE”是指不属于例外 NFFE 的 NFFE。对于提交 8966 表格以报告其账户和收款人的报告模型 2 FFI，被动 NFFE 是指不是主动 NFFE 的 NFFE（如适用的 IGA 中所述）。

**Qualified derivatives dealer (QDD).**

A “qualified derivatives dealer” (QDD) is a QI that is an eligible entity (as defined in Regulations section 1.1441-1(e)(6)(ii)) that agrees to meet the requirements of Regulations section 1.1441-1(e)(6)(i) and the QI agreement.

  

**合格衍生品交易商（QDD）。** 

“合格衍生品交易商”(QDD) 是指符合法规第 1.1441-1(e)(6)(ii) 条规定的合格实体，同意满足法规第 1.1441-1(e) 条要求的 QI。 )(6)(i) 和 QI 协议。

**Recalcitrant account holder.**

A “recalcitrant account holder” is an account holder (other than an account holder that is an FFI or is presumed to be an FFI) of a participating FFI or registered deemed-compliant FFI that has failed to provide the FFI maintaining its account with the information required under Regulations section 1.1471-5(g).

  

**顽固的账户持有人。** 

“顽固账户持有人”是指参与 FFI 或注册的视为合规 FFI 的账户持有人（作为 FFI 或被推定为 FFI 的账户持有人除外），但未能向维护其账户的 FFI 提供条例第 1.1471-5(g) 条要求的信息。

**Registered deemed-compliant FFI.**

A “registered deemed-compliant FFI” is an FFI described in Regulations section 1.1471-5(f)(1) and includes a reporting Model 1 FFI and a QI branch of a U.S. financial institution that is a reporting Model 1 FFI.

  

**已注册视为合规的 FFI。** 

“已注册的视为合规 FFI”是指《条例》第 1.1471-5(f)(1) 条中描述的 FFI，包括报告模型 1 FFI 和作为报告模型 1 FFI 的美国金融机构的 QI 分支机构。

**Reporting Model 1 FFI.**

A “reporting Model 1 FFI” is an FI, including a foreign branch of a U.S. financial institution, treated as a reporting financial institution under a Model 1 IGA.

  

**报告模型 1 FFI。** 

“报告模式 1 FFI”是指根据模式 1 IGA 被视为报告金融机构的金融机构，包括美国金融机构的外国分支机构。

**Reporting Model 2 FFI.**

A “reporting Model 2 FFI” is an FFI described in a Model 2 IGA that has agreed to comply with the requirements of an FFI agreement with respect to a branch.

  

**报告模型 2 FFI。** 

“报告模型 2 FFI”是模型 2 IGA 中描述的已同意遵守 FFI 协议有关分支机构的要求的 FFI。

**Territory financial institution.**

A “territory financial institution” is a financial institution that is incorporated or organized under the laws of any U.S. territory, excluding a territory entity that is a financial institution only because it is an investment entity, as defined in Regulations section 1.1471-5(e)(4).

  

**领土金融机构。** 

“领土金融机构”是指根据任何美国领土法律成立或组建的金融机构，不包括仅因为其是投资实体而成为金融机构的领土实体，如《条例》第 1.1471-5(e) 节中所定义。 ）（4）。

**Withholdable payment.**

A “withholdable payment” is a payment described in Regulations section 1.1473-1(a). See [_Income Subject to Withholding_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224880 "Income Subject to Withholding"), earlier, for a discussion of which payments qualify as withholdable payments.

  

**可预扣的付款。** 

“可预扣的付款”是指条例第 1.1473-1(a) 条中描述的付款。请参阅前面的[_“应预扣税款的收入”_](#en_US_2024_publink1000224880 "Income Subject to Withholding") ，了解哪些付款符合可预扣税款的讨论。

#### Tax Treaties税收协定

The United States has bilateral income tax treaties, also known as “conventions,” with a number of foreign countries under which residents (sometimes limited to citizens) of those countries are taxed at a reduced rate or are exempt from U.S. income taxes on certain income received from within the United States.  
美国与许多国家签订了双边所得税条约，也称为“公约”，根据这些条约，这些国家的居民（有时仅限于公民）可以按降低的税率征税或对某些收入免征美国所得税从美国境内收到。

Withholding at source under the statutory rules discussed in this publication may not be required for income that is exempt under a tax treaty, so long as the taxpayer claiming such exemption satisfies all of the relevant requirements, including providing to its withholding agent any applicable withholding certificates (or documentary evidence, when permitted) supporting the treaty claim.  
对于根据税收协定免税的收入，可能不需要根据本出版物中讨论的法定规则从源头扣缴税款，只要申请此类免税的纳税人满足所有相关要求，包括向扣缴义务人提供任何适用的扣缴证明（或书面证据，如果允许的话）支持条约主张。

**Obtaining treaty information.**

You can obtain the full text of these treaties, and accompanying technical explanations, at [IRS.gov/Businesses/International-Businesses/United-States-Income-Tax-Treaties-A-to-Z](https://www.irs.gov/businesses/international-businesses/united-states-income-tax-treaties-a-to-z).

  

**获取条约信息。** 

您可以访问[IRS.gov/Businesses/International-Businesses/United-States-Income-Tax-Treaties-A-to-Z](https://www.irs.gov/businesses/international-businesses/united-states-income-tax-treaties-a-to-z)获取这些条约的全文以及随附的技术说明。

Detailed information about treaty provisions can be found at [IRS.gov/Individuals/International-Taxpayers/Tax-Treaties](https://www.irs.gov/Individuals/International-Taxpayers/Tax-Treaties).  
有关条约条款的详细信息，请访问[IRS.gov/Individuals/International-Taxpayers/Tax-Treaties](https://www.irs.gov/Individuals/International-Taxpayers/Tax-Treaties) 。

**Tax treaty tables.**

The tax treaty tables previously contained in this publication have been updated and moved to [IRS.gov/Individuals/International-Taxpayers/Tax-Treaty-Tables](https://www.irs.gov/Individuals/International-Taxpayers/Tax-Treaty-Tables).

  

**税收协定表。** 

本出版物之前包含的税收协定表已更新并移至[IRS.gov/Individuals/International-Taxpayers/Tax-Treaty-Tables](https://www.irs.gov/Individuals/International-Taxpayers/Tax-Treaty-Tables) 。

#### How To Get Tax Help  
如何获得税务帮助

If you have questions about a tax issue; need help preparing your tax return; or want to download free publications, forms, or instructions, go to [IRS.gov](https://www.irs.gov) to find resources that can help you right away.  
如果您对税务问题有疑问；需要帮助准备您的纳税申报表；或者想要下载免费出版物、表格或说明，请访问[IRS.gov](https://www.irs.gov)查找可以立即为您提供帮助的资源。

**Preparing and filing your tax return.**

After receiving all your wage and earnings statements (Forms W-2, W-2G, 1099-R, 1099-MISC, 1099-NEC, etc.); unemployment compensation statements (by mail or in a digital format) or other government payment statements (Form 1099-G); and interest, dividend, and retirement statements from banks and investment firms (Forms 1099), you have several options to choose from to prepare and file your tax return. You can prepare the tax return yourself, see if you qualify for free tax preparation, or hire a tax professional to prepare your return.

  

**准备并提交纳税申报表。** 

收到您的所有工资和收入报表（表格 W-2、W-2G、1099-R、1099-MISC、1099-NEC 等）后；失业补偿声明（通过邮寄或数字格式）或其他政府付款声明（表格 1099-G）；以及银行和投资公司的利息、股息和退休报表（1099 表），您有多种选择来准备和提交纳税申报表。您可以自己准备纳税申报表，看看您是否有资格获得免费报税，或聘请税务专业人士来准备您的纳税申报表。

**Free options for tax preparation.**

Your options for preparing and filing your return online or in your local community, if you qualify, include the following.

  

**税务准备的免费选择。** 

如果您符合资格，您可以选择在线或在当地社区准备和提交纳税申报表，包括以下内容。

*   **Free File.** This program lets you prepare and file your federal individual income tax return for free using software or Free File Fillable Forms. However, state tax preparation may not be available through Free File. Go to [IRS.gov/FreeFile](https://www.irs.gov/freefile) to see if you qualify for free online federal tax preparation, e-filing, and direct deposit or payment options.  
    **免费文件。** 该计划可让您使用软件或免费文件填写表格免费准备和提交联邦个人所得税申报表。但是，州税准备可能无法通过免费归档提供。请访问[IRS.gov/FreeFile](https://www.irs.gov/freefile)查看您是否有资格获得免费的在线联邦报税、电子报税以及直接存款或付款选项。
    
*   **VITA.** The Volunteer Income Tax Assistance (VITA) program offers free tax help to people with low-to-moderate incomes, persons with disabilities, and limited-English-speaking taxpayers who need help preparing their own tax returns. Go to [IRS.gov/VITA](https://www.irs.gov/vita), download the free IRS2Go app, or call 800-906-9887 for information on free tax return preparation.  
    **维塔。** 志愿者所得税援助 (VITA) 计划为需要帮助准备自己的纳税申报表的中低收入人士、残疾人和英语能力有限的纳税人提供免费税务帮助。请访问[IRS.gov/VITA](https://www.irs.gov/vita) ，下载免费的 IRS2Go 应用程序，或致电 800-906-9887 了解有关免费报税表准备的信息。
    
*   **TCE.** The Tax Counseling for the Elderly (TCE) program offers free tax help for all taxpayers, particularly those who are 60 years of age and older. TCE volunteers specialize in answering questions about pensions and retirement-related issues unique to seniors. Go to [IRS.gov/TCE](https://www.irs.gov/tce) or download the free IRS2Go app for information on free tax return preparation.  
    **三氯乙烯。** 老年人税务咨询 (TCE) 计划为所有纳税人，特别是 60 岁及以上的纳税人提供免费税务帮助。 TCE 志愿者专门回答老年人特有的养老金和退休相关问题。请访问[IRS.gov/TCE](https://www.irs.gov/tce)或下载免费的 IRS2Go 应用程序，了解有关免费报税表准备的信息。
    
*   **MilTax.** Members of the U.S. Armed Forces and qualified veterans may use MilTax, a free tax service offered by the Department of Defense through Military OneSource. For more information, go to [MilitaryOneSource](https://www.militaryonesource.mil/miltax) ([MilitaryOneSource.mil/MilTax](https://www.militaryonesource.mil/miltax)).  
    **军用税。** 美国武装部队成员和合格的退伍军人可以使用 MilTax，这是国防部通过 Military OneSource 提供的免费税务服务。欲了解更多信息，请访问[MilitaryOneSource](https://www.militaryonesource.mil/miltax) ( [MilitaryOneSource.mil/MilTax](https://www.militaryonesource.mil/miltax) ）。
    
    Also, the IRS offers Free Fillable Forms, which can be completed online and then e-filed regardless of income.  
    此外，美国国税局还提供免费填写的表格，无论收入如何，都可以在线填写，然后通过电子方式提交。
    

**Using online tools to help prepare your return.**

Go to [IRS.gov/Tools](https://www.irs.gov/tools) for the following.

  

**使用在线工具帮助您准备报税表。** 

请访问[IRS.gov/Tools](https://www.irs.gov/tools)获取以下信息。

*   The [Earned Income Tax Credit Assistant](https://www.irs.gov/eitcassistant) ([IRS.gov/EITCAssistant](https://www.irs.gov/eitcassistant)) determines if you’re eligible for the earned income credit (EIC).  
    [劳动收入税收抵免助理](https://www.irs.gov/eitcassistant)( [IRS.gov/EITCAssistant](https://www.irs.gov/eitcassistant) ) 确定您是否有资格获得劳动收入税收抵免 (EIC)。
    
*   The [Online EIN Application](https://www.irs.gov/ein) ([IRS.gov/EIN](https://www.irs.gov/ein)) helps you get an employer identification number (EIN) at no cost.  
    [在线 EIN 申请](https://www.irs.gov/ein)( [IRS.gov/EIN](https://www.irs.gov/ein) ) 可帮助您免费获得雇主识别号 (EIN)。
    
*   The [Tax Withholding Estimator](https://www.irs.gov/individuals/tax-withholding-estimator) ([IRS.gov/W4App](https://www.irs.gov/W4app)) makes it easier for you to estimate the federal income tax you want your employer to withhold from your paycheck. This is tax withholding. See how your withholding affects your refund, take-home pay, or tax due.  
    [预扣税估算器](https://www.irs.gov/individuals/tax-withholding-estimator)( [IRS.gov/W4App](https://www.irs.gov/W4app) ) 让您更轻松地估算您希望雇主从您的工资中预扣的联邦所得税。这是预扣税。查看您的预扣税如何影响您的退款、实得工资或应缴税款。
    

*   The [First-Time Homebuyer Credit Account Look-up](https://www.irs.gov/credits-deductions/individuals/first-time-homebuyer-credit-account-look-up) ([IRS.gov/HomeBuyer](https://www.irs.gov/homebuyer)) tool provides information on your repayments and account balance.  
    [首次购房者信用账户查询](https://www.irs.gov/credits-deductions/individuals/first-time-homebuyer-credit-account-look-up)( [IRS.gov/HomeBuyer](https://www.irs.gov/homebuyer) ) 工具提供有关您的还款和账户余额的信息。
    
*   The [Sales Tax Deduction Calculator](https://www.irs.gov/salestax) ([IRS.gov/SalesTax](https://www.irs.gov/salestax)) figures the amount you can claim if you itemize deductions on Schedule A (Form 1040).  
    如果您在附表 A（表格 1040）上逐项列出扣除额[，销售税扣除计算器](https://www.irs.gov/salestax)( [IRS.gov/SalesTax](https://www.irs.gov/salestax) ) 会计算出您可以申请的金额。
    

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/compute.gif)
  **Getting answers to your tax questions.** _On IRS.gov, you can get up-to-date information on current events and changes in tax law._  
获取税务问题的答案。在 IRS.gov 上，您可以获得有关时事和税法变更的最新信息。.

*   [IRS.gov/Help](https://www.irs.gov/help): A variety of tools to help you get answers to some of the most common tax questions.  
    [IRS.gov/Help](https://www.irs.gov/help) ：各种工具可帮助您获得一些最常见税务问题的答案。
    
*   [IRS.gov/ITA](https://www.irs.gov/ita): The Interactive Tax Assistant, a tool that will ask you questions and, based on your input, provide answers on a number of tax topics.  
    [IRS.gov/ITA](https://www.irs.gov/ita) ：交互式税务助手，该工具会向您提出问题，并根据您的输入提供有关许多税务主题的答案。
    
*   [IRS.gov/Forms](https://www.irs.gov/forms): Find forms, instructions, and publications. You will find details on the most recent tax changes and interactive links to help you find answers to your questions.  
    [IRS.gov/Forms](https://www.irs.gov/forms) ：查找表格、说明和出版物。您将找到有关最新税务变更的详细信息以及互动链接，以帮助您找到问题的答案。
    
*   You may also be able to access tax information in your e-filing software.  
    您还可以在电子申报软件中访问税务信息。
    

.

**Need someone to prepare your tax return?**

There are various types of tax return preparers, including enrolled agents, certified public accountants (CPAs), accountants, and many others who don’t have professional credentials. If you choose to have someone prepare your tax return, choose that preparer wisely. A paid tax preparer is:

  

**需要有人准备您的纳税申报表吗？**

报税员有多种类型，包括注册代理人、注册会计师 (CPA)、会计师以及许多其他没有专业资格的人。如果您选择让某人准备您的纳税申报表，请明智地选择该准备者。付费报税员是：

*   Primarily responsible for the overall substantive accuracy of your return,  
    主要对您的申报表的整体实质性准确性负责，
    
*   Required to sign the return, and  
    需要签署申报表，并且
    
*   Required to include their preparer tax identification number (PTIN).  
    需要包含其编制者税务识别号 (PTIN)。
    

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_Although the tax preparer always signs the return, you're ultimately responsible for providing all the information required for the preparer to accurately prepare your return and for the accuracy of every item reported on the return. Anyone paid to prepare tax returns for others should have a thorough understanding of tax matters. For more information on how to choose a tax preparer, go to_ [Tips for Choosing a Tax Preparer](https://www.irs.gov/tax-professionals/choosing-a-tax-professional) _on IRS.gov._  
尽管报税员总是在报税表上签名，但您最终有责任提供报税员准确准备报税表所需的所有信息以及报税表上报告的每个项目的准确性。任何受薪为他人准备纳税申报表的人都应该对税务问题有透彻的了解。有关如何选择报税员的更多信息，请访问 IRS.gov 上的选择报税员的提示。.

**Employers can register to use Business Services Online.**

The Social Security Administration (SSA) offers online service at [SSA.gov/employer](https://www.ssa.gov/employer/) for fast, free, and secure W-2 filing options to CPAs, accountants, enrolled agents, and individuals who process Form W-2, Wage and Tax Statement, and Form W-2c, Corrected Wage and Tax Statement.

  

**雇主可以注册使用在线商业服务。** 

社会保障管理局 (SSA) 在[SSA.gov/employer](https://www.ssa.gov/employer/)上提供在线服务[](https://www.ssa.gov/employer/)为注册会计师、会计师、注册代理人和处理 W-2 表“工资和税务报表”以及 W-2c 表“更正工资和税务报表”的个人提供快速、免费和安全的 W-2 归档选项。

**IRS social media.**

Go to [IRS.gov/SocialMedia](https://www.irs.gov/socialmedia) to see the various social media tools the IRS uses to share the latest information on tax changes, scam alerts, initiatives, products, and services. At the IRS, privacy and security are our highest priority. We use these tools to share public information with you. **Don’t** post your social security number (SSN) or other confidential information on social media sites. Always protect your identity when using any social networking site.

  

**国税局社交媒体。** 

请访问[IRS.gov/SocialMedia](https://www.irs.gov/socialmedia)查看 IRS 用于分享有关税收变化、诈骗警报、举措、产品和服务的最新信息的各种社交媒体工具。在国税局，隐私和安全是我们的首要任务。我们使用这些工具与您共享公共信息。**请勿**在社交媒体网站上发布您的社会安全号码 (SSN) 或其他机密信息。使用任何社交网站时始终保护您的身份。

The following IRS YouTube channels provide short, informative videos on various tax-related topics in English, Spanish, and ASL.  
以下 IRS YouTube 频道以英语、西班牙语和美国手语提供有关各种税务相关主题的信息简短视频。

*   [Youtube.com/irsvideos](https://www.youtube.com/irsvideos).  
    [Youtube.com/irsvideos](https://www.youtube.com/irsvideos) 。
    
*   [Youtube.com/irsvideosmultilingua](https://www.youtube.com/IRSvideosmultilingua).  
    [Youtube.com/irsvideosmultilingua](https://www.youtube.com/IRSvideosmultilingua) 。
    
*   [Youtube.com/irsvideosASL](https://www.youtube.com/IRSvideosASL).  
    [Youtube.com/irsvideosASL](https://www.youtube.com/IRSvideosASL) 。
    

**Watching IRS videos.**

The IRS Video portal (IRSVideos.gov) contains video and audio presentations for individuals, small businesses, and tax professionals.

  

**观看国税局视频。** 

IRS 视频门户 (IRSVideos.gov) 包含面向个人、小型企业和税务专业人士的视频和音频演示。

**Online tax information in other languages.**

You can find information on [IRS.gov/MyLanguage](https://www.irs.gov/mylanguage) if English isn’t your native language.

  

**其他语言的在线税务信息。** 

如果英语不是您的母语，您可以在[IRS.gov/MyLanguage](https://www.irs.gov/mylanguage)上找到信息。

**Free Over-the-Phone Interpreter (OPI) Service.**

The IRS is committed to serving taxpayers with limited-English proficiency (LEP) by offering OPI services. The OPI Service is a federally funded program and is available at Taxpayer Assistance Centers (TACs), most IRS offices, and every VITA/TCE tax return site. The OPI Service is accessible in more than 350 languages.

  

**免费电话口译员 (OPI) 服务。** 

IRS 致力于通过提供 OPI 服务为英语水平有限 (LEP) 的纳税人提供服务。 OPI 服务是一项联邦政府资助的计划，可在纳税人援助中心 (TAC)、大多数 IRS 办事处以及每个 VITA/TCE 纳税申报点获取。 OPI 服务支持 350 多种语言。

**Accessibility Helpline available for taxpayers with disabilities.**

Taxpayers who need information about accessibility services can call 833-690-0598. The Accessibility Helpline can answer questions related to current and future accessibility products and services available in alternative media formats (for example, braille, large print, audio, etc.). The Accessibility Helpline does not have access to your IRS account. For help with tax law, refunds, or account-related issues, go to [IRS.gov/LetUsHelp](https://www.irs.gov/letushelp).

  

**为残疾纳税人提供无障碍帮助热线。** 

需要有关无障碍服务信息的纳税人可以致电 833-690-0598。无障碍帮助热线可以回答与当前和未来以替代媒体格式（例如盲文、大字体、音频等）提供的无障碍产品和服务相关的问题。辅助服务热线无权访问您的 IRS 帐户。如需税法、退款或账户相关问题的帮助，请访问[IRS.gov/LetUsHelp](https://www.irs.gov/letushelp) 。

### Note.
