Form 9000, Alternative Media Preference, or Form 9000(SP) allows you to elect to receive certain types of written correspondence in the following formats.

  

### 笔记。

表格 9000、替代媒体偏好或表格 9000(SP) 允许您选择接收以下格式的某些类型的书面信件。

*   Standard Print.标准打印。
    

*   Large Print.大字印刷。
    

*   Braille.盲文。
    

*   Audio (MP3).音频（MP3）。
    

*   Plain Text File (TXT).纯文本文件 (TXT)。
    

*   Braille Ready File (BRF).  
    盲文就绪文件 (BRF)。

**灾难。** 

请访问[IRS.gov/DisasterRelief](https://www.irs.gov/DisasterRelief)查看可用的灾难税减免。

**Getting tax forms and publications.**

Go to [IRS.gov/Forms](https://www.irs.gov/forms) to view, download, or print all the forms, instructions, and publications you may need. Or, you can go to [IRS.gov/OrderForms](https://www.irs.gov/orderforms) to place an order.

  

**获取税务表格和出版物。** 

请访问[IRS.gov/Forms](https://www.irs.gov/forms)查看、下载或打印您可能需要的所有表格、说明和出版物。或者，您可以访问[IRS.gov/OrderForms](https://www.irs.gov/orderforms)下订单。

**Getting tax publications and instructions in eBook format.**

Download and view most tax publications and instructions (including the Instructions for Form 1040) on mobile devices as eBooks at [IRS.gov/eBooks](https://www.irs.gov/ebooks).

  

**获取电子书格式的税务出版物和说明。** 

在[IRS.gov/eBooks](https://www.irs.gov/ebooks)上以电子书形式在移动设备上下载并查看大多数税务出版物和说明（包括 1040 表格的说明）。

IRS eBooks have been tested using Apple's iBooks for iPad. Our eBooks haven’t been tested on other dedicated eBook readers, and eBook functionality may not operate as intended.  
IRS 电子书已使用 Apple iPad 版 iBooks 进行了测试。我们的电子书尚未在其他专用电子书阅读器上进行测试，并且电子书功能可能无法按预期运行。

**Access your online account (individual taxpayers only).**

Go to [IRS.gov/Account](https://www.irs.gov/account) to securely access information about your federal tax account.

  

**访问您的在线帐户（仅限个人纳税人）。** 

请访问[IRS.gov/Account](https://www.irs.gov/account)以安全地访问有关您的联邦税务账户的信息。

*   View the amount you owe and a breakdown by tax year.  
    查看您所欠的金额以及按纳税年度的明细。
    
*   See payment plan details or apply for a new payment plan.  
    查看付款计划详细信息或申请新的付款计划。
    
*   Make a payment or view 5 years of payment history and any pending or scheduled payments.  
    进行付款或查看 5 年的付款历史记录以及任何待处理或计划的付款。
    
*   Access your tax records, including key data from your most recent tax return, and transcripts.  
    访问您的税务记录，包括您最近的纳税申报表和成绩单中的关键数据。
    
*   View digital copies of select notices from the IRS.  
    查看 IRS 精选通知的数字副本。
    
*   Approve or reject authorization requests from tax professionals.  
    批准或拒绝税务专业人员的授权请求。
    
*   View your address on file or manage your communication preferences.  
    查看您存档的地址或管理您的通讯偏好。
    

**Get a transcript of your return.**

With an online account, you can access a variety of information to help you during the filing season. You can get a transcript, review your most recently filed tax return, and get your adjusted gross income. Create or access your online account at [IRS.gov/Account](https://www.irs.gov/payments/your-online-account).

  

**获取您的退货记录。** 

通过在线帐户，您可以访问各种信息，以在申请季节为您提供帮助。您可以获得成绩单，查看最近提交的纳税申报表，并获得调整后的总收​​入。在[IRS.gov/Account](https://www.irs.gov/payments/your-online-account)创建或访问您的在线帐户。

**Tax Pro Account.**

This tool lets your tax professional submit an authorization request to access your individual taxpayer IRS online account. For more information, go to [IRS.gov/TaxProAccount](https://www.irs.gov/taxproaccount).

  

**税务专业帐户。** 

该工具可让您的税务专业人员提交授权请求以访问您的个人纳税人 IRS 在线帐户。欲了解更多信息，请访问[IRS.gov/TaxProAccount](https://www.irs.gov/taxproaccount) 。

**Using direct deposit.**

The safest and easiest way to receive a tax refund is to e-file and choose direct deposit, which securely and electronically transfers your refund directly into your financial account. Direct deposit also avoids the possibility that your check could be lost, stolen, destroyed, or returned undeliverable to the IRS. Eight in 10 taxpayers use direct deposit to receive their refunds. If you don’t have a bank account, go to [IRS.gov/DirectDeposit](https://www.irs.gov/directdeposit) for more information on where to find a bank or credit union that can open an account online.

  

**使用直接存款。** 

获得退税最安全、最简单的方法是通过电子方式提交并选择直接存款，这样可以安全地以电子方式将您的退税直接转入您的财务账户。直接存款还可以避免您的支票丢失、被盗、毁坏或无法送达国税局而被退回的可能性。十分之八的纳税人使用直接存款来获得退款。如果您没有银行账户，请访问[IRS.gov/DirectDeposit，](https://www.irs.gov/directdeposit)了解有关在哪里查找可以在线开户的银行或信用合作社的更多信息。

**Reporting and resolving your tax-related identity theft issues.  
报告并解决您与税务相关的身份盗窃问题。** 

*   Tax-related identity theft happens when someone steals your personal information to commit tax fraud. Your taxes can be affected if your SSN is used to file a fraudulent return or to claim a refund or credit.  
    当有人窃取您的个人信息以进行税务欺诈时，就会发生与税务相关的身份盗窃。如果您的 SSN 被用来提交欺诈性申报表或申请退款或抵免，您的税款可能会受到影响。
    

*   The IRS doesn’t initiate contact with taxpayers by email, text messages (including shortened links), telephone calls, or social media channels to request or verify personal or financial information. This includes requests for personal identification numbers (PINs), passwords, or similar information for credit cards, banks, or other financial accounts.  
    美国国税局不会通过电子邮件、短信（包括缩短的链接）、电话或社交媒体渠道与纳税人联系，以请求或验证个人或财务信息。这包括请求提供信用卡、银行或其他金融账户的个人识别码 (PIN)、密码或类似信息。
    
*   Go to [IRS.gov/IdentityTheft](https://www.irs.gov/identitytheft), the IRS Identity Theft Central webpage, for information on identity theft and data security protection for taxpayers, tax professionals, and businesses. If your SSN has been lost or stolen or you suspect you’re a victim of tax-related identity theft, you can learn what steps you should take.  
    请访问[IRS.gov/IdentityTheft（IRS](https://www.irs.gov/identitytheft)身份盗窃中心网页），了解有关纳税人、税务专业人员和企业的身份盗窃和数据安全保护的信息。如果您的 SSN 丢失或被盗，或者您怀疑自己是与税务相关的身份盗窃的受害者，您可以了解应该采取哪些步骤。
    
*   Get an Identity Protection PIN (IP PIN). IP PINs are six-digit numbers assigned to taxpayers to help prevent the misuse of their SSNs on fraudulent federal income tax returns. When you have an IP PIN, it prevents someone else from filing a tax return with your SSN. To learn more, go to [IRS.gov/IPPIN](https://www.irs.gov/ippin).  
    获取身份保护 PIN (IP PIN)。 IP PIN 是分配给纳税人的六位数字，有助于防止在欺诈性联邦所得税申报表上滥用其 SSN。当您拥有 IP PIN 时，可以防止其他人使用您的 SSN 提交纳税申报表。要了解更多信息，请访问[IRS.gov/IPPIN](https://www.irs.gov/ippin) 。
    

**Ways to check on the status of your refund.  
检查退款状态的方法。** 

*   Go to [IRS.gov/Refunds](https://www.irs.gov/refunds).  
    请访问[IRS.gov/Refunds](https://www.irs.gov/refunds) 。
    
*   Download the official IRS2Go app to your mobile device to check your refund status.  
    将官方 IRS2Go 应用程序下载到您的移动设备以检查您的退款状态。
    
*   Call the automated refund hotline at 800-829-1954.  
    请拨打自动退款热线 800-829-1954。
    

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_The IRS can’t issue refunds before mid-February for returns that claimed the EIC or the additional child tax credit (ACTC). This applies to the entire refund, not just the portion associated with these credits.  
对于申请 EIC 或额外儿童税收抵免 (ACTC) 的申报表，IRS 无法在 2 月中旬之前发放退款。这适用于整个退款，而不仅仅是与这些积分相关的部分。_.

**Making a tax payment.**

Payments of U.S. tax must be remitted to the IRS in U.S. dollars. [Digital assets](https://www.irs.gov/businesses/small-businesses-self-employed/digital-assets) are **not** accepted. Go to [IRS.gov/Payments](https://www.irs.gov/payments) for information on how to make a payment using any of the following options.

  

**纳税。** 

美国税款必须以美元汇给 IRS。**不**接受[数字资产](https://www.irs.gov/businesses/small-businesses-self-employed/digital-assets)。请访问[IRS.gov/Payments](https://www.irs.gov/payments) ，了解有关如何使用以下任一选项进行付款的信息。

*   [IRS Direct Pay](https://www.irs.gov/directpay): Pay your individual tax bill or estimated tax payment directly from your checking or savings account at no cost to you.  
    [IRS 直接付款](https://www.irs.gov/directpay)：直接从您的支票或储蓄账户支付您的个人税单或预估税款，无需支付任何费用。
    
*   [Debit Card, Credit Card, or Digital Wallet](https://www.irs.gov/payments/pay-your-taxes-by-debit-or-credit-card): Choose an approved payment processor to pay online or by phone.  
    [借记卡、信用卡或数字钱包](https://www.irs.gov/payments/pay-your-taxes-by-debit-or-credit-card)：选择经批准的支付处理商进行在线或电话支付。
    
*   [Electronic Funds Withdrawal](https://www.irs.gov/efw): Schedule a payment when filing your federal taxes using tax return preparation software or through a tax professional.  
    [电子资金提款](https://www.irs.gov/efw)：使用纳税申报表准备软件或通过税务专业人员提交联邦税时安排付款。
    
*   [Electronic Federal Tax Payment System](https://www.irs.gov/eftps): Best option for businesses. Enrollment is required.  
    [电子联邦纳税系统](https://www.irs.gov/eftps)：企业的最佳选择。需要报名。
    
*   [Check or Money Order](https://www.irs.gov/payments/pay-by-check-or-money-order): Mail your payment to the address listed on the notice or instructions.  
    [支票或汇票](https://www.irs.gov/payments/pay-by-check-or-money-order)：将您的付款邮寄到通知或说明中列出的地址。
    
*   [Cash](https://www.irs.gov/payments/pay-with-cash-at-a-retail-partner): You may be able to pay your taxes with cash at a participating retail store.  
    [现金](https://www.irs.gov/payments/pay-with-cash-at-a-retail-partner)：您可以在参与计划的零售店用现金缴税。
    
*   [Same-Day Wire](https://www.irs.gov/samedaywire): You may be able to do same-day wire from your financial institution. Contact your financial institution for availability, cost, and time frames.  
    [当日电汇](https://www.irs.gov/samedaywire)：您也许可以从金融机构进行当日电汇。请联系您的金融机构了解可用性、费用和时间范围。
    

### Note.

The IRS uses the latest encryption technology to ensure that the electronic payments you make online, by phone, or from a mobile device using the IRS2Go app are safe and secure. Paying electronically is quick, easy, and faster than mailing in a check or money order.

  

### 笔记。

IRS 使用最新的加密技术来确保您使用 IRS2Go 应用程序在线、通过电话或移动设备进行的电子支付安全可靠。电子支付比邮寄支票或汇票快捷、方便且快捷。

**What if I can’t pay now?**

Go to [IRS.gov/Payments](https://www.irs.gov/payments) for more information about your options.

  

**如果我现在无法付款怎么办？**

请访问[IRS.gov/Payments](https://www.irs.gov/payments)了解有关您的选择的更多信息。

*   Apply for an [online payment agreement](https://www.irs.gov/opa) ([IRS.gov/OPA](https://www.irs.gov/opa)) to meet your tax obligation in monthly installments if you can’t pay your taxes in full today. Once you complete the online process, you will receive immediate notification of whether your agreement has been approved.  
    如果您今天无法全额缴纳税款，请申请[在线付款协议](https://www.irs.gov/opa)( [IRS.gov/OPA](https://www.irs.gov/opa) )，以按月分期付款履行纳税义务。完成在线流程后，您将立即收到有关您的协议是否已获得批准的通知。
    
*   Use the [Offer in Compromise Pre-Qualifier](https://irs.treasury.gov/oic_pre_qualifier/) to see if you can settle your tax debt for less than the full amount you owe. For more information on the Offer in Compromise program, go to [IRS.gov/OIC](https://www.irs.gov/oic).  
    [在妥协预选赛中使用该优惠](https://irs.treasury.gov/oic_pre_qualifier/)看看您是否可以以低于您所欠全额的金额清偿您的税款。有关妥协要约计划的更多信息，请访问[IRS.gov/OIC](https://www.irs.gov/oic) 。
    

**Filing an amended return.**

Go to [IRS.gov/Form1040X](https://www.IRS.gov/Form1040X) for information and updates.

  

**提交修改后的申报表。** 

请访问[IRS.gov/Form1040X](https://www.IRS.gov/Form1040X)了解信息和更新。

**Checking the status of your amended return.**

Go to [IRS.gov/WMAR](https://www.irs.gov/wmar) to track the status of Form 1040-X amended returns.

  

**检查修改后的申报表的状态。** 

请访问[IRS.gov/WMAR](https://www.irs.gov/wmar)跟踪 1040-X 表格修订申报表的状态。

.![](https://www.irs.gov/pub/xml_bc/caution.gif)
_It can take up to 3 weeks from the date you filed your amended return for it to show up in our system, and processing it can take up to 16 weeks.  
从您提交修改后的纳税申报表之日起，最多可能需要 3 周的时间才能将其显示在我们的系统中，而处理该纳税申报表最多可能需要 16 周的时间。_.

**Understanding an IRS notice or letter you’ve received.**

Go to [IRS.gov/Notices](https://www.irs.gov/notices) to find additional information about responding to an IRS notice or letter.

  

**了解您收到的 IRS 通知或信件。** 

请访问[IRS.gov/Notices](https://www.irs.gov/notices)查找有关回复 IRS 通知或信件的更多信息。

**Responding to an IRS notice or letter.**

You can now upload responses to all notices and letters using the Document Upload Tool. For notices that require additional action, taxpayers will be redirected appropriately on IRS.gov to take further action. To learn more about the tool, go to [IRS.gov/Upload](https://www.irs.gov/help/irs-document-upload-tool).

  

**回复 IRS 通知或信件。** 

您现在可以使用文档上传工具上传对所有通知和信件的回复。对于需要采取额外行动的通知，纳税人将在 IRS.gov 上适当重定向以采取进一步行动。要了解有关该工具的更多信息，请访问[IRS.gov/Upload](https://www.irs.gov/help/irs-document-upload-tool) 。

### Note.

You can use Schedule LEP (Form 1040), Request for Change in Language Preference, to state a preference to receive notices, letters, or other written communications from the IRS in an alternative language. You may not immediately receive written communications in the requested language. The IRS’s commitment to LEP taxpayers is part of a multi-year timeline that began providing translations in 2023. You will continue to receive communications, including notices and letters, in English until they are translated to your preferred language.

  

### 笔记。

您可以使用附表 LEP（表格 1040）“语言偏好变更请求”来表明偏好以其他语言接收 IRS 发出的通知、信件或其他书面通信。您可能不会立即收到以所要求的语言提供的书面通信。 IRS 对 LEP 纳税人的承诺是从 2023 年开始提供翻译的多年时间表的一部分。您将继续收到英文通讯，包括通知和信件，直到它们被翻译成您的首选语言。

**Contacting your local TAC.**

Keep in mind, many questions can be answered on IRS.gov without visiting a TAC. Go to [IRS.gov/LetUsHelp](https://www.irs.gov/letushelp) for the topics people ask about most. If you still need help, TACs provide tax help when a tax issue can’t be handled online or by phone. All TACs now provide service by appointment, so you’ll know in advance that you can get the service you need without long wait times. Before you visit, go to [IRS.gov/TACLocator](https://www.irs.gov/taclocator) to find the nearest TAC and to check hours, available services, and appointment options. Or, on the IRS2Go app, under the Stay Connected tab, choose the Contact Us option and click on “Local Offices.”

  

**联系您当地的 TAC。** 

请记住，许多问题无需访问 TAC 即可在 IRS.gov 上得到解答。请访问[IRS.gov/LetUsHelp](https://www.irs.gov/letushelp)了解人们最常询问的主题。如果您仍需要帮助，当税务问题无法在线或通过电话处理时，TAC 可以提供税务帮助。所有 TAC 现在都提供预约服务，因此您会提前知道您可以获得所需的服务，而无需长时间等待。在您前往之前，请访问[IRS.gov/TACLocator](https://www.irs.gov/taclocator)查找最近的 TAC 并查看营业时间、可用服务和预约选项。或者，在 IRS2Go 应用程序的“保持联系”选项卡下，选择“联系我们”选项，然后单击“本地办事处”。

#### The Taxpayer Advocate Service (TAS) Is Here To Help You  
纳税人倡导服务 (TAS) 随时为您提供帮助

#### What Is TAS?什么是 TAS？

TAS is an independent organization within the IRS that helps taxpayers and protects taxpayer rights. TAS strives to ensure that every taxpayer is treated fairly and that you know and understand your rights under the [Taxpayer Bill of Rights](https://www.taxpayeradvocate.irs.gov/get-help/taxpayer-rights).  
TAS 是 IRS 内的一个独立组织，旨在帮助纳税人并保护纳税人的权利。 TAS 努力确保每一位纳税人都受到公平对待，并确保您了解并理解[《纳税人权利法案》](https://www.taxpayeradvocate.irs.gov/get-help/taxpayer-rights)规定的您的权利。

#### How Can You Learn About Your Taxpayer Rights?  
您如何了解您的纳税人权利？

The Taxpayer Bill of Rights describes 10 basic rights that all taxpayers have when dealing with the IRS. Go to [TaxpayerAdvocate.IRS.gov](https://www.taxpayeradvocate.irs.gov/) to help you understand what these rights mean to you and how they apply. These are **_**your**_** rights. Know them. Use them.  
纳税人权利法案描述了所有纳税人在与 IRS 打交道时所享有的 10 项基本权利。请访问[TaxpayerAdvocate.IRS.gov](https://www.taxpayeradvocate.irs.gov/) ，帮助您了解这些权利对您意味着什么以及它们如何适用。这些是**_**你的**_**权利。了解他们。使用它们。

#### What Can TAS Do for You?  
TAS 能为您做什么？

TAS can help you resolve problems that you can’t resolve with the IRS. And their service is free. If you qualify for their assistance, you will be assigned to one advocate who will work with you throughout the process and will do everything possible to resolve your issue. TAS can help you if:  
TAS 可以帮助您解决 IRS 无法解决的问题。而且他们的服务是免费的。如果您有资格获得他们的帮助，您将被分配给一名倡导者，他将在整个过程中与您合作，并尽一切可能解决您的问题。如果出现以下情况，TAS 可以为您提供帮助：

*   Your problem is causing financial difficulty for you, your family, or your business;  
    您的问题正在给您、您的家人或您的企业带来财务困难；
    
*   You face (or your business is facing) an immediate threat of adverse action; or  
    您面临（或您的企业面临）不利行动的直接威胁；或者
    
*   You’ve tried repeatedly to contact the IRS but no one has responded, or the IRS hasn’t responded by the date promised.  
    您已多次尝试联系 IRS，但无人回复，或者 IRS 未在承诺的日期前回复。
    

#### How Can You Reach TAS?  
如何才能到达 TAS？

TAS has offices [in every state, the District of Columbia, and Puerto Rico](https://www.irs.gov/advocate/local-taxpayer-advocate). To find your advocate’s number:  
TAS[在每个州、哥伦比亚特区和波多黎各均](https://www.irs.gov/advocate/local-taxpayer-advocate)设有办事处。要查找您的辩护人的电话号码：

*   Go to [TaxpayerAdvocate.IRS.gov/Contact-Us](https://www.TaxpayerAdvocate.IRS.gov/contact-us);  
    前往[TaxpayerAdvocate.IRS.gov/Contact-Us](https://www.TaxpayerAdvocate.IRS.gov/contact-us) ；
    
*   Download Pub. 1546, The Taxpayer Advocate Service Is Your Voice at the IRS, available at [IRS.gov/pub/irs-pdf/p1546.pdf](https://www.irs.gov/pub/irs-pdf/p1546.pdf);  
    下载酒吧。 1546，《纳税人倡导服务是您在国税局的声音》，可在[IRS.gov/pub/irs-pdf/p1546.pdf](https://www.irs.gov/pub/irs-pdf/p1546.pdf)获取；
    
*   Call the IRS toll free at 800-TAX-FORM (800-829-3676) to order a copy of Pub. 1546;  
    请拨打 IRS 免费电话 800-TAX-FORM (800-829-3676) 订购 Pub 的副本。 1546;
    
*   Check your local directory; or  
    检查您的本地目录；或者
    
*   Call TAS toll free at 877-777-4778.  
    请拨打 TAS 免费电话 877-777-4778。
    

#### How Else Does TAS Help Taxpayers?  
TAS 还如何帮助纳税人？

TAS works to resolve large-scale problems that affect many taxpayers. If you know of one of these broad issues, report it to TAS at [IRS.gov/SAMS](https://www.irs.gov/sams). Be sure to not include any personal taxpayer information.  
TAS 致力于解决影响许多纳税人的大规模问题。如果您知道这些广泛问题之一，请通过[IRS.gov/SAMS](https://www.irs.gov/sams)向 TAS 报告。请务必不要包含任何个人纳税人信息。

#### Low Income Taxpayer Clinics (LITCs)  
低收入纳税人诊所 (LITC)

LITCs are independent from the IRS and TAS. LITCs represent individuals whose income is below a certain level and who need to resolve tax problems with the IRS. LITCs can represent taxpayers in audits, appeals, and tax collection disputes before the IRS and in court. In addition, LITCs can provide information about taxpayer rights and responsibilities in different languages for individuals who speak English as a second language. Services are offered for free or a small fee. For more information or to find an LITC near you, go to the LITC page at [TaxpayerAdvocate.IRS.gov/LITC](https://www.taxpayeradvocate.irs.gov/about-us/low-income-taxpayer-clinics-litc/) or see IRS Pub. 4134, [Low Income Taxpayer Clinic List](https://www.irs.gov/pub/irs-pdf/p4134.pdf), at [IRS.gov/pub/irs-pdf/4134.pdf](https://www.irs.gov/pub/irs-pdf/p4134.pdf).  
LITC 独立于 IRS 和 TAS。 LITC 代表收入低于一定水平且需要向 IRS 解决税务问题的个人。 LITC 可以在 IRS 和法庭上代表纳税人处理审计、上诉和税收纠纷。此外，LITC 还可以为以英语为第二语言的个人提供不同语言的有关纳税人权利和责任的信息。服务免费或收取少量费用。如需了解更多信息或查找您附近的 LITC，请访问[TaxpayerAdvocate.IRS.gov/LITC](https://www.taxpayeradvocate.irs.gov/about-us/low-income-taxpayer-clinics-litc/)的 LITC 页面或参阅 IRS Pub。 4134，[低收入纳税人诊所名单](https://www.irs.gov/pub/irs-pdf/p4134.pdf)，位于[IRS.gov/pub/irs-pdf/4134.pdf](https://www.irs.gov/pub/irs-pdf/p4134.pdf) 。
